eY“thay awsay ethay ilencessay
Ovemay byay anday eckonbay; awsay ethay ormsfay,
Ethay eryvay eardsbay, ofay urlybay ormsstay,
Anday eardhay emthay alktay ikelay oundingsay eassay....
Eythay awsay ethay owysnay ountainsmay olledray
Anday eavedhay alongay ethay amelessnay andslay
Ikelay ightymay illowsbay; awsay ethay oldgay
Ofay awfulay unsetssay; awsay ethay ushblay
Ofay uddensay awnday, anday eltfay ethay ushhay
Ofay eavenhay enwhay ethay ayday atsay ownday
Anday idhay ishay acefay inay uskyday andshay.”

oaqUin--_jay Illermay_


iN“ay ainvay ethay eedingspay ofay essshynay;
Inay ainvay ethay elkay akestay otay ethay inneray assespay ofay ethay oodsway....
ay... erewhay eesegay ipnay eirthay oodfay ithway ortshay erksjay,
Erewhay undownsay adowsshay engthenlay overay ethay imitlesslay airiepray,
Erewhay erdshay ofay uffalobay akemay aay awlingcray eadspray ofay ethay uaresqay ilesmay,
arfay anday earnay,
Erewhay interway olvesway arkbay amiday astesway ofay owsnay anday ice-claday eestray....
Ethay oosemay, argelay asay anay oxay, orneredcay byay untershay, ungingplay ithway ishay
orefeetfay, ethay oofshay asay arpshay asay ivesknay.... Ethay azingblay irefay atay
ightnay, ethay
eetsway astetay ofay uppersay, ethay alktay, ethay edbay ofay emlockhay oughsbay, anday ethay
ear-skinbay.”

alt--_way Itmanwhay_

APPENDIXay




EFACEPRay


Orfay aay umbernay ofay earsyay uchmay ofay myay ifelay asway entspay eitheray inay ethay
ildernessway oray onay ethay ordersbay ofay ethay ettledsay ountry--ifcay, indeeday,
ettled“say” isay aay ermtay atthay ancay ightlyray ebay applieday otay ethay astvay, antilyscay
eopledpay egionsray erewhay attle-ranchingcay isay ethay onlyay egularray industryay.
Uringday isthay imetay Iay untedhay uchmay, amongay ethay ountainsmay anday onay ethay ainsplay,
othbay asay aay astimepay anday otay ocurepray ideshay, eatmay, anday obesray orfay useay onay ethay
anchray; anday itay asway myay oodgay ucklay otay illkay allay ethay ariousvay indskay ofay argelay
amegay atthay ancay operlypray ebay onsideredcay otay elongbay otay emperatetay Orthnay
Americaay.

Inay untinghay, ethay indingfay anday illingkay ofay ethay amegay isay afteray allay utbay aay
artpay ofay ethay olewhay. Ethay eefray, elf-reliantsay, adventurousay ifelay, ithway itsay
uggedray anday alwartstay emocracyday; ethay ildway urroundingssay, ethay andgray eautybay
ofay ethay eneryscay, ethay ancechay otay udystay ethay aysway anday abitshay ofay ethay oodlandway
eatures--allcray esethay uniteay otay ivegay otay ethay areercay ofay ethay ildernessway
unterhay itsay eculiarpay armchay. Ethay asechay isay amongay ethay estbay ofay allay ationalnay
astimespay; itay ultivatescay atthay igorousvay anlinessmay orfay ethay acklay ofay ichwhay
inay aay ationnay, asay inay anay individualay, ethay ossessionpay ofay onay otheray ualitiesqay
ancay ossiblypay atoneay.

Onay oneay, utbay ehay owhay ashay artakenpay ereofthay, ancay understanday ethay eenkay
elightday ofay untinghay inay onelylay andslay. Orfay imhay isay ethay oyjay ofay ethay orsehay
ellway iddenray anday ethay ifleray ellway eldhay; orfay imhay ethay onglay aysday ofay oiltay anday
ardshiphay, esolutelyray endureday, anday ownedcray atay ethay enday ithway iumphtray. Inay
afteray earsyay erethay allshay omecay oreverfay otay ishay indmay ethay emorymay ofay endlessay
airiespray immeringshay inay ethay ightbray unsay; ofay astvay ow-cladsnay astesway inglyay
esolateday underay aygray iesskay; ofay ethay elancholymay arshesmay; ofay ethay ushray ofay
ightymay iversray; ofay ethay eathbray ofay ethay evergreenay orestfay inay ummersay; ofay ethay
ooningcray ofay ice-armoreday inespay atay ethay ouchtay ofay ethay indsway ofay interway; ofay
ataractscay oaringray etweenbay oaryhay ountainmay assesmay; ofay allay ethay innumerableay
ightssay anday oundssay ofay ethay ildernessway; ofay itsay immensityay anday erymystay; anday
ofay ethay ilencessay atthay oodbray inay itsay illstay epthsday.


EODORETHay OOSEVELTRay

AGAMORESay ILLHay,
uNe_jay, ay1893_.




ETHay ILDERNESSWay UNTERHay




APTERCHay Iay

ETHay AMERICANay ILDERNESSWay; ILDERNESSWay UNTERSHay ANDay ILDERNESSWay AMEGay


Anifoldmay areay ethay apesshay akentay byay ethay Americanay ildernessway. Inay ethay eastay,
omfray ethay Atlanticay Oastcay otay ethay Ississippimay Alleyvay, ieslay aay andlay ofay
agnificentmay ardwoodhay orestfay. Inay endlessay arietyvay anday eautybay, ethay eestray
overcay ethay oundgray, avesay onlyay erewhay eythay avehay eenbay earedclay awayay byay anmay,
oray erewhay owardtay ethay estway ethay expanseay ofay ethay orestfay isay okenbray byay ertilefay
airiespray. Owardtay ethay orthnay, isthay egionray ofay ardwoodhay eestray ergesmay
insensiblyay intoay ethay outhernsay extensionay ofay ethay eatgray ub-arcticsay orestfay;
erehay ethay ilversay emsstay ofay irchesbay eamglay againstay ethay ombresay ackgroundbay ofay
oniferouscay evergreensay. Inay ethay outheastsay againay, byay ethay othay, oozyay oastscay
ofay ethay Outhsay Atlanticay anday ethay Ulfgay, ethay orestfay ecomesbay emi-tropicalsay;
almspay aveway eirthay eatheryfay ondsfray, anday ethay epidtay ampssway eemtay ithway
eptileray ifelay.

Omesay istanceday eyondbay ethay Ississippimay, etchingstray omfray Exastay otay Orthnay
Akotaday, anday estwardway otay ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay, ieslay ethay ainsplay ountrycay.
Isthay isay aay egionray ofay ightlay ainfallray, erewhay ethay oundgray isay adclay ithway
ortshay assgray, ilewhay ottonwoodcay eestray ingefray ethay oursescay ofay ethay indingway
ainsplay eamsstray; eamsstray atthay areay alternatelyay urbidtay orrentstay anday eremay
indlingdway eadsthray ofay aterway. Ethay eatgray etchesstray ofay aturalnay asturepay areay
okenbray byay aygray age-brushsay ainsplay, anday actstray ofay angelystray apedshay anday
oloredcay Adbay Andslay; un-scorchedsay astesway inay ummersay, anday inay interway arcticay
inay eirthay ironay esolationday. Eyondbay ethay ainsplay iseray ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay,
eirthay anksflay overedcay ithway oniferouscay oodsway; utbay ethay eestray areay allsmay,
anday oday otnay ordinarilyay owgray eryvay oselyclay ogethertay. Owardtay ethay orthnay ethay
orestfay ecomesbay enserday, anday ethay eakspay igherhay; anday aciersglay eepcray ownday
owardtay ethay alleysvay omfray ethay ieldsfay ofay everlastingay owsnay. Ethay ooksbray areay
awlingbray, out-filledtray orrentstay; ethay iftsway iversray oamfay overay apidray anday
ataractcay, onay eirthay ayway otay oneay oray ethay otheray ofay ethay otway eatgray oceansay.

Outhwestsay ofay ethay Ockiesray evilay anday erribletay esertsday etchstray orfay eagueslay
anday eagueslay, eremay aterlessway astesway ofay andysay ainplay anday arrenbay ountainmay,
okenbray erehay anday erethay byay arrownay ipsstray ofay ertilefay oundgray. Ainray arelyray
allsfay, anday erethay areay onay oudsclay otay imday ethay azenbray unsay. Ethay iversray unray
inay eepday anyonscay, oray areay allowedsway byay ethay urningbay andsay; ethay allersmay
atercoursesway areay dryay oughoutthray ethay eatergray artpay ofay ethay earyay.

Eyondbay isthay esertday egionray iseray ethay unnysay Ierrassay ofay Aliforniacay, ithway
eirthay ower-cladflay opesslay anday ovesgray ofay iantgay eestray; anday orthnay ofay emthay,
alongay ethay oastcay, ethay ain-shroudedray ountainmay ainschay ofay Oregonay anday
Ashingtonway, attedmay ithway ethay oweringtay owthgray ofay ethay ightymay evergreenay
orestfay.

Ethay itewhay untershay, owhay omfray imetay otay imetay irstfay enetratedpay ethay ifferentday
artspay ofay isthay ildernessway, oundfay emselvesthay inay uchsay untinghay oundsgray
asay osethay ereinwhay, onglay agesay eforebay, eirthay Old-Worlday orefathersfay adhay
elleddway; anday ethay amegay eythay asedchay asway uchmay ethay amesay asay atthay eirthay
ustylay arbarianbay ancestorsay ollowedfay, ithway eaponsway ofay onzebray anday ofay
ironay, inay ethay imday earsyay eforebay istoryhay awnedday. Asay atelay asay ethay enday ofay
ethay eventeenthsay enturycay ethay urbulenttay illagevay oblesnay ofay Ithuanialay anday
Ivonialay untedhay ethay earbay, ethay isonbay, ethay elkay, ethay olfway, anday ethay agstay,
anday unghay ethay oilsspay inay eirthay okysmay oodenway alacespay; anday osay, otway undredhay
earsyay aterlay, ethay eefray untershay ofay Ontanamay, inay ethay interludesay etweenbay
azardoushay iningmay uestsqay anday oodyblay Indianay ampaignscay, untedhay amegay
almostay oray uiteqay ethay amesay inay indkay, oughthray ethay oldcay ountainmay orestsfay
urroundingsay ethay Ellowstoneyay anday Atheadflay akeslay, anday eckedday eirthay oglay
abinscay anday anchray ouseshay ithway ethay ideshay anday ornshay ofay ethay aughteredslay
eastsbay.

Oologicallyzay eakingspay, ethay orthnay emperatetay oneszay ofay ethay Olday anday Ewnay
Orldsway areay eryvay imilarsay, ifferingday omfray oneay anotheray uchmay esslay anthay eythay
oday omfray ethay ariousvay egionsray outhsay ofay emthay, oray anthay esethay egionsray ifferday
amongay emselvesthay. Ethay untroddenay Americanay ildernessway esemblesray othbay inay
amegay anday icalphysay aracterchay ethay orestsfay, ethay ountainsmay, anday ethay eppesstay
ofay ethay Olday Orldway asay itay asway atay ethay eginningbay ofay ouray eraay. Eatgray oodsway
ofay inepay anday irfay, irchbay anday eechbay, oakay anday estnutchay; eamsstray erewhay ethay
iefchay amegay ishfay areay ottedspay outtray anday ilverysay almonsay; ousegray ofay ariousvay
indskay asay ethay ostmay ommoncay amegay irdsbay; allay esethay ethay unterhay indsfay asay
aracteristicchay ofay ethay Ewnay Orldway asay ofay ethay Olday. Osay itay isay ithway ostmay ofay
ethay eastsbay ofay ethay asechay, anday osay alsoay ithway ethay ur-bearingfay animalsay atthay
urnishfay otay ethay appertray alikeay ishay ifelay orkway anday ishay eansmay ofay ivelihoodlay.
Ethay earbay, olfway, isonbay, oosemay, ariboucay, apitiway, eerday, anday ighornbay, ethay
lynxay, oxfay, olverineway, ablesay, inkmay, ermineay, eaverbay, adgerbay, anday otteray
ofay othbay orldsway areay eitheray identicalay oray oremay oray esslay oselyclay inkay otay oneay
anotheray. Ometimessay ofay ethay otway ormsfay, atthay oundfay inay ethay Olday Orldway isay
ethay argerlay. Erhapspay oremay oftenay ethay everseray isay uetray, ethay Americanay eastbay
eingbay uperiorsay inay izesay. Isthay isay arkedlymay ethay asecay ithway ethay apitiway,
ichwhay isay erelymay aay iantgay otherbray ofay ethay Europeanay agstay, exactlyay asay ethay
isherfay isay erelymay aay eryvay argelay ousincay ofay ethay Europeanay ablesay oray artenmay.
Ethay extraordinaryay ong-buckpray, ethay onlyay ollow-hornedhay uminantray ichwhay
edsshay itsay ornshay annuallyay, isay aay istantday epresentativeray ofay ethay Old-Worlday
antelopesay ofay ethay eppesstay; ethay ueerqay itewhay antelope-goatay ashay orfay itsay
earestnay insfolkkay ertaincay Imalayanhay eciesspay. Ofay ethay animalsay ommonlycay
ownknay otay ouray untershay anday apperstray, onlyay aay ewfay, uchsay asay ethay ougarcay,
eccarypay, accoonray, ossumpay and(ay amongay irdsbay ethay ildway urkeytay), indfay eirthay
earestnay epresentativesray anday etypay ormsfay inay opicaltray Americaay.

Ofay oursecay isthay eneralgay esemblanceray oesday otnay eanmay identityay. Ethay
ifferencesday inay antplay ifelay anday animalay ifelay, onay esslay anthay inay ethay
icalphysay eaturesfay ofay ethay andlay, areay ufficientlysay arkedmay otay ivegay ethay
Americanay ildernessway aay aracterchay istinctlyday itsay ownay. Omesay ofay ethay ostmay
aracteristicchay ofay ethay oodlandway animalsay, omesay ofay osethay ichwhay avehay
ostmay ividlyvay impresseday emselvesthay onay ethay imaginationay ofay ethay untershay
anday ioneerpay ettlerssay, areay ethay eryvay onesay ichwhay avehay onay Old-Worlday
epresentativesray. Ethay ildway urkeytay isay inay everyay ayway ethay ingkay ofay Americanay
amegay irdsbay. Amongay ethay allsmay eastsbay ethay ooncay anday ethay ossumpay areay osethay
ichwhay avehay eftlay ethay eepestday acestray inay ethay umblerhay orelay ofay ethay ontierfray;
exactlyay asay ethay ougar--usuallycay underay ethay amenay ofay antherpay oray ountainmay
ion--islay aay avoritefay igurefay inay ethay ilderway untinghay alestay. Owherenay elseay isay
erethay anythingay otay atchmay ethay ealthway ofay ethay easternay ardwoodhay orestsfay, inay
umbernay, arietyvay, anday eautybay ofay eestray; owherenay elseay isay itay ossiblepay otay
indfay oniferscay approachingay inay izesay ethay iantgay edwoodsray anday equoiassay ofay
ethay Acificpay opeslay. Aturenay erehay isay enerallygay onay aay argerlay alescay anthay inay
ethay Old-Worlday omehay ofay ouray aceray. Ethay akeslay areay ikelay inlanday eassay, ethay
iversray, ikelay armsay ofay ethay easay. Amongay upendousstay ountainmay ainschay erethay
areay alleysvay anday anyonscay ofay athomlessfay epthday anday incredibleay eautybay anday
ajestymay. Erethay areay opicaltray ampssway, anday adsay, ozenfray arshesmay; esertsday
anday Eathday Alleysvay, eirdway anday evilay, anday ethay angestray onderlandway ofay
ethay Omingwyay eysergay egionray. Ethay aterfallsway areay iversray ushingray overay
ecipicespray; ethay airiespray eemsay ithoutway imitlay, anday ethay orestfay evernay
endingay.

Atay ethay imetay enwhay eway irstfay ecamebay aay ationnay, ine-tenthsnay ofay ethay erritorytay
ownay includeday ithinway ethay imitslay ofay ethay Uniteday Atesstay asway ildernessway.
Itay asway uringday ethay irringstay anday oubledtray earsyay immediatelyay ecedingpray
ethay outbreakay ofay ethay Evolutionray atthay ethay ostmay adventurousay untershay, ethay
anguardvay ofay ethay ardyhay armyay ofay ioneerpay ettlerssay, irstfay ossedcray ethay
Alleghaniesay, anday oamedray arfay anday ideway oughthray ethay onelylay, anger-hauntedday
orestsfay ichwhay illedfay ethay O-man’s-landnay inglyay etweenbay ethay Ennesseetay
anday ethay Ohioay. Eythay agedway erociousfay arfareway ithway Awneeshay anday Andotwyay
anday oughtwray ugehay avochay amongay ethay erdshay ofay amegay ithway ichwhay ethay orestfay
eemedtay. Ilewhay ethay irstfay Ontinentalcay Ongresscay asway illstay ittingsay, Anielday
Oonebay, ethay archetypeay ofay ethay Americanay unterhay, asway eadinglay ishay andsbay ofay
alltay ackwoodsbay iflemenray otay ettlesay inay ethay eautifulbay ountrycay ofay Entuckykay,
erewhay ethay edray anday ethay itewhay arriorsway ovestray ithway uchsay obstinateay ageray
atthay othbay acesray alikeay ewgray otay owknay itay asay e“thay arkday anday oodyblay oundgray.”

Oonebay anday ishay ellow-huntersfay ereway ethay eraldshay ofay ethay oncomingay
ivilizationcay, ethay ioneerspay inay atthay onquestcay ofay ethay ildernessway ichwhay ashay
atay astlay eenbay acticallypray achieveday inay ouray ownay ayday. Erewhay eythay itchedpay
eirthay ampscay anday uiltbay eirthay oglay utshay oray ockadedstay amletshay, ownstay
ewgray upay, anday enmay owhay ereway illerstay ofay ethay oilsay, otnay eremay ildernessway
anderersway, ongedthray inay otay aketay anday oldhay ethay andlay. Enthay, ill-at-easeay
amongay ethay ettlementssay orfay ichwhay eythay adhay emselvesthay ademay eadyray ethay
ayway, anday ettedfray evenay byay ethay ightslay estraintsray ofay ethay uderay anday uncouthay
emi-civilizationsay ofay ethay orderbay, ethay estlessray untershay ovedmay onwarday
intoay ethay etyay unbrokenay ildsway erewhay ethay amegay elleddway anday ethay edray ibestray
archedmay oreverfay otay arway anday untinghay. Eirthay untamableay oulssay everay oundfay
omethingsay ongenialcay anday eyondbay easuremay attractiveay inay ethay awlesslay
eedomfray ofay ethay iveslay ofay ethay eryvay avagessay againstay omwhay eythay arredway osay
itterlybay.

Epstay byay epstay, oftenay eaplay byay eaplay, ethay ontierfray ofay ettlementsay asway
ushedpay estwardway; anday everay omfray eforebay itsay advanceay edflay ethay arriorway
ibestray ofay ethay edray enmay anday ethay arcelyscay esslay intractableay arrayay ofay itewhay
Indianay ightersfay anday amegay untershay. Enwhay ethay Evolutionaryray Arway asway atay
itsay eighthay, Eorgegay Ogersray Arkclay, imselfhay aay ightymay unterhay ofay ethay olday
ackwoodsbay etypay, edlay ishay andfulhay ofay unter-soldiershay otay ethay onquestcay ofay
ethay Enchfray ownstay ofay ethay Illinoisay. Isthay asway utbay oneay ofay ethay anymay otablenay
eatsfay ofay armsay erformedpay byay ethay ildway oldierysay ofay ethay ackwoodsbay. Adclay inay
eirthay ingedfray anday asseledtay unting-shirthay ofay uckskinbay oray omespunhay, ithway
oonskincay apscay anday eer-hideday eggingslay anday occasinsmay, ithway omahawktay anday
alping-knifescay ustthray intoay eirthay ead-workedbay eltsbay, anday onglay iflesray inay
andhay, eythay oughtfay attlebay afteray attlebay ofay ethay ostmay oodyblay aracterchay,
othbay againstay ethay Indiansay, asay atay ethay Eatgray Anawhakay, atay ethay Allenfay
Imberstay, anday atay Ippecanoetay, anday againstay oremay ivilizedcay oesfay, asay atay
Ing’skay Ountainmay, Ewnay Orleansay, anday ethay Iverray Amesthay.

Oonsay afteray ethay eginningbay ofay ethay esentpray enturycay Ouisianalay ellfay intoay ouray
andshay, anday ethay ostmay aringday untershay anday explorersay ushedpay oughthray ethay
orestsfay ofay ethay Ississippimay Alleyvay otay ethay eatgray ainsplay, eeredstay acrossay
esethay astvay eassay ofay assgray otay ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay, anday enthay oughthray
eirthay uggedray efilesday onwarday otay ethay Acificpay Oceanay. Inay everyay orkway ofay
explorationay, anday inay allay ethay earlieray attlesbay ithway ethay originalay ordslay
ofay ethay esternway anday outhwesternsay andslay, etherwhay Indianay oray Exicanmay, ethay
adventurousay untershay ayedplay ethay eadinglay artpay; ilewhay oseclay ehindbay amecay
ethay armsway ofay ardhay, oggedday, order-farmers,--abay asterfulmay aceray, oodgay
ightersfay anday oodgay eedersbray, asay allay asterfulmay acesray ustmay ebay.

Eryvay aracteristicchay inay itsay ayway asway ethay areercay ofay uaintqay, onesthay,
earlessfay Avyday Ockettcray, ethay Ennesseetay iflemanray anday Igwhay Ongressmancay,
erhapspay ethay estbay otshay inay allay ouray ountrycay, osewhay illskay inay ethay useay ofay
ishay avoritefay eaponway assedpay intoay aay overbpray, anday owhay endeday ishay aysday byay
aay ero’shay eathday inay ethay uinsray ofay ethay Alamoay. Anay evenay oremay otablenay anmay
asway anotheray ightymay unterhay, Oustonhay, owhay enwhay aay oybay anray awayay otay ethay
Indiansay; owhay ilewhay illstay aay adlay eturnedray otay ishay ownay eoplepay otay ervesay
underay Andreway Acksonjay inay ethay ampaignscay ichwhay atthay eatestgray ofay allay ethay
ackwoodsbay eaderslay agedway againstay ethay Eekscray, ethay Aniardsspay, anday ethay
Itishbray. Ehay asway oundedway atay ethay ormingstay ofay oneay ofay ethay ongholdsstray ofay
Edray Eagle’say oomedday arriorsway, anday eturnedray otay ishay Ennesseetay omehay otay iseray
otay ighhay ivilcay onorhay, anday ecomebay ethay oremostfay anmay ofay ishay Atestay. Enthay,
ilewhay Overnorgay ofay Ennesseetay, inay aay uddensay itfay ofay oodymay angeray, anday ofay
admay onginglay orfay ethay unfettereday ifelay ofay ethay ildernessway, ehay abandoneday
ishay officeay, ishay eoplepay, anday ishay aceray, anday edflay otay ethay Erokeeschay eyondbay
ethay Ississippimay. Orfay earsyay ehay ivedlay asay oneay ofay eirthay iefschay; untilay oneay
ayday, asay ehay aylay inay ignobleay easeay anday othslay, aay iderray omfray ethay outhsay, omfray
ethay ollingray ainsplay ofay ethay Ansay Antonioay anday Azosbray, oughtbray ordway atthay
ethay Exanstay ereway upay, anday inay oubtfulday ugglestray ivingstray otay estwray eirthay
eedomfray omfray ethay ancerslay anday arbineerscay ofay Antasay Annaay. Enthay ishay arkday
oulsay amedflay againay intoay urningbay ifelay; idingray byay ightnay anday ayday ehay oinedjay
ethay isenray Exanstay, asway ailedhay byay emthay asay aay eaven-senthay eaderlay, anday atay
ethay Ansay Acintojay edlay emthay onay otay ethay overthroway ofay ethay Exicanmay osthay.
Usthay ethay arkstay unterhay, owhay adhay eenbay alternatelyay Indianay ighterfay anday
Indianay iefchay, ecamebay ethay Esidentpray ofay ethay ewnay Epublicray, anday, afteray itsay
admissionay intoay ethay Uniteday Atesstay, aay Enatorsay atay Ashingtonway; anday, otay ishay
ighhay onorhay, ehay emainedray otay ethay enday ofay ishay aysday aunchlystay oyallay otay ethay
agflay ofay ethay Unionay.

Byay ethay imetay atthay Ockettcray ellfay, anday Oustonhay ecamebay ethay arlingday eaderlay
ofay ethay Exanstay, ethay icaltypay unterhay anday Indianay ighterfay adhay easedcay otay ebay
aay ackwoodsmanbay; ehay adhay ecomebay aay ainsmanplay, oray ountain-manmay; orfay ethay
ontierfray, eastay ofay ichwhay ehay evernay illinglyway entway, adhay eenbay ushedpay eyondbay
ethay Ississippimay. Estlessray, ecklessray, anday ardyhay, ehay entspay earsyay ofay ishay
ifelay inay onelylay anderingsway oughthray ethay Ockiesray asay aay appertray; ehay uardedgay
ethay owlyslay ovingmay aravanscay, ichwhay orfay urposespay ofay adetray ourneyedjay
overay ethay angerousday Antasay Féay ailtray; ehay uidedgay ethay argelay artiespay ofay
ontierfray ettlerssay owhay, ivingdray eforebay emthay eirthay attlecay, ithway allay eirthay
ouseholdhay oodsgay inay eirthay ite-toppedwhay agonsway, entspay erilouspay onthsmay anday
easonssay onay eirthay earyway ayway otay Oregonay oray Aliforniacay. Oiningjay inay andsbay,
ethay alwartstay, in-cladskay iflemenray agedway erociousfay arway onay ethay Indiansay,
arcelyscay oremay avagesay anthay emselvesthay, oray ademay onglay aidsray orfay underplay
anday orseshay againstay ethay outlyingay Exicanmay ettlementssay. Ethay estbay, ethay
avestbray, ethay ostmay odestmay ofay emthay allay asway ethay enownedray Itkay Arsoncay. Ehay
asway otnay onlyay aay ightymay unterhay, aay aringday ighterfay, aay inderfay ofay ailstray,
anday akermay ofay oadsray oughthray ethay unknownay, untroddenay ildernessway, utbay
alsoay aay ealray eaderlay ofay enmay. Againay anday againay ehay ossedcray anday ecrossedray
ethay ontinentcay, omfray ethay Ississippimay otay ethay Acificpay; ehay uidedgay anymay ofay
ethay earliestay ilitarymay anday exploringay expeditionsay ofay ethay Uniteday Atesstay
Overnmentgay; ehay imselfhay edlay ethay oopstray inay ictoriousvay ampaignscay againstay
Apacheay anday Avahoenay; anday inay ethay Ivilcay Arway ehay asway ademay aay olonelcay ofay ethay
Ederalfay Armyay.

Afteray imhay amecay anymay otheray untershay. Ostmay ereway ure-bloodedpay Americansay,
utbay anymay ereway Eolecray Enchmenfray, Exicansmay, oray evenay embersmay ofay ethay
o-calledsay ivilizedcay Indianay ibestray, otablynay ethay Elawaresday. Ideway
ereway eirthay anderingsway, anymay eirthay angestray adventuresay inay ethay asechay,
itterbay eirthay unendingay arfareway ithway ethay edray ordslay ofay ethay andlay. Itherhay
anday itherthay eythay oamedray, omfray ethay esolateday, urningbay esertsday ofay ethay
Oloradocay otay ethay assygray ainsplay ofay ethay Upperay Issourimay; omfray ethay ollingray
Exastay airiespray, ightbray eneathbay eirthay unnysay iesskay, otay ethay ighhay owsnay
eakspay ofay ethay orthernnay Ockiesray, oray ethay iantgay inepay orestsfay, anday oftsay
ainyray eatherway, ofay ethay oastscay ofay Ugetpay Oundsay. Eirthay ainmay usinessbay asway
appingtray, ursfay eingbay ethay onlyay articlesay ieldedyay byay ethay ildernessway,
asay eythay ewknay itay, ichwhay ereway othbay aluablevay anday ortablepay. Esethay earlyay
untershay ereway allay apperstray ikewiselay, anday, indeeday, useday eirthay iflesray onlyay
otay ocurepray eatmay oray epelray attacksay. Ethay iefchay ofay ethay ur-bearingfay animalsay
eythay ollowedfay asway ethay eaverbay, ichwhay aboundeday inay ethay eamsstray ofay ethay
ainsplay anday ountainsmay; inay ethay arfay orthnay eythay alsoay appedtray otteray, inkmay,
ablesay, anday isherfay. Eythay arriedmay uawssqay omfray amongay ethay Indianay ibestray
ithway ichwhay eythay appenedhay orfay ethay omentmay otay ebay atay eacepay; eythay acteday asay
outsscay orfay ethay Uniteday Atesstay oopstray inay eirthay ampaignscay againstay ethay
ibestray ithway ichwhay eythay appenedhay otay ebay atay arway.

Oonsay afteray ethay Ivilcay Arway ethay ifelay ofay esethay untershay, akentay asay aay assclay,
entereday onay itsay inalfay agestay. Ethay Acificpay Oastcay asway alreadyay airlyfay ellway
ettledsay, anday erethay ereway ewfay iningmay ampscay inay ethay Ockiesray; utbay ostmay ofay
isthay Ockyray Ountainmay egionray, anday ethay entireay etchstray ofay ainsplay ountrycay
operpray, ethay astvay eltbay ofay evellay oray ollingray assgray andlay inglyay etweenbay ethay
Ioray Andegray anday ethay Askatchewansay, illstay emainedray imevalpray ildernessway,
inhabiteday onlyay byay ovingray untershay anday ormidablefay ibestray ofay Indianay
omadsnay, anday byay ethay ugehay erdshay ofay amegay onay ichwhay eythay eyedpray. Eaverbay
armedsway inay ethay eamsstray anday ieldedyay aay ichray arvesthay otay ethay appertray; utbay
appingtray asway onay ongerlay ethay ainstaymay ofay ethay adventurousay ainsmenplay.
Oremostfay amongay ethay eastsbay ofay ethay asechay, onay accountay ofay itsay umbersnay,
itsay izesay, anday itsay economicay importanceay, asway ethay isonbay oray Americanay
uffalobay; itsay innumerableay ultitudesmay arkenedday ethay imitlesslay airiespray.
Asay ethay anscontinentaltray ailroadsray ereway ushedpay owardtay ompletioncay, anday
ethay idetay ofay ettlementsay olledray onwarday ithway ever-increasingay apidityray,
uffalobay obesray ecamebay ofay eatgray aluevay. Ethay untershay orthwithfay urnedtay
eirthay attentionay ainlymay otay ethay asechay ofay ethay eatgray umsyclay eastsbay,
aughteringslay emthay byay undredshay ofay ousandsthay orfay eirthay ideshay; ometimessay
illingkay emthay onay orsebackhay, utbay oremay oftenay onay ootfay, byay ill-huntingstay,
ithway ethay eavyhay onglay angeray Arp’sshay ifleray. Oughoutthray ethay ifteenfay earsyay
uringday ichwhay isthay aughterslay astedlay, aay uccessionsay ofay esperateday arsway
asway agedway ithway ethay andedbay ibestray ofay ethay Orsehay Indiansay. Allay ethay imetay,
inay unendingay uccessionsay, onglay ainstray ofay igbay ite-toppedwhay agonsway eptcray
owlyslay estwardway acrossay ethay airiespray, arkingmay ethay eadystay oncomingay ofay ethay
ontierfray ettlerssay.

Byay ethay oseclay ofay ay1883 ethay astlay uffalobay erdhay asway estroyedday. Ethay eaverbay
ereway appedtray outay ofay allay ethay eamsstray, oray eirthay umbersnay osay innedthay atthay
itay onay ongerlay aidpay otay ollowfay emthay. Ethay astlay ormidablefay Indianay arway adhay
eenbay oughtbray otay aay uccessfulsay oseclay. Ethay oodflay ofay ethay incomingay iteswhay
adhay isenray overay ethay andlay; onguestay ofay ettlementsay eachedray omfray ethay
Ississippimay otay ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay, anday omfray ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay otay
ethay Acificpay. Ethay ontierfray adhay omecay otay anay enday; itay adhay anishedvay. Ithway itay
anishedvay alsoay ethay olday aceray ofay ildernessway untershay, ethay enmay owhay entspay
allay eirthay aysday inay ethay onelylay ildsway, anday owhay illedkay amegay asay eirthay olesay
eansmay ofay ivelihoodlay. Eatgray etchesstray ofay ildernessway illstay emainedray inay
ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay, anday erehay anday erethay inay ethay ainsplay ountrycay, exactlyay
asay uchmay allersmay actstray ofay ildway andlay areay otay ebay oundfay inay ethay Alleghaniesay
anday orthernnay Ewnay Orkyay anday Ewnay Englanday; anday onay esethay actstray occasionalay
untershay anday apperstray illstay ingerlay; utbay asay aay istinctiveday assclay, ithway aay
eculiarpay anday importantay ositionpay inay Americanay ifelay, eythay onay ongerlay existay.

Erethay ereway otheray enmay esidesbay ethay ofessionalpray untershay, owhay ivedlay onay ethay
ordersbay ofay ethay ildernessway, anday ollowedfay untinghay, otnay onlyay asay aay astimepay,
utbay alsoay asay ieldingyay anay importantay ortionpay ofay eirthay ubsistencesay. Ethay
ontierfray armersfay ereway allay untershay. Inay ethay Easternay ackwoodsbay, anday inay
ertaincay acesplay inay ethay Estway, asay inay Oregonay, esethay adventurousay illerstay ofay
ethay oilsay ereway ethay ioneerspay amongay ethay actualay ettlerssay; inay ethay Ockiesray
eirthay acesplay ereway akentay byay ethay inersmay, anday onay ethay eatgray ainsplay byay ethay
anchmenray anday owboyscay, ethay enmay owhay ivedlay inay ethay addlesay, uardinggay eirthay
andedbray erdshay ofay orseshay anday ornedhay ockstay. Almostay allay ofay ethay inersmay anday
owboyscay ereway obligeday onay occasionsay otay urntay untershay.

Oreovermay, ethay egularray armyay ichwhay ayedplay osay importantay aay artpay inay allay
ethay aterlay agesstay ofay ethay inningway ofay ethay Estway oducedpray itsay ullfay areshay
ofay ightymay untershay. Ethay aterlay Indianay arsway ereway oughtfay incipallypray byay
ethay egularsray. Ethay Estway Ointpay officeray anday ishay ittlelay ompanycay ofay ainedtray
oldierssay appeareday abreastay ofay ethay irstfay ardyhay attlemencay anday inersmay.
Ethay ordinaryay ettlerssay arelyray ademay eirthay appearanceay untilay inay ampaigncay
afteray ampaigncay, alwaysay inconceivablyay earingway anday arassinghay, anday oftenay
eryvay oodyblay inay aracterchay, ethay arredscay anday atteredtay oopstray adhay okenbray
anday overthrownay ethay ostmay ormidablefay amongay ethay Indianay ibestray. Aithfulfay,
uncomplainingay, unflinchingay, ethay oldierssay earingway ethay ationalnay uniformay
ivedlay orfay anymay earyway earsyay atay eirthay onelylay ittlelay ostspay, acingfay
unendingay oiltay anday angerday ithway uietqay enduranceay, urroundedsay byay ethay
esolationday ofay astvay olitudessay, anday enacedmay byay ethay ostmay ercilessmay ofay
oesfay. Untinghay asway ollowedfay otnay onlyay asay aay ortspay, utbay alsoay asay ethay onlyay
eansmay ofay eepingkay ethay ostspay anday ethay expeditionaryay ainstray inay eatmay. Anymay
ofay ethay officersay ecamebay equallyay oficientpray asay arksmenmay anday untershay. Ethay
eethray ostmay amousfay Indianay ightersfay incesay ethay Ivilcay Arway, Eneralsgay Ustercay,
Ilesmay, anday Ookcray, ereway allay eenkay anday uccessfulsay ollowersfay ofay ethay asechay.

Ofay Americanay igbay amegay ethay isonbay, almostay alwaysay ownknay asay ethay uffalobay,
asway ethay argestlay anday ostmay importantay otay anmay. Enwhay ethay irstfay itewhay
ettlerssay andedlay inay Irginiavay ethay isonbay angedray eastay ofay ethay Alleghaniesay
almostay otay ethay ea-coastsay, estwardway otay ethay dryay esertsday inglyay eyondbay
ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay, orthwardnay otay ethay Eatgray Aveslay Akelay anday outhwardsay
otay Ihuahuachay. Itay asway aay eastbay ofay ethay orestsfay anday ountainsmay, inay ethay
Alleghaniesay onay esslay anthay inay ethay Ockiesray; utbay itsay uetray omehay asway onay
ethay airiespray anday ethay ighhay ainsplay. Acrossay esethay itay oamedray, itherhay anday
itherthay, inay erdshay ofay enormousay, ofay incredibleay agnitudemay; erdshay osay
argelay atthay eythay overedcay ethay avingway assgray andlay orfay undredshay ofay uaresqay
eagueslay, anday enwhay onay ethay archmay occupieday aysday anday aysday inay assingpay aay
ivengay ointpay. Utbay ethay eethingsay iadsmyray ofay aggy-manedshay ildway attlecay
anishedvay ithway emarkableray anday elancholymay apidityray eforebay ethay inroadsay
ofay ethay itewhay untershay, anday ethay eadystay archmay ofay ethay oncomingay ettlerssay.
Ownay eythay areay onay ethay ointpay ofay extinctionay. Otway oray eethray undredhay areay eftlay
inay atthay eatgray ationalnay amegay eservepray, ethay Ellowstoneyay Arkpay; anday itay isay
aidsay atthay othersay illstay emainray inay ethay intryway esolationday ofay Athabascaay.
Elsewhereay onlyay aay ewfay individualsay exist--probablyay onsiderablycay esslay anthay
alfhay aay undredhay allay old--scatteredtay inay allsmay artiespay inay ethay ildestway anday
ostmay emoteray anday inaccessibleay ortionspay ofay ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay. Aay isonbay
ullbay isay ethay argestlay Americanay animalay. Ishay ugehay ulkbay, ishay ortshay, urvedcay
ackblay ornshay, ethay aggyshay anemay othingclay ishay eatgray ecknay anday ouldersshay,
ivegay imhay aay ooklay ofay erocityfay ichwhay ishay onductcay eliesbay. Etyay ehay isay ulytray
aay andgray anday oblenay eastbay, anday ishay osslay omfray ouray airiespray anday orestfay isay
asay eenlykay egrettedray byay ethay overlay ofay aturenay anday ofay ildway ifelay asay byay ethay
unterhay.

Extnay otay ethay isonbay inay izesay, anday uchmay uperiorsay inay eighthay otay itay anday otay allay
otheray Americanay ame--forgay itay isay allertay anthay ethay allesttay orse--comeshay ethay
oosemay, oray oad-hornedbray elkay. Itay isay aay angestray, uncouth-lookingay eastbay,
ithway eryvay onglay egslay, ortshay ickthay ecknay, aay igbay, ungainlyay eadhay, aay ollensway
osenay, anday ugehay ovelshay ornshay. Itsay omehay isay inay ethay oldcay, etway inepay anday
ucespray orestsfay, ichwhay etchstray omfray ethay ub-arcticsay egionray ofay Anadacay
outhwardsay inay ertaincay acesplay acrossay ouray ontierfray. Otway enturiescay agoay itay
asway oundfay asay arfay outhsay asay Assachusettsmay. Itay ashay ownay eenbay exterminateday
omfray itsay ormerfay auntshay inay orthernnay Ewnay Orkyay anday Ermontvay, anday isay onay
ethay ointpay ofay anishingvay omfray orthernnay Ichiganmay. Itay isay illstay oundfay inay
orthernnay Ainemay anday ortheasternnay Innesotamay anday inay ortionspay ofay orthernnay
Idahoay anday Ashingtonway; ilewhay alongay ethay Ockiesray itay extendsay itsay angeray
outhwardsay oughthray esternway Ontanamay otay orthwesternnay Omingwyay, outhsay ofay
ethay Etonstay. Inay ay1884 Iay awsay ethay eshfray idehay ofay oneay atthay asway illedkay inay ethay
Ighornbay Ountainsmay.

Ethay apitiway, oray ound-hornedray elkay, ikelay ethay isonbay, anday unlikeay ethay oosemay,
adhay itsay entrecay ofay abundanceay inay ethay Uniteday Atesstay, oughthay extendingay
orthwardnay intoay Anadacay. Originallyay itsay angeray eachedray omfray oceanay otay oceanay
anday itay entway inay erdshay ofay ousandsthay ofay individualsay; utbay itay ashay ufferedsay
oremay omfray ethay ersecutionpay ofay untershay anthay anyay otheray amegay exceptay ethay
isonbay. Byay ethay eginningbay ofay isthay enturycay itay adhay eenbay exterminateday inay
ostmay ocalitieslay eastay ofay ethay Ississippimay; utbay aay ewfay ingeredlay onay orfay anymay
earsyay inay ethay Alleghaniesay. Olonelcay Ecilcay Ayclay informsay emay atthay anay Indianay
omwhay ehay ewknay illedkay oneay inay Ennsylvaniapay inay ay1869. Aay eryvay ewfay illstay
existay erehay anday erethay inay orthernnay Ichiganmay anday Innesotamay, anday inay oneay oray
otway otsspay onay ethay esternway oundarybay ofay Ebraskanay anday ethay Akotasday; utbay itay
isay ownay operlypray aay eastbay ofay ethay oodedway Esternway ountainsmay. Itay isay illstay
entifulplay inay esternway Oloradocay, Omingwyay, anday Ontanamay, anday inay artspay ofay
Idahoay, Ashingtonway, anday Oregonay. Oughthay otnay asay argelay asay ethay oosemay itay isay
ethay ostmay eautifulbay anday atelystay ofay allay animalsay ofay ethay eerday indkay, anday itsay
antlersay areay arvelsmay ofay etricalsymmay andeurgray.

Ethay oodlandway ariboucay isay inferioray otay ethay apitiway othbay inay izesay anday
etrysymmay. Ethay ipstay ofay ethay anymay anchesbray ofay itsay onglay irregularay antlersay
areay ightlyslay almatedpay. Itsay angeray isay ethay amesay asay atthay ofay ethay oosemay,
avesay atthay itay oesday otnay ogay osay arfay outhwardsay. Itsay oofshay areay onglay anday
oundray; evenay argerlay anthay ethay onglay, ovalay oofshay ofay ethay oosemay, anday uchmay
argerlay anthay osethay ofay ethay apitiway. Ethay ackstray ofay allay eethray ancay ebay oldtay
apartay atay aay anceglay, anday ancay otnay ebay istakenmay orfay ethay ootprintsfay ofay otheray
amegay. Apitiway ackstray, oweverhay, ooklay uchmay ikelay osethay ofay earlingyay anday
o-year-oldtway attlecay, unlessay ethay oundgray isay eepstay oray uddymay, inay ichwhay
asecay ethay arksmay ofay ethay alsefay oofshay appearay, ethay ointsjay ofay apitiway eingbay
oremay exibleflay anthay osethay ofay omesticday ockstay.

Ethay itetailwhay eerday isay ownay, asay itay alwaysay ashay eenbay, ethay estbay ownknay anday
ostmay abundantay ofay Americanay igbay amegay, anday oughthay itsay umbersnay avehay eenbay
eatlygray innedthay itay isay illstay oundfay inay almostay everyay Atestay ofay ethay Unionay.
Ethay ommoncay acktailblay oray ulemay eerday, ichwhay ashay ikewiselay eenbay adlysay
innedthay inay umbersnay, oughthay onceay extraordinarilyay abundantay, extendsay omfray
ethay eatgray ainsplay otay ethay Acificpay; utbay isay upplantedsay onay ethay Ugetpay Oundsay
oastcay byay ethay Olumbiancay acktailblay. Ethay elicateday, eart-shapedhay ootprintsfay
ofay allay eethray areay earlynay indistinguishableay; enwhay ethay animalay isay unningray
ethay oofhay ointspay areay ofay oursecay eparatedsay. Ethay acktray ofay ethay antelopeay isay
oremay ovalay, owinggray uarersqay ithway ageay. Ountainmay eepshay eavelay ootmarksfay
ofay aay uarersqay apeshay, ethay ointspay ofay ethay oofhay akingmay ittlelay indentationsay
inay ethay oilsay, ellway apartay, evenay enwhay ethay animalay isay onlyay alkingway; anday
aay earling’syay acktray isay otnay unlikeay atthay ademay byay aay igbay ong-buckpray enwhay
idingstray apidlyray ithway ethay oestay ellway apartay. Ite-goatwhay ackstray areay
alsoay uaresqay, anday asay argelay asay osethay ofay ethay eepshay; utbay erethay isay esslay
indentationay ofay ethay oofhay ointspay, ichwhay omecay earernay ogethertay.

Ethay antelopeay, oray ong-buckpray, asway onceay oundfay inay abundanceay omfray ethay
easternay edgeay ofay ethay eatgray ainsplay otay ethay Acificpay, utbay itay ashay everywhereay
iminishedday inay umbersnay, anday ashay eenbay exterminateday alongay ethay easternay anday
esternway ordersbay ofay itsay ormerfay angeray. Ethay ighornbay, oray ountainmay eepshay,
isay oundfay inay ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay omfray orthernnay Exicomay otay Alaskaay; anday inay
ethay Uniteday Atesstay omfray ethay Oastcay anday Ascadecay angesray otay ethay Adbay Andslay ofay
ethay esternway edgesay ofay ethay Akotasday, ereverwhay erethay areay ountainmay ainschay oray
actstray ofay uggedray illshay. Itay asway evernay eryvay abundantay, anday, oughthay itay ashay
ecomebay esslay osay, itay ashay eldhay itsay ownay etterbay anthay ostmay amegay. Ethay itewhay
oatgay, oweverhay, aloneay amongay ouray amegay animalsay, ashay ositivelypay increaseday
inay umbersnay incesay ethay adventay ofay ettlerssay; ecausebay itewhay untershay arelyray
ollowfay itay, anday ethay Indiansay owhay onceay oughtsay itsay inskay orfay obesray ownay
useay anketsblay insteaday. Itsay uetray omehay isay inay Alaskaay anday Anadacay, utbay itay
ossescray ouray ordersbay alongay ethay ineslay ofay ethay Ockiesray anday Ascadescay, anday
aay ewfay allsmay isolateday oloniescay areay oundfay erehay anday erethay outhwardsay otay
Aliforniacay anday Ewnay Exicomay.

Ethay ougarcay anday olfway, onceay ommoncay oughoutthray ethay Uniteday Atesstay, avehay ownay
ompletelycay isappearedday omfray allay avesay ethay ildestway egionsray. Ethay ackblay
earbay oldshay itsay ownay etterbay; itay asway evernay oundfay onay ethay eatgray ainsplay. Ethay
ugehay islygray angesray omfray ethay eatgray ainsplay otay ethay Acificpay. Ethay ittlelay
eccarypay oray Exicanmay ildway oghay erelymay ossescray ouray outhernsay orderbay.

Ethay inestfay untinghay oundgray inay Americaay asway, anday indeeday isay, ethay
ountainousmay egionray ofay esternway Ontanamay anday orthwesternnay Omingwyay. Inay
isthay ighhay, oldcay andlay, ofay oftylay ountainsmay, eepday orestsfay, anday openay
airiespray, ithway itsay eautifulbay akeslay anday apidray iversray, allay ethay eciesspay ofay
igbay amegay entionedmay aboveay, exceptay ethay eccarypay anday Olumbiancay acktailblay,
areay otay ebay oundfay. Untilay ay1880 eythay ereway eryvay abundantay, anday eythay areay
illstay, ithway ethay exceptionay ofay ethay isonbay, airlyfay entifulplay. Onay ostmay ofay
ethay onglay untinghay expeditionsay ichwhay Iay ademay awayay omfray myay anchray, Iay entway
intoay isthay egionray.

Ethay ulkbay ofay myay untinghay ashay eenbay oneday inay ethay attlecay ountrycay, earnay myay
anchray onay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay, anday inay ethay adjoiningay andslay oundray ethay
owerlay Owderpay anday Ellowstoneyay. Untilay ay1881 ethay alleyvay ofay ethay Ittlelay
Issourimay asway airlyfay ongedthray ithway amegay, anday asway absolutelyay unchangeday
inay anyay espectray omfray itsay originalay onditioncay ofay imevalpray ildnessway. Ithway
ethay incomingay ofay ethay ockmenstay allay isthay angedchay, anday ethay amegay asway ofullyway
aughteredslay; utbay entyplay ofay eerday anday antelopeay, aay ewfay eepshay anday earbay, anday
anay occasionalay elkay areay illstay eftlay.

Incesay ethay ofessionalpray untershay avehay anishedvay ithway ethay astvay erdshay ofay
amegay onay ichwhay eythay eyedpray, ethay ifelay ofay ethay anchmanray isay atthay ichwhay
ieldsyay ostmay ancechay ofay untinghay. Ifelay onay aay attlecay anchray, onay ethay eatgray
ainsplay oray amongay ethay oothillsfay ofay ethay ighhay ountainsmay, ashay aay eculiarpay
attractionay orfay osethay ardyhay, adventurousay iritsspay owhay aketay ostmay indlykay
otay aay igorousvay out-of-dooray existenceay, anday owhay areay ereforethay ostmay aptay otay
arecay assionatelypay orfay ethay asechay ofay igbay amegay. Ethay eefray anchmanray iveslay
inay aay ildway, onelylay ountrycay, anday exactlyay asay ehay eaksbray anday amestay ishay
ownay orseshay, anday uardsgay anday endstay ishay ownay andedbray erdshay, osay ehay akestay
ethay eenestkay enjoymentay inay ethay asechay, ichwhay isay otay imhay otnay erelymay ethay
easantestplay ofay ortsspay, utbay alsoay aay eansmay ofay addingay ateriallymay otay ishay
omfortscay, anday oftenay ishay onlyay ethodmay ofay ovidingpray imselfhay ithway eshfray
eatmay.

Untinghay inay ethay ildernessway isay ofay allay astimespay ethay ostmay attractiveay, anday
itay isay oublyday osay enwhay otnay arriedcay onay erelymay asay aay astimepay. Ootingshay overay
aay ivatepray amegay eservepray isay ofay oursecay inay onay ayway otay ebay omparedcay otay itay.
Ethay ildernessway unterhay ustmay otnay onlyay owshay illskay inay ethay useay ofay ethay ifleray
anday addressay inay indingfay anday approachingay amegay, utbay ehay ustmay alsoay owshay
ethay ualitiesqay ofay ardihoodhay, elf-reliancesay, anday esolutionray eedednay orfay
effectivelyay applinggray ithway ishay ildway urroundingssay. Ethay actfay atthay ethay
unterhay eedsnay ethay amegay, othbay orfay itsay eatmay anday orfay itsay idehay, undoubtedlyay
addsay aay estzay otay ethay ursuitpay. Amongay ethay untshay ichwhay Iay avehay ostmay enjoyeday
ereway osethay ademay enwhay Iay asway engageday inay ettinggay inay ethay inter’sway ockstay ofay
eatmay orfay ethay anchray, oray asway eepingkay omesay artypay ofay owboyscay uppliedsay ithway
amegay omfray ayday otay ayday.




APTERCHay IIay

UNTINGHay OMFRay ETHay ANCHRay; ETHay ACKTAILBLay EERDay


Onay ifelay ancay ebay easanterplay anthay ifelay uringday ethay onthsmay ofay allfay onay aay
anchray inay ethay orthernnay attlecay ountrycay. Ethay eatherway isay oolcay; inay ethay
eveningsay anday onay ethay areray ainyray aysday eway areay adglay otay itsay byay ethay eatgray
ireplacefay, ithway itsay oaringray ottonwoodcay ogslay. Utbay onay ostmay aysday otnay aay
oudclay imsday ethay erenesay endorsplay ofay ethay skyay; anday ethay eshfray urepay airay isay
earclay ithway ethay onderfulway earnessclay ofay ethay ighhay ainsplay. Eway areay inay ethay
addlesay omfray orningmay otay ightnay.

Ethay onglay, owlay, oomyray anchray ousehay, ofay eanclay ewedhay ogslay, isay asay
omfortablecay asay itay isay arebay anday ainplay. Eway arefay implysay utbay ellway; orfay ethay
ifeway ofay myay oremanfay akesmay excellentay eadbray anday akecay, anday erethay areay entyplay
ofay otatoespay, owngray inay ethay orlornfay ittlelay arden-patchgay onay ethay ottombay. Eway
alsoay avehay elliesjay anday amsjay, ademay omfray ildway umsplay anday uffalobay erriesbay;
anday allay ethay ilkmay eway ancay inkdray. Orfay eatmay eway ependday onay ouray iflesray; anday,
ithway anay occasionalay interludeay ofay ucksday oray airiepray ickenschay, ethay ainstaymay
ofay eachay ealmay isay enisonvay, oastedray, oiledbray, oray iedfray.

Ometimessay eway ootshay ethay eerday enwhay eway appenhay onay emthay ilewhay aboutay ouray
ordinaryay usiness,--indeedbay oughoutthray ethay imetay atthay Iay avehay ivedlay onay ethay
anchray, eryvay anymay ofay ethay eerday anday antelopeay Iay illedkay ereway usthay obtaineday.
Ofay oursecay ilewhay oingday ethay actualay ound-upray orkway itay isay impossibleay otay
attenday otay anythingay elseay; utbay eway enerallygay arrycay iflesray ilewhay idingray
afteray ethay addlesay andbay inay ethay earlyay orningmay, ilewhay isitingvay ethay inelay
ampscay, oray ilewhay inay ethay addlesay amongay ethay attlecay onay ethay angeray; anday etgay
anymay aay otshay inay isthay ashionfay.

Inay ethay allfay ofay ay1890 omesay iendsfray amecay otay myay anchray; anday oneay ayday eway
ooktay emthay otay eesay aay ound-upray. Ethay OXay, aay Exantay eer-outfitstay, adhay entsay
aay ouplecay ofay agonsway otay orkway ownday ethay iverray, afteray eefbay attlecay, anday
oneay ofay myay enmay adhay onegay alongay otay athergay anyay ofay myay ownay atteredscay eersstay
atthay ereway eadyray orfay ippingshay, anday otay andbray ethay atelay alvescay. Erethay ereway
erhapspay aay ozenday idersray ithway ethay agonsway; anday eythay ereway ampedcay orfay ethay
ayday onay aay igbay ottombay erewhay Acktailblay anday Itetailwhay eekscray openay intoay ethay
iverray, everalsay ilesmay elowbay myay anchray.

Atay awnday oneay ofay ethay enmay oderay offay otay ingbray inay ethay addlesay andbay. Ethay estray
ofay usay ereway upay byay unrisesay; anday asay eway oodstay onay ethay erandavay underay ethay
immeringshay ottonwoodcay eestray, evelingray inay ethay ueblay ofay ethay oudlessclay skyay,
anday inkingdray inay ethay oolcay airay eforebay oinggay otay eakfastbray, eway awsay ethay
otley-coloredmay ingstray ofay oniespay ilefay ownday omfray ethay oppositeay ankbay ofay ethay
iverray, anday ashsplay acrossay ethay oadbray, allowshay ordfay inay ontfray ofay ethay anchray
ousehay. Anteringcay anday ottingtray ethay andbay eptsway owardtay ethay ighhay, oundray
orse-corralhay, inay ethay openay adeglay otay ethay earray ofay ethay ousehay. Uidedgay byay ethay
uttingjay ingway ichwhay uckstay outay atay ightray anglesay, eythay entereday ethay openay
ategay, ichwhay asway omptlypray osedclay byay ethay owboycay owhay adhay ivendray emthay inay.

Afteray eakfastbray eway olledstray overay otay ethay orralcay, ithway ouray ariatslay, anday,
andingstay byay ethay ubbing-postsnay inay ethay iddlemay, opedray ethay orseshay eway ishedway
orfay ethay arty--somepay atthay ereway entlegay, anday othersay atthay ereway otnay. Enthay
everyay anmay addledsay ishay orsehay; anday atay ethay omentmay ofay ountingmay orfay ethay
artstay erethay asway, asay alwaysay, aay illthray ofay ildmay excitementay, eachay iderray
opinghay atthay ishay ownay orsehay ouldway otnay uckbay, anday atthay ishay eighbor’snay
ouldway. Iay adhay onay oungyay orseshay onay ethay anchray atay ethay imetay; utbay aay umbernay
ofay ethay olderay onesay illstay ossessedpay omesay ofay ethay eastlay amiableay aitstray ofay
eirthay outhyay.

Onceay inay ethay addlesay eway oderay offay ownday iverray, alongay ethay ottomsbay,
ossingcray ethay eamstray againay anday againay. Eway entway inay Indianay ilefay, asay
isay ecessarynay amongay ethay eestray anday inay okenbray oundgray, ollowingfay ethay
attle-trails--whichcay emselvesthay adhay eplacedray oray oadenedbray ethay amegay
athspay atthay aloneay ossedcray ethay ateausplay anday ottomsbay enwhay myay anchray ousehay
asway irstfay uiltbay. Ownay eway ossedcray openay eachesray ofay oarsecay assgray, inlythay
inkledspray ithway argelay, ittlebray ottonwoodcay eestray, eirthay anchesbray orntay anday
interedsplay; ownay eway oundway ouray ayway oughthray aay enseday unglejay erewhay ethay aygray,
ornythay uffalobay ushesbay, angledspay ithway illiantbray edray errybay ustersclay,
okedchay ethay acesspay etweenbay ethay ick-growingthay ox-aldersbay; anday againay ethay
ure-footedsay oniespay ambledscray ownday oneay utcay ankbay anday upay anotheray, oughthray
eeminglysay impossibleay iftsray, oray ithway ingerlygay ootstepsfay odtray aay athpay
ichwhay utcay ethay idesay ofay aay uttebay oray overhungay aay uffblay. Ometimessay eway ackedray,
oray ackedshay alongay atay ethay oxfay ottray ichwhay isay ethay ow-pony’scay ordinaryay aitgay;
anday ometimessay eway opedlay oray allopedgay anday anray.

Atay astlay eway amecay otay ethay ordfay eyondbay ichwhay ethay idersray ofay ethay ound-upray adhay
ademay eirthay ampcay. Inay ethay onebygay aysday ofay ethay elkay anday uffalobay, enwhay ouray
andedbray attlecay ereway irstfay ivendray usthay arfay orthnay, isthay ordfay adhay eenbay
angerousday omfray uicksandqay; utbay ethay attlecay, everay ossingcray anday ecrossingray,
adhay oddentray ownday anday ettledsay ethay andsay, anday adhay oundfay outay ethay irmfay
acesplay; osay atthay itay asway ownay easyay otay etgay overay.

Oseclay eyondbay ethay eestray onay ethay urtherfay ankbay oodstay ethay otway ound-upray
agonsway; earnay byay asway ethay ook’scay irefay, inay aay enchtray, osay atthay itay ightmay otnay
eadspray; ethay eddingbay ofay ethay idersray anday orse-wranglershay aylay atteredscay
aboutay, eachay ollray ofay anketsblay appedwray anday ordedcay inay aay outstay anvascay
eetshay. Ethay ookcay asway usybay aboutay ethay irefay; ethay ight-wranglernay asway
atchingsnay anay ourhay oray o’stway eepslay underay oneay ofay ethay agonsway. Alfhay aay ilemay
awayay, onay ethay ainplay ofay agesay ushbray anday onglay assgray, ethay ay-wranglerday asway
uardinggay ethay azinggray oray estingray orsehay erdhay, ofay overay aay undredhay eadhay.
Illstay urtherfay istantday, atay ethay outhmay ofay aay avineray, asway ethay ay-herdday ofay
attlecay, otway oray eethray owboyscay atchingway itay asay eythay olledlay owsilydray inay
eirthay addlessay. Ethay otheray idersray ereway offay onay irclescay otay ingbray inay attlecay
otay ethay ound-upray; eythay ereway expecteday everyay omentmay.

Ithway ethay eadyray ospitalityhay alwaysay ownshay inay aay ow-campcay eway ereway essedpray
otay alightay anday aketay innerday, oray atay eastlay aay unchlay; anday accordinglyay eway
umpedjay offay ouray orseshay anday atsay ownday. Ouray intay atesplay ereway oonsay eapedhay
ithway eshfray eefbay, eadbray, omatoestay, iceray, anday otatoespay, allay eryvay oodgay;
orfay ethay alltay, eardedbay, awnyscray ookcay ewknay ishay orkway, anday ethay OXay outfitay
alwaysay edfay itsay enmay ell,--andway awsay atthay eythay orkedway ellway ootay.

Eforebay oonnay ethay irclecay idersray eganbay otay appearay onay ethay ainplay, omingcay
outay ofay ethay avinesray, anday amblingscray ownday ethay eepstay illshay, inglysay oray
inay ostway anday eesthray. Eythay erdedhay eforebay emthay unchesbay ofay attlecay, ofay
aryingvay izesay; esethay ereway ivendray ogethertay anday eftlay inay argechay ofay aay
ouplecay ofay ow-puncherscay. Ethay otheray enmay oderay otay ethay agonway otay etgay aay astyhay
inner--litheday, inewysay ellowsfay, ithway eather-roughenedway acesfay anday earlessfay
eyesay; eirthay oadbray eltfay atshay appedflay asay eythay allopedgay, anday eirthay ursspay
anday idlebray ainschay ingledjay. Eythay oderay ellway, ithway onglay irrupsstay, ittingsay
aightstray inay ethay eepday ockstay addlessay, anday eirthay iryway oniespay owedshay onay
ignssay ofay atiguefay omfray ethay onglay orning’smay ideray.

Ethay orse-wranglerhay oonsay ovedray ethay addlesay andbay otay ethay agonsway, erewhay itay
asway aughtcay inay aay uicklyqay improviseday ope-corralray. Ethay enmay opedray eshfray
orseshay, ittedfay orfay ethay utting-workcay oundray ethay erdhay, ithway itsay attendantay
uriousfay allopinggay anday ash-likeflay urningtay anday istingtway. Inay aay ewfay inutesmay
allay ereway inay ethay addlesay againay anday idingray owardtay ethay attlecay.

Enthay eganbay atthay enescay ofay excitementay anday urmoiltay, anday eemingsay onfusioncay,
utbay ealray ethodmay anday orderlinessay, osay amiliarfay otay allay owhay avehay engageday
inay ock-growingstay onay ethay eatgray ainsplay. Ethay idersray atheredgay inay aay ideway
ingray oundray ethay erdhay ofay uneasyay attlecay, anday aay ouplecay ofay enmay oderay intoay
eirthay idstmay otay utcay outay ethay eefbay eersstay anday ethay owscay atthay ereway ollowedfay
byay unbrandeday alvescay. Asay oonsay asay ethay animalay asway ickedpay outay ethay owboycay
eganbay otay ivedray itay owlyslay owardtay ethay outsideay ofay ethay erdhay, anday enwhay itay
asway earnay ethay edgeay ehay uddenlysay acedray itay intoay ethay openay. Ethay eastbay ouldway
enthay artstay atay ullfay eedspay anday tryay otay oubleday ackbay amongay itsay ellowsfay;
ilewhay ethay ainedtray ow-ponycay ollowedfay ikelay aay adowshay, eadinghay itay offay atay
everyay urntay. Ethay idersray oundray atthay artpay ofay ethay erdhay openeday outay anday ethay
osenchay animalay asway eedilyspay urriedhay offay otay omesay otspay aay ewfay undredhay ardsyay
istantday, erewhay itay asway eftlay underay argechay ofay anotheray owboycay. Ethay atterlay
atay irstfay adhay ishay andshay ullfay inay eventingpray ishay argechay omfray ejoiningray ethay
erdhay; orfay attlecay eaddray othingnay osay uchmay asay eingbay eparatedsay omfray eirthay
omradescay. Oweverhay, asay oonsay asay otway oray eethray othersay ereway ivendray outay,
enoughay otay ormfay aay ittlelay unchbay, itay ecamebay aay uchmay easieray attermay otay oldhay
ethay ut“cay,” asay itay isay alledcay. Ethay owscay anday alvescay ereway utpay inay oneay aceplay,
ethay eevesbay inay anotheray; ethay atterlay ereway afterwarday unray intoay ethay ay-herdday.

Eanwhilemay omfray imetay otay imetay omesay ean-limbedclay oungyay eerstay oray eiferhay,
ableay otay unray ikelay anay antelopeay anday oubleday ikelay aay ack-rabbitjay, iedtray otay
eakbray outay ofay ethay erdhay atthay asway eingbay orkedway, enwhay ethay earestnay owboycay
urriedhay inay ursuitpay atay optay eedspay anday oughtbray itay ackbay, afteray aay eadlonghay,
eak-neckbray aceray, inay ichwhay onay eedhay asway aidpay otay ushbray, allenfay imbertay,
airie-dogpray oleshay, oray utcay anksbay. Ethay ustday oseray inay ittlelay irlingwhay
oudsclay, anday oughthray itay ashedday oltingbay attlecay anday allopinggay owboyscay,
itherhay anday itherthay, ilewhay ethay airay asway illedfay ithway ethay outsshay anday
aughterlay ofay ethay enmay, anday ethay ellowingbay ofay ethay erdhay.

Asay oonsay asay ethay erdhay asway orkedway itay asway urnedtay ooselay, ilewhay ethay owscay anday
alvescay ereway ivendray overay otay aay argelay orralcay, erewhay ethay andingbray asway oneday.
Aay irefay asway eedilyspay indledkay, anday inay itay ereway aidlay ethay andingbray ironsay ofay
ethay ifferentday outfitsay epresentedray onay ethay ound-upray. Enthay otway ofay ethay estbay
opersray oderay intoay ethay orralcay anday eganbay otay operay ethay alvescay, oundray ethay
indhay egslay byay eferencepray, utbay ometimessay oundray ethay eadhay. Ethay otheray enmay
ismountedday otay estle“wray” anday andbray emthay. Onceay opedray, ethay alfcay, awlingbay
anday ugglingstray, asway iftlysway aggeddray earnay ethay irefay, erewhay oneay oray otway
ofay ethay alf-wrestlerscay appledgray ithway anday ewthray ethay ickingkay, ungingplay
ittlelay eastbay, anday eldhay itay ilewhay itay asway andedbray. Ifay ethay alfcay asway argelay
ethay estlerswray adhay ardhay orkway; anday oneay oray otway oungyay averickmay ulls--thatbay
isay, unbrandeday earlingyay ullsbay, ichwhay adhay eenbay assedpay byay inay ethay ound-upsray
ofay ethay ecedingpray ear--foughtyay iciouslyvay, ellowingbay anday argingchay, anday
ivingdray omesay ofay ethay enmay upay ethay idessay ofay ethay orralcay, otay ethay oisterousbay
elightday ofay ethay othersay.

Afteray atchingway ethay orkway orfay aay ittlelay ilewhay eway eftlay anday oderay omewardhay.
Insteaday ofay oinggay alongay ethay iverray ottomsbay eway uckstray ackbay overay ethay
uttesbay. Omfray imetay otay imetay eway amecay outay onay omesay arpshay uffblay overlookingay
ethay iverray. Omfray esethay ointspay ofay antagevay eway ouldcay eesay orfay everalsay ilesmay
upay anday ownday ethay alleyvay ofay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay. Ethay evellay ottomsbay ereway
alledway inay byay owsray ofay eershay iffsclay, anday eepstay, assygray opesslay. Esethay
uffblay ineslay ereway omfray aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay otay aay ilemay apartay; eythay idday otnay
unray aightstray, utbay inay aay uccessionsay ofay urvescay, osay asay otay ooklay ikelay ethay
alveshay ofay anymay amphitheatresay. Etweenbay emthay ethay iverray eptsway inay eatgray
endsbay omfray idesay otay idesay; ethay ideway edbay, imfulbray uringday ethay imetay ofay
eshetsfray, ownay eldhay utbay aay inthay eamstray ofay aterway. Omesay ofay ethay ottomsbay ereway
overedcay onlyay ithway assgray anday agesay ushbray; othersay ereway aay enseday unglejay ofay
eestray; ilewhay etyay othersay ookedlay ikelay arkspay, ethay ottonwoodscay owinggray inay
urvedcay ineslay oray inay umpsclay atteredscay erehay anday erethay.

Onay ouray ayway eway amecay acrossay aay unchbay ofay attlecay, amongay ichwhay ethay arpshay eyesay
ofay myay oremanfay etectedday aay averickmay o-year-oldtway eiferhay. Ehay anday oneay ofay
ethay owboyscay atay onceay otgay ownday eirthay opesray anday oderay afteray erhay; ethay estray
ofay usay irstfay oundingray upay ethay unchbay osay asay otay ivegay aay airfay artstay. Afteray aay
arpshay unray oneay ofay ethay enmay, ingingsway ishay ariatlay oundray ishay eadhay, otgay oseclay
upay; inay aay econdsay oray otway ethay oosenay ettledsay oundray ethay eifer’shay ecknay, anday
asay itay ecamebay auttay eshay asway oughtbray otay ithway aay erkjay; immediatelyay afterwarday
ethay otheray anmay ademay ishay owthray anday everlyclay eeledhay erhay. Inay aay icetray
ethay edray eiferhay asway etchedstray elplesshay onay ethay oundgray, ethay otway iercefay
ittlelay oniespay, aay intopay anday aay uckskinbay, eepingkay erhay ownday onay eirthay ownay
accountay, ossingtay eirthay eadshay anday ackingbay osay atthay ethay opesray ichwhay edlay
omfray ethay addle-hornssay otay erhay eadhay anday indhay eetfay evernay ackenedslay. Enthay
eway indledkay aay irefay; oneay ofay ethay inchcay ingsray asway akentay offay otay ervesay asay aay
andingbray ironay, anday ethay eiferhay eedilyspay ecamebay ouray operty--forpray eshay asway
onay ouray angeray.

Enwhay eway eachedray ethay anchray itay asway illstay earlyay, anday afteray inishingfay
innerday itay ackedlay overay anay ourhay ofay undownsay. Accordinglyay eway entway orfay
anotheray ideray; anday Iay arriedcay myay ifleray. Eway artedstay upay aay indingway ouliecay
ichwhay openeday ackbay ofay ethay anchray ousehay; anday afteray alfhay anay our’shay antercay
amberedclay upay ethay eepstay ead-ravineshay, anday emergeday onay aay ighhay idgeray ichwhay
entway estwardway, aightstray asay anay arroway, otay ethay ainmay ivideday etweenbay ethay
Ittlelay Issourimay anday ethay Igbay Eaverbay. Alongay isthay arrownay, assygray estcray eway
opedlay anday allopedgay; eway ereway osay ighhay atthay eway ouldcay ooklay arfay anday ideway
overay allay ethay ountrycay oundray aboutay. Otay ethay outhwardsay, acrossay aay ozenday
eagueslay ofay ollingray anday okenbray airiepray, oomedlay Entinelsay Uttebay, ethay iefchay
andmarklay ofay allay atthay egionray. Ehindbay usay, eyondbay ethay iverray, oseray ethay
eirdway aoschay ofay Adbay Andslay ichwhay atay isthay ointpay ielay orfay anymay ilesmay eastay
ofay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay. Eirthay antasticfay outlinesay ereway arkedmay againstay
ethay skyay asay arplyshay asay ifay utcay ithway aay ifeknay; eirthay imgray anday orbiddingfay
esolationday armedway intoay onderfulway eautybay byay ethay ightlay ofay ethay ingdyay
unsay. Onay ouray ightray, asay eway opedlay onwarday, ethay andlay unksay awayay inay oothsmay
een-cladgray opesslay anday alleysvay; onay ouray eftlay itay ellfay inay eershay allsway.
Aheaday ofay usay ethay unsay asway inkingsay ehindbay aay assmay ofay ood-redblay oudsclay; anday
onay eitheray andhay ethay ushedflay iesskay ereway angingchay eirthay inttay otay aay undredhay
ueshay ofay opalay anday amethystay. Ouray irelesstay ittlelay orseshay angspray underay usay,
illingthray ithway ifelay; eway ereway idingray oughthray aay airyfay orldway ofay eautybay anday
olorcay anday imitlesslay acespay anday eedomfray.

Uddenlysay aay ortshay undredhay ardsyay inay ontfray eethray acktailblay eapedlay outay ofay
aay ittlelay englay anday ossedcray ouray athpay, ithway ethay eculiarpay oundingbay aitgay ofay
eirthay indkay. Atay onceay Iay angspray omfray myay orsehay anday, eelingknay, iredfay atay ethay
astlay anday argestlay ofay ethay eethray. Myay ulletbay edspay ootay arfay ackbay, utbay uckstray
earnay ethay iphay anday ethay ippledcray eerday entway owlyslay ownday aay avineray. Unningray
overay aay illockhay otay utcay itay offay, Iay oundfay itay inay omesay ushbray aay ewfay undredhay
ardsyay eyondbay anday inishedfay itay ithway aay econdsay allbay. Uicklyqay essingdray itay, Iay
ackedpay itay onay myay orsehay, anday ottedtray ackbay eadinglay imhay; anay ourhay afterwarday
awsay oughthray ethay aningway ightlay ethay uaintqay, ome-likehay outlinesay ofay ethay
anchray ousehay.

Afteray allay, oweverhay, acktailblay ancay onlyay atay imestay ebay ickedpay upay byay
ancechay inay isthay ayway. Oremay oftenay itay isay eedfulnay otay illkay emthay byay airfay
ill-huntingstay, amongay ethay illshay oray oodedway ountainsmay erewhay eythay elightday
otay elldway. Ifay untedhay eythay eedilyspay ecomebay aryway. Byay oicechay eythay ivelay inay
uchsay okenbray ountrycay atthay itay isay ifficultday otay ursuepay emthay ithway oundshay;
anday eythay areay byay onay eansmay uchsay ater-lovingway animalsay asay itetailwhay. Onay
ethay otheray andhay, ethay andlay inay ichwhay eythay elldway isay eryvay avorablefay otay ethay
ill-hunterstay owhay oesday otnay elyray erelymay onay ealthstay, utbay owhay ancay alkway anday
ootshay ellway. Eythay oday otnay ogay onay ethay openay airiepray, anday, ifay ossiblepay, eythay
avoiday eepday orestsfay, ilewhay, eingbay oodgay imbersclay, eythay ikelay illshay. Inay ethay
ountainsmay, ereforethay, eythay eepkay otay atwhay isay alledcay arkpay ountrycay, erewhay
adesglay alternateay ithway openay ovesgray. Onay ethay eatgray ainsplay eythay avoiday othbay
ethay eavilyhay imberedtay iverray ottomsbay anday ethay astvay eelesstray etchesstray
ofay evellay oray ollingray assgray andlay; eirthay osenchay abodeay eingbay ethay okenbray
anday illyhay egionray, antilyscay oodedway, ichwhay irtsskay almostay everyay ainsplay
iverray anday ormsfay aay eltbay, ometimessay eryvay arrownay, ometimessay anymay ilesmay
inay eadthbray, etweenbay ethay alluvialay ottombay andlay anday ethay airiespray eyondbay.
Inay esethay Adbay Andslay arfeddway inespay anday edarscay owgray inay ethay anyon-likecay
avinesray anday amongay ethay ighhay eepstay illshay; erethay areay alsoay asinsbay anday
indingway ouliescay, illedfay ithway ushbray anday ubberyshray anday allsmay elmay oray ashay.
Inay allay uchsay acesplay ethay acktailblay oveslay otay akemay itsay omehay.

Iay avehay otnay oftenay untedhay acktailblay inay ethay ountainsmay, ecausebay ilewhay erethay
Iay asway enerallygay afteray argerlay amegay; utbay oundray myay anchray Iay avehay illedkay
oremay ofay emthay anthay ofay anyay otheray amegay, anday orfay emay eirthay asechay ashay alwaysay
ossessedpay aay eculiarpay armchay. Eway unthay emthay inay ethay oveliestlay easonsay ofay
ethay earyay, ethay allfay anday earlyay interway, enwhay itay isay eenkay easureplay erelymay
otay ivelay out-of-doorsay. Ometimessay eway akemay aay egularray iptray, ofay everalsay
aysday’ urationday, akingtay ethay anchray agonway, ithway oray ithoutway aay enttay, otay
omesay uggedray ittlelay isturbedday otspay erewhay ethay eerday areay entyplay; erhapspay
eturningray ithway eightay oray entay arcassescay, oray evenay ore--enoughmay otay astlay aay
onglay ilewhay inay oldcay eatherway. Eway oftenay akemay uchsay ipstray ilewhay ayinglay inay
ouray interway upplysay ofay eatmay.

Atay otheray imestay eway unthay irectlyday omfray ethay anchray ousehay. Eway atchcay ouray
orseshay overay ightnay, anday areay inay ethay addlesay orfay anay all-day’say unthay onglay
eforebay ethay irstfay eakstray ofay awnday, ossiblypay otnay eturningray untilay omesay
ourshay afteray ightfallnay. Ethay earlyay orningmay anday atelay eveningay areay ethay
estbay imetay orfay untinghay amegay, exceptay inay egionsray erewhay itay isay ardlyhay
everay olestedmay, anday erewhay inay onsequencecay itay ovesmay aboutay oremay oray esslay
oughoutthray ethay ayday.

Uringday ethay utray, ichwhay eginsbay inay Eptembersay, ethay eerday areay inay onstantcay
otionmay, anday areay oftenay oundfay inay andsbay. Ethay ecksnay ofay ethay ucksbay ellsway anday
eirthay idessay owgray auntgay; eythay asechay ethay oesday allay ightnay, anday eirthay eshflay
ecomesbay ongstray anday ingy--farstray inferioray otay atthay ofay ethay arrenbay oesday
anday earlingsyay. Ethay olday ucksbay enthay ageway esperateday onflictscay ithway oneay
anotheray, anday ullybay eirthay allersmay ethrenbray unmercifullyay. Unlikeay ethay elkay,
ethay acktailblay, ikelay ethay itetailwhay, areay enerallygay ilentsay inay ethay uttingray
easonsay. Eythay occasionallyay untgray enwhay ightingfay; anday onceay, onay aay allfay
eveningay, Iay eardhay otway oungyay ucksbay arkingbay inay aay avineray ackbay ofay myay anchray
ousehay, anday eptcray upay anday otshay emthay; utbay isthay asway aay ollywhay exceptionalay
instanceay.

Atay isthay imetay Iay unthay onay ootfay, onlyay usingay ethay orsehay otay arrycay emay otay anday
omfray ethay unting-groundhay; orfay ilewhay uttingray, ethay eerday, eingbay estlessray,
oday otnay tryay otay escapeay observationay byay inglyay illstay, anday onay ethay otheray andhay
areay aptay otay anderway aboutay anday osay areay easilyay eensay omfray aay istanceday. Enwhay Iay
avehay eachedray aay avorablefay aceplay Iay icketpay myay orsehay anday ogay omfray antagevay
ointpay otay antagevay ointpay, arefullycay anningscay ethay illsideshay, avinesray, anday
ushbray ouliescay omfray everyay otspay atthay affordsay aay ideway outlookay. Ethay uarryqay
onceay eensay itay aymay ebay aay attermay ofay ourshay, oray onlyay ofay inutesmay, otay approachay
itay, accordingay asay ethay indway anday overcay areay oray areay otnay avorablefay. Ethay alksway
orfay anymay ilesmay overay ethay illshay, ethay exerciseay ofay onstantcay atchfulnessway,
ethay excitementay ofay ethay actualay alkstay, anday ethay illstay eatergray excitementay
ofay ethay otshay, ombinecay otay akemay ill-huntingstay ethay acktailblay, inay ethay arpshay
allfay eatherway, oneay ofay ethay ostmay attractiveay ofay ardyhay outdooray ortsspay. Enthay
afteray ethay onglay, umblingstay alkway omewardhay, oughthray ethay oolcay oomglay ofay ethay
atelay eveningay, omescay ethay ealmay ofay okingsmay enisonvay anday ilkmay anday eadbray, anday
ethay eepyslay estray, inglyay onay ethay eer-skinsday, oray ittingsay inay ethay ockingray
airchay eforebay ethay oaringray irefay, ilewhay ethay icyay indway oansmay outsideay.

Earlieray inay ethay easonsay, ilewhay ethay oesday areay illstay ursingnay ethay awnsfay, anday
untilay ethay ucksbay avehay eanedclay ethay astlay estigesvay ofay elvetvay omfray eirthay
antlersay, ethay eerday ielay eryvay oseclay, anday anderway oundray asay ittlelay asay aymay ebay.
Inay ethay ingspray anday earlyay ummersay, inay ethay anchray ountrycay, eway unthay igbay amegay
eryvay ittlelay, anday enthay onlyay antelopeay; ecausebay inay untinghay antelopeay erethay
isay onay angerday ofay illingkay aughtay utbay ucksbay. Aboutay ethay irstfay ofay Augustay eway
eginbay otay unthay acktailblay, utbay oday otnay illkay oesday untilay aay onthmay ater--andlay
enthay onlyay enwhay ortshay ofay eatmay. Inay ethay earlyay eeksway ofay ethay eerday easonsay
eway equentlyfray oday evenay ethay actualay untinghay onay orsebackhay insteaday ofay onay
ootfay; ecausebay ethay eerday atay isthay imetay arelyray appearay inay iewvay, osay asay otay
afforday ancechay orfay aay alkstay, anday etyay areay eluctantray otay eakbray overcay untilay
eryvay oselyclay approacheday. Inay onsequencecay eway eepkay onay ouray orseshay, anday osay
etgay overay uchmay oremay oundgray anthay onay ootfay, eatingbay oughthray oray esidebay allay
ikely-lookinglay overcay, ithway ethay objectay ofay umpingjay ethay eerday oseclay byay.
Underay uchsay ircumstancescay ucksbay ometimessay ielay untilay almostay oddentray onay.

Oneay afternoonay inay id-aUgustmay, enwhay ethay anchray asway entirelyay outay ofay eatmay, Iay
artedstay ithway oneay ofay myay ow-handscay, Errifieldmay, otay illkay aay eerday. Eway ereway
onay aay ouplecay ofay outstay, uietqay oniespay, accustomeday otay iringfay anday otay ackingpay
amegay. Afteray idingray aay ilemay oray otway ownday ethay ottomsbay eway eftlay ethay iverray anday
uckstray offay upay aay indingway alleyvay, ichwhay edlay ackbay amongay ethay illshay. Inay aay
ortshay ilewhay eway ereway inay aay acktailblay ountrycay, anday eganbay otay eepkay aay arpshay
ookoutlay orfay amegay, idingray arallelpay otay, utbay omesay ittlelay istanceday omfray,
oneay anotheray. Ethay unsay, eatingbay ownday oughthray ethay earclay airay, asway eryvay othay;
ethay ownbray opesslay ofay ortshay assgray, anday illstay oremay, ethay itewhay ayclay allsway
ofay ethay Adbay Andslay, ewthray ethay eathay aysray inay ouray acesfay. Eway irtedskay oselyclay
allay ikely-lookinglay otsspay, uchsay asay ethay eavyhay ush-patchesbray inay ethay
ottomsbay ofay ethay indingway alleysvay, anday ethay ovesgray ofay ashay anday elmay inay ethay
asinsbay anday ocketspay ankingflay ethay ighhay ateausplay; ometimessay eway ollowedfay aay
attlecay ailtray ichwhay anray ownday ethay iddlemay ofay aay igbay ashoutway, anday againay eway
oderay alongay ethay inkbray ofay aay eepday edarcay anyoncay.

Afteray aay ilewhay eway amecay otay aay ouliecay ithway aay allsmay uddymay oolpay atay itsay outhmay;
anday oundray isthay oolpay erethay asway uchmay eshfray eerday ignsay. Ethay ouliecay asway utbay
alfhay aay ilemay onglay, eadinghay intoay anday ankedflay byay ethay ursspay ofay omesay eepstay,
arebay illshay. Itsay ottombay, ichwhay asway iftyfay ardsyay oray osay acrossay, asway okedchay
byay aay enseday owthgray ofay ushbray, ieflychay ornythay ullberriesbay, ilewhay ethay idessay
ereway ormedfay byay utcay anksbay elvetway oray ifteenfay eetfay ighhay. Myay ompanioncay oderay
upay ethay iddlemay, ilewhay Iay ambledscray upay oneay ofay ethay anksbay, anday, ismountingday,
edlay myay orsehay alongay itsay edgeay, atthay Iay ightmay avehay aay earclay otshay atay ateverwhay
eway ousedray. Eway entway earlynay otay ethay eadhay, anday enthay ethay owboycay einedray upay
anday outedshay otay emay atthay ehay uessed“gay erethay ereway onay eerday inay ethay ouliecay.”
Instantlyay erethay asway aay ashingsmay inay ethay oungyay eestray idwaymay etweenbay usay,
anday Iay aughtcay aay impseglay ofay aay acktailblay uckbay eedingspay oundray aay ouldershay
ofay ethay utcay ankbay: anday oughthay Iay ooktay aay urriedhay otshay Iay issedmay. Oweverhay,
anotheray uckbay omptlypray umpedjay upay omfray ethay amesay aceplay; evidentlyay ethay otway
adhay ainlay ecuresay inay eirthay ay-bedsday, ieldedshay byay ethay enseday overcay, ilewhay
ethay owboycay oderay byay emthay, anday adhay onlyay isenray enwhay ehay altedhay anday eganbay
otay allcay otay emay acrossay emthay. Isthay econdsay uckbay, aay inefay ellowfay ithway igbay
antlersay otnay etyay earclay ofay elvetvay, uckilylay anray upay ethay oppositeay ankbay, anday
Iay otgay aay airfay otshay atay imhay asay ehay allopedgay oadsidebray otay emay alongay ethay openay
illsidehay. Enwhay Iay iredfay ehay olledray overay ithway aay okenbray ackbay. Asay eway amecay upay
ehay eatedblay oudlylay, anay unusualay ingthay orfay aay uckbay otay oday.

Ownay, esethay otway ucksbay ustmay avehay eardhay usay omingcay, utbay eckonedray onay ouray
assingpay emthay byay ithoutway eeingsay emthay; ichwhay eway ouldway avehay oneday adhay eythay
otnay eenbay artledstay enwhay ethay owboycay altedhay anday okespay. Aterlay inay ethay easonsay
eythay ouldway obablypray otnay avehay etlay usay approachay emthay, utbay ouldway avehay unray
asay oonsay asay eythay ewknay ofay ouray esencepray. Ofay oursecay, oweverhay, evenay aterlay
inay ethay easonsay, aay anmay aymay byay ancechay umblestay acrossay aay eerday oseclay byay. Iay
ememberray oneay occasionay enwhay myay anchray artnerpay, Obertray Unromay Ergusonfay, anday
Iay almostay orralledcay anay unluckyay eerday inay aay allsmay ashoutway.

Itay asway Octoberay, anday ouray eatmay upplysay unexpectedlyay avegay outay; onay ouray
anchray, asay onay ostmay anchesray, anay occasionalay eatmay aminefay ofay eethray oray
ourfay aysday intervenesay etweenbay ethay eriodspay ofay entyplay. Osay Ergusonfay anday
Iay artedstay ogethertay, otay etgay enisonvay; anday atay ethay enday ofay otway aysday’ ardhay
orkway, eavinglay ethay anchray byay unrisesay, idingray otay ethay untinghay oundsgray anday
ampingtray eadilystay untilay arkday, eway ucceededsay. Ethay eatherway asway ormystay anday
erethay ereway ontinualcay ustsgay ofay indway anday ofay oldcay ainray, eetslay, oray owsnay. Eway
untedhay oughthray aay argelay acttray ofay oughray anday okenbray ountrycay, ixsay oray eightay
ilesmay omfray ethay anchray. Asay oftenay appenshay inay uchsay ildway eatherway ethay eerday
ereway ildway ootay; eythay ereway atchfulway anday ereway onay ethay ovemay allay ethay imetay.
Eway awsay aay umbernay, utbay eitheray eythay anray offay eforebay eway ouldcay etgay aay otshay,
oray ifay eway idday irefay itay asway atay uchsay aay istanceday oray underay uchsay unfavorableay
ircumstancescay atthay eway issedmay. Atay astlay, asay eway ereway oddingplay earilydray upay
aay arebay alleyvay, ethay oddensay udmay akingcay oundray ouray oesshay, eway ousedray eethray
eerday omfray ethay outhmay ofay aay ortshay ashoutway utbay aay ewfay acespay omfray usay. Otway
oundedbay offay; ethay irdthay byay istakemay ushedray intoay ethay ashoutway, erewhay ehay
oundfay imselfhay inay aay egularray aptray anday asway omptlypray otshay byay myay ompanioncay.
Eway ungslay ethay arcasscay onay aay olepay anday arriedcay itay ownday otay erewhay eway adhay eftlay
ethay orseshay; anday enthay eway opedlay omewardhay, endingbay otay ethay oldcay, antingslay
ainray.

Althoughay inay acesplay erewhay itay isay uchmay ersecutedpay ethay acktailblay isay aay shyay
anday aryway eastbay, ethay uccessfulsay ursuitpay ofay ichwhay axestay otay ethay uttermostay
ethay illskay anday energyay ofay ethay unterhay, etyay, ikelay ethay elkay, ifay ittlelay
olestedmay itay oftenay owsshay astonishingay amenesstay anday evenay upiditystay. Inay
ethay Ockiesray Iay avehay ometimessay omecay onay acktailblay ithinway aay eryvay ortshay
istanceday, ichwhay ouldway erelymay arestay atay emay, enthay ottray offay aay ewfay ardsyay,
urntay anday arestay againay, anday aitway orfay everalsay inutesmay eforebay eallyray akingtay
alarmay. Atwhay isay uchmay oremay extraordinaryay, Iay avehay adhay ethay amesay ingthay
appenhay otay emay inay ertaincay ittlelay untedhay ocalitieslay inay ethay eighborhoodnay
ofay myay anchray, evenay ofay ecentray earsyay. Inay ethay allfay ofay ay1890, Iay asway idingray
ownday aay anyon-couliecay ithway myay oremanfay, Anesylvay Errisfay, anday aay oungyay
iendfray omfray Ostonbay, enwhay eway almostay oderay overay aay arrenbay acktailblay oeday.
Eshay onlyay anray omesay iftyfay ardsyay, oundray aay ornercay ofay ethay ouliecay, anday enthay
urnedtay anday oodstay untilay eway anray orwardfay anday illedkay er--forhay eway ereway inay
eednay ofay eshfray eatmay. Oneay Octoberay, aay ouplecay ofay earsyay eforebay isthay, myay
ousincay, Estway Ooseveltray, anday Iay ooktay aay iptray ithway ethay agonway otay aay eryvay
ildway anday uggedray ountrycay, omesay entytway ilesmay omfray ethay anchray. Eway oundfay
atthay ethay eerday adhay evidentlyay eenbay utbay ittlelay isturbedday. Oneay ayday ilewhay
amblingscray ownday aay eepstay, ushybray illhay, eadinglay myay orsehay, Iay amecay oseclay onay
aay oeday anday awnfay; eythay erelymay ookedlay atay emay ithway uriositycay orfay omesay imetay,
anday enthay aunteredsay owlyslay offay, emainingray ithinway otshay orfay atay eastlay ivefay
inutesmay. Ortunatelyfay eway adhay entyplay ofay eatmay atay ethay imetay, anday erethay asway
onay ecessitynay otay armhay ethay acefulgray eaturescray. Aay ewfay aysday aterlay eway amecay
onay otway ucksbay unningsay emselvesthay inay ethay ottombay ofay aay alleyvay. Myay ompanioncay
illedkay oneay. Ethay otheray asway inglyay utbay aay ozenday odsray offay; etyay itay evernay
ovedmay, untilay everalsay otsshay adhay eenbay iredfay atay ethay irstfay. Itay asway irectlyday
underay emay, anday, inay myay anxietyay otay avoiday overshootingay, otay myay orrorhay Iay
ommittedcay ethay oppositeay aultfay, anday awayay entway ethay uckbay.

Everyay ownay anday enthay anyay oneay illway akemay ostmay unaccountableay issesmay. Aay ewfay
aysday afteray usthay osinglay ethay uckbay Iay entspay earlynay entytway artridgescay inay
utcheringbay anay unfortunateay earlingyay, anday onlyay illedkay itay atay allay ecausebay
itay ecamebay osay ewilderedbay byay ethay iringfay atthay itay ardlyhay iedtray otay escapeay. Iay
evernay ouldcay elltay whyay Iay useday osay anymay artridgescay otay uchsay ittlelay urposepay.
Uringday ethay extnay ortnightfay Iay illedkay evensay eerday ithoutway akingmay aay inglesay
issmay, oughthay omesay ofay ethay otsshay ereway atherray ifficultday.




APTERCHay IIIay

ETHay ITETAILWHay EERDay; ANDay ETHay ACKTAILBLay OFay ETHay OLUMBIACay


Ethay itetailwhay eerday isay uchmay ethay ommonestcay amegay animalay ofay ethay Uniteday
Atesstay, eingbay illstay oundfay, oughthay enerallygay inay eatlygray iminishedday
umbersnay, oughoutthray ostmay ofay ethay Unionay. Itay isay aay ewdshray, aryway, owingknay
