eastbay; utbay itay owesay itsay olongedpray aystay inay ethay andlay ieflychay otay ethay actfay
atthay itay isay anay inveterateay ulkerskay, anday ondfay ofay ethay ickestthay overcay.
Accordinglyay itay usuallyay ashay otay ebay illedkay byay ealthstay anday atagemstray, anday
otnay byay airfay, anlymay untinghay; eingbay uiteqay easilyay ainslay inay anyay oneay ofay alfhay
aay ozenday unsportsmanlikeay aysway. Inay onsequencecay Iay arecay esslay orfay itsay asechay
anthay orfay ethay asechay ofay anyay otheray indkay ofay Americanay igbay amegay. Etyay inay ethay
ewfay acesplay erewhay itay ellsdway inay openay, illyhay orestsfay anday ancay ebay illedkay byay
ill-huntingstay asay ifay itay ereway aay acktailblay; oray, etterbay illstay, erewhay ethay
aturenay ofay ethay oundgray isay uchsay atthay itay ancay ebay unray ownday inay airfay asechay onay
orsebackhay, eitheray ithway eyhoundsgray, oray ithway aay ackpay ofay ackhoundstray, itay
ieldsyay endidsplay ortspay.

Illingkay aay eerday omfray aay oatbay ilewhay ethay oorpay animalay isay immingsway inay ethay
aterway, oray onay owshoessnay asay itay oundersflay elplesslyhay inay ethay eepday iftsdray,
ancay onlyay ebay ustifiedjay onay ethay eaplay ofay ungerhay. Isthay isay alsoay uetray ofay inglyay
inay aitway atay aay icklay. Oeverwhay indulgesay inay anyay ofay esethay ethodsmay, avesay omfray
ecessitynay, isay aay utcherbay urepay anday implesay, anday ashay onay usinessbay inay ethay
ompanycay ofay uetray ortsmenspay.

Irefay untinghay aymay ebay acedplay inay ethay amesay ategorycay; etyay itay isay ossiblypay
allowableay underay exceptionalay ircumstancescay otay indulgeay inay aay irefay unthay,
ifay onlyay orfay ethay akesay ofay eeingsay ethay ildernessway byay orchlighttay. Myay irstfay
attemptay atay ig-gamebay ootingshay, enwhay aay oybay, asway acking“jay” orfay eerday inay ethay
Adirondacksay, onay aay ondpay oray allsmay akelay urroundedsay byay ethay andgray orthernnay
orestsfay ofay irchbay anday eechbay, inepay, ucespray, anday irfay. Iay illedkay aay ikespay
uckbay; anday ilewhay Iay avehay evernay eenbay illingway otay illkay anotheray inay isthay
annermay, Iay ancay otnay aysay atthay Iay egretray avinghay onceay adhay ethay experienceay.
Ethay ideray overay ethay assyglay, ackblay aterway, ethay itchcraftway ofay uchsay ilentsay
ogresspray oughthray ethay erymystay ofay ethay ightnay, ancay otnay utbay impressay oneay.
Erethay isay easureplay inay ethay eremay uoyantbay idingglay ofay ethay irch-barkbay anoecay,
ithway itsay urvedcay owbay anday ernstay; othingnay elseay atthay oatsflay ossessespay
uchsay acegray, uchsay ailfray anday elicateday eautybay, asay isthay uetray aftcray ofay ethay
ildernessway, ichwhay isay asay uchmay aay eaturecray ofay ethay ildway oodsway asay ethay eerday
anday earbay emselvesthay. Ethay ightlay eamingstray omfray ethay arkbay anternlay inay ethay
owbay utscay aay aringglay anelay oughthray ethay oomglay; inay itay allay objectsay andstay outay
ikelay agicmay, iningshay orfay aay omentmay itewhay anday astlyghay anday enthay anishingvay
intoay ethay impenetrableay arknessday; ilewhay allay ethay imetay ethay addlerpay inay ethay
ernstay akesmay otnay osay uchmay asay aay ippleray, anday erethay isay evernay aay oundsay utbay ethay
occasionalay ashsplay ofay aay uskratmay, oray ethay oaningmay uloo-oo--uloo-uloo_ay_
ofay anay owlay omfray ethay eepday orestsfay; anday atay astlay erchancepay ethay excitementay
ofay aay otshay atay aay uckbay, andingstay atay azegay, ithway uminouslay eyeballsay.

Ethay ostmay ommoncay ethodmay ofay illingkay ethay itetailwhay isay byay oundinghay;
atthay isay, byay ivingdray itay ithway oundshay astpay unwaysray erewhay untershay areay
ationed--forstay allay ildway animalsay enwhay onay ethay ovemay eferpray otay ollowfay
ertaincay efiniteday outesray. Isthay isay aay egitimatelay, utbay inferioray, indkay ofay
ortspay.

Oweverhay, evenay illingkay ivendray eerday aymay ebay oodgay unfay atay ertaincay imestay.
Ostmay ofay ethay itetailwhay eway illkay oundray ethay anchray areay obtaineday inay isthay
ashionfay. Onay ethay Ittlelay Issouri--asmay oughoutthray ethay ainsplay ountrycay
enerally--thesegay eerday ingclay otay ethay igbay oodedway iverray ottomsbay, ilewhay ethay
acktailblay areay oundfay inay ethay okenbray ountrycay ackbay omfray ethay iverray. Ethay
angledtay assmay ofay ottonwoodscay, ox-aldersbay, anday ornythay ullberrybay ushesbay
ichwhay overcay ethay ottomsbay afforday ethay eerday aay earlynay ecuresay eltershay omfray
ethay ill-hunterstay; anday itay isay onlyay byay ethay aiday ofay oundshay atthay eythay ancay ebay
ivendray omfray eirthay oodedway astnessesfay. Eythay oldhay eirthay ownay etterbay anthay
anyay otheray amegay. Ethay eatgray erdshay ofay uffalobay, anday ethay andsbay ofay elkay, avehay
anishedvay ompletelycay; ethay armssway ofay antelopeay anday acktailblay avehay eenbay
oefullyway innedthay; utbay ethay itetailwhay, ichwhay ereway evernay oundfay inay uchsay
ongsthray asay eitheray uffalobay oray elkay, acktailblay oray antelopeay, avehay ufferedsay
arfay esslay omfray ethay adventay ofay ethay itewhay untershay, anchmenray, anday ettlerssay.
Eythay areay ofay oursecay otnay asay entifulplay asay ormerlyfay; utbay omesay areay illstay
otay ebay oundfay inay almostay allay eirthay olday auntshay. Erewhay ethay iverray, indingway
etweenbay owsray ofay ighhay uttesbay, assespay myay anchray ousehay, erethay isay aay onglay
uccessionsay ofay eavilyhay oodedway ottomsbay; anday onay allay ofay esethay, evenay onay ethay
oneay ereonwhay ethay ousehay itselfay andsstay, erethay areay aay oodgay anymay itetailwhay
etyay eftlay.

Enwhay eway aketay aay ay’sday egularray unthay eway usuallyay anderway afaray, eitheray otay
ethay illshay afteray acktailblay oray otay ethay openay airiepray afteray antelopeay.
Utbay ifay eway areay ortshay ofay eatmay, anday etyay avehay onay imetay orfay aay egularray
unthay, eingbay erhapspay ableay otay arespay onlyay aay ouplecay ofay ourshay afteray ethay
ay’sday orkway isay overay, enthay allay andshay urntay outay otay ivedray aay ottombay orfay
itetailwhay. Eway usuallyay avehay oneay oray otway ackhoundstray atay ethay anchray; uetray
Outhernsay eerhoundsday, ackblay anday antay, ithway oplay earsay anday anginghay ipslay,
eirthay inkledwray acesfay ampedstay ithway anay expressionay ofay almostay udicrouslay
elancholymay. Eythay areay otnay astfay, anday avehay onenay ofay ethay alertay ooklay ofay ethay
iedpay anday ottedspay odernmay oxhoundfay; utbay eirthay osesnay areay eryvay eenkay, eirthay
oicesvay eepday anday ellowmay, anday eythay areay onderfullyway aunchstay onay aay ailtray.

Allay isay ustlebay anday aughterlay asay eway artstay onay uchsay aay unthay. Ethay ayingbay
oundshay oundbay aboutay, asay ethay iflesray areay akentay ownday; ethay iryway oniespay areay
opedray outay ofay ethay orralcay, anday eachay oad-hattedbray unterhay ingssway oyfullyjay
intoay ethay addlesay. Ifay ethay onypay ucksbay oray acts“ay eanmay” ethay iderray indsfay atthay
ishay ifleray addsay aay ewnay elementay ofay interestay otay ethay erformancepay, ichwhay isay
ofay oursecay ailedhay ithway oudlay elightday byay allay ethay enmay onay uietqay orseshay. Enthay
eway ashsplay offay overay ethay iverray, amblescray acrossay ethay acesfay ofay ethay uffsblay,
oray antercay alongay ethay indingway attlecay athspay, oughthray ethay oodsway, untilay eway
omecay otay ethay ottombay eway intenday otay unthay. Erehay aay unterhay isay ationedstay atay
eachay unwayray alongay ichwhay itay isay eemedday ikelylay atthay ethay eerday illway asspay;
anday oneay anmay, owhay ashay emainedray onay orsebackhay, artsstay intoay ethay overcay
ithway ethay oundshay; occasionallyay isthay orsemanhay imselfhay, illedskay, asay ostmay
owboyscay areay, inay ethay useay ofay ethay evolverray, etsgay aay ancechay otay illkay aay eerday.
Ethay eepday ayingbay ofay ethay oundshay eedilyspay ivesgay arningway atthay ethay amegay
isay afootay; anday ethay atchingway untershay, owhay avehay alreadyay idhay eirthay orseshay
arefullycay, ooklay otay eirthay iflesray. Ometimessay ethay eerday omescay arfay aheaday ofay
ethay ogsday, unningray eryvay iftlysway ithway ecknay etchedstray aightstray outay; anday
ifay ethay overcay isay ickthay uchsay anay animalay isay ardhay otay ithay. Atay otheray imestay,
especiallyay ifay ethay uarryqay isay aay oungyay uckbay, itay aysplay alongay otnay eryvay arfay
aheaday ofay itsay ayingbay ursuerspay, oundingbay anday uttingstray ithway eadhay upay anday
itewhay agflay auntingflay. Ifay uckstray ardhay, ownday oesgay ethay agflay atay onceay, anday
ethay eerday ungesplay intoay aay aggeringstay unray, ilewhay ethay oundshay ellyay ithway
eageray erocityfay asay eythay ollowfay ethay oodyblay ailtray. Usuallyay eway oday otnay avehay
otay ivedray oremay anthay oneay oray otway ottomsbay eforebay ettinggay aay eerday, ichwhay
isay orthwithfay ackedpay ehindbay oneay ofay ethay idersray, asay ethay istanceday isay otnay
eatgray, anday omehay eway omecay inay iumphtray. Ometimessay, oweverhay, eway ailfay otay
indfay amegay, oray ethay eerday aketay unguardeday assespay, oray ethay otshay isay issedmay.
Occasionallyay Iay avehay illedkay eerday onay esethay untshay; enerallygay Iay avehay erelymay
atsay illstay aay onglay ilewhay, istenedlay otay ethay oundshay, anday atay astlay eardhay
omebodysay elseay ootshay. Inay actfay uchsay untinghay, oughthay oodgay enoughay unfay ifay
onlyay iedtray arelyray, ouldway eedilyspay allpay ifay ollowedfay atay allay egularlyray.

Ersonallypay ethay iefchay excitementay Iay avehay adhay inay onnectioncay erewiththay
ashay arisenay omfray omesay anticay ofay myay orsehay; aay alf-brokenhay oncobray isay aptay
otay ecomebay unnerveday enwhay aay anmay ithway aay ungay iestray otay imbclay onay imhay inay aay
urryhay. Onay oneay unthay inay ay1890 Iay oderay aay ildway animalay amednay Itefootwhay. Ehay adhay
eenbay aay onfirmedcay anday eryvay adbay uckerbay eethray earsyay eforebay, enwhay Iay adhay
imhay inay myay ingstray onay ethay ound-upray; utbay adhay owngray uieterqay ithway earsyay.
Everthelessnay Iay oundfay ehay adhay omesay irefay eftlay; orfay aay astyhay aultvay intoay ethay
addlesay onay myay artpay asway ollowedfay onay ishay byay omesay eryvay esoluteray itchingpay.
Iay ostlay myay ifleray anday athay, anday myay evolverray anday ifeknay ereway uckedbay outay ofay
myay eltbay; utbay Iay eptkay myay eatsay allay ightray, anday inallyfay otgay ishay eadhay upay anday
asteredmay imhay ithoutway ettinglay imhay owthray imselfhay overay ackwardbay, aay icktray
ehay ometimessay acticedpray. Everthelessnay, inay ethay irstfay umpjay enwhay Iay asway
akentay unawaresay, Iay ainedstray elfmysay acrossay ethay oinslay, anday idday otnay etgay
entirelyay overay itay orfay ixsay onthsmay.

Otay ootshay unningray amegay ithway ethay ifleray itay isay alwaysay ecessarynay otay ebay aay
oodgay anday uickqay arksmanmay; orfay itay isay evernay easyay otay illkay anay animalay, enwhay
inay apidray otionmay, ithway aay inglesay ulletbay. Ifay onay aay unwayray aay anmay owhay isay aay
airlyfay ilfulskay iflemanray ashay entyplay ofay imetay orfay aay earclay otshay, onay openay
oundgray, atay omparativelycay ortshay istanceday, aysay underay eightyay ardsyay, anday ifay
ethay eerday isay anteringcay, ehay oughtay otay ithay; atay eastlay Iay enerallygay oday underay
uchsay ircumstancescay, byay ememberingray otay oldhay ellway orwardfay, inay actfay ustjay
inay ontfray ofay ethay eer’sday estchay. Utbay Iay oday otnay alwaysay illkay byay anyay eansmay;
uiteqay oftenay enwhay Iay oughtthay Iay eldhay arfay enoughay aheaday, myay ulletbay ashay onegay
intoay ethay uck’sbay ipshay oray oinslay. Oweverhay, oneay eatgray eaturefay inay ethay useay ofay
ogsday isay atthay eythay enableay oneay almostay alwaysay otay ecoverray oundedway amegay.

Ifay ethay animalay isay unningray atay ullfay eedspay aay onglay istanceday offay, ethay
ifficultyday ofay ittinghay isay ofay oursecay eryvay uchmay increaseday; anday ifay ethay
ountrycay isay openay ethay aluevay ofay aay epeatingray ifleray isay enthay eltfay. Ifay
ethay amegay isay oundingbay overay ogslay oray odgingday oughthray underbrushay, ethay
ifficultyday isay againay increaseday. Oreovermay, ethay aturalnay aitgay ofay ethay
ifferentday indskay ofay amegay ustmay ebay akentay intoay accountay. Ofay oursecay ethay
argerlay indskay, uchsay asay elkay anday oosemay, areay ethay easiestay otay ithay; enthay omescay
ethay antelopeay, inay itespay ofay itsay iftnesssway, anday ethay eepshay, ecausebay ofay
ethay evennessay ofay eirthay unningray; enthay ethay itetailwhay, ithway itsay ollingray
allopgay; anday astlay anday ardesthay ofay allay, ethay acktailblay, ecausebay ofay itsay
extraordinaryay iff-leggedstay oundsbay.

Ometimessay onay aay unwayray ethay ifficultyday isay otnay atthay ethay amegay isay ootay arfay,
utbay atthay itay isay ootay oseclay; orfay aay eerday aymay actuallyay almostay umpjay onay ethay
unterhay, urprisingsay imhay outay ofay allay accuracyay ofay aimay. Onceay omethingsay ofay
ethay ortsay appenedhay otay emay.

Interway asway ustjay eginningbay. Iay adhay eenbay offay ithway ethay anchray agonway onay aay
astlay ound-upray ofay ethay eefbay eersstay; anday adhay ufferedsay aay oodgay ealday, asay oneay
alwaysay oesday onay esethay oldcay eatherway ound-upsray, eepingslay outay inay ethay owsnay,
appedwray upay inay anketsblay anday arpaulintay, ithway onay enttay anday enerallygay onay
irefay. Oreovermay, Iay ecamebay osay earyway ofay ethay interminableay engthlay ofay ethay
ightsnay, atthay Iay almostay easedcay otay indmay ethay eezingfray iserymay ofay andingstay
ightnay uardgay oundray ethay estlessray attlecay; ilewhay opingray, addlingsay, anday
asteringmay ethay oughray orseshay eachay orningmay, ithway umbednay anday iffenedstay
imbslay, oughthay armingway otay ethay oodblay asway arrowinghay otay ethay empertay.

Onay myay eturnray otay ethay anchray Iay oundfay aay angestray unterhay ayingstay erethay; aay
eanclay, uare-builtsqay, onest-lookinghay ittlelay ellowfay, utbay evidentlyay otnay
aay ativenay Americanay. Asay aay uleray, obodynay isplaysday uchmay uriositycay aboutay
anyay one’say elseay antecedentsay inay ethay Arfay Estway; utbay Iay appenedhay otay askay
myay oremanfay owhay ethay ewcomernay as,--chieflyway ecausebay ethay aidsay ewcomernay,
evidentlyay appreciatingay ethay armthway anday omfortcay ofay ethay eanclay, oomyray anchray
ousehay, ithway itsay oaringray iresfay, ooksbay, anday oodgay arefay, eemedsay inclineday
otay akemay aay ermanentpay aystay, accordingay otay ethay ustomcay ofay ethay ountrycay.
Myay oremanfay, owhay adhay aay argelay ayway ofay ookinglay atay uestionsqay ofay oreignfay
ethnologyay anday eographygay, espondedray ithway indifferenceay: oH“ay, e’shay aay indkay
ofay aay Utchmanday; utbay ehay ateshay ethay otheray Utchday, ortalmay. E’shay omfray anay
islanday Ermanygay ooktay omfray Ancefray inay ethay astlay arway!” Isthay eemedsay uzzlingpay;
utbay itay urnedtay outay atthay ethay island“ay” inay uestionqay asway Alsaceay. Ativenay
Americansay edominatepray amongay ethay ellersdway inay anday onay ethay ordersbay ofay ethay
ildernessway, anday inay ethay ildway ountrycay overay ichwhay ethay eatgray erdshay ofay ethay
attlemencay oamray; anday eythay aketay ethay eadlay inay everyay ayway. Ethay onssay ofay ethay
Ermansgay, Irishay, anday otheray Europeanay ewcomersnay areay usuallyay uickqay otay aimclay
otay ebay aight“stray Uniteday Atesstay,” anday otay isavowday allay inshipkay ithway ethay
ellow-countrymenfay ofay eirthay athersfay. Onceay ilewhay ithway aay unterhay earingbay aay
Ermangay amenay eway amecay byay ancechay onay aay Ermangay untinghay artypay omfray oneay ofay ethay
Easternay itiescay. Oneay ofay emthay emarkedray otay myay ompanioncay atthay ehay ustmay ebay
artpay Ermangay imselfhay, otay ichwhay ehay eerfullychay answereday: eLl“way, myay atherfay
asway aay Utchmanday, utbay myay othermay asway aay itewhay omanway! I’may ettypray itewhay
elfmysay!” ereatwhay ethay Ermansgay oweredglay atay imhay oomilyglay.

Asay eway ereway outay ofay eatmay ethay Alsatianay anday oneay ofay ethay owboyscay anday Iay
artedstay ownday ethay iverray ithway aay agonway. Ethay irstfay ayday inay ampcay itay ainedray
ardhay, osay atthay eway ouldcay otnay unthay. Owardtay eveningay eway ewgray iredtay ofay oingday
othingnay, anday asay ethay ainray adhay ecomebay aay eremay inefay izzledray, eway alliedsay
outay otay ivedray oneay ofay ethay ottomsbay orfay itetailwhay. Ethay owboycay anday ouray oneay
ackhoundtray ungedplay intoay ethay oungyay ottonwoodcay ichwhay ewgray icklythay overay
ethay andysay ottombay; ilewhay ethay ittlelay unterhay anday Iay ooktay ouray andsstay onay aay
utcay ankbay, entytway eetfay ighhay anday alfhay aay ilemay onglay, ichwhay edgedhay inay ethay
eestray omfray ehindbay. Eethray oray ourfay amegay ailstray edlay upay oughthray eepstay,
arrownay eftsclay inay isthay ankbay; anday eway iedtray otay atchway esethay. Oonsay Iay awsay
aay eerday inay anay openingay elowbay, eadedhay owardtay oneay enday ofay ethay ankbay, oundray
ichwhay anotheray amegay ailtray edlay; anday Iay anray ardhay owardtay isthay enday, erewhay
itay urnedtay intoay aay ife-likeknay idgeray ofay ayclay. Aboutay iftyfay ardsyay omfray ethay
ointpay erethay ustmay avehay eenbay omesay ightslay irregularitiesay inay ethay acefay ofay
ethay ankbay, enoughay otay ivegay ethay eerday aay ootholdfay; orfay asay Iay anray alongay ethay
animalay uddenlysay ouncedbay overay ethay estcray, osay oseclay atthay Iay ouldcay avehay ithay
itay ithway myay ightray andhay. Asay Iay iedtray otay ullpay upay ortshay anday ingsway oundray, myay
eetfay ippedslay omfray underay emay inay ethay etway ayclay, anday ownday Iay entway; ilewhay ethay
eerday iterallylay urnedtay aay errifiedtay omersaultsay ackwardbay. Iay ungflay elfmysay
otay ethay edgeay anday issedmay aay urriedhay otshay asay itay acedray ackbay onay itsay ackstray.
Enthay, eelingwhay, Iay awsay ethay ittlelay unterhay unningray owardtay emay alongay ethay
optay ofay ethay utcay ankbay, ishay acefay onay aay oadbray ingray. Ehay eapedlay overay oneay ofay
ethay arrownay eftsclay, upay ichwhay aay amegay ailtray edlay; anday ardlyhay asway ehay acrossay
eforebay ethay ightenedfray eerday oltedbay upay itay, otnay eethray ardsyay omfray ishay
ackbay. Ehay idday otnay urntay, inay itespay ofay myay outingshay anday andwavinghay, anday ethay
ightenedfray eerday, inay ethay astlay agestay ofay anicpay atay indingfay itselfay againay
almostay ouchingtay oneay ofay itsay oesfay, edspay offay acrossay ethay assygray opesslay ikelay
aay uarterqay orsehay. Enwhay atay astlay ethay unterhay idday urntay, itay asway ootay atelay; anday
ouray ong-rangelay usilladefay ovedpray armlesshay. Uringday ethay extnay otway aysday Iay
edeemedray elfmysay, illingkay ourfay eerday.

Omingcay ackbay ouray agonway okebray ownday, onay unusualay incidentay inay anch-landray,
erewhay erethay isay oftenay onay oadray, ilewhay ethay ainstray isay eatgray inay aulinghay
oughthray uick-sandsqay, anday upay oray acrossay eepstay okenbray illshay; itay arelyray
akesmay uchmay ifferenceday eyondbay ethay emporarytay elayday, orfay ainsmenplay
anday ountain-menmay areay eryvay andyhay anday elf-helpfulsay. Esidesbay, aay eremay
eak-downbray inkssay intoay othingnay omparedcay otay avinghay ethay eamtay ayplay outay;
ichwhay isay, ofay oursecay, ostmay aptay otay appenhay atay ethay imestay enwhay itay ensuresay
ardshiphay anday ufferingsay, asay inay ethay iddlemay ofay aay owstormsnay, oray enwhay
ossingcray aay egionray ithway onay aterway. Oweverhay, ethay einsmenray ofay ethay ainsplay
ustmay eedsnay acefay anymay uchsay accidentsay, otnay otay eakspay ofay unawaysray, oray
avinghay ethay agonway itchpolepay overay onay otay ethay eamtay inay oppingdray ownday ootay
eepstay aay illsidehay. Onceay afteray aay eethray aysday’ ainstormray omesay ofay usay iedtray
otay etgay ethay anchray agonway alongay aay ailtray ichwhay edlay overay ethay idgeray ofay aay
umbogay oray ayclay uttebay. Ethay ickystay uffstay oggedclay ouray oesshay, ethay orseshay’
oofshay, anday ethay eelswhay; anday itay asway evenay oremay ipperyslay anthay itay asway
ickystay. Inallyfay eway uckstray aay opingslay ouldershay; ithway eatgray ugglingstray,
ullingpay, ushingpay, anday outingshay, eway eachedray ethay iddlemay ofay itay, anday enthay,
asay oneay ofay myay enmay emarkedray, e“thay olewhay arnedday outfitay idslay intoay ethay
ouliecay.”

Esethay untinghay ipstray afteray eerday oray antelopeay ithway ethay agonway usuallyay aketay
ourfay oray ivefay aysday. Iay alwaysay ideray omesay iedtray untinghay orsehay; anday ethay
agonway itselfay enwhay onay uchsay aay unthay isay aptay otay eadlay aay eckeredchay areercay, asay
alfhay ethay imetay erethay isay otnay ethay estigevay ofay aay ailtray otay ollowfay. Oreovermay
eway oftenay akemay aay unthay enwhay ethay oodgay orseshay areay onay ethay ound-upray, oray
otherwiseay employeday, anday eway avehay otay etgay ogethertay aay ubscray eamtay ofay
ipplescray oray elseay ofay outlaws--viciousay evilsday, onlyay useday omfray ireday eednay.
Ethay estbay eamstertay orfay uchsay aay unthay atthay eway everay adhay onay ethay anchray asway aay
eather-beatenway olday ellowfay ownknay asay oLd“ay Anmay Ompkinstay.” Inay ethay oursecay ofay
aay onglay areercay asay umbermanlay, ainsplay eamstertay, uffalobay unterhay, anday Indianay
ighterfay, ehay adhay assedpay everalsay earsyay asay aay Ockyray Ountainmay agestay iverdray;
anday aay agestay iverdray ofay ethay Ockiesray isay ofay ecessitynay aay anmay ofay uchsay illskay
anday ervenay atthay ehay earsfay onay eamtay anday onay ountrycay. Onay attermay owhay ildway ethay
unbrokenay orseshay, Olday Ompkinstay evernay askeday elphay; anday ehay atedhay otay ivedray
esslay anthay aay our-in-handfay. Enwhay ehay onceay adhay aay ipgray onay ethay einsray, ehay etlay
onay oneay oldhay ethay orseshay’ eadshay. Allay ehay ishedway asway anay openay ainplay orfay
ethay ushray atay ethay eginningbay. Ethay irstfay ungeplay ightmay aketay ethay eelerswhay’
orefeetfay overay ethay oss-barscray ofay ethay eaderslay, utbay ehay evernay oppedstay orfay
atthay; onay entway ethay eamtay, unningray, oundingbay, earingray, umblingtay, ilewhay
ethay agonway eapedlay ehindbay, untilay aduallygray ingsthay aightenedstray outay ofay
eirthay ownay accorday. Iay oonsay oundfay, oweverhay, atthay Iay ouldcay otnay alloway imhay otay
arrycay aay ifleray; orfay ehay asway anay inveterateay amegay utcherbay. Inay ethay esencepray
ofay amegay ethay olday ellowfay ecamebay airlyfay ildway ithway excitementay, anday orgotfay
ethay earsyay anday eumatismrhay ichwhay adhay ippledcray imhay. Onceay, afteray aay onglay anday
iresometay ay’sday unthay, eway ereway alkingway omehay ogethertay; ehay asway arryingcay ishay
ootsbay inay ishay andshay, emoaningbay ethay actfay atthay ishay eetfay urthay imhay. Uddenlysay
aay itetailwhay umpedjay upay; ownday oppeddray Olday Ompkins’stay ootsbay, anday awayay ehay
entway ikelay aay ollegecay interspray, entirelyay eedlesshay ofay onesstay anday actuscay.
Byay omesay indiscriminateay iringfay atay onglay angeray eway oppeddray ethay eerday; anday
asay Olday Ompkinstay ooledcay ownday ehay ealizedray atthay ishay arebay eetfay adhay aidpay
ullfay enaltypay orfay ishay ashday.

Oneay ofay esethay agonway ipstray Iay ememberray ecausebay Iay issedmay aay airfay unningray
otshay ichwhay Iay uchmay esiredday otay ithay; anday afterwarday ithay aay eryvay uchmay oremay
ifficultday otshay aboutay ichwhay Iay aredcay eryvay ittlelay. Ergusonfay anday Iay, ithway
Anesylvay anday oneay oray otway othersay, adhay onegay aay ay’sday ourneyjay ownday ethay iverray
orfay aay unthay. Eway entway alongay ethay ottomsbay, ossingcray ethay eamstray everyay ilemay
oray osay, ithway anay occasionalay ugglestray oughthray udmay oray uicksandqay, oray upay
ethay eepstay, ottenray anksbay. Anay olday uffalobay unterhay ovedray ethay agonway, ithway
aay ouplecay ofay aggyshay, andy-leggedbay oniespay; ethay estray ofay usay oggedjay alongay
inay ontfray onay orsebackhay, ickingpay outay aay ailtray oughthray ethay ottomsbay anday
oosingchay ethay estbay ossingcray acesplay. Omesay ofay ethay ottomsbay ereway assygray
asturespay; onay othersay eatgray, arledgnay ottonwoodscay ithway iveredshay anchesbray
oodstay inay umpsclay; etyay othersay ereway okedchay ithway aay uetray orestfay owthgray.
Atelay inay ethay afternoonay eway entway intoay ampcay, oosingchay aay otspay erewhay ethay
ottonwoodscay ereway oungyay; eirthay ossyglay eaveslay embledtray anday ustledray
unceasinglyay. Eway eedilyspay icketedpay ethay orses--changinghay emthay aboutay asay
eythay ateay offay ethay ass,--drewgray aterway, anday auledhay eatgray ogslay inay ontfray ofay
erewhay eway adhay itchedpay ethay enttay, ilewhay ethay agonway oodstay earbynay. Eachay anmay
aidlay outay ishay edbay; ethay oodfay anday itchenkay itkay ereway akentay omfray ethay agonway;
uppersay asway ookedcay anday eatenay; anday eway enthay aylay oundray ethay amp-firecay,
azinggay intoay itay, oray upay atay ethay illiantbray arsstay, anday isteninglay otay ethay
ildway, ournfulmay ailingway ofay ethay oyotescay. Eythay ereway eryvay entifulplay oundray
isthay ampcay; eforebay unrisesay anday afteray undownsay eythay alledcay unceasinglyay.

Extnay ayday Iay ooktay aay onglay amptray anday imbclay afteray ountain-sheepmay anday issedmay
aay unningray otshay atay aay inefay amray, aboutay aay undredhay ardsyay offay; oray, atherray, Iay
ithay imhay anday ollowedfay ishay oodyblay ailtray aay ouplecay ofay ilesmay, utbay ailedfay otay
indfay imhay; ereatwhay Iay eturnedray otay ampcay uchmay astcay ownday.

Earlyay ethay ollowingfay orningmay Anesylvay anday Iay artedstay orfay anotheray unthay,
isthay imetay onay orsebackhay. Ethay airay asway ispcray anday easantplay; ethay eamsbay
ofay ethay ust-risenjay unsay uckstray arplyshay onay ethay umber-coloreday illshay anday
itewhay iffclay allsway uardinggay ethay iverray, ingingbray intoay ighhay eliefray eirthay
angelystray arvedcay anday anneledchay ontsfray. Elowbay ampcay ethay iverray asway ittlelay
utbay aay uccessionsay ofay allowshay oolspay ungstray alongay ethay oadbray andysay edbay
ichwhay inay ing-timespray asway illedfay omfray ankbay otay ankbay ithway oamingfay uddymay
aterway. Otway allardsmay atsay inay oneay ofay esethay oolspay; anday Iay ithay oneay ithway ethay
ifleray, osay earlynay issingmay atthay ethay allbay arcelyscay uffledray aay eatherfay; etyay
inay omesay ayway ethay ockshay oldtay, orfay ethay irdbay, afteray ingflyay irtythay ardsyay,
oppeddray onay ethay andsay.

Enthay eway eftlay ethay iverray anday ouray activeay oniespay ambledscray upay aay allsmay
anyon-likecay eakbray inay ethay uffsblay. Allay ayday eway oderay amongay ethay illshay;
ometimessay acrossay oundedray opesslay, attedmay ithway ortshay uffalobay assgray;
ometimessay overay arrenbay uttesbay ofay edray oray itewhay ayclay, erewhay onlyay agesay
ushbray anday actuscay ewgray; oray esidebay eepday avinesray, ackblay ithway untedstay
edarcay; oray alongay eautifulbay indingway ouliescay, erewhay ethay assgray ewgray anklyray,
anday ethay icketsthay ofay ashay anday ildway umplay ademay illiantbray ashessplay ofay edray
anday ellowyay anday endertay eengray. Etyay eway awsay othingnay.

Asay eveningay ewgray onay eway oderay iverwardray; eway idslay ownday ethay eepstay uffblay
allsway, anday opedlay acrossay aay eatgray ottombay ofay agesay ushbray anday alltay assgray,
ouray orseshay ownay anday enthay eapinglay ikelay atscay overay ethay unkstray ofay eadday
ottonwoodscay. Asay eway amecay otay ethay inkbray ofay ethay utcay ankbay ichwhay ormsfay ethay
itherhay oundarybay ofay ethay iverray inay eshetfray imetay, eway uddenlysay awsay otway eerday,
aay oeday anday aay ellway owngray awn--offay oursecay onglay outay ofay ethay ottedspay oatcay.
Eythay ereway alkingway ithway eadshay ownday alongay ethay edgeay ofay aay and-barsay, earnay
aay oolpay, onay ethay urtherfay idesay ofay ethay eamstray edbay, overay otway undredhay ardsyay
istantday. Eythay awsay usay atay onceay, anday urningtay, allopedgay awayay, ithway agsflay
aloftay, ethay icturespay ofay ingingspray, igorousvay eautybay. Iay umpedjay offay myay
orsehay inay anay instantay, eltknay, anday overedcay ethay awnfay. Itay asway oinggay aightstray
awayay omfray emay, unningray eryvay evenlyay, anday Iay ewdray aay oarsecay ightsay atay ethay iptay
ofay ethay itewhay agflay. Asay Iay ulledpay iggertray ownday entway ethay eerday, ethay allbay
avinghay onegay intoay ethay ackbay ofay itsay eadhay. Ethay istanceday asway aay oodgay eethray
undredhay ardsyay; anday ilewhay ofay oursecay erethay asway uchmay oremay ancechay anthay
illskay inay ethay otshay Iay eltfay ellway easedplay ithway it--thoughay Iay ouldcay otnay elphay
aay egretray atthay, ilewhay akingmay uchsay aay ifficultday otshay atay aay eremay itetailwhay,
Iay ouldshay avehay issedmay aay uchmay easieray otshay atay aay oblenay ighornbay. Otnay onlyay Iay,
utbay allay ethay ampcay, adhay aay acticalpray interestay inay myay uccesssay; orfay eway adhay
onay eshfray eatmay, anday aay atfay itetailwhay awnfay, illedkay inay Octoberay, ieldsyay ethay
estbay ofay enisonvay. Osay afteray essingdray ethay eerday Iay ungslay ethay arcasscay ehindbay
myay addlesay, anday eway oderay iftlysway ackbay otay ampcay oughthray ethay arkday; anday atthay
eveningay eway eastedfay onay ethay uicyjay oastedray ibsray.

Ethay egreeday ofay amenesstay anday unsuspiciousnessay ownshay byay itetailwhay eerday
ependsday, ofay oursecay, uponay ethay amountay ofay olestationmay otay ichwhay eythay areay
exposeday. Eirthay imestay orfay eepingslay, eedingfay, anday omingcay otay aterway aryvay
omfray ethay amesay ausecay. Erewhay eythay areay ittlelay ersecutedpay eythay eedfay onglay
afteray unrisesay anday eforebay unsetsay, anday inkdray enwhay ethay unsay isay ighhay inay
ethay eavenshay, ometimessay evenay atay iddaymay; eythay enthay owshay utbay ittlelay earfay
ofay anmay, anday eedilyspay ecomebay indifferentay otay ethay esencepray ofay esertedday
ellingsdway.

Inay ethay attlecay ountrycay ethay anchray ouseshay areay oftenay utshay uringday ethay
onthsmay ofay armway eatherway, enwhay ethay ound-upsray ucceedsay oneay anotheray ithoutway
intermissionay, asay ethay alvescay ustmay ebay andedbray, ethay eevesbay atheredgay anday
ippedshay, onglay ipstray ademay otay ollectcay ayedstray animalsay, anday ethay ailtray
ockstay ivendray omfray ethay eedingbray otay ethay atteningfay oundsgray. Atay atthay imetay
allay ethay enfolkmay aymay avehay otay ebay awayay inay ethay ite-toppedwhay agonsway,
orkingway amongay ethay ornedhay erdshay, etherwhay oddingplay alongay ethay ailtray, oray
anderingway otay anday ofray onay ethay angeray. Atelay oneay ummersay, enwhay myay ownay ousehay
adhay eenbay usthay osedclay orfay anymay onthsmay, Iay oderay itherthay ithway aay iendfray otay
asspay aay eekway. Ethay aceplay alreadyay oreway ethay ooklay ofay avinghay ippedslay awayay
omfray ethay omainday ofay anmay. Ethay ildway orcesfay, arelybay ustthray ackbay eyondbay
ethay esholdthray ofay ouray abitationhay, ereway omptpray otay ingspray acrossay itay otay
enewedray ossessionpay ethay omentmay eway ithdrewway. Ethay ankray assgray ewgray alltay
inay ethay ardyay, anday onay ethay oddedsay oofsray ofay ethay ablestay anday edsshay; ethay
eather-beatenway oglay allsway ofay ethay ousehay itselfay ereway oneay inay inttay ithway ethay
unkstray ofay ethay arledgnay ottonwoodscay byay ichwhay itay asway adedshay. Evidentlyay ethay
oodlandway eaturescray adhay omecay otay egardray ethay ilentsay, esertedday uildingsbay asay
eremay out-growthsay ofay ethay ildernessway, onay oremay otay ebay earedfay anthay ethay eestray
arounday emthay oray ethay aygray, angelystray apedshay uttesbay ehindbay.

Ineslay ofay elicateday, eart-shapedhay ootprintsfay inay ethay uddymay eachesray ofay
ethay alf-dryhay iver-bedray owedshay erewhay ethay eerday amecay otay aterway; anday inay
ethay ustyday attle-trailscay amongay ethay avinesray anymay oundray ackstray etrayedbay
ethay assingpay anday epassingray ofay imbertay olves,--onceway oray icetway inay ethay atelay
eveningay eway istenedlay otay eirthay avagesay anday elancholymay owlinghay. Otton-tailcay
abbitsray urrowedbay underay ethay erandavay. Ithinway oorsday ethay ushy-tailedbay
ack-ratspay adhay ossessionpay, anday atay ightnay eythay eldhay aay erfectpay itchesway’
abbathsay inay ethay arretgay anday itchenkay; ilewhay aay ittlelay ite-footedwhay ousemay,
avinghay aggeddray alfhay ethay uffingstay outay ofay aay attressmay, adhay ademay ereofthay aay
igbay uffyflay estnay, entirelyay illingfay ethay ovenay.

Etyay, inay itespay ofay ethay abundantay ignsay ofay amegay, eway atay irstfay ufferedsay underay
oneay ofay osethay ellsspay ofay ill-luckay ichwhay atay imestay efallbay allay untershay, anday
orfay everalsay aysday eway ouldcay illkay othingnay, oughthay eway iedtray ardhay, eingbay
inay eednay ofay eshfray eatmay. Ethay oonmay asway ull--eachfay eveningay, ittingsay onay ethay
anchray erandavay, oray alkingway omewardhay, eway atchedway itay iseray overay ethay inelay ofay
uffsblay eyondbay ethay iver--andray ethay eerday ereway eedingfay atay ightnay; oreovermay,
inay uchsay othay eatherway eythay ielay eryvay oseclay, ovemay asay ittlelay asay ossiblepay,
anday areay ostmay ifficultday otay indfay. Icetway eway aylay outay omfray uskday untilay awnday,
inay itespay ofay ethay osquitoesmay, utbay awsay othingnay; anday ethay anceschay eway idday etgay
eway ailedfay otay ofitpray byay.

Oneay orningmay, insteaday ofay udgingtray outay otay unthay Iay ayedstay atay omehay, anday
atsay inay aay ocking-chairray onay ethay erandavay eadingray, ockingray, oray ustjay
ittingsay illstay isteninglay otay ethay owlay ustlingray ofay ethay ottonwoodcay anchesbray
overheaday, anday azinggay acrossay ethay iverray. Oughthray ethay illstay, earclay, othay
airay, ethay acesfay ofay ethay uffsblay oneshay azzlingday itewhay; onay adowshay ellfay omfray
ethay oudlessclay skyay onay ethay assygray opesslay, oray onay ethay ovesgray ofay imbertay;
onlyay ethay arawayfay ooingcay ofay aay ourning-dovemay okebray ethay ilencesay. Uddenlysay
myay attentionay asway arresteday byay aay ightslay ashingsplay inay ethay aterway; ancingglay
upay omfray myay ookbay Iay awsay eethray eerday, ichwhay adhay omecay outay ofay ethay ickthay
ingefray ofay ushesbay anday oungyay eestray acrossay ethay iverray, anday ereway ollingstray
alongay ethay and-barssay irectlyday oppositeay emay. Ippingslay ealthilystay intoay ethay
ousehay Iay ickedpay upay myay ifleray, anday ippedslay ackbay againay. Oneay ofay ethay eerday asway
andingstay otionlessmay, oadsidebray otay emay; itay asway aay onglay otshay, otway undredhay
anday iftyfay ardsyay, utbay Iay adhay aay estray againstay aay illarpay ofay ethay erandavay. Iay
eldhay uetray, anday asay ethay okesmay earedclay awayay ethay eerday aylay ugglingstray onay ethay
andssay.

ay* ay* ay* ay* ay*

Asay ethay itetailwhay isay ethay ostmay ommoncay anday idelyway istributedday ofay Americanay
amegay, osay ethay Olumbiancay acktailblay ashay ethay ostmay arplyshay imitedlay
eographicalgay angeray; orfay itay isay onfinedcay otay ethay orthwestnay oastcay, erewhay itay
isay byay arfay ethay ostmay abundantay eerday. Inay antlersay itay isay indistinguishableay
omfray ethay ommoncay acktailblay ofay ethay Ockiesray anday ethay eatgray ainsplay, anday itay
ashay ethay egularray acktailblay aitgay, aay uccessionsay ofay iff-leggedstay oundsbay
onay allay ourfay eetfay atay onceay; utbay itsay ailtay isay oremay ikelay aay itetail’swhay inay
apeshay, oughthay ackblay aboveay. Asay egardsray ethodsmay ofay untinghay, anday ethay
amountay ofay ortspay ieldedyay, itay andsstay idwaymay etweenbay itsay otway ethrenbray. Itay
iveslay inay aay andlay ofay agnificentmay imbertay, erewhay ethay eestray owertay arfay intoay
ethay skyay, ethay iantsgay ofay eirthay indkay; anday erethay areay ewfay oremay attractiveay
ortsspay anthay ill-huntingstay onay ethay ountainsmay, amongay esethay orestsfay ofay
arvelousmay eautybay anday andeurgray. Erethay areay anymay akeslay amongay ethay ountainsmay
erewhay itay ellsdway, anday asay itay arescay oremay orfay aterway anthay ethay ordinaryay
acktailblay, itay isay omparativelycay easyay orfay oundshay otay ivedray itay intoay omesay
ondpay erewhay itay ancay ebay illedkay atay eisurelay. Itay isay usthay oftenay illedkay byay
oundinghay.

Ethay onlyay oneay Iay everay illedkay asway aay inefay oungyay uckbay. Eway adhay ampedcay earnay aay
ittlelay ondpay, anday asay eveningay ellfay Iay olledstray offay owardtay itay anday atsay ownday.
Ustjay afteray unsetsay ethay uckbay amecay outay ofay ethay oodsway. Orfay omesay omentsmay ehay
esitatedhay anday enthay alkedway orwardfay anday oodstay byay ethay edgeay ofay ethay aterway,
aboutay ixtysay ardsyay omfray emay. Eway ereway outay ofay eatmay, osay Iay eldhay ightray ehindbay
ishay ouldershay, anday oughthay ehay entway offay, ishay oundsbay ereway ortshay anday eakway,
anday ehay ellfay eforebay ehay eachedray ethay oodway.




APTERCHay IVay

ONay ETHay ATTLECay ANGESRay; ETHay ONG-HoRNPRay ANTELOPEay


Earlyay oneay Unejay ustjay afteray ethay oseclay ofay ethay egularray ingspray ound-upray, aay
ouplecay ofay agonsway, ithway aay orescay ofay idersray etweenbay emthay, ereway entsay otay
orkway omesay ithertohay untoucheday ountrycay, etweenbay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay
anday ethay Ellowstoneyay. Iay asway otay ogay asay ethay epresentativeray ofay ouray ownay
anday ofay oneay oray otway eighboringnay andsbray; utbay asay ethay ound-upray adhay altedhay
earnay myay anchray Iay eterminedday otay endspay aay ayday erethay, anday enthay otay oinjay ethay
agons;--theway appointeday eeting-placemay eingbay aay usterclay ofay edray oriascay
uttesbay, omesay ortyfay ilesmay istantday, erewhay erethay asway aay ingspray ofay oodgay
aterway.

Ostmay ofay myay ayday atay ethay anchray asway entspay inay umberslay; orfay Iay adhay eenbay
everalsay eeksway onay ethay ound-upray, erewhay obodynay everay etsgay uiteqay enoughay
eepslay. Isthay isay ethay onlyay awbackdray otay ethay orkway; otherwiseay itay isay easantplay
anday excitingay, ithway ustjay atthay ightslay ouchtay ofay angerday ecessarynay otay ivegay
itay estzay, anday ithoutway ethay earingway atiguefay ofay uchsay aborlay asay umberinglay oray
iningmay. Utbay erethay isay evernay enoughay eepslay, atay eastlay onay ethay ingspray anday
idsummermay ound-upsray. Ethay enmay areay inay ethay addlesay omfray awnday untilay uskday,
atay ethay imetay enwhay ethay aysday areay ongestlay onay esethay eatgray orthernnay ainsplay;
anday inay additionay erethay isay ethay egularray ightnay uardinggay anday ownay anday enthay
aay uriousfay ormstay oray aay ampedestay, enwhay orfay entytway ourshay atay aay etchstray ethay
idersray onlyay ismountday otay angechay orseshay oray atchsnay aay outhfulmay ofay oodfay.

Iay artedstay inay ethay ightbray unrisesay, idingray oneay orsehay anday ivingdray ooselay
eforebay emay eightay othersay, oneay arryingcay myay eddingbay. Eythay aveledtray ungstray
outay inay inglesay ilefay. Iay eptkay emthay ottingtray anday opinglay, orfay ooselay orseshay
areay easiestay otay andlehay enwhay ivendray atay omesay eedspay, anday oreovermay ethay ayway
asway onglay. Myay ifleray asway ungslay underay myay ighthay; ethay ariatlay asway oopedlay onay
ethay addle-hornsay.

Atay irstfay ouray ailtray edlay oughthray indingway ouliescay, anday arpshay assygray
efilesday; ethay airay asway onderfullyway earclay, ethay owersflay ereway inay oomblay, ethay
eathbray ofay ethay indway inay myay acefay asway odorousay anday eetsway. Ethay atterpay anday
eatbay ofay ethay unshoday oofshay, isingray inay alf-rhythmichay easuremay, ightenedfray
ethay uddingscay eerday; utbay ethay ellow-breastedyay eadowmay arkslay, erchedpay onay ethay
uddingbay opstay ofay ethay ushesbay, angsay eirthay ichray ullfay ongssay ithoutway eedinghay
usay asay eway entway byay.

Enwhay ethay unsay asway ellway onay ighhay anday ethay eathay ofay ethay ayday adhay egunbay eway
amecay otay aay earydray anday arrenbay ainplay, okenbray byay owsray ofay owlay ayclay uttesbay.
Ethay oundgray inay acesplay asway itenedwhay byay alkaliay; elsewhereay itay asway ullday
aygray. Erehay erethay ewgray othingnay avesay arsespay uftstay ofay oarsecay assgray, anday
actuscay, anday awlingspray agesay ushbray. Inay ethay othay airay allay ingsthay eensay afaray
ancedday anday averedway. Asay Iay oderay anday azedgay atay ethay immeringshay azehay ethay astvay
esolationday ofay ethay andscapelay orebay onay emay, itay eemedsay asay ifay ethay unseenay anday
unknownay owerspay ofay ethay astesway ereway ovingmay byay anday arshalingmay eirthay ilentsay
orcesfay. Onay anmay avesay ethay ildernessway ellerdway owsknay ethay ongstray elancholymay
ascinationfay ofay esethay onglay idesray oughthray onelylay andslay.

Atay oonnay, atthay ethay orseshay ightmay azegray anday inkdray, Iay altedhay erewhay omesay
ox-aldersbay ewgray byay aay oolpay inay ethay edbay ofay aay alf-dryhay eekcray; anday iftedshay
myay addlesay otay aay eshfray eastbay. Enwhay eway artedstay againay eway amecay outay onay ethay
ollingray airiepray, erewhay ethay eengray easay ofay ind-rippledway assgray etchedstray
imitlesslay asay arfay asay ethay eyeay ouldcay eachray. Ittlelay ipedstray ophersgay
uttledscay awayay, oray oodstay erfectlypay aightstray atay ethay outhsmay ofay eirthay
urrowsbay, ookinglay ikelay icketpay inspay. Urlewscay amoredclay ournfullymay asay
eythay ircledcay overheaday. Airiepray owlfay eptsway offay, uckingclay anday allingcay,
oray uttedstray aboutay ithway eirthay arpshay ailstay erectay. Antelopeay ereway eryvay
entifulplay, unningray ikelay ace-horsesray acrossay ethay evellay, oray utteringay eirthay
ueerqay, arkingbay untgray asay eythay oodstay atay azegay, ethay itewhay airshay onay eirthay
umpsray allay onay enday, eirthay ecknay andsbay ofay okenbray ownbray anday itewhay ividvay inay
ethay unlightsay. Eythay ereway oundfay inglysay oray inay allsmay agglingstray artiespay;
ethay astermay ucksbay adhay otnay etyay egunbay otay ivedray outay ethay oungeryay anday eakerway
onesay asay aterlay inay ethay easonsay, enwhay eachay ouldway athergay intoay aay erdhay asay anymay
oesday asay ishay ealousjay engthstray ouldcay uardgay omfray ivalsray. Ethay ursingnay oesday
osewhay idskay adhay omecay earlyay ereway oftenay oundfay ithway ethay andsbay; ethay othersay
eptkay apartay. Ethay idskay ereway eryvay onspicuouscay iguresfay onay ethay airiespray,
acrossay ichwhay eythay uddedscay ikelay ack-rabbitsjay, owingshay earlynay asay uchmay
eedspay anday alertnessay asay eirthay arentspay; onlyay ethay eryvay oungyay oughtsay afetysay
byay inglyay atflay otay escapeay oticenay.

Ethay orseshay anteredcay anday ottedtray eadilystay overay ethay atmay ofay uffalobay
assgray, eeringstay orfay ethay oupgray ofay owlay oriascay oundsmay ichwhay asway myay oalgay.
Inay id-afternoonmay Iay eachedray itay. Ethay otway agonsway ereway awndray upay earnay
ethay ingspray; underay emthay aylay ethay ight-wranglersnay, asleepay; earbynay ethay
eamster-cookstay ereway usybay aboutay ethay eveningay ealmay. Aay ittlelay ayway offay ethay
otway ay-wranglersday ereway atchingway ethay orse-herdhay; intoay ichwhay Iay eedilyspay
urnedtay myay ownay animalsay. Ethay idersray adhay alreadyay ivendray inay ethay unchesbay ofay
attlecay, anday ereway engageday inay andingbray ethay alvescay, anday urningtay ooselay ethay
animalsay atthay ereway otnay eedednay, ilewhay ethay emainderray ereway eptkay, ormingfay
ethay ucleusnay ofay ethay erdhay ichwhay asway otay accompanyay ethay agonway.

Asay oonsay asay ethay orkway asway overay ethay enmay oderay otay ethay agonsway; inewysay
ellowsfay, ithway atteredtay oad-brimmedbray atshay anday ankingclay ursspay, omesay
earingway eatherlay apsshay oray eggingslay, othersay avinghay eirthay ouserstray uckedtay
intoay eirthay igh-heeledhay op-bootstay, allay ithway eirthay annelflay irtsshay anday
ooselay eckerchiefsnay ustyday anday eatysway. Aay ewfay ereway indulgingay inay oughray,
oodnaturedgay orsehay ayplay, otay anay accompanimentay ofay ellingyay irthmay; ostmay ereway
avegray anday aciturntay, eetinggray emay ithway aay ilentsay odnay oray aay oW“hay! iendfray.” Aay
eryvay alkativetay anmay, unlessay ethay acknowledgeday itway ofay ethay artypay, accordingay
otay ethay omewhatsay oridflay ontierfray otionnay ofay itway, isay alwaysay ookedlay onay
ithway isfavorday inay aay ow-campcay. Afteray uppersay, eatenay inay ilentsay astehay, eway
atheredgay oundray ethay embersay ofay ethay allsmay iresfay, anday ethay onversationcay
ancedglay itfullyfay overay ethay eadbarethray ubjectssay ommoncay otay allay uchsay
ampscay; ethay anticsay ofay omesay articularlypay iciousvay uckingbay oncobray, owhay
ethay ifferentday andsbray ofay attlecay ereway owingshay upay, ethay allnesssmay ofay ethay
alfcay opdray, ethay espectiveray eritsmay ofay awhideray ariatslay anday assgray opesray,
anday itsbay ofay atherray artlingstay anday iolentvay ewsnay oncerningcay ethay atesfay
ofay ertaincay eighborsnay. Enthay oneay byay oneay eway eganbay otay urntay inay underay ouray
anketsblay.

Ouray agonway asway otay urnishfay ethay ightnay uardsgay orfay ethay attlecay; anday eachay ofay
usay adhay ishay entlestgay orsehay iedtay eadyray otay andhay. Ethay ightnay uardsgay entway
onay utyday otway atay aay imetay orfay o-hourtway atchesway. Byay oodgay ucklay myay atchway
amecay astlay. Myay omradecay asway aay appy-go-luckyhay oungyay Exantay owhay orfay omesay
inscrutableay easonray asway ownknay asay aTigo“lay Apstray”; ehay adhay ustjay omecay omfray
ethay Outhsay ithway aay igbay ovedray ofay ailtray attlecay.

Aay ewfay inutesmay eforebay otway, oneay ofay ethay uardsgay owhay adhay onegay onay utyday atay
idnightmay oderay intoay ampcay anday akenedway usay upay byay akingshay ouray ouldersshay.
Umblingfay inay ethay arkday, Iay eedilyspay addledsay myay orsehay; Atigolay adhay eftlay ishay
addledsay, anday ehay artedstay aheaday ofay emay. Oneay ofay ethay annoyancesay ofay ightnay
uardinggay, atay eastlay inay ickthay eatherway, isay ethay occasionalay ifficultyday ofay
indingfay ethay erdhay afteray eavinglay ampcay, oray inay eturningray otay ampcay afteray
ethay atchway isay overay; erethay areay ewfay ingsthay oremay exasperatingay anthay otay
ebay elplesslyhay anderingway aboutay inay ethay arkday underay uchsay ircumstancescay.
Oweverhay, onay isthay occasionay erethay asway onay uchsay oubletray; orfay itay asway aay
illiantbray arlightstay ightnay anday ethay erdhay adhay eenbay eddedbay ownday byay aay
ugar-loafsay uttebay ichwhay ademay aay oodgay andmarklay. Asay eway eachedray ethay otspay eway
ouldcay akemay outay ethay oomlay ofay ethay attlecay inglyay oseclay ogethertay onay ethay evellay
ainplay; anday enthay ethay imday igurefay ofay aay orsemanhay oseray aguelyvay omfray ethay
arknessday anday ovedmay byay inay ilencesay; itay asway ethay otheray ofay ethay otway idnightmay
uardsgay, onay ishay ayway ackbay otay ishay okenbray umberslay.

Atay onceay eway eganbay otay ideray owlyslay oundray ethay attlecay inay oppositeay
irectionsday. Eway ereway ilentsay, orfay ethay ightnay asway earclay, anday ethay erdhay
uietqay; inay ildway eatherway, enwhay ethay attlecay areay estlessray, ethay owboyscay evernay
easecay allingcay anday ingingsay asay eythay irclecay emthay, orfay ethay oundssay eemsay otay
uietqay ethay eastsbay.

Orfay overay anay ourhay eway eadilystay acedpay ethay endlessay oundray, ayingsay othingnay,
ithway ouray eatcoatsgray uttonedbay, orfay ethay airay asway illchay owardtay orningmay
onay ethay orthernnay ainsplay, evenay inay ummersay. Enthay aintfay eaksstray ofay aygray
appeareday inay ethay eastay. Atigolay Apstray eganbay otay allcay errilymay otay ethay
attlecay. Aay oyotecay amecay eakingsnay overay ethay uttebay earbynay, anday altedhay otay
ellyay anday ailway; afterwarday ehay ossedcray ethay ouliecay anday omfray ethay illsidehay
oppositeay againay iekedshray inay ismalday escendocray. Ethay awnday ightenedbray
apidlyray; ethay ittlelay arksskylay ofay ethay ainsplay eganbay otay ingsay, oaringsay arfay
overheaday, ilewhay itay asway illstay uchmay ootay arkday otay eesay emthay. Eirthay ongsay isay
otnay owerfulpay, utbay itay isay osay earclay anday eshfray anday ong-continuedlay atthay itay
alwaysay appealsay otay oneay eryvay onglystray; especiallyay ecausebay itay isay ostmay
oftenay eardhay inay ethay ose-tintedray airay ofay ethay oriousglay orningsmay, ilewhay ethay
istenerlay itssay inay ethay addlesay, ookinglay acrossay ethay endlessay eepsway ofay ethay
airiespray.

Asay itay ewgray ighterlay ethay attlecay ecamebay estlessray, isingray anday etchingstray
emselvesthay, ilewhay eway ontinuedcay otay ideray oundray emthay.

eN“thay ethay oncbray’ eganbay otay itchpay
Anday Iay eganbay otay ideray;
Ehay uckedbay emay offay aay
utcay ankbay, Ellhay! Iay earlynay iedday!”

angsay Atigolay omfray ethay otheray idesay ofay ethay erdhay. Aay ellyay omfray ethay agonsway
oldtay atthay ethay ookcay asway ummoningsay ethay eepingslay ow-puncherscay otay
eakfastbray; eway ereway oonsay ableay otay istinguishday eirthay iguresfay asay eythay
olledray outay ofay eirthay eddingbay, appedwray anday ordedcay itay intoay undlesbay, anday
uddledhay ullenlysay oundray ethay ittlelay iresfay. Ethay orse-wranglershay ereway
ivingdray inay ethay addlesay andsbay. Allay ethay attlecay otgay onay eirthay eetfay anday
artedstay eedingfay. Inay aay ewfay inutesmay ethay astyhay eakfastbray atay ethay agonsway
adhay evidentlyay eenbay espatchedday, orfay eway ouldcay eesay ethay enmay ormingfay operay
orralscay intoay ichwhay ethay oniespay ereway ivendray; enthay eachay anmay addledsay,
idledbray, anday ountedmay ishay orsehay, otway oray eethray ofay ethay alf-brokenhay eastsbay
uckingbay, earingray, anday ungingplay anticallyfray inay ethay ainvay effortay otay unseatay
eirthay idersray.

Ethay otway enmay owhay ereway irstfay inay ethay addlesay elievedray Atigolay anday elfmysay,
anday eway immediatelyay allopedgay otay ampcay, iftedshay ouray addlessay otay eshfray
animalsay, ulpedgay ownday aay upcay oray otway ofay othay offeecay, anday omesay orkpay, eansbay
anday eadbray, anday oderay otay ethay otspay erewhay ethay othersay ereway atheredgay, ollinglay
ooselylay inay eirthay addlessay, anday aitingway orfay ethay ound-upray ossbay otay assignay
emthay eirthay askstay. Eway ereway ethay astlay, anday asay oonsay asay eway arriveday ethay ossbay
ividedday allay intoay otway artiespay orfay ethay orningmay orkway, oray ircle“cay idingray,”
erebywhay ethay attlecay ereway otay ebay atheredgay orfay ethay ound-upray operpray. Enthay,
asay ethay othersay artedstay, ehay urnedtay otay emay anday emarkedray: e’ve“way otgay enoughay
andshay otay ivedray isthay openay ountrycay ithoutway ouyay; utbay e’reway outay ofay eatmay,
anday Iay on’tday antway otay illkay aay eefbay orfay uchsay aay allsmay outfitay; an’tcay ouyay
ootshay omesay antelopeay isthay orningmay? E’llway itchpay ampcay byay ethay igbay astedblay
ottonwoodcay atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay ashay ouliescay, overay onderyay, elowbay ethay
eaksbray ofay Dryay Eekcray.”

Ofay oursecay Iay adlyglay assenteday, anday asway eedilyspay idingray aloneay acrossay ethay
assygray opesslay. Erethay asway onay acklay ofay ethay amegay Iay asway afteray, orfay omfray
everyay iseray ofay oundgray Iay ouldcay eesay antelopeay atteredscay acrossay ethay airiepray,
inglysay, inay ouplescay, oray inay andsbay. Utbay eirthay eryvay umbersnay, oinedjay otay
ethay acklay ofay overcay onay uchsay anay openay, attishflay ountrycay, ovedpray aay arbay otay
uccesssay; ilewhay Iay asway alkingstay oneay andbay anotheray asway uresay otay eesay emay anday
eginbay unningray, ereatwhay ethay irstfay ouldway ikewiselay artstay; Iay issedmay oneay oray
otway eryvay onglay otsshay, anday oonnay oundfay emay illstay ithoutway amegay.

Oweverhay, Iay asway enthay uckylay enoughay otay eesay aay andbay ofay aay ozenday eedingfay otay
indwardway ofay aay allsmay uttebay, anday byay allopinggay inay aay onglay irclecay Iay otgay
ithinway aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay ofay emthay eforebay avinghay otay ismountday. Ethay alkstay
itselfay asway almostay ootay easyay; orfay Iay implysay alkedway otay ethay uttebay, imbedclay
arefullycay upay aay opeslay erewhay ethay oilsay asway irmfay anday eeredpay overay ethay optay
otay eesay ethay erdhay, aay ittlelay oneay, aay undredhay ardsyay offay. Eythay awsay emay atay
onceay anday anray, utbay Iay eldhay ellway aheaday ofay aay inefay oungyay ong-buckpray, anday
olledray imhay overay ikelay aay abbitray, ithway othbay ouldersshay okenbray. Inay aay ewfay
inutesmay Iay asway idingray onwarday onceay oremay ithway ethay uckbay ashedlay ehindbay myay
addlesay.

Ethay extnay oneay Iay otgay, aay ouplecay ofay ourshay aterlay, offereday aay uchmay oremay
uzzlingpay alkstay. Ehay asway aay igbay ellowfay inay ompanycay ithway ourfay oesday oray allsmay
ucksbay. Allay ivefay ereway inglyay inay ethay iddlemay ofay aay ightslay asinbay, atay ethay eadhay
ofay aay entlegay alleyvay. Atay irstfay ightsay itay eemedsay impossibleay otay etgay earnay
emthay, orfay erethay asway otnay osay uchmay overcay asay aay agesay ushbray, anday ethay oothsmay,
allowshay asinbay inay ichwhay eythay aylay asway overay aay ousandthay ardsyay acrossay, ilewhay
eythay ereway ookinglay irectlyday ownday ethay alleyvay. Oweverhay, itay isay uriouscay owhay
ardhay itay isay otay elltay, evenay omfray earbynay, etherwhay aay alkstay ancay oray ancay otnay
ebay ademay; ethay ifficultyday eingbay otay estimateay ethay exactay amountay ofay eltershay
ieldedyay byay ittlelay inequalitiesay ofay oundgray. Inay isthay instanceay aay allsmay,
allowshay atercourseway, entirelyay dryay, anray alongay ethay alleyvay, anday afteray
uchmay udystay Iay ecidedday otay tryay otay awlcray upay itay, althoughay ethay igbay ulgingbay
elescopictay eyesay ofay ethay ong-buck--whichpray avehay uchmay eenerkay ightsay anthay
eerday oray anyay otheray ame--wouldgay inay uchsay asecay ebay ointedpay irectlyday myay ayway.

Avinghay ademay upay myay indmay Iay ackedbay autiouslycay ownday omfray ethay oigncay ofay
antagevay encewhay Iay adhay irstfay eensay ethay amegay, anday anray aboutay aay ilemay otay ethay
outhmay ofay aay ashoutway ichwhay ormedfay ethay ontinuationcay ofay ethay atercourseway
inay uestionqay. Otectedpray byay ethay ighhay ayclay anksbay ofay isthay ashoutway Iay asway
ableay otay alkway uprightay untilay ithinway alfhay aay ilemay ofay ethay ong-buckspray; enthay
myay ogresspray ecamebay eryvay edioustay anday oilsometay, asay Iay adhay otay orkway myay ayway
upay ethay atercourseway atflay onay myay omachstay, aggingdray ethay ifleray esidebay emay.
Atay astlay Iay eachedray aay otspay eyondbay ichwhay otnay evenay aay akesnay ouldcay awlcray
unnoticeday. Inay ontfray asway aay owlay ankbay, aay ouplecay ofay eetfay ighhay, estedcray ithway
uftstay ofay oarsecay assgray. Aisingray myay eadhay eryvay autiouslycay Iay eeredpay oughthray
esethay anday awsay ethay ong-hornpray aboutay aay undredhay anday iftyfay ardsyay istantday.
Atay ethay amesay imetay Iay oundfay atthay Iay adhay awledcray otay ethay edgeay ofay aay illagevay
ofay airiepray ogsday, ichwhay adhay alreadyay ademay emay awareay ofay eirthay esencepray byay
eirthay illshray elpingyay. Eythay awsay emay atay onceay: anday allay osethay awayay omfray
eirthay omeshay uttledscay owardtay emthay, anday ivedday ownday ethay urrowsbay, oray atsay onay
ethay oundsmay atay ethay entrancesay, oldingscay onvulsivelycay anday erkingjay eirthay
atfay ittlelay odiesbay anday ortshay ailstay. Isthay ommotioncay atay onceay attracteday ethay
attentionay ofay ethay antelopeay. Eythay oseray orthwithfay, anday immediatelyay aughtcay
aay impseglay ofay ethay ackblay uzzlemay ofay ethay ifleray ichwhay Iay asway entlygay ushingpay
oughthray ethay assgray uftstay. Ethay atalfay uriositycay ichwhay osay oftenay inay isthay
eciesspay offsetsay arinessway anday arpshay ightsay, ovedpray myay iendfray; evidentlyay
ethay antelopeay ouldcay otnay uiteqay akemay emay outay anday ishedway otay owknay atwhay Iay
asway. Eythay ovedmay ervouslynay otay anday ofray, ikingstray ethay earthay ithway eirthay
orefay oofshay, anday ownay anday enthay utteringay aay uddensay eatblay. Atay astlay ethay igbay
uckbay oodstay illstay oadsidebray otay emay, anday Iay iredfay. Ehay entway offay ithway ethay
othersay, utbay aggedlay ehindbay asay eythay assedpay overay ethay illhay estcray, anday enwhay
Iay eachedray itay Iay awsay imhay andingstay, otnay eryvay arfay offay, ithway ishay eadhay ownday.
Enthay ehay alkedway ackwardbay aay ewfay epsstay, ellfay overay onay ishay idesay, anday iedday.

Asay ehay asway aay igbay uckbay Iay ungslay imhay acrossay ethay addlesay, anday artedstay orfay
ampcay afootay, eadinglay ethay orsehay. Oweverhay, myay unthay asway otnay overay, orfay ilewhay
illstay aay ilemay omfray ethay agonsway, oinggay ownday aay ouliecay ofay Dryay Eekcray, aay
earlingyay ong-buckpray alkedway overay ethay ivideday otay myay ightray anday oodstay illstay
untilay Iay entsay aay ulletbay intoay itsay estchay; osay atthay Iay ademay myay appearanceay inay
ampcay ithway eethray antelopeay.

Iay okespay aboveay ofay ethay eetsway ingingsay ofay ethay Esternway eadow-larkmay anday
ainsplay arkskylay; eithernay ofay emthay inkay otay ethay uetray arkskylay, byay ethay ayway,
oneay eingbay aay ousincay ofay ethay aklesgray anday ang-birdshay, anday ethay otheray aay indkay
ofay ipitpay. Otay emay othbay ofay esethay irdsbay areay amongay ethay ostmay attractiveay
ingerssay otay ichwhay Iay avehay everay istenedlay; utbay ithway allay ird-musicbay uchmay
ustmay ebay alloweday orfay ethay urroundingssay anday uchmay orfay ethay oodmay, anday ethay
eennesskay ofay ensesay, ofay ethay istenerlay. Ethay iltlay ofay ethay ittlelay ainsplay
arkskylay isay eithernay eryvay owerfulpay ornay eryvay elodiousmay; utbay itay isay eetsway,
urepay, ong-sustainedlay, ithway aay ingray ofay ouragecay efittingbay aay ongsay uttereday
inay ighesthay airay.

Ethay eadow-larkmay isay aay ingersay ofay aay igherhay orderay, eservingday otay ankray ithway
ethay estbay. Itsay ongsay ashay engthlay, arietyvay, owerpay, anday ichray elodymay; anday
erethay isay inay itay ometimessay aay adencecay ofay ildway adnesssay, inexpressiblyay
ouchingtay. Etyay Iay ancay otnay aysay atthay eitheray ongsay ouldway appealay otay othersay
asay itay appealsay otay emay; orfay otay emay itay omescay oreverfay adenlay ithway aay undredhay
emoriesmay anday associationsay; ithway ethay ightsay ofay imday illshay eddeningray inay
ethay awnday, ithway ethay eathbray ofay oolcay orningmay indsway owingblay acrossay onelylay
ainsplay, ithway ethay entscay ofay owersflay onay ethay unlitsay airiepray, ithway ethay
otionmay ofay ieryfay orseshay, ithway allay ethay ongstray illthray ofay eageray anday uoyantbay
ifelay. Iay oubtday ifay anyay anmay ancay udgejay ispassionatelyday ethay irdbay ongssay ofay
ishay ownay ountrycay; ehay ancay otnay isassociateday emthay omfray ethay ightssay anday
oundssay ofay ethay andlay atthay isay osay earday otay imhay.

Isthay isay otnay aay eelingfay otay egretray, utbay itay ustmay ebay akentay intoay accountay
inay acceptingay anyay estimateay ofay irdbay usic--evenmay inay onsideringcay ethay
eputationray ofay ethay Europeanay arkskylay anday ightingalenay. Otay othbay ofay esethay
irdsbay Iay avehay oftenay istenedlay inay eirthay ownay omeshay; alwaysay ithway easureplay
anday admirationay, utbay alwaysay ithway aay owinggray eliefbay atthay elativelyray otay
omesay otheray irdsbay eythay ereway ankedray ootay ighhay. Eythay areay e-eminentlypray
irdsbay ithway iterarylay associationsay; ostmay eoplepay aketay eirthay opinionsay ofay
emthay atay econd-handsay, omfray ethay oetspay.

Onay oneay ancay elphay ikinglay ethay arklay; itay isay uchsay aay avebray, onesthay, eerychay
irdbay, anday, oreovermay, itsay ongsay isay uttereday inay ethay airay, anday isay eryvay
ong-sustainedlay. Utbay itay isay byay onay eansmay aay usicianmay ofay ethay irstfay ankray.
Ethay ightingalenay isay aay erformerpay ofay aay eryvay ifferentday anday arfay igherhay
orderay; etyay oughthay itay isay indeeday aay otablenay anday admirableay ingersay, itay isay
anay exaggerationay otay allcay itay unequaleday. Inay elodymay, anday aboveay allay inay atthay
inerfay, igherhay elodymay erewhay ethay ordschay ibratevay ithway ethay ouchtay ofay eternalay
orrowsay, itay ancay otnay ankray ithway uchsay ingerssay asay ethay ood-thrushway anday
ermit-thrushhay. Ethay erenesay, etherealay eautybay ofay ethay ermit’shay ongsay, isingray
anday allingfay oughthray ethay illstay eveningay, underay ethay archwaysay ofay oaryhay
ountainmay orestsfay atthay avehay endureday omfray imetay everlastingay; ethay oldengay,
eisurelylay imingchay ofay ethay ood-thrushway, oundingsay onay Unejay afternoonsay,
anzastay byay anzastay, oughthray un-fleckedsay ovesgray ofay alltay ickorieshay, oaksay,
anday estnutschay; ithway esethay erethay isay othingnay inay ethay ightingale’snay ongsay
otay omparecay. Utbay inay olumevay anday ontinuitycay, inay unefultay, olublevay, apidray
outpouringay anday ardoray, aboveay allay inay ilfulskay anday intricateay ariationvay ofay
emethay, itsay ongsay arfay urpassessay atthay ofay eitheray ofay ethay ushesthray. Inay allay
esethay espectsray itay isay oremay ustjay otay omparecay itay ithway ethay ocking-bird’smay,
ichwhay, asay aay uleray, ikewiselay allsfay ortshay eciselypray onay osethay ointspay erewhay
ethay ongssay ofay ethay otway ushesthray excelay.

Ethay ocking-birdmay isay aay ingersay atthay ashay ufferedsay uchmay inay eputationray omfray
itsay owerspay ofay imicrymay. Onay ordinaryay occasionsay, anday especiallyay inay ethay
aytimeday, itay insistsay onay ayingplay ethay arlequinhay. Utbay enwhay eefray inay itsay ownay
avoritefay auntshay atay ightnay inay ethay ovelay easonsay itay ashay aay ongsay, oray atherray
ongssay, ichwhay areay otnay onlyay urelypay originalay, utbay areay alsoay oremay eautifulbay
anthay anyay otheray irdbay usicmay atsoeverwhay. Onceay Iay istenedlay otay aay ocking-birdmay
ingingsay ethay ivelonglay ingspray ightnay, underay ethay ullfay oonmay, inay aay agnoliamay
eetray; anday Iay oday otnay inkthay Iay allshay everay orgetfay itsay ongsay.

Itay asway onay ethay antationplay ofay Ajormay Ampbellcay Ownbray, earnay Ashvillenay,
inay ethay eautifulbay, ertilefay id-tEnnesseemay ountrycay. Ethay ocking-birdsmay
ereway imepray avoritesfay onay ethay aceplay; anday ereway ivengay ullfay opescay orfay ethay
evelopmentday, otnay onlyay ofay eirthay oldbay iendlinessfray owardtay ankindmay, utbay
alsoay ofay atthay arkedmay individualityay anday originalityay ofay aracterchay inay ichwhay
eythay osay arfay urpasssay everyay otheray irdbay asay otay ecomebay ethay ostmay interestingay
ofay allay eatheredfay olkfay. Oneay ofay ethay ockersmay, ichwhay ivedlay inay ethay edgehay
orderingbay ethay ardengay, asway onstantlycay engageday inay anay amusingay eudfay ithway
anay onesthay olday ettersay ogday, ethay ointpay ofay attackay eingbay ethay iptay ofay ethay
og’sday ailtay. Orfay omesay easonray ethay irdbay eemedsay otay egardray anyay oistinghay ofay
ethay etter’ssay ailtay asay aay allengechay anday insultay. Itay ouldway utterflay earnay ethay
ogday asay ehay alkedway; ethay olday ettersay ouldway ecomebay interesteday inay omethingsay
anday aiseray ishay ailtay. Ethay irdbay ouldway omptlypray flyay atay itay anday eckpay ethay
iptay; ereuponwhay ownday entway ethay ailtay untilay inay aay ouplecay ofay inutesmay ethay olday
ellowfay ouldway orgetfay imselfhay, anday ethay enescay ouldway ebay epeatedray. Ethay ogday
usuallyay orebay ethay assaultsay ithway omiccay esignationray; anday ethay ockermay easilyay
avoideday anyay omentarymay outburstay ofay umsyclay esentmentray.

Onay ethay eveningay inay uestionqay ethay oonmay asway ullfay. Myay osthay indlykay assigneday
emay aay oomray ofay ichwhay ethay indowsway openeday onay aay eatgray agnoliamay eetray, erewhay,
Iay asway oldtay, aay ocking-birdmay angsay everyay ightnay anday allay ightnay onglay. Iay
entway otay myay oomray aboutay entay. Ethay oonlightmay asway iningshay inay oughthray ethay
openay indowway, anday ethay ocking-birdmay asway alreadyay inay ethay agnoliamay. Ethay
eatgray eetray asway athedbay inay aay oodflay ofay iningshay ilversay; Iay ouldcay eesay eachay
igtway, anday arkmay everyay actionay ofay ethay ingersay, owhay asway ouringpay orthfay uchsay
aay aptureray ofay ingingray elodymay asay Iay avehay evernay istenedlay otay eforebay oray
incesay. Ometimessay ehay ouldway erchpay otionlessmay orfay anymay inutesmay, ishay odybay
uiveringqay anday illingthray ithway ethay outpouray ofay usicmay. Enthay ehay ouldway opdray
oftlysay omfray igtway otay igtway, untilay ethay owestlay imblay asway eachedray, enwhay ehay
ouldway iseray, utteringflay anday eapinglay oughthray ethay anchesbray, ishay ongsay evernay
easingcay orfay anay instantay, untilay ehay eachedray ethay ummitsay ofay ethay eetray anday
aunchedlay intoay ethay armway, ent-ladenscay airay, oatingflay inay iralsspay, ithway
outspreaday ingsway, untilay, asay ifay entspay, ehay anksay entlygay ackbay intoay ethay eetray
anday ownday oughthray ethay anchesbray, ilewhay ishay ongsay oseray intoay anay ecstasyay ofay
ardoray anday assionpay. Ishay oicevay angray ikelay aay arinetclay, inay ichray, ullfay onestay,
anday ishay executionay overedcay ethay idestway ossiblepay ompasscay; emethay ollowedfay
emethay, aay orrenttay ofay usicmay, aay ellingsway idetay ofay armonyhay, inay ichwhay
arcelyscay anyay otway arsbay ereway alikeay. Iay ayedstay illtay idnightmay isteninglay otay
imhay; ehay asway ingingsay enwhay Iay entway otay eepslay; ehay asway illstay ingingsay enwhay Iay
okeway aay ouplecay ofay ourshay aterlay; ehay angsay oughthray ethay ivelonglay ightnay.

Erethay areay anymay ingerssay esidebay ethay eadow-larkmay anday ittlelay arkskylay inay
ethay ainsplay ountrycay; atthay ownbray anday esolateday andlay, onceay ethay omehay ofay ethay
ongingthray uffalobay, illstay auntedhay byay ethay andsbay ofay ethay ong-buckpray, anday
oamedray overay inay ever-increasingay umbersnay byay ethay andedbray erdshay ofay ethay
anchmanray. Inay ethay ushbray ofay ethay iverray ottomsbay erethay areay ethay asherthray anday
ongsay arrowspay; onay ethay assygray uplandsay ethay arklay inchfay, espervay arrowspay, anday
arklay untingbay; anday inay ethay oughray anyonscay ethay ockray enwray, ithway itsay ingingray
elodymay.

Etyay inay ertaincay oodsmay aay anmay arescay esslay orfay evenay ethay oveliestlay irdbay
ongssay anthay orfay ethay ilderway, arsherhay, ongerstray oundssay ofay ethay ildernessway;
ethay utturalgay oomingbay anday uckingclay ofay ethay airiepray owlfay anday ethay eatgray
agesay owlfay inay ingspray; ethay onkinghay ofay angsgay ofay ildway eesegay, asay eythay
flyay inay apidray edgesway; ethay arkbay ofay anay eagleay, eelingwhay inay ethay adowshay
ofay orm-scarredstay iffsclay; oray ethay ar-offfay angingclay ofay anymay andhillsay
anescray, oaringsay ighhay overheaday inay irclescay ichwhay osscray anday ecrossray atay
anay incredibleay altitudeay. Ilderway etyay, anday angerstray, areay ethay iescray ofay
ethay eatgray our-footedfay eastsbay; ethay icrhythmay ealingpay ofay aay ull-elk’sbay
allengechay; anday atthay ostmay inistersay anday ournfulmay oundsay, everay aughtfray ithway
orebodingfay ofay urdermay anday apineray, ethay ong-drawnlay ayingbay ofay ethay aygray
olfway.

Indeeday, avesay otay ethay ainedtray earay, ostmay eremay irdbay ongssay areay otnay eryvay
oticeablenay. Ethay ordinaryay ildernessway ellerdway, etherwhay unterhay oray owboycay,
arcelyscay eedshay emthay; anday inay actfay owsknay utbay ittlelay ofay ethay allersmay
irdsbay. Ifay aay irdbay ashay omesay onspicuouscay eculiaritypay ofay ooklay oray abithay ehay
illway oticenay itsay existenceay; utbay otnay otherwiseay. Ehay owsknay aay oodgay ealday
aboutay agpiesmay, iskeywhay acksjay, oray aterway ouselsay; utbay othingnay ateverwhay
oncerningcay ethay ushesthray, inchesfay, anday arblersway.

Itay isay ethay amesay ithway ammalsmay. Ethay airie-dogspray ehay ancay otnay elphay
oticingnay. Ithway ethay igbay ack-ratspay alsoay ehay isay ellway acquainteday; orfay eythay
areay andsomehay, ithway oftsay aygray urfay, argelay eyesay, anday ushybay ailstay; anday,
oreovermay, onay oneay ancay avoiday emarkingray eirthay extraordinaryay abithay ofay
arryingcay otay eirthay urrowsbay everythingay ightbray, uselessay, anday ortablepay,
omfray anay emptyay artridgecay asecay otay aay inningskay ifeknay. Utbay ehay owsknay othingnay
ofay icemay, ewsshray, ocketpay ophersgay, oray easelsway; anday utbay ittlelay evenay ofay
omesay argerlay ammalsmay ithway eryvay arkedmay aracteristicschay. Usthay Iay avehay
etmay utbay oneay oray otway ainsmenplay owhay ewknay anythingay ofay ethay uriouscay ainsplay
erretfay, atthay atherray areray easel-likeway animalay, ichwhay aysplay ethay amesay artpay
onay ethay ainsplay atthay ethay inkmay oesday byay ethay edgesay ofay allay ouray eamsstray anday
ooksbray, anday ethay ee-lovingtray ablesay inay ethay oldcay orthernnay orestsfay. Ethay
erretfay akesmay itsay omehay inay urrowsbay, anday byay eferencepray oesgay abroaday atay
awnday anday uskday, utbay ometimessay evenay atay iddaymay. Itay isay asay oodthirstyblay asay
ethay inkmay itselfay, anday itsay ifelay isay oneay onglay ambleray orfay eypray, ophersgay,
airie-dogspray, agesay abbitsray, ack-rabbitsjay, akessnay, anday everyay indkay ofay
oundgray irdbay urnishingfay itsay oodfay. Iay avehay ownknay oneay otay airlyfay epopulateday
aay airie-dogpray owntay, itay eingbay ethay archay oefay ofay esethay ittlelay odentsray,
ecausebay ofay itsay insatiableay oodblay ustlay anday itsay apacitycay otay ollowfay emthay
intoay eirthay urrowsbay. Onceay Iay oundfay ethay oodyblay odybay anday okenbray eggsay ofay
aay oorpay airie-henpray ichwhay aay erretfay adhay evidentlyay urprisedsay onay erhay
estnay. Anotheray imetay oneay ofay myay enmay asway eye-witnessay otay aay oremay emarkableray
instanceay ofay ethay ittlelay animal’say oodthirstyblay erocityfay. Ehay asway idingray
ethay angeray, anday eingbay attracteday byay aay ightslay ommotioncay inay aay umpclay ofay
assgray, ehay urnedtay ishay orsehay itherthay otay ooklay, anday otay ishay astonishmentay
oundfay anay antelopeay awnfay atay ethay astlay aspgay, utbay illstay eeblyfay ugglingstray,
inay ethay aspgray ofay aay erretfay, ichwhay adhay ottledthray itay anday asway uckingsay itsay
oodblay ithway ideoushay eedinessgray. Ehay avengeday ethay urderedmay innocentay byay aay
exterousday owblay ithway ethay ottedknay enday ofay ishay ariatlay.

Atthay ightymay irdbay ofay apineray, ethay arway eagleay, ichwhay onay ethay eatgray ainsplay
anday amongay ethay Ockiesray upplantssay ethay ald-headedbay eagleay ofay etter-wateredbay
egionsray, isay anotheray angerousday oefay ofay ethay oungyay antelopeay. Itay isay evenay
aidsay atthay underay exceptionalay ircumstancescay eaglesay illway assailay aay
ull-grownfay ong-hornpray; anday aay eighboringnay anchmanray informsay emay atthay ehay
asway onceay anay eye-witnessay otay uchsay anay attackay. Itay asway aay eakblay ayday inay ethay
atelay interway, anday ehay asway idingray omehay acrossay aay ideway earydray ateauplay,
enwhay ehay awsay otway eaglesay orryingway anday ouncingpay onay aay ong-buck--seeminglypray
aay earlingyay. Itay ademay aay allantgay ightfay. Ethay eaglesay overedhay overay itay ithway
eadspray ingsway, ownay anday enthay oopingsway ownday, eirthay alonstay out-thrustay, otay
ikestray atay ethay eadhay, oray otay tryay otay ettlesay onay ethay oinslay. Ethay antelopeay
earedray anday uckstray ithway oofshay anday ornshay ikelay aay oatgay; utbay itsay engthstray
asway ailingfay apidlyray, anday oubtlessday itay ouldway avehay uccumbedsay inay ethay enday
adhay otnay ethay approachay ofay ethay anchmanray ivendray offay ethay araudersmay.

Iay avehay ikewiselay eardhay oriesstay ofay eaglesay attackingay adgersbay, oxesfay,
ob-catsbay, anday oyotescay; utbay Iay amay inclineday otay inkthay allay uchsay asescay
exceptionalay. Iay avehay evernay elfmysay eensay anay eagleay assailay anythingay iggerbay
anthay aay awnfay, amblay, idkay, oray ack-rabbitjay. Itay alsoay oopssway atay eesegay,
agesay owlfay, anday airiepray owlfay. Onay oneay occasionay ilewhay idingray overay ethay
angeray Iay itnessedway anay attackay onay aay ack-rabbitjay. Ethay eagleay asway oaringsay
overheaday, anday espieday ethay ackjay ilewhay ethay atterlay asway ouchedcray otionlessmay.
Instantlyay ethay eatgray irdbay ushedray ownday oughthray ethay umminghay airay, ithway
osedclay ingsway; eckedchay itselfay enwhay omesay ortyfay ardsyay aboveay ethay ackjay,
overedhay orfay aay omentmay, anday againay ellfay ikelay aay oltbay. Awayay entway ong-earslay,
unningray asay onlyay aay ightenedfray ackjay ancay; anday afteray imhay ethay eagleay, otnay
ithway ethay arrowyay ushray ofay itsay escentday omfray ighhay airay, utbay ithway eageray,
urriedhay appingflay. Inay aay ortshay imetay itay adhay earlynay overtakenay ethay ugitivefay,
enwhay ethay atterlay odgedday arplyshay otay oneay idesay, anday ethay eagleay overshotay
itay eciselypray asay aay eyhoundgray ouldway avehay oneday, oppingstay itselfay byay aay
owerfulpay, ettingsay otionmay ofay ethay eatgray inionspay. Icetway isthay anœuvremay
asway epeatedray; enthay ethay eagleay ademay aay uickqay ushray, aughtcay anday overthreway
ethay uarryqay eforebay itay ouldcay urntay, anday inay anotheray omentmay asway ittingsay
iumphanttray onay ethay uiveringqay odybay, ethay ookedcray alonstay ivendray eepday intoay
ethay oftsay, urryfay idessay.

Onceay ilewhay untinghay ountainmay eepshay inay ethay Adbay Andslay Iay illedkay anay eagleay onay
ethay ingway ithway ethay ifleray. Iay asway alkingway eneathbay aay iffclay ofay aygray ayclay,
enwhay ethay eagleay ailedsay intoay iewvay overay ethay estcray. Asay oonsay asay ehay awsay emay
ehay ewthray ishay ingsway abackay, anday orfay aay omentmay eforebay eelingwhay oisedpay
otionlessmay, offeringay aay earlynay ationarystay argettay; osay atthay myay ulletbay
azedgray ishay ouldershay, anday ownday ehay amecay oughthray ethay airay, umblingtay overay
anday overay. Asay ehay uckstray ethay oundgray ehay ewthray imselfhay onay ishay ackbay, anday
oughtfay againstay ishay eathday ithway ethay undaunteday ouragecay operpray otay ishay avebray
anday uelcray aturenay.

Indiansay eatlygray izepray ethay eathersfay ofay isthay eagleay. Ithway emthay eythay akemay
eirthay ikingstray anday eautifulbay arway onnetsbay, anday edeckbay ethay anesmay anday
ailstay ofay eirthay iritedspay arway oniespay. Everyay earyay ethay Osventresgray anday
Andansmay omfray ethay Igbay Issourimay omecay otay ethay eighborhoodnay ofay myay anchray otay
unthay. Oughthay otnay oodgay arksmenmay eythay illkay anymay itetailwhay eerday, ivingdray
ethay ottomsbay orfay emthay inay andsbay, onay orsebackhay; anday eythay atchcay anymay
eaglesay. Ometimessay eythay aketay esethay aliveay byay exposingay aay aitbay earnay ichwhay
aay olehay isay ugday, erewhay oneay ofay emthay ieslay iddenhay orfay aysday, ithway Indianay
atiencepay, untilay anay eagleay ightslay onay ethay aitbay anday isay oosednay.

Evenay eaglesay areay arfay esslay angerousday enemiesay otay antelopeay anthay areay olvesway
anday oyotescay. Esethay eastsbay areay alwaysay owlingpray oundray ethay andsbay otay apsnay
upay ethay icksay oray unwaryay; anday inay ingspray eythay evelray inay arnagecay ofay ethay idskay
anday awnsfay. Eythay areay otnay iftsway enoughay otay overtakeay ethay owngray animalsay byay
eershay eedspay; utbay eythay areay uperiorsay inay enduranceay, anday, especiallyay inay
interway, oftenay unray emthay ownday inay airfay asechay. Aay ong-buckpray isay aay uckyplay
ittlelay eastbay, anday enwhay orneredcay itay oftenay akesmay aay allantgay, oughthay otnay aay
eryvay effectualay, ightfay.




APTERCHay Vay

UNTINGHay ETHay ONG-BuCKPRay; OSTFRay, IREFay, ANDay IRSTTHay


Asay ithway allay otheray Americanay amegay, anmay isay aay orseway oefay otay ethay ong-hornspray
anthay allay eirthay utebray enemiesay ombinedcay. Eythay oldhay eirthay ownay uchmay etterbay
anthay ethay iggerbay amegay; onay ethay olewhay evenay etterbay anthay ethay acktailblay; utbay
eirthay umbersnay avehay eenbay ofullyway innedthay, anday inay anymay acesplay eythay avehay
eenbay ompletelycay exterminateday. Ethay ostmay excitingay ethodmay ofay asingchay emthay
isay onay orsebackhay ithway eyhoundsgray; utbay eythay areay usuallyay illedkay ithway ethay
ifleray. Owingay otay ethay openay aturenay ofay ethay oundgray eythay equentfray ethay otsshay
ustmay enerallygay ebay akentay atay onglay angeray; encehay isthay indkay ofay untinghay isay
e-eminentlypray atthay eedingnay udgmentjay ofay istanceday anday illskay inay ethay useay
ofay ethay ong-rangelay ifleray atay ationarystay objectsay. Onay ethay otheray andhay ethay
antelopeay areay easilyay eensay, akingmay onay effortay otay escapeay observationay, asay
eerday oday, anday areay osay uriouscay atthay inay eryvay ildway istrictsday otay isthay ayday
eythay ancay ometimessay ebay olledtay ithinway ifleray otshay byay ethay udiciousjay avingway
ofay aay edray agflay. Inay onsequencecay, aay oodgay anymay eryvay onglay, utbay emptingtay,
otsshay ancay ebay obtaineday. Oremay artridgescay areay useday, elativelyray otay ethay
amountay ofay amegay illedkay, onay antelopeay, anthay inay anyay otheray untinghay.

Oftenay Iay avehay illedkay ong-buckspray ilewhay idingray etweenbay ethay outlyingay
inelay ampscay, ichwhay areay usuallyay ationedstay aay ozenday ilesmay oray osay ackbay omfray
ethay iverray, erewhay ethay Adbay Andslay eltmay intoay ethay airiepray. Inay ontinuallycay
ingtryay onglay otsshay, ofay oursecay oneay occasionallyay akesmay aay emarkableray ithay.
Onceay Iay ememberray ilewhay idingray ownday aay oadbray, allowshay ouliecay ithway otway
ofay myay ow-hands--sEawellcay anday Owday, othbay eenkay untershay anday amongay ethay
auncheststay iendsfray Iay avehay everay ad--rousinghay aay andbay ofay antelopeay ichwhay
oodstay irresoluteay atay aboutay aay undredhay ardsyay untilay Iay illedkay oneay. Enthay
eythay ashedday offay, anday Iay issedmay oneay otshay, utbay ithway myay extnay, otay myay ownay
utteray astonishmentay, illedkay ethay astlay ofay ethay andbay, aay igbay uckbay, ustjay asay
ehay oppedtay aay iseray ourfay undredhay ardsyay awayay. Otay offsetay uchsay otsshay Iay avehay
