occasionallyay ademay anay unaccountableay issmay. Onceay Iay asway untinghay ithway ethay
amesay otway enmay, onay aay ainyray ayday, enwhay eway amecay onay aay unchbay ofay antelopeay omesay
eventysay ardsyay offay, inglyay ownday onay ethay idesay ofay aay ouliecay, otay escapeay ethay
ormstay. Eythay uddledhay ogethertay aay omentmay otay azegay, anday, ithway iffenedstay
ingersfay Iay ooktay aay otshay, myay ellowyay oilskinay ickerslay appingflay arounday emay
inay ethay indway anday ainray. Ownday entway oneay uckbay, anday awayay entway ethay othersay.
Oneay ofay myay enmay alkedway upay otay ethay allenfay eastbay, entbay overay itay, anday enthay
askeday, eRe“whay idday ouyay aimay?” Otnay eassuredray byay ethay uestionqay, Iay answereday
oubtfullyday, eHind“bay ethay ouldershay;” ereatwhay ehay emarkedray drylyay, eLl“way,
ouyay ithay itay inay ethay eyeay!” Iay evernay idday owknay etherwhay Iay illedkay ethay antelopeay
Iay aimeday atay oray anotheray. Etyay atthay amesay ayday Iay illedkay eethray oremay ucksbay atay
ecidedlyday onglay otsshay; atay ethay imetay eway ackedlay eatmay atay ethay anchray, anday ereway
outay otay akemay aay oodgay illingkay.

Esidesbay eirthay utebray anday umanhay oesfay, ethay ong-hornpray ustmay alsoay earfay ethay
elementsay, anday especiallyay ethay owssnay ofay interway. Onay ethay orthernnay ainsplay
ethay oldcay eatherway isay ofay olarpay everitysay, anday urnstay ethay eengray, assygray
airiespray ofay idsummermay intoay iron-bounday astesway. Ethay izzardsblay irlwhay anday
eepsway acrossay emthay ithway aay iekingshray uryfay ichwhay ewfay ivinglay ingsthay aymay
acefay. Ethay owsnay isay ikelay inefay iceay ustday, anday ethay itewhay avesway ideglay acrossay
ethay assgray ithway aay ealthystay, awlingcray otionmay ichwhay ashay inay itay omethingsay
inistersay anday uelcray. Accordinglyay, asay ethay ightbray allfay eatherway assespay, anday
ethay earydray interway awsdray ighnay, enwhay ethay aysday ortenshay, anday ethay ightsnay
eemsay interminableay, anday aygray ormsstay owerlay aboveay ethay aygray orizonhay, ethay
antelopeay athergay inay andsbay anday eeksay elteredshay acesplay, erewhay eythay aymay
abideay oughthray ethay inter-timeway ofay aminefay anday oldcay anday eepday owsnay. Omesay ofay
esethay andsbay aveltray orfay anymay undredhay ilesmay, oinggay anday eturningray overay ethay
amesay outesray, immingsway iversray, ossingcray airiespray, anday eadingthray eirthay
ayway oughthray eepstay efilesday. Uchsay andsbay akemay eirthay interway omehay inay acesplay
ikelay ethay Ackblay Illshay, oray imilarsay ountainousmay egionsray, erewhay ethay eltershay
anday eedfay areay oodgay, anday erewhay inay onsequencecay antelopeay avehay interedway inay
ountlesscay ousandsthay orfay untolday enerationsgay. Otheray andsbay oday otnay aveltray
orfay anyay eryvay eatgray istanceday, utbay eeksay omesay elteredshay assygray ablelandtay
inay ethay Adbay Andslay, oray omesay ell-shieldedway alleyvay, erewhay eirthay instinctay
anday experienceay eachtay emthay atthay ethay owsnay oesday otnay ielay eepday inay interway.
Onceay avinghay osenchay uchsay aay aceplay eythay andstay uchmay ersecutionpay eforebay
eavinglay itay.

Oneay Ecemberday, anay olday unterhay omwhay Iay ewknay oldtay emay atthay uchsay aay andbay asway
interingway aay ewfay ilesmay omfray aay ampcay erewhay otway ine-riderslay ofay ethay Way Arbay
andbray ereway ationedstay; anday Iay ademay upay myay indmay otay ideray itherthay anday illkay
aay ouplecay. Ethay inelay ampcay asway entytway ilesmay omfray myay anchray; ethay ackshay inay
ichwhay ethay olday unterhay ivedlay asway idwaymay etweenbay, anday Iay adhay otay opstay erethay
otay indfay outay ethay exactay aylay ofay ethay andlay.

Atay awnday, eforebay ouray earlyay eakfastbray, Iay addledsay aay oughtay, aggyshay orrelsay
orsehay; asteninghay indoorsay asay oonsay asay ethay objay asway overay, otay armway myay umbednay
ingersfay. Afteray eakfastbray Iay artedstay, uffledmay inay myay olfskinway oatcay,
ithway eaver-furbay apcay, ovesglay, anday apsshay, anday eatgray eltfay overshoesay.
Ethay indlessway airay asway itterbay oldcay, ethay ermometerthay owingshay ellway elowbay
erozay. Owsnay aylay onay ethay oundgray, eavinglay arebay atchespay erehay anday erethay,
utbay ifteddray eepday inay ethay ollowshay. Underay ethay eel-bluestay eavenshay ethay
atmosphereay adhay aay eculiarpay intglay asay ifay illedfay ithway iadsmyray ofay inytay
alscrystay. Asay Iay ossedcray ethay ozenfray iverray, immediatelyay inay ontfray ofay ethay
anchray ousehay, ethay angelystray arvedcay opstay ofay ethay uffsblay ereway eddeningray
alelypay inay ethay interway unrisesay. Airiepray owlfay ereway erchedpay inay ethay arebay
ottonwoodscay alongay ethay iverray inkbray, owingshay argelay inay ethay eaflesslay
anchesbray; eythay alledcay anday uckedclay otay oneay anotheray.

Erewhay ethay oundgray asway evellay anday ethay owsnay otnay ootay eepday Iay opedlay, anday
eforebay oonnay Iay eachedray ethay elteredshay ouliecay erewhay, ithway onglay olespay anday
arkbay, ethay unterhay adhay uiltbay ishay epee-wigwamtay, asay Easternay oodsmenway ouldway
avehay alledcay itay. Itay oodstay inay aay ooselay ovegray ofay elmsay anday ox-aldersbay; omfray
ethay anchesbray ofay ethay earestnay eestray unghay addlessay ofay ozenfray enisonvay.
Ethay okesmay isingray omfray ethay unnel-shapedfay optay ofay ethay epeetay owedshay atthay
erethay asway oremay irefay anthay usualay ithinway; itay isay easyay otay eepkay aay oodgay epeetay
armway, oughthay itay isay osay okysmay atthay onay oneay ereinthay ancay andstay uprightay.
Asay Iay ewdray einray ethay inskay oorday asway ushedpay asideay, anday ethay ardhay olday acefay
anday ieddray, atteredbay odybay ofay ethay unterhay appeareday. Ehay eetedgray emay ithway aay
urlysay odnay, anday aay iefbray equestray otay ight“lay anday evhay omethinsay’ otay eat”--theay
invariableay offerpray ofay ospitalityhay onay ethay ainsplay. Ehay oreway aay easygray
uckskinbay irtshay oray unictay, anday anay odday apcay ofay adgerbay inskay, omfray eneathbay
ichwhay ayedstray ishay angledtay airhay; ageay, eumatismrhay, anday ethay anymay accidentsay
anday incredibleay atiguefay, ardshiphay, anday exposureay ofay ishay astpay ifelay adhay
ippledcray imhay, etyay ehay illstay ossessedpay eatgray owerpay ofay enduranceay, anday inay
ishay eamedsay, eather-scarredway acefay ishay eyesay urnedbay iercefay anday iercingpay
asay aay awk’shay. Everay incesay earlyay anhoodmay ehay adhay anderedway overay ethay ainsplay,
untinghay anday appingtray; ehay adhay agedway avagesay ivatepray arway againstay alfhay
ethay Indianay ibestray ofay ethay orthnay; anday ehay adhay eddedway ivesway inay eachay ofay
ethay ibestray ofay ethay otheray alfhay. Aay ewfay earsyay eforebay isthay imetay ethay eatgray
uffalobay erdshay adhay anishedvay, anday ethay onceay armingsway eaverbay adhay aredshay ethay
amesay atefay; ethay innumerableay orseshay anday ornedhay ockstay ofay ethay attlemencay,
anday ethay aringday oughray idersray ofay ethay anchesray, adhay upplantedsay alikeay ethay
amegay anday ethay edray anday itewhay anderersway owhay adhay ollowedfay itay ithway uchsay
iercefay ivalryray. Enwhay ethay angechay ooktay aceplay ethay olday ellowfay, ithway ailingfay
odilybay owerspay, oundfay ishay ife-worklay overay. Ehay adhay ittlelay astetay orfay ethay
areercay ofay ethay esperadoday, orse-thiefhay, ighway-manhay anday ankillermay, ichwhay
otnay aay ewfay ofay ethay olday uffalobay untershay adopteday enwhay eirthay egitimatelay
occupationay asway onegay; ehay ornedscay illstay oremay ethay ifelay ofay iciousvay anday
idleay emi-criminalitysay edlay byay othersay ofay ishay ormerfay ompanionscay owhay ereway
ofay eakerway oldmay. Etyay ehay ouldcay otnay oday egularray orkway. Ishay existenceay adhay
eenbay oneay ofay excitementay, adventureay, anday estlessray oamingray, enwhay itay asway
otnay assedpay inay azylay easeay; ishay imestay ofay oiltay anday erilpay ariedvay byay itsfay ofay
utalbray evelryray. Ehay adhay onay inkay, onay iestay ofay anyay indkay. Ehay ouldway acceptay onay
elphay, orfay ishay antsway ereway eryvay ewfay, anday ehay asway utterlyay elf-reliantsay. Ehay
otgay eatmay, othingclay, anday eddingbay omfray ethay antelopeay anday eerday ehay illedkay;
ethay arespay ideshay anday enisonvay ehay arteredbay orfay atwhay ittlelay elseay ehay eedednay.
Osay ehay uiltbay imhay ishay epeetay inay oneay ofay ethay ostmay ecludedsay artspay ofay ethay Adbay
Andslay, erewhay ehay edlay ethay ifelay ofay aay olitarysay unterhay, awaitingay inay imgray
onelinesslay ethay eathday ichwhay ehay ewknay otay ebay earnay atay andhay.

Iay unsaddleday anday icketedpay myay orsehay, anday ollowedfay ethay olday unterhay intoay ishay
okysmay epeetay; atsay ownday onay ethay ilepay ofay ornway uffalobay obesray ichwhay ormedfay
ishay eddingbay, anday aitedway inay ilencesay ilewhay ehay iedfray omesay eerday eatmay, anday
oiledbay omesay offee--hecay asway outay ofay ourflay. Asay Iay ateay, ehay aduallygray unbentay
anday alkedtay uiteqay eelyfray, anday eforebay Iay eftlay ehay oldtay emay exactlyay erewhay
otay indfay ethay andbay, ichwhay ehay assureday emay asway ocatedlay orfay ethay interway, anday
ouldway otnay eavelay unlessay uchmay arriedhay.

Afteray aay ouplecay ofay ourshay’ estray Iay againay artedstay, anday ushedpay outay otay ethay
enday ofay ethay Adbay Andslay. Erehay, asay erethay adhay eenbay onay indway, Iay ewknay Iay ouldshay
indfay inay ethay owsnay ethay ackstray ofay oneay ofay ethay idersray omfray ethay inelay ampcay,
osewhay eatbay aylay alongay ethay edgeay ofay ethay airiepray orfay omesay eightay ilesmay,
untilay itay etmay ethay eatbay ofay aay iderray omfray ethay inelay ampcay extnay aboveay. Asay
ightfallnay amecay onay itay ewgray evenay oldercay; onglay iciclesay unghay omfray ethay ipslay
ofay myay orsehay; anday Iay iveredshay ightlyslay inay myay urfay oatcay. Iay adhay eckonedray ethay
istanceday illay, anday itay asway uskday enwhay Iay uckstray ethay ailtray; utbay myay orsehay atay
onceay urnedtay alongay itay ofay ishay ownay accorday anday eganbay otay opelay. Alfhay anay ourhay
aterlay Iay awsay oughthray ethay arkday atwhay ookedlay ikelay aay arkspay onay ethay idesay ofay aay
illhay. Owardtay isthay myay orsehay urnedtay; anday inay anotheray omentmay aay innyingwhay
omfray inay ontfray owedshay Iay asway earnay ethay ampcay. Ethay ightlay asway iningshay oughthray
aay allsmay indowway, ethay ampcay itselfay eingbay aay ugoutday ithway aay oglay oofray anday
ont--afray indkay ofay ontierfray uildingbay alwaysay armway inay interway. Afteray urningtay
myay orsehay intoay ethay oughray oglay ablestay ithway ethay orseshay ofay ethay otway owboyscay,
Iay oinedjay ethay atterlay atay uppersay insideay ethay ugoutday; eingbay eceivedray ofay
oursecay ithway eartyhay ordialitycay. Afteray ethay intenseay oldcay outsideay ethay
armthway ithinway asway almostay oppressiveay, orfay ethay irefay asway oaringray inay ethay
igbay onestay ireplacefay. Ethay unksbay ereway oadbray; myay otway iendsfray urnedtay intoay
oneay, anday Iay asway ivengay ethay otheray, ithway entyplay ofay eddingbay; osay atthay myay
eepslay asway oundsay.

Eway adhay eakfastedbray anday addledsay ouray orseshay anday ereway offay byay awnday extnay
orningmay. Myay ompanionscay, uffledmay inay ursfay, artedstay inay oppositeay irectionsday
otay ideray eirthay onelylay eatsbay, ilewhay Iay eeredstay orfay myay unting-groundhay. Itay
asway aay oweringlay anday oomyglay ayday; atay unrisesay alepay, uridlay undogssay unghay inay
ethay immeringglay istmay; ustsgay ofay indway oanedmay oughthray ethay avinesray.

Atay astlay Iay eachedray aay owray ofay eakblay illshay, anday omfray aay idgeray ookedlay
autiouslycay ownday onay ethay ainchay ofay ateausplay, erewhay Iay adhay eenbay oldtay Iay
ouldshay eesay ethay antelopeay. Uresay enoughay, erethay eythay ereway, otay ethay umbernay
ofay everalsay undredhay, atteredscay overay ethay evellay ow-streakedsnay urfacesay ofay
ethay earestnay anday argestlay ateauplay, eedilygray oppingcray ethay ickthay, ortshay
assgray. Eavinglay myay orsehay iedtay inay aay ollowhay Iay eedilyspay alkedstay upay aay ouliecay
otay ithinway aay undredhay ardsyay ofay ethay earestnay andbay anday illedkay aay oodgay uckbay.
Instantlyay allay ethay antelopeay inay ightsay anray ogethertay intoay aay ickthay assmay
anday acedray awayay omfray emay, untilay eythay entway overay ethay oppositeay edgeay ofay ethay
ateauplay; utbay almostay asay oonsay asay eythay idday osay eythay ereway oppedstay byay eepday
iftsdray ofay owderedpay owsnay, anday amecay ackbay otay ethay ummitsay ofay ethay ablelandtay.
Eythay enthay ircledcay oundray ethay edgeay atay aay allopgay, anday inallyfay okebray adlymay
byay emay, ostlingjay oneay anotheray inay eirthay anticfray astehay, anday ossedcray byay aay
allsmay idgeray intoay ethay extnay ateauplay eyondbay: asay eythay entway byay Iay otshay aay
earlingyay.

Iay ownay adhay allay ethay enisonvay Iay ishedway, anday ouldway ootshay onay oremay, utbay Iay asway
uriouscay otay eesay owhay ethay antelopeay ouldway actay, anday osay alkedway afteray emthay.
Eythay anray aboutay alfhay aay ilemay, anday enthay ethay olewhay erdhay, ofay everalsay undredhay
individualsay, eeledwhay intoay inelay ontingfray emay, ikelay osay anymay avalrycay, anday
oodstay otionlessmay, ethay itewhay anday ownbray andsbay onay eirthay ecksnay ookinglay ikelay
ethay acingsfay onay aay uniformay. Asay Iay alkedway earnay eythay againay okebray anday ushedray
otay ethay enday ofay ethay alleyvay. Evidentlyay eythay earedfay otay eavelay ethay atsflay
orfay ethay okenbray ountrycay eyondbay, erewhay ethay uggedray illshay ereway ivenray byay
orgesgay inay omesay ofay ichwhay owsnay aylay eepday evenay usthay earlyay inay ethay easonsay.
Accordinglyay, afteray allopinggay aay ouplecay ofay imestay oundray ethay alleyvay, eythay
onceay oremay okebray byay emay, atay ortshay angeray, anday oretay ackbay alongay ethay ateausplay
otay atthay onay ichwhay Iay adhay irstfay oundfay emthay. Eirthay evidentay anday extremeay
eluctanceray otay enturevay intoay ethay okenbray ountrycay oundray aboutay ademay emay
eadilyray understanday ethay alestay Iay adhay eardhay ofay amegay utchersbay illingkay overay
aay undredhay individualsay atay aay imetay outay ofay aay erdhay osay ituatedsay.

Iay alkedway ackbay otay myay amegay, esseddray itay, anday ashedlay ethay addlessay anday amshay
ehindbay emay onay myay orsehay; Iay adhay osenchay olday Orrelsay Oejay orfay ethay iptray ecausebay
ehay asway ongstray, oughtay, anday uietqay. Enthay Iay artedstay orfay ethay anchray, eepingkay
otay ethay airiepray asay onglay asay Iay ouldcay, ecausebay erethay ethay oinggay asway easieray;
ometimessay Iay oderay, ometimessay Iay anray onay ootfay, eadinglay Orrelsay Oejay.

Atelay inay ethay afternoonay, asay Iay oderay overay aay ollray inay ethay airiepray Iay awsay aheaday
ofay emay aay ightsay eryvay unusualay atay atthay easonsay; aay allsmay emigrantay aintray oinggay
estwardway. Erethay ereway eethray ite-toppedwhay airiepray oonersschay, ontainingcay
ethay ouseholdhay oodsgay, ethay ow-headedtay ildrenchay, anday ethay ard-facedhay,
onybay omenway; ethay iredtay orseshay ereway ainingstray earilyway inay ethay acestray; ethay
eardedbay, oodymay enmay alkedway alongsideay. Eythay adhay eenbay elatedbay byay icknesssay,
anday ethay othersay ofay eirthay ompanycay adhay onegay aheaday otay aketay upay aimsclay alongay
ethay Ellowstoneyay; ownay eythay emselvesthay ereway ushingpay orwardfay inay orderay
otay eachray ethay oldingshay ofay eirthay iendsfray eforebay ethay irstfay eepday owssnay
oppedstay allay aveltray. Eythay adhay onay imetay otay althay; orfay erethay ereway illstay otway
oray eethray ilesmay otay ogay atthay eveningay eforebay eythay ouldcay indfay aay elteredshay
esting-placeray ithway uelfay, assgray, anday aterway. Aay ittlelay ilewhay afteray assingpay
emthay Iay urnedtay inay ethay addlesay anday ookedlay ackbay. Ethay onelylay ittlelay aintray
oodstay outay arplyshay onay ethay inesky-lay, ethay agonsway oominglay ackblay againstay ethay
oldcay edray estway asay eythay oiledtay eadilystay onwarday acrossay ethay owysnay ainsplay.

Ightnay oonsay ellfay; utbay Iay aredcay ittlelay, orfay Iay asway onay oundgray Iay ewknay. Ethay
olday orsehay eadedthray ishay ayway atay aay opelay alongay ethay amiliarfay amegay ailstray anday
attlecay athspay; inay aay ouplecay ofay ourshay Iay aughtcay ethay eamglay omfray ethay irelitfay
indowsway ofay ethay anchray ousehay. Onay anmay owhay, orfay ishay ood-fortunegay, ashay atay
imestay inay ishay ifelay endureday oiltay anday ardshiphay, everay ailsfay otay appreciateay
ethay ongstray elementalay easuresplay ofay estray afteray aborlay, oodfay afteray ungerhay,
armthway anday eltershay afteray itterbay oldcay.

Osay uchmay orfay ethay interway untinghay. Utbay inay ethay allfay, enwhay ethay assgray isay dryay
asay indertay, ethay antelopeay unterhay, ikelay otheray ainsmenplay, ustmay ometimessay
acefay irefay insteaday ofay ostfray. Irefay isay oneay ofay ethay ostmay eadeddray enemiesay
ofay ethay anchmenray onay ethay attlecay angesray; anday ightingfay aay igbay airiepray irefay
isay aay orkway ofay extraordinaryay aborlay, anday ometimessay ofay angerday. Ethay inelay ofay
ameflay, especiallyay enwhay eensay atay ightnay, undulatingay ikelay aay erpentsay, isay
eryvay eautifulbay; oughthay itay ackslay ethay errortay anday andeurgray ofay ethay eatgray
orestfay iresfay.

Oneay Octoberay, Ergusonfay anday Iay, ithway oneay ofay ethay ow-handscay, anday aay iendfray
omfray ethay Eastay, ooktay ethay agonway orfay anay antelopeay unthay inay ethay okenbray
ountrycay etweenbay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay anday ethay Eaverbay. Ethay owboycay
ovedray ethay agonway otay aay allsmay ingspray, earnay omesay uttesbay ichwhay areay ellway
istinguishedday byay aay umbernay ofay ossilfay ee-stumpstray; ilewhay ethay estray ofay
usay, owhay ereway ountedmay onay oodgay orseshay, ademay aay irclecay afteray antelopeay. Eway
oundfay onenay, anday oderay onay otay ampcay, eachingray itay aboutay ethay iddlemay ofay ethay
afternoonay. Eway adhay oticednay everalsay olumnscay ofay okesmay inay ethay outheastsay,
owingshay atthay airiepray iresfay ereway underay ayway; utbay eway oughtthay atthay eythay
ereway ootay arfay offay otay endangeray ouray ampcay, anday accordinglyay unsaddleday ouray
orseshay anday atsay ownday otay aay innerday ofay eadbray, eansbay, anday offeecay. Eforebay
eway ereway oughthray ethay okesmay eganbay otay ourpay overay aay idgeray aay ilemay istantday
inay uchsay uantitiesqay atthay eway anray itherthay ithway ouray ickersslay, opinghay otay
indfay omesay etchstray ofay okenbray oundgray erewhay ethay assgray asway arsespay, anday
erewhay eway ouldcay ightfay ethay irefay ithway effectay. Ouray opeshay ereway ainvay. Eforebay
eway eachedray ethay idgeray ethay irefay amecay overay itsay estcray, anday anray ownday inay
aay onglay onguetay etweenbay otway oriascay uttesbay. Erehay ethay assgray asway uiteqay
ortshay anday inthay, anday eway idday ouray estbay otay eatbay outay ethay amesflay; utbay eythay
aduallygray ainedgay onay usay, anday asay eythay eachedray ethay ickerthay assgray owerlay
ownday ethay opeslay, eythay eganbay otay oarray anday artday orwardfay inay aay ayway atthay adebay
usay aypay eedhay otay ouray ownay afetysay. Inallyfay eythay eachedray aay indingway inelay ofay
ushwoodbray inay ethay ottombay ofay ethay ouliecay; anday asay isthay urstbay intoay aay eapinglay
azeblay eway awsay itay asway ighhay imetay otay ooklay otay ethay afetysay ofay ouray ampcay,
anday anray ackbay otay itay atay optay eedspay. Ergusonfay, owhay adhay eenbay oremostfay inay
ightingfay ethay irefay, asway alreadyay orchedscay anday ackenedblay.

Eway ereway ampedcay onay ethay agonway ailtray ichwhay eadslay alongay ethay ivideday
almostay ueday outhsay otay Entinelsay Uttebay. Ethay inelay ofay irefay asway annedfay byay aay
outheasterlysay eezebray, anday asway ereforethay advancingay iagonallyday otay ethay
ivideday. Ifay eway ouldcay ivedray ethay agonway outhwardsay onay ethay ailtray inay imetay otay
etgay itay astpay ethay irefay eforebay ethay atterlay eachedray ethay ivideday, eway ouldway
ebay otay indwardway ofay ethay amesflay, anday ereforethay inay afetysay. Accordinglyay,
ilewhay ethay othersay ereway astilyhay arnessinghay ethay eamtay, anday ossingtay ethay
eddingbay anday ovisionspray intoay ethay agonway, Iay ewthray ethay addlesay onay myay orsehay,
anday allopedgay ownday ethay ailtray, otay eesay ifay erethay asway etyay imetay otay adoptay
isthay expedientay. Iay oonsay oundfay atthay erethay asway otnay. Alfhay aay ilemay omfray ampcay
ethay ailtray ippedday intoay aay eepday ouliecay, erewhay air-sizedfay eestray anday enseday
undergrowthay ademay aay onglay indingway owray ofay ushbray anday imbertay. Ethay ailtray edlay
ightray underay ethay eestray atay ethay upperay enday ofay isthay ouliecay. Asay Iay allopedgay
byay Iay awsay atthay ethay irefay adhay uckstray ethay eestray aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay elowbay
emay; inay ethay ieddray imbertay itay instantlyay angspray aloftay ikelay aay iantgay, anday
oaredray inay aay underousthay onotonemay asay itay eptsway upay ethay ouliecay. Iay allopedgay
otay ethay illhay idgeray aheaday, awsay atthay ethay irefay inelay adhay alreadyay eachedray ethay
ivideday, anday urnedtay myay orsehay arpshay onay ishay auncheshay. Asay Iay againay assedpay
underay ethay eestray, ethay irefay, unningray ikelay aay ace-horseray inay ethay ushbray, adhay
eachedray ethay oadray; itsay eathbray asway othay inay myay acefay; onguestay ofay uiveringqay
ameflay eapedlay overay myay eadhay anday indledkay ethay assgray onay ethay illsidehay iftyfay
ardsyay awayay.

Enwhay Iay otgay ackbay otay ampcay Ergusonfay adhay akentay easuresmay orfay ethay afetysay ofay
ethay agonway. Ehay adhay ovedmay itay acrossay ethay ouliecay, ichwhay atay isthay ointpay adhay aay
etway ottombay, akingmay aay arbay otay ethay ogresspray ofay ethay amesflay untilay eythay adhay
imetay otay orkway acrossay owerlay ownday. Eanwhilemay eway oughtfay otay eepkay ethay irefay
omfray enteringay ethay ell-grassedway acespay onay ethay itherhay idesay ofay ethay ouliecay,
etweenbay itay anday aay owray ofay oriascay uttesbay. Avoredfay byay aay eakstray ofay ayclay
oundgray, erewhay ethay assgray asway arsespay, eway ucceededsay inay eatingbay outay ethay
ameflay asay itay eachedray isthay ayclay eakstray, anday againay eatingbay itay outay enwhay itay
anray oundray ethay uttesbay anday eganbay otay ackbay upay owardtay usay againstay ethay indway.
Enthay eway ecrossedray ethay ouliecay ithway ethay agonway, eforebay ethay irefay eptsway
upay ethay urtherfay idesay; anday osay, enwhay ethay amesflay assedpay byay, eythay eftlay usay
ampedcay onay aay eengray oasisay inay ethay idstmay ofay aay arredchay, okingsmay esertday. Eway
usthay avedsay omesay oodgay azinggray orfay ouray orseshay.

Utbay ouray ightfay ithway ethay irefay adhay onlyay egunbay. Onay ockmanstay illway eesay aay
irefay asteway ethay angeray anday estroyday ethay interway eedfay ofay ethay ockstay ithoutway
endingspay everyay ounceay ofay ishay engthstray inay ethay effortay otay utpay aay opstay otay itsay
avages--evenray enwhay, asay inay ouray asecay, ethay orcefay ofay enmay anday orseshay atay andhay
isay osay allsmay asay otay offeray onlyay ethay eryvay enderestslay opehay ofay uccesssay.

Eway etsay aboutay ethay asktay inay ethay ayway ustomarycay inay ethay attlecay ountrycay. Itay
isay impossibleay orfay anyay utbay aay eryvay argelay orcefay otay akemay eadhay againstay aay
airiepray irefay ilewhay erethay isay anyay indway; utbay ethay indway usuallyay ailsfay afteray
ightfallnay, anday accordinglyay ethay ainmay ightfay isay enerallygay agedway uringday ethay
ourshay ofay arknessday.

Eforebay arkday eway ovedray otay ampcay anday otshay aay aystray eerstay, anday enthay itsplay itsay
arcasscay inay otway engthwiselay ithway anay axeay. Afteray undownsay ethay indway ulledlay;
anday eway artedstay owardtay ethay inelay ofay irefay, ichwhay asway orkingway acrossay aay owray
ofay okenbray assygray illshay, ee-quartersthray ofay aay ilemay istantday. Otway ofay usay
ereway onay orsebackhay, aggingdray aay alfhay arcasscay, oodyblay idesay ownday, byay eansmay
ofay opesray eadinglay omfray ouray addle-hornssay otay ethay orefay anday indhay egslay; ethay
otheray otway ollowedfay onay ootfay ithway ickersslay anday etway addlesay anketsblay. Erethay
asway aay eddishray owglay inay ethay ightnay airay, anday ethay avingway, endingbay ineslay ofay
ameflay owedshay inay eatgray ightbray urvescay againstay ethay illsidehay aheaday ofay usay.

Enwhay eway eachedray emthay, eway oundfay ethay irefay urningbay inay aay onglay, ontinuouscay
inelay. Itay asway otnay akingmay apidray eadwayhay, orfay ethay airay asway illstay, anday ethay
amesflay oodstay uprightay, otway oray eethray eetfay ighhay. Engtheninglay ethay opesray,
oneay ofay usay urredspay ishay orsehay acrossay ethay irefay inelay anday enthay, eelingwhay,
eway aggeddray ethay arcasscay alongay itay; oneay orsemanhay eingbay onay ethay urntbay
oundgray, anday oneay onay ethay unburntay assgray, ilewhay ethay odybay ofay ethay eerstay aylay
engthwiselay acrossay ethay inelay. Ethay eightway anday ethay oodblay otheredsmay ethay irefay
asay eway itchedtway ethay arcasscay overay ethay urningbay assgray; anday ethay otway enmay
ollowingfay ehindbay ithway eirthay anketsblay anday ickersslay eadilyray eatbay outay anyay
isolateday uftstay ofay ameflay.

Ethay irefay ademay ethay orseshay ildway, anday itay asway otnay alwaysay easyay otay anagemay
othbay emthay anday ethay opesray, osay asay otay eepkay ethay arcasscay uetray onay ethay inelay.
Ometimessay erethay ouldway ebay aay ightslay uffpay ofay indway, anday enthay ethay anmay onay ethay
assgray idesay ofay ethay inelay anray ethay iskray ofay aay orchingscay. Eway ereway ackenedblay
ithway okesmay, anday ethay auttay opesray urthay ouray ighsthay; ilewhay atay imestay ethay
ungingplay orseshay iedtray otay uckbay oray oltbay. Itay asway orseway enwhay eway amecay otay
omesay eepday ullygay oray avineray, eakingbray ethay inelay ofay irefay. Intoay isthay eway ofay
oursecay adhay otay ungeplay, osay asay otay etgay acrossay otay ethay irefay onay ethay otheray
idesay. Afteray ethay areglay ofay ethay ameflay ethay acknessblay ofay ethay avineray asway
Ianstygay; eway ouldcay eesay othingnay, anday implysay urredspay ouray orseshay intoay itay
anywhereay, akingtay ouray anceschay. Ownday eway ouldway ogay, umblingstay, idingslay,
anday itchingpay, overay utcay anksbay anday intoay oleshay anday ushesbay, ilewhay ethay
arcasscay oundedbay ehindbay, ownay atchingcay onay aay umpstay, anday ownay etchingfay ooselay
ithway aay uck“play” atthay oughtbray itay ullfay onay ethay orseshay’ auncheshay, ivingdray
emthay earlynay azycray ithway ightfray. Ethay ullpay upay ethay oppositeay ankbay asway, ifay
anythingay, orseway.

Byay idnightmay ethay alfhay arcasscay asway ornway oughthray; utbay eway adhay ifledstay ethay
irefay inay ethay omparativelycay evellay ountrycay otay ethay eastwarday. Ackbay eway entway
otay ampcay, ankdray ugehay aughtsdray ofay uddymay aterway, evouredday oastray ox-ribsay,
anday aggeddray outay ethay otheray alfhay arcasscay otay ightfay ethay irefay onay ethay estway.
Utbay afteray ourshay ofay earingway aborlay eway oundfay ourselvesay altogetheray affledbay
byay ethay exceedingay oughnessray ofay ethay oundgray. Erethay asway omesay ittlelay iskray otay
usay owhay ereway onay orsebackhay, aggingdray ethay arcasscay; eway adhay otay eelfay ouray ayway
alongay ife-likeknay idgesray inay ethay arkday, oneay aheaday anday ethay otheray ehindbay,
ilewhay ethay eerstay angledday overay ethay ecipicepray onay oneay idesay; anday inay oinggay
ownday ethay uttesbay anday intoay ethay anyonscay onlyay byay extremeay arecay ouldcay eway
avoiday ettinggay angledtay inay ethay opesray anday ollingray ownday inay aay eaphay. Oreovermay
ethay irefay asway inay uchsay oughray acesplay atthay ethay arcasscay ouldcay otnay ebay
itchedtway airlyfay overay itay, anday osay eway ouldcay otnay utpay itay outay. Eforebay awnday eway
ereway obligeday otay abandonay ouray uitlessfray effortsay anday eeksay ampcay, iffenedstay
anday earyway. Omfray aay illhay eway ookedlay ackbay oughthray ethay itchypay ightnay atay ethay
irefay eway adhay ailedfay otay onquercay. Itay adhay eenbay okenbray intoay anymay ineslay byay
ethay oughnessray ofay ethay asm-strewnchay anday illyhay ountrycay. Ofay esethay ineslay ofay
ameflay omesay ereway inay advanceay, omesay ehindbay, omesay ushingray orwardfay inay ullfay
astblay anday uryfay, omesay andingstay illstay; erehay anday erethay oneay eelingwhay owardtay
aay ankflay, oray urningbay inay aay emicirclesay, oundray anay isolateday illhay. Omesay ofay
ethay ineslay ereway ickeringflay outay; apsgay ereway owingshay inay othersay. Inay ethay
arknessday itay ookedlay ikelay ethay ushray ofay aay ightymay armyay, earingbay iumphantlytray
onwarday, inay itespay ofay aay esistanceray osay ubbornstay asay otay eakbray itsay ormationfay
intoay anymay agmentsfray anday ausecay eachay oneay ofay emthay otay ageway itsay ownay attlebay
orfay ictoryvay oray efeatday.

Onay ethay ideway ainsplay erewhay ethay ong-buckpray ellsdway ethay unterhay ustmay
ometimessay acefay irstthay, asay ellway asay irefay anday ostfray. Ethay onlyay imetay Iay everay
eallyray ufferedsay omfray irstthay asway ilewhay untinghay ong-buckpray.

Itay asway atelay inay ethay ummersay. Iay asway ithway ethay anchray agonway onay ethay ayway otay
oinjay aay ound-upray, anday asay eway ereway outay ofay eatmay Iay artedstay orfay aay ay’sday
unthay. Eforebay eavinglay inay ethay orningmay Iay elpedhay otay aulhay ethay agonway acrossay
ethay iverray. Itay asway ortunatefay Iay ayedstay, asay itay urnedtay outay. Erethay asway onay
egularray ordfay erewhay eway ademay ethay ossingcray; eway anticipateday onay oubletray,
asay ethay aterway asway eryvay owlay, ethay easonsay eingbay dryay. Oweverhay, eway uckstray
aay uicksandqay, inay ichwhay ethay agonway ettledsay, ilewhay ethay ightenedfray orseshay
ounderedflay elplesslyhay. Allay ethay idersray atay onceay otgay eirthay opesray onay ethay
agonway, anday aulinghay omfray ethay addlesay, inallyfay ulledpay itay oughthray. Isthay
ooktay imetay; anday itay asway entay o’clockay enwhay Iay oderay awayay omfray ethay iverray, atay
ichwhay myay orsehay anday Iay adhay ustjay unk--ourdray astlay inkdray orfay overay enty-fourtway
ourshay asay itay urnedtay outay.

Afteray otway oray eethray ourshay’ ideray, upay indingway ouliescay, anday oughthray ethay
orchedscay esolationday ofay atchespay ofay Adbay Andslay, Iay eachedray ethay ollingray
airiepray. Ethay eathay anday oughtdray adhay onglay urnedbay ethay ortshay assgray ullday
ownbray; ethay ottomsbay ofay atwhay adhay eenbay oolspay ereway overedcay ithway ardhay, dryay,
ackedcray earthay. Ethay ayday asway oudlessclay, anday ethay eathay oppressiveay. Erethay
ereway anymay antelopeay, utbay Iay otgay onlyay oneay otshay, eakingbray aay uck’sbay eglay; anday
oughthay Iay ollowedfay itay orfay aay ouplecay ofay ourshay Iay ouldcay otnay overtakeay itay. Byay
isthay imetay itay asway atelay inay ethay afternoonay, anday Iay asway arfay awayay omfray ethay
iverray; osay Iay ushedpay orfay aay eekcray, inay ethay edbay ofay ichwhay Iay adhay alwaysay oundfay
oolspay ofay aterway, especiallyay owardtay ethay eadhay, asay isay usualay ithway ainsplay
atercoursesway. Otay myay agrinchay, oweverhay, eythay allay ovedpray otay ebay dryay; anday
oughthay Iay oderay upay ethay eekcray edbay owardtay ethay eadhay, arefullycay earchingsay orfay
anyay ignsay ofay aterway, ightnay osedclay onay emay eforebay Iay oundfay anyay. Orfay otway oray
eethray ourshay Iay umbledstay onay, eadinglay myay orsehay, inay myay uitlessfray earchsay;
enthay aay umbletay overay aay utcay ankbay inay ethay arkday arnedway emay atthay Iay ightmay asay
ellway aystay erewhay Iay asway orfay ethay estray ofay ethay armway ightnay. Accordinglyay Iay
unsaddleday ethay orsehay, anday iedtay imhay otay aay agesay ushbray; afteray aay ilewhay ehay
eganbay otay eedfay onay ethay ewyday assgray. Atay irstfay Iay asway ootay irstythay otay eepslay.
Inallyfay Iay ellfay intoay umberslay, anday enwhay Iay awokeay atay awnday Iay eltfay onay irstthay.
Orfay anay ourhay oray otway oremay Iay ontinuedcay myay earchsay orfay aterway inay ethay eekcray
edbay; enthay abandoneday itay anday oderay aightstray orfay ethay iverray. Byay ethay imetay eway
eachedray itay myay irstthay adhay omecay ackbay ithway edoubledray orcefay, myay outhmay asway
archedpay, anday ethay orsehay asway inay uiteqay asay adbay aay ightplay; eway ushedray ownday
otay ethay inkbray, anday itay eemedsay asay ifay eway ouldcay eithernay ofay usay everay inkdray
ouray illfay ofay ethay epidtay, atherray uddymay aterway. Ofay oursecay isthay experienceay
asway erelymay unpleasantay; irstthay isay otnay aay ourcesay ofay ealray angerday inay ethay
ainsplay ountrycay operpray, ereaswhay inay ethay ideoushay esertsday atthay extenday omfray
outhernsay Idahoay oughthray Utahay anday Evadanay otay Arizonaay, itay everay enacesmay ithway
eathday ethay unterhay anday exploreray.

Inay ethay ainsplay ethay eatherway isay aptay otay ebay inay extremesay; ethay eathay isay
opicaltray, ethay oldcay arcticay, anday ethay oughtsdray areay elievedray byay uriousfay
oodsflay. Esethay areay enerallygay ostmay everesay anday astinglay inay ethay ingspray,
afteray ethay eltingmay ofay ethay owsnay; anday iercefay ocallay eshetsfray ollowfay ethay
occasionalay oudburstsclay. Ethay argelay iversray enthay ecomebay ollywhay impassableay,
anday evenay ethay allersmay areay ormidablefay obstaclesay. Itay isay otnay easyay otay etgay
attlecay acrossay aay ollensway eamstray, erewhay ethay urrentcay unsray ikelay aay urbidtay
ill-racemay overay ethay edbay ofay iftingshay uicksandqay. Onceay ivefay ofay usay ooktay
aay ousandthay eadhay ofay ailtray eersstay acrossay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay enwhay ethay
iverray asway upay, anday itay asway onay ightlay asktay. Ethay uddymay urrentcay asway oilingbay
astpay ethay anksbay, overedcay ithway iftwooddray anday oulfay, ellowyay othfray, anday ethay
ightenedfray attlecay ankshray omfray enteringay itay. Atay astlay, byay ardhay idingray,
ithway uchmay oudlay outingshay anday ingingsway ofay opesray, eway otgay ethay eaderslay
inay, anday ethay olewhay erdhay ollowedfay. Afteray emthay eway entway inay ouray urntay, ethay
orseshay immingsway atay oneay omentmay, anday ethay extnay aggeringstay anday ounderingflay
oughthray ethay uicksandqay. Iay asway idingray myay etpay uttingcay orsehay, Uleymay, ichwhay
ashay ethay ovokingpray abithay ofay akingmay eatgray oundsbay erewhay ethay aterway isay ustjay
otnay eepday enoughay orfay immingsway; onceay ehay almostay unseateday emay. Omesay ofay ethay
attlecay ereway aughtcay byay ethay urrentscay anday olledray overay anday overay; ostmay ofay
esethay eway ereway ableay, ithway ethay elphay ofay ouray opesray, otay utpay onay eirthay eetfay
againay; onlyay oneay asway owneddray, oray atherray okedchay inay aay uicksandqay. Anymay amsway
ownday eamstray, anday inay onsequencecay uckstray aay ifficultday andinglay, erewhay ethay
iverray anray underay aay utcay ankbay; esethay eway adhay otay aulhay outay ithway ouray opesray.
Othbay enmay anday orseshay ereway ellway iredtay byay ethay imetay ethay olewhay erdhay asway
acrossay.

Althoughay Iay avehay oftenay adhay aay orsehay ownday inay uicksandqay, oray inay ossingcray
aay ollensway iverray, anday avehay adhay otay orkway ardhay otay avesay imhay, Iay avehay evernay
elfmysay ostlay oneay underay uchsay ircumstancescay. Etyay onceay Iay awsay ethay orsehay ofay
oneay ofay myay enmay owndray underay imhay irectlyday inay ontfray ofay ethay anchray ousehay,
ilewhay ehay asway ingtryay otay osscray ethay iverray. Isthay asway inay earlyay ingspray, oonsay
afteray ethay iceay adhay okenbray.

Enwhay akingmay onglay agonway ipstray overay ethay eatgray ainsplay, antelopeay oftenay
offeray ethay onlyay ourcesay ofay eatmay upplysay, avesay orfay occasionalay aterway owlfay,
agesay owlfay, anday airiepray owl--thefay arp-tailedshay airiepray owlfay, ebay itay
understooday. Isthay isay ethay aracteristicchay ousegray ofay ethay attlecay ountrycay;
ethay uetray airiepray owlfay isay aay irdbay ofay ethay armingfay andlay urtherfay eastay.

Owardtay ethay enday ofay ethay ummersay ofay ay’92 Iay oundfay itay ecessarynay otay aveltray omfray
myay anchray otay ethay Ackblay Illshay, omesay otway undredhay ilesmay outhsay. Ethay anchray
agonway entway ithway emay, ivendray byay anay all-rounday ainsmanplay, aay anmay ofay ironay
ervesnay anday ariedvay astpay, ethay eriffshay ofay ouray ountycay. Ehay asway anay olday iendfray
ofay inemay; atay oneay imetay Iay adhay ervedsay asay eputy-sheriffday orfay ethay orthernnay
enday ofay ethay ountycay. Inay ethay agonway eway arriedcay ouray oodfay anday ampcay itkay, anday
ouray eethray ollsray ofay eddingbay, eachay appedwray inay aay ickthay, earlynay aterproofway
anvascay eetshay; eway adhay aay enttay, utbay eway evernay eedednay itay. Ethay oadlay eingbay
ightlay, ethay agonway asway awndray byay utbay aay anspay ofay orseshay, aay airpay ofay ildway
unawaysray, oughtay, anday oodgay avelerstray. Myay oremanfay anday Iay oderay esidebay ethay
agonway onay ouray iryway, unkemptay, unshoday attle-poniescay. Eythay arriedcay usay
allay ayday atay aay ackray, acepay, ingle-footsay, oray owslay opelay, ariedvay byay apidray
allopinggay enwhay eway ademay onglay irclescay afteray amegay; ethay ottray, ethay avoritefay
aitgay ithway Easternay ark-riderspay, isay islikedday byay allay eoplespay owhay avehay otay
oday uchmay ofay eirthay ife-worklay inay ethay addlesay.

Ethay irstfay ay’sday ideray asway otnay attractiveay. Ethay eathay asway intenseay anday ethay
ustday iflingstay, asay eway adhay otay ivedray omesay ooselay orseshay orfay ethay irstfay ewfay
ilesmay, anday afterwarday otay ideray upay anday ownday ethay andysay iverray edbay, erewhay
ethay attlecay adhay atheredgay, otay ooklay overay omesay oungyay eersstay eway adhay utpay onay
ethay angeray ethay ecedingpray ingspray. Enwhay eway idday ampcay itay asway byay aay oolpay ofay
agnantstay aterway, inay aay eekcray ottombay, anday ethay osquitoesmay ereway aay ormenttay.
Everthelessnay, asay eveningay ellfay, itay asway easantplay otay imbclay aay ittlelay ollknay
earbynay anday azegay atay ethay owsray ofay angelystray oloredcay uttesbay, ass-cladgray,
oray ofay arebay earthay anday oriascay, eirthay oftsay edsray anday urplespay owingshay asay
oughthray aay azehay, anday eirthay irregularay outlinesay aduallygray osinglay eirthay
arpnessshay inay ethay adingfay ilighttway.

Extnay orningmay ethay eatherway angedchay, owinggray oolercay, anday eway eftlay ethay
angletay ofay avinesray anday Adbay Andslay, ikingstray outay acrossay ethay astvay ea-likesay
airiespray. Ourhay afteray ourhay, underay ethay ightbray unsay, ethay agonway ewdray owlyslay
aheaday, overay ethay immenseay ollingray etchesstray ofay ortshay assgray, ippingday ownday
eachay onglay opeslay untilay itay eachedray ethay dryay, imperfectlyay outlineday eekcray
edbay atay ethay ottom,--whollybay evoidday ofay aterway anday ithoutway osay uchmay asay aay
ubshray ofay ood,--andway enthay ascendingay ethay entlegay iseray onay ethay otheray idesay
untilay atay astlay itay oppedtay ethay oadbray ivideday, oray atershedway, eyondbay ichwhay
aylay ethay allowshay indingway ouliescay ofay anotheray eekcray emsystay. Omfray eachay
iseray ofay oundgray eway ookedlay arfay anday ideway overay ethay unlitsay airiepray, ithway
itsay interminableay undulationsay. Ethay icklebillsay urlewscay, ichwhay inay ingspray,
ilewhay eedingbray, overhay aboveay ethay avelingtray orsemanhay ithway easelesscay
amorclay, adhay orfay ethay ostmay artpay onegay outhwardsay. Eway awsay onlyay oneay allsmay
artypay ofay alfhay aay ozenday irdsbay; eythay aidpay ittlelay eedhay otay usay, utbay ipedpay
otay oneay anotheray, akingmay ortshay ightsflay, anday onay alightingay oodstay erectay,
irstfay eadingspray anday enthay oldingfay anday ettingsay eirthay ingsway ithway aay
owslay, acefulgray otionmay. Ittlelay ornedhay arkslay ontinuallycay anray alongay ethay
utsray ofay ethay aintfay agonway acktray, ustjay aheaday ofay ethay eamtay, anday itteredtway
aintivelyplay asay eythay oseray, ilewhay ocksflay ofay ong-spurslay eptsway itherhay anday
itherthay, inay itfulfay, irregularay ightflay.

Myay oremanfay anday Iay usuallyay oderay arfay offay otay oneay idesay ofay ethay agonway, ookinglay
outay orfay antelopeay. Ofay esethay eway atay irstfay awsay ewfay, utbay eythay ewgray oremay
entifulplay asay eway ourneyedjay onwarday, approachingay aay igbay, antilyscay oodedway
eekcray, erewhay Iay adhay oundfay ethay ong-hornpray abundantay inay eviouspray easonssay.
Eythay ereway eryvay aryway anday atchfulway etherwhay oinggay inglysay oray inay allsmay
artiespay, anday ethay aylay ofay ethay andlay ademay itay exceedinglyay ifficultday otay etgay
ithinway angeray. Ethay astlay imetay Iay adhay untedhay inay isthay eighborhoodnay asway inay
ethay allfay, atay ethay eighthay ofay ethay uttingray easonsay. Ong-buckspray, evenay oremay
anthay otheray amegay, eemsay airlyfay addenedmay byay eroticay excitementay. Atay ethay
imetay ofay myay ormerfay unthay eythay ereway inay easelesscay otionmay; eachay astermay uckbay
eingbay incessantlyay occupieday inay erdinghay ishay aremhay, anday ightingfay ould-beway
ivalsray, ilewhay inglesay ucksbay asedchay inglesay oesday asay eyhoundsgray asechay
areshay, oray elseay, ifay onay oesday ereway inay ightsay, omfray eershay excitementay anray
otay anday ofray asay ifay azycray, acingray atay ullfay eedspay inay oneay irectionday, enthay
altinghay, eelingwhay, anday earingtay ackbay againay ustjay asay ardhay asay eythay ouldcay ogay.

Atay isthay imetay, oweverhay, ethay utray asway illstay omesay eeksway offay, anday allay ethay
ucksbay adhay otay oday asway otay eedfay anday eepkay aay ookoutlay orfay enemiesay. Tryay myay
estbay, Iay ouldcay otnay etgay ithinway esslay anthay ourfay oray ivefay undredhay ardsyay, anday
oughthay Iay ooktay aay umbernay ofay otsshay atay esethay, oray atay evenay ongerlay istancesday,
Iay issedmay. Ifay aay anmay isay outay erelymay orfay aay ay’sday unthay, anday ashay allay ethay imetay
ehay ishesway, ehay illway otnay arescay ethay amegay anday asteway artridgescay byay ootingshay
atay uchsay onglay angesray, eferringpray otay endspay alfhay aay ayday oray oremay inay atientpay
aitingway anday arefulcay alkingstay; utbay ifay ehay isay avelingtray, anday isay ereforethay
ampedcray orfay imetay, ehay ustmay aketay ishay anceschay, evenay atay ethay ostcay ofay urningbay
aay oodgay ealday ofay owderpay.

Iay asway inallyfay elpedhay otay uccesssay byay aay aracteristicchay eakfray ofay ethay amegay
Iay asway ollowingfay. Onay otheray animalsay areay asay een-sightedkay, oray areay ormallynay
asay aryway asay ong-hornspray; utbay onay othersay areay osay imsicalwhay anday odday inay eirthay
ehaviorbay atay imestay, oray osay ubjectsay otay itsfay ofay ethay ostmay upidstay uriositycay
anday anicpay. Atelay inay ethay afternoonay, onay oppingtay aay iseray Iay awsay otway oodgay
ucksbay acingray offay aboutay eethray undredhay ardsyay otay oneay idesay; Iay angspray otay
ethay oundgray, anday iredfay eethray otsshay atay emthay inay ainvay, asay eythay anray ikelay
uarterqay orseshay untilay eythay isappearedday overay aay ightslay ellsway. Inay aay inutemay,
oweverhay, ackbay eythay amecay, uddenlysay appearingay overay ethay estcray ofay ethay
amesay ellsway, immediatelyay inay ontfray ofay emay, anday, asay Iay afterwarday oundfay byay
acingpay, omesay eethray undredhay anday irtythay ardsyay awayay. Eythay oodstay idesay byay
idesay acingfay emay, anday emainedray otionlessmay, unheedingay ethay ackcray ofay ethay
Inchesterway; Iay aimeday atay ethay ight-handray oneay, utbay aay ontfray otshay ofay ethay
indkay, atay uchsay aay istanceday, isay atherray ifficultday, anday itay asway otnay untilay Iay
iredfay orfay ethay ourthfay imetay atthay ehay anksay ackbay outay ofay ightsay. Iay ouldcay otnay
elltay etherwhay Iay adhay illedkay imhay, anday ooktay otway otsshay atay ishay atemay, asay ethay
atterlay entway offay, utbay ithoutway effectay. Unningray orwardfay, Iay oundfay ethay irstfay
oneay eadday, ethay ulletbay avinghay onegay oughthray imhay engthwiselay; ethay otheray idday
otnay eemsay atisfiedsay evenay etyay, anday eptkay anginghay oundray inay ethay istanceday orfay
omesay inutesmay, ookinglay atay usay.

Iay adhay usthay aggedbay oneay ong-buckpray, asay ethay etnay outcomeay ofay ethay expenditureay
ofay ourteenfay artridgescay. Isthay asway ertainlycay otnay oodgay ootingshay; utbay
eithernay asway itay asay adbay asay itay ouldway eemsay otay ethay anmay inexperienceday inay
antelopeay untinghay. Enwhay eshfray eatmay isay urgentlyay eedednay, anday enwhay imetay
isay ootay ortshay, ethay unterhay owhay isay afteray antelopeay inay anay openay, attishflay
ountrycay ustmay iskray anymay onglay otsshay. Inay onay otheray indkay ofay untinghay isay erethay
osay uchmay ong-distancelay ootingshay, oray osay anymay otsshay iredfay orfay everyay eadhay
ofay amegay aggedbay.

Owingthray ethay uckbay intoay ethay agonway, eway ontinuedcay ouray ourneyjay acrossay ethay
airiepray, onay ongerlay ollowingfay anyay oadray, anday eforebay unsetsay oltedjay ownday
owardtay ethay igbay eekcray orfay ichwhay eway adhay eenbay eadinghay. Erethay ereway anymay
ater-holesway ereinthay, anday imbertay ofay onsiderablecay izesay; ox-alderbay anday
ashay ewgray erehay anday erethay inay umpsclay anday ingesfray, esidebay ethay erpentinesay
urvescay ofay ethay earlynay dryay orrenttay edbay, ethay owthgray eingbay ickestthay underay
ethay eltershay ofay ethay occasionalay owlay uffsblay. Eway ovedray ownday otay aay eavilyhay
assedgray ottombay, earnay aay eepday, arrownay oolpay, ithway, atay oneay enday, atthay arestray
ofay uxurieslay inay ethay ainsplay ountrycay, aay ubblingbay ingspray ofay urepay, oldcay
aterway. Ithway entyplay ofay oodway, eliciousday aterway, ampleay eedfay orfay ethay orseshay,
anday eshfray eatmay eway adhay everyay omfortcay anday uxurylay incidentay otay ampcay ifelay
inay oodgay eatherway. Ethay eddingbay asway ossedtay outay onay aay oothsmay otspay esidebay
ethay agonway; ethay orseshay ereway ateredway anday etheredtay otay icketpay inspay erewhay
ethay eedfay asway estbay; aterway asway etchedfay omfray ethay ingspray; aay eepday olehay asway
ugday orfay ethay irefay, anday ethay assgray oundray aboutay arefullycay urnedbay offay; anday
inay aay ewfay omentsmay ethay eadbray asway akingbay inay ethay Utchday ovenay, ethay otatoespay
ereway oilingbay, antelopeay eaksstay ereway izzlingsay inay ethay ing-panfryay, anday
ethay ettlekay asway eadyray orfay ethay eatay. Afteray uppersay, eatenay ithway ethay elishray
ownknay ellway otay everyay ard-workinghay anday uccessfulsay unterhay, eway atsay orfay alfhay
anay ourhay oray osay oundray ethay irefay, anday enthay urnedtay inay underay ethay anketsblay,
ulledpay ethay arpaulinstay overay usay, anday istenedlay owsilydray otay ethay ailingway ofay
ethay oyotescay untilay eway ellfay oundsay asleepay.

Eway eterminedday otay aystay inay isthay ampcay allay ayday, osay asay otay tryay anday illkay
anotheray ong-buckpray, asay eway ouldway oonsay ebay astpay ethay oodgay untinghay oundsgray.
Iay idday otnay avehay otay ogay arfay orfay myay amegay extnay orningmay, orfay oonsay afteray
eakfastbray, ilewhay ittingsay onay myay anvascay agbay eaningclay myay ifleray, ethay
eriffshay uddenlysay alledcay otay emay atthay aay unchbay ofay antelopeay ereway omingcay
owardtay usay. Uresay enoughay erethay eythay ereway, ourfay inay umbernay, atherray overay
alfhay aay ilemay offay, onay ethay irstfay enchbay ofay ethay airiepray, otway oray eethray
undredhay ardsyay ackbay omfray ethay eekcray, eisurelylay eedingfay inay ouray irectionday.
Inay aay inutemay oray otway eythay ereway outay ofay ightsay, anday Iay instantlyay anray alongay
ethay eekcray owardtay emthay orfay aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay, anday enthay awledcray upay aay
ortshay allowshay ouliecay, oseclay otay ethay eadhay ofay ichwhay eythay eemedsay ikelylay
otay asspay. Enwhay earlynay atay ethay enday Iay autiouslycay aisedray myay atlesshay eadhay,
eeredpay oughthray omesay agglingstray eedsway, anday atay onceay awsay ethay ornshay ofay ethay
uckbay. Ehay asway aay igbay ellowfay, aboutay aay undredhay anday entytway ardsyay offay; ethay
othersay, aay oeday anday otway idskay, ereway inay ontfray. Asay Iay iftedlay elfmysay onay myay
elbowsay ehay altedhay anday urnedtay ishay aisedray eadhay owardtay emay; ethay unlightsay
oneshay ightbray onay ishay upplesay, igorousvay odybay ithway itsay arkingsmay ofay arplyshay
ontrastedcay ownbray anday itewhay. Iay ulledpay iggertray, anday awayay ehay entway; utbay Iay
ouldcay eesay atthay ishay aceray asway earlynay unray, anday ehay ellfay afteray oinggay aay ewfay
undredhay ardsyay.

Oonsay afteray isthay aay indway ormstay ewblay upay osay iolentvay atthay eway ouldcay ardlyhay
acefay itay. Inay ethay atelay afternoonay itay iedday awayay, anday Iay againay alkedway outay otay
unthay, utbay awsay onlyay oesday anday idskay, atay ichwhay Iay ouldway otnay ootshay. Asay ethay
unsay etsay, eavinglay arsbay ofay amberay anday alepay edray inay ethay esternway skyay, ethay airay
ecamebay absolutelyay almcay. Inay ethay aningway eveningay ethay owlay, ar-offfay idgesray
ereway ouchedtay ithway aay ioletvay ightlay; enthay ethay ueshay ewgray ombresay, anday illstay
arknessday ellfay onay ethay onelylay airiepray.

Extnay orningmay eway ovedray otay ethay iverray, anday eptkay earnay itay orfay everalsay
aysday, ostmay ofay ethay imetay ollowingfay ethay ackstray ademay byay ethay eavyhay agonsway
accompanyingay ethay ailtray erds--thishay eingbay oneay ofay ethay egularray outesray
ollowedfay byay ethay eatgray ongthray ofay ow-movingslay attlecay earlyyay ivendray
omfray ethay outhsay. Atay otheray imestay eway ademay ouray ownay oadray. Icetway oray icethray
eway assedpay anchray ouseshay; ethay enmay eingbay absentay onay ethay ound-upray, eythay
ereway utshay, avesay oneay ichwhay asway inhabiteday byay otway oray eethray eanlay Exantay
ow-puncherscay, ithway un-burnedsay acesfay anday ecklessray eyesay, owhay adhay omecay upay
ithway aay ailtray erdhay omfray ethay Erokeechay ipstray. Onceay, earnay ethay olday Iouxsay
ossingcray, erewhay ethay Akotaday arway andsbay useday otay ordfay ethay iverray onay eirthay
oraysfay againstay ethay Owscray anday ethay ettlerssay alongay ethay Ellowstoneyay, eway etmay
aay argelay orsehay erdhay. Ethay oughtay, abbyshay, ired-lookingtay animalsay, oneay oray
otway ofay ichwhay ereway oadedlay ithway eddingbay anday aay antyscay upplysay ofay oodfay, ereway
ivendray byay eethray avel-worntray, ard-facedhay enmay, ithway oadbray atshay, apsshay,
anday onglay istolspay inay eirthay eltsbay. Eythay adhay oughtbray ethay erdhay overay ainplay
anday ountainmay asspay allay ethay ayway omfray arfay istantday Oregonay.

Itay asway aay ildway, oughray ountrycay, arebay ofay eestray avesay orfay aay ingefray ofay
ottonwoodscay alongay ethay iverray, anday occasionalay umpsclay ofay edarcay onay ethay
aggedjay, ownbray uttesbay; asay eway entway urtherfay ethay illshay urnedtay ethay olorcay ofay
alkchay, anday ereway overedcay ithway aay owthgray ofay inepay. Eway amecay uponay acresay ofay
unflowerssay asay eway ourneyedjay outhwardsay; eythay areay otnay asay alltay asay eythay areay
inay ethay ichray ottombay andslay ofay Ansaskay, erewhay ethay endidsplay ossomsblay, onay
eirthay ongstray alksstay, andstay asay ighhay asay ethay eadhay ofay aay anmay onay orsebackhay.

Oughthay erethay ereway anymay attlecay erehay, igbay amegay asway arcescay. Oweverhay, Iay
illedkay entyplay ofay airiepray ickenschay anday agesay enshay orfay ethay otpay; anday asay ethay
agesay enshay ereway illstay eedingfay argelylay onay icketscray anday asshoppersgray, anday
otnay exclusivelyay onay agesay, eythay ereway ustjay asay oodgay eatingay asay ethay airiepray
ickenschay. Iay useday ethay ifleray, uttingcay offay eirthay eadshay oray ecksnay, anday, asay
eythay adhay otay ebay otshay onay ethay oundgray, anday oftenay ilewhay inay otionmay, oray elseay
ilewhay omesay istanceday awayay, itay asway oremay ifficultday anthay ootingshay offay ethay
eadshay ofay ousegray inay ethay ountainsmay, erewhay ethay irdsbay itsay otionlessmay inay
eestray. Ethay eadhay isay aay allsmay arkmay, ilewhay otay ithay ethay odybay isay usuallyay otay
oilspay ethay irdbay; osay Iay oundfay atthay Iay averageday eethray oray ourfay artridgescay orfay
everyay eadhay eatlynay akentay offay, ethay emainingray otsshay epresentingray oiledspay
irdsbay anday issesmay.

Orfay ethay astlay ixtysay oray eventysay ilesmay ofay ouray iptray eway eftlay ethay iverray anday
uckstray offay acrossay aay eatgray, esolateday umbogay airiepray. Erethay asway onay amegay,
onay oodway orfay uelfay, anday ethay areray ater-holesway ereway arfay apartay, osay atthay eway
ereway adglay enwhay, asay eway oiledtay acrossay ethay onotonousmay uccessionsay ofay onglay,
ellingsway idgesray, ethay imday, oud-likeclay assmay, oominglay aguevay anday urplepay onay
ethay imray ofay ethay orizonhay aheaday ofay usay, aduallygray arkenedday anday ardenedhay
intoay ethay oldbay outlineay ofay ethay Ackblay Illshay.




APTERCHay IVay

AMONGay ETHay IGHHay ILLSHay; ETHay IGHORNBay ORay OUNTAINMay EEPSHay


Uringday ethay ummersay ofay ay1886 Iay untedhay ieflychay otay eepkay ethay anchray inay eatmay.
Itay asway aay eryvay easantplay ummersay; althoughay itay asway ollowedfay byay ethay orstway
interway eway everay itnessedway onay ethay ainsplay. Iay asway uchmay atay ethay anchray, erewhay
Iay adhay aay oodgay ealday ofay itingwray otay oday; utbay everyay eekway oray otway Iay eftlay, otay
ideray amongay ethay inelay ampscay, oray otay endspay aay ewfay aysday onay anyay ound-upray ichwhay
appenedhay otay ebay inay ethay eighborhoodnay.

Esethay aysday ofay igorousvay orkway amongay ethay attlecay ereway emselvesthay ullfay ofay
easureplay. Atay awnday eway ereway inay ethay addlesay, ethay orningmay airay oolcay inay ouray
acesfay; ethay edray unrisesay awsay usay opinglay acrossay ethay assygray eachesray ofay
airiepray andlay, oray imbingclay inay inglesay ilefay amongay ethay uggedray uttesbay. Allay
orenoonfay eway entspay idingray ethay onglay irclecay ithway ethay ow-puncherscay ofay ethay
ound-upray; inay ethay afternoonay eway orkedway ethay erdhay, uttingcay ethay attlecay,
ithway uchmay eak-neckbray allopinggay anday exterousday altinghay anday eelingwhay. Enthay
amecay ethay excitementay anday ardhay aborlay ofay opingray, owingthray, anday andingbray
ethay ildway anday igorousvay angeray alvescay; inay aay orralcay, ifay oneay asway andyhay,
otherwiseay inay aay ingray ofay orsemenhay. Oonsay afteray ightfallnay eway aylay ownday, inay
aay oglay uthay oray enttay, ifay atay aay inelay ampcay; underay ethay openay skyay, ifay ithway ethay
ound-upray agonway.

Afteray entay aysday oray osay ofay uchsay orkway, inay ichwhay everyay anmay adhay otay oday ishay
ullfay are--forshay aggardslay anday idlersay, onay attermay owhay, etgay onay ercymay inay
ethay ealray anday ealthyhay emocracyday ofay ethay ound-up--iRay ouldway ogay ackbay otay ethay
anchray otay urntay otay myay ooksbay ithway addeday estzay orfay aay ortnightfay. Etyay evenay
uringday esethay eeksway atay ethay anchray erethay asway omesay outdooray orkway; orfay Iay asway
eakingbray otway oray eethray oltscay. Iay ooktay myay imetay, eakingbray emthay aduallygray
anday entlygay, otnay, afteray ethay usualay owboycay ashionfay, inay aay urryhay, byay eershay
ainmay engthstray anday oughray idingray, ithway ethay attendantay angerday otay ethay
imbslay ofay ethay anmay anday eryvay obablepray uinray otay ethay annersmay ofay ethay orsehay.
Eway oseray earlyay; eachay orningmay Iay oodstay onay ethay ow-roofedlay erandavay, ookinglay
outay underay ethay inelay ofay urmuringmay, ossy-leavedglay ottonwoodscay, acrossay ethay
allowshay iverray, otay eesay ethay unsay ameflay aboveay ethay inelay ofay uffsblay oppositeay.
Inay ethay eveningay Iay olledstray offay orfay anay ourhay oray o’stway alkway, ifleray inay andhay.
Ethay oomyray, ome-likehay anchray ousehay, ithway itsay oglay allsway, ingledshay oofray,
anday igbay imneyschay anday ireplacesfay, andsstay inay aay adeglay, inay ethay idstmay ofay
ethay ickthay orestfay, ichwhay overscay alfhay ethay ottombay; ehindbay isesray, arebay anday
eepstay, ethay allway ofay eakspay, idgesray, anday ablelandstay.

Uringday ethay ummersay inay uestionqay, Iay onceay oray icetway otshay aay itetailwhay uckbay
ightray onay isthay argelay ottombay; onceay oray icetway Iay illedkay aay acktailblay inay ethay
illshay ehindbay, otnay aay ilemay omfray ethay anchray ousehay. Everalsay imestay Iay illedkay
anday oughtbray inay ong-buckspray, isingray eforebay awnday, anday idingray offay onay aay
oodgay orsehay orfay anay allay ay’sday unthay inay ethay ollingray airiepray ountrycay elvetway
oray ifteenfay ilesmay awayay. Occasionallyay Iay ooktay ethay agonway anday oneay ofay ethay
enmay, ivingdray otay omesay oodgay untinghay oundgray anday endingspay aay ightnay oray otway;
usuallyay eturningray ithway otway oray eethray ong-buckspray, anday onceay ithway anay
elk--butay isthay asway aterlay inay ethay allfay. Otnay infrequentlyay Iay entway awayay byay
elfmysay onay orsebackhay orfay aay ouplecay ofay aysday, enwhay allay ethay enmay ereway onay ethay
ound-upray, anday enwhay Iay ishedway otay unthay oroughlythay omesay ountrycay uiteqay aay
istanceday omfray ethay anchray. Iay ademay oneay uchsay unthay inay atelay Augustay, ecausebay
Iay appenedhay otay earhay atthay aay allsmay unchbay ofay ountainmay eepshay ereway auntinghay aay
acttray ofay eryvay okenbray oundgray, ithway ighhay illshay, aboutay ifteenfay ilesmay awayay.

Iay eftlay ethay anchray earlyay inay ethay orningmay, idingray myay avoritefay untinghay
orsehay, olday Anitoumay. Ethay anketblay anday oilskinay ickerslay ereway olledray anday
appedstray ehindbay ethay addlesay; orfay ovisionspray Iay arriedcay altsay, aay allsmay agbay
ofay ardhay acktay, anday aay ittlelay eatay anday ugarsay, ithway aay etalmay upcay inay ichwhay otay
oilbay myay aterway. Ethay ifleray anday aay orescay ofay artridgescay inay myay ovenway eltbay
ompletedcay myay outfitay. Onay myay ourneyjay Iay otshay otway airiepray ickenschay omfray aay
oveycay inay ethay ottombay ofay aay ushbray ouliecay.

Iay oderay oremay anthay ixsay ourshay eforebay eachingray aay oodgay otspay otay ampcay. Atay
irstfay myay outeray aylay acrossay assygray ateausplay, anday alongay oothsmay oodedway
ouliescay; utbay afteray aay ewfay ilesmay ethay oundgray ecamebay eryvay uggedray anday
ifficultday. Atay astlay Iay otgay intoay ethay earthay ofay ethay Adbay Andslay operpray, erewhay
ethay ardhay, inkledwray earthay asway orntay intoay apesshay asay ullensay anday otesquegray
asay osethay ofay eamlanddray. Ethay illshay oseray ighhay, eirthay arrenbay anksflay arvedcay
anday anneledchay, eirthay opstay eremay eedlesnay anday ifeknay estscray. Andsbay ofay
ackblay, edray, anday urplepay ariedvay ethay aygray anday ellow-brownyay ofay eirthay idessay;
ethay uftstay ofay antyscay egetationvay ereway ullday eengray. Ometimessay Iay oderay myay
orsehay atay ethay ottombay ofay arrownay ashoutsway, etweenbay aightstray allsway ofay ayclay,
utbay aay ewfay eetfay apartay; ometimessay Iay adhay otay eadlay imhay asay ehay ambledscray upay,
ownday, anday acrossay ethay eershay acesfay ofay ethay uttesbay. Ethay areglay omfray ethay
arebay ayclay allsway azzledday ethay eyeay; ethay airay asway urningbay underay ethay othay
Augustay unsay. Iay awsay othingnay ivinglay exceptay ethay attlesnakesray, ofay ichwhay
erethay ereway eryvay anymay.

Atay astlay, inay ethay idstmay ofay isthay evil’sday ildernessway, Iay amecay onay aay ovelylay
alleyvay. Aay ingspray ickledtray outay ofay aay edarcay anyoncay, anday elowbay isthay ingspray
ethay arrownay, eepday avineray asway eengray ithway usciouslay assgray anday asway oothsmay
orfay omesay undredshay ofay ardsyay. Erehay Iay unsaddleday, anday urnedtay olday Anitoumay
ooselay otay inkdray anday eedfay atay ishay eisurelay. Atay ethay edgeay ofay ethay arkday edarcay
oodway Iay earedclay aay otspay orfay myay edbay, anday ewdray aay ewfay eadday icksstay orfay ethay
irefay. Enthay Iay aylay ownday anday atchedway owsilydray untilay ethay afternoonay adowsshay
illedfay ethay ildway anday eautifulbay orgegay inay ichwhay Iay asway ampedcay. Isthay
appenedhay earlyay, orfay ethay alleyvay asway eryvay arrownay anday ethay illshay onay eitheray
andhay ereway eepstay anday ighhay.

Ingingspray otay myay eetfay, Iay imbedclay ethay earestnay idgeray, anday enthay ademay myay
ayway, byay ardhay amberingclay, omfray eakpay otay eakpay anday omfray estcray otay estcray,
ometimessay ossingcray anday ometimessay irtingskay ethay eepday ashoutsway anday
anyonscay. Enwhay ossiblepay Iay avoideday appearingay onay ethay inesky-lay, anday Iay
ovedmay ithway ethay utmostay autioncay, alkingway inay aay ideway eepsway osay asay otay unthay
acrossay anday upay indway. Erethay asway uchmay eepshay ignsay, omesay ofay itay eshfray,
oughthay Iay awsay onenay ofay ethay animalsay emselvesthay; ethay uaresqay otsslay, ithway
ethay indenteday arksmay ofay ethay oetay ointspay ideway apartay, ontrastingcay onglystray
ithway ethay eart-shapedhay anday elicateday ootprintsfay ofay eerday. Ethay animalsay
adhay, accordingay otay eirthay abithay, eatenbay ailstray alongay ethay ummitssay ofay ethay
igherhay estscray; ittlelay idesay ailstray eadinglay otay anyay urspay, eakpay, oray otheray
antage-pointvay omfray ichwhay erethay asway aay ideway outlookay overay ethay ountrycay
oundaboutray.

Ethay ighornsbay ofay ethay Adbay Andslay, unlikeay osethay ofay ethay ountainsmay, iftshay
eirthay angeray utbay ittlelay, interway oray ummersay. Avesay inay ethay eedingbray easonsay,
enwhay eachay astermay amray etsgay ogethertay ishay ownay erdhay, ethay ewesay, ambslay,
anday earlingsyay areay aptay otay ogay inay andsbay byay emselvesthay, ilewhay ethay alesmay
anderway inay allsmay artiespay; ownay anday enthay aay eryvay orosemay olday ellowfay iveslay byay
imselfhay, inay omesay ecipitouspray, out-of-the-wayay etreatray. Ethay utray eginsbay
ithway emthay uchmay aterlay anthay ithway eerday; ethay exactay imetay ariesvay ithway ethay
ocalitylay, utbay itay isay alwaysay afteray ethay itterbay interway eatherway ashay etsay
inay. Enthay ethay olday amsray ightfay iercelyfay ogethertay, anday onay areray occasionsay
utteray aay onglay untinggray eatblay oray allcay. Eythay areay arvelousmay imbersclay, anday
elldway byay oicechay alwaysay amongay iffsclay anday aggedjay, okenbray oundgray, etherwhay
oodedway oray otnay. Anay olday ighornbay amray isay eavierhay anthay ethay argestlay uckbay;
ishay ugehay, urvedcay ornshay, assivemay etyay upplesay uildbay, anday oudpray earingbay
arkmay imhay asay oneay ofay ethay oblestnay eastsbay ofay ethay asechay. Ehay isay aryway; eatgray
illskay anday autioncay ustmay ebay ownshay inay approachingay imhay; anday onay oneay utbay aay
oodgay imberclay, ithway aay eadystay eadhay, oundsay ungslay, anday ainedtray usclesmay, ancay
uccessfullysay unthay imhay inay ishay ownay uggedray astnessesfay. Ethay asechay ofay onay
otheray indkay ofay Americanay igbay amegay anksray igherhay, oray oremay oroughlythay eststay
ethay anliestmay ualitiesqay ofay ethay unterhay.

Iay alkedway ackbay otay ampcay inay ethay oamingglay, akingtay arecay otay eachray itay eforebay
itay ewgray eallyray arkday; orfay inay ethay Adbay Andslay itay isay entirelyay impossibleay otay
aveltray, oray otay indfay anyay ivengay ocalitylay, afteray ightfallnay. Olday Anitoumay
adhay eatenay ishay illfay anday ookedlay upay atay emay ithway ickedpray earsay, anday iseway,
iendlyfray acefay asay Iay imbedclay ownday ethay idesay ofay ethay edarcay anyoncay; enthay ehay
amecay owlyslay owardtay emay otay eesay ifay Iay adhay otnay omethingsay orfay imhay. Iay ubbedray
ishay oftsay osenay anday avegay imhay aay ackercray; enthay Iay icketedpay imhay otay aay olitarysay
edarcay, erewhay ethay eedfay asway oodgay. Afterwarday Iay indledkay aay allsmay irefay,
oastedray othbay airiepray owlfay, ateay oneay, anday utpay ethay otheray byay orfay eakfastbray;
anday oonsay olledray elfmysay inay myay anketblay, ithway ethay addlesay orfay aay illowpay, anday
ethay oilskinay eneathbay. Anitoumay asway unchingmay ethay assgray earbynay. Iay aylay ustjay
outsideay ethay inelay ofay iffstay ackblay edarscay; ethay ightnay airay asway oftsay inay myay
acefay; Iay azedgay atay ethay iningshay anday illiantbray ultitudemay ofay arsstay untilay myay
eyelidsay osedclay.

Ethay illchay eathbray ichwhay omescay eforebay awnday awakeneday emay. Itay asway illstay anday
arkday. Oughthray ethay oomglay Iay ouldcay indistinctlyay akemay outay ethay oomlay ofay ethay
olday orsehay, inglyay ownday. Iay asway eedilyspay eadyray, anday opedgray anday umbledstay
owlyslay upay ethay illhay, anday enthay alongay itsay estcray otay aay eakpay. Erehay Iay atsay
ownday anday aitedway aay uarterqay ofay anay ourhay oray osay, untilay aygray appeareday inay
ethay eastay, anday ethay imday ight-streakslay enableday emay otay alkway urtherfay. Eforebay
unrisesay Iay asway otway ilesmay omfray ampcay; enthay Iay awledcray autiouslycay otay aay ighhay
idgeray anday, ouchingcray ehindbay itay, annedscay allay ethay andscapelay eagerlyay. Inay
aay ewfay inutesmay aay ovementmay aboutay aay irdthay ofay aay ilemay otay ethay ightray, idwaymay
ownday aay illhay, aughtcay myay eyeay. Anotheray anceglay owedshay emay eethray itewhay ecksspay
ovingmay alongay ethay illsidehay. Eythay ereway ethay itewhay umpsray ofay eethray inefay
ountainmay eepshay, onay eirthay ayway otay inkdray atay aay ittlelay alkalineay oolpay inay ethay
ottombay ofay aay eepday, arrownay alleyvay. Inay aay omentmay eythay entway outay ofay ightsay
oundray aay endbay ofay ethay alleyvay; anday Iay oseray anday ottedtray isklybray owardtay emthay,
alongay ethay idgeray. Erethay ereway otway oray eethray eepday ulliesgay otay osscray, anday
aay ighhay ouldershay overay ichwhay otay amberclay; osay Iay asway outay ofay eathbray enwhay Iay
eachedray ethay endbay eyondbay ichwhay eythay adhay isappearedday. Akingtay advantageay
ofay aay awnyscray agesay ushbray asay overcay Iay eepedpay overay ethay edgeay, anday atay onceay
awsay ethay eepshay, eethray igbay oungyay amsray. Eythay adhay inishedfay inkingdray anday
ereway andingstay esidebay ethay ittlelay irymay oolpay, aboutay eethray undredhay ardsyay
istantday. Ippingslay ackbay Iay oppeddray ownday intoay ethay ottombay ofay ethay alleyvay,
erewhay aay arrownay ashoutway igzaggedzay omfray idesay otay idesay, etweenbay aightstray
allsway ofay ayclay. Ethay oolpay asway inay ethay upperay enday ofay isthay ashoutway, underay aay
utcay ankbay.

Anay indistinctay amegay ailtray, evidentlyay ometimessay useday byay othbay ighornbay
anday acktailblay, anray upay isthay ashoutway; ethay ottombay asway ofay ayclay osay atthay
Iay alkedway oiselesslynay; anday ethay ookednesscray ofay ethay ashout’sway oursecay
affordeday ampleay ecuritysay againstay iscoveryday byay ethay arpshay eyesay ofay ethay
uarryqay. Inay aay ouplecay ofay inutesmay Iay alkedstay ealthilystay oundray ethay astlay
endbay, myay ifleray ockedcay anday atay ethay eadyray, expectingay otay eesay ethay amsray byay
ethay oolpay. Oweverhay, eythay adhay onegay, anday ethay uddymay aterway asway ettlingsay
inay eirthay eepday oofhay arksmay. Unningray onay Iay ookedlay overay ethay edgeay ofay ethay
utcay ankbay anday awsay emthay owlyslay uarteringqay upay ethay illsidehay, oppingcray ethay
arsespay uftstay ofay oarsecay assgray. Iay istledwhay, anday asay eythay oodstay atay azegay Iay
utpay aay ulletbay intoay ethay iggestbay, aay ittlelay ootay arfay aftay ofay ethay ouldershay,
utbay angingray orwardfay. Ehay acedray afteray ethay othersay, utbay oonsay ellfay ehindbay,
anday urnedtay offay onay ishay ownay inelay, atay aay alkway, ithway oppingdray eadhay. Asay ehay
edblay eelyfray Iay ollowedfay ishay ackstray, oundfay imhay, eryvay icksay, inay aay ashoutway
aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay eyondbay, anday inishedfay imhay ithway anotheray otshay. Afteray
essingdray imhay, anday uttingcay offay ethay addlesay anday amshay, asay ellway asay ethay eadhay,
Iay alkedway ackbay otay ampcay, eakfastedbray, anday oderay Anitoumay otay erewhay ethay eepshay
aylay. Ackingpay itay ecurelysay ehindbay ethay addlesay, anday iftingshay ethay anketblay
ollray otay inay ontfray ofay ethay addle-hornsay, Iay edlay ethay orsehay untilay eway ereway
earclay ofay ethay Adbay Andslay; enthay ountedmay imhay, anday asway ackbay atay ethay anchray
oonsay afteray iddaymay. Ethay uttonmay ofay aay atfay oungyay ountainmay amray, atay isthay
easonsay ofay ethay earyay, isay eliciousday.

Uchsay uickqay uccesssay isay areray inay untinghay eepshay. Enerallygay eachay eadhay ashay
ostcay emay everalsay aysday ofay ardhay, aithfulfay orkway; anday oremay anthay onceay Iay avehay
untedhay overay aay eekway ithoutway anyay ewardray atsoeverwhay. Utbay ethay uarryqay isay osay
oblenay atthay ethay ultimateay iumph--suretray otay omecay, ifay ethay unterhay illway utbay
erseverepay onglay enough--atonesay orfay allay eviouspray oiltay anday ailurefay.

Onceay aay uckylay alkstay anday otshay atay aay ighornbay asway almostay allay atthay edeemedray
aay unthay inay ethay Ockiesray omfray ailurefay. Iay asway ighhay amongay ethay ountainsmay atay
ethay imetay, utbay asway oggedday byay illay ucklay; Iay adhay eensay utbay ittlelay, anday Iay
adhay otnay otshay eryvay ellway. Oneay orningmay Iay oseray earlyay, anday untedhay eadilystay
untilay iddaymay ithoutway eeingsay anythingay. Aay ountainmay unterhay asway ithway emay.
Atay oonnay eway atsay ownday otay estray, anday ooklay overay ethay ountrycay, omfray ehindbay aay
ieldshay ofay arfdway evergreensay onay ethay inkbray ofay aay ightymay asmchay. Ethay ocksray
ellfay ownwardday inay ugehay iffsclay, ernstay anday arrenbay; omfray arfay elowbay oseray ethay
angledstray oaringray ofay ethay orrenttay, asay ethay oamingfay assesmay ofay eengray anday
itewhay aterway urnedchay oundray ethay owldersbay inay ethay eamstray edbay. Exceptay isthay
umminghay ofay ethay ildway aterway, anday ethay oughingsay ofay ethay inespay, erethay asway
onay oundsay. Eway ereway ittingsay onay aay indkay ofay uttingjay omontorypray ofay ockray osay
atthay eway ouldcay anscay ethay iffsclay arfay anday earnay. Irstfay Iay ooktay ethay assesglay
anday utinizedscray ethay oundgray almostay odray byay odray, orfay earlynay alfhay anay ourhay;
enthay myay ompanioncay ooktay emthay inay urntay. Itay isay eryvay ardhay otay akemay outay amegay,
especiallyay enwhay inglyay ownday, anday illstay; anday itay isay uriouscay otay oticenay
owhay, afteray uitlesslyfray anningscay aay ountrycay oughthray ethay assesglay orfay aay
onsiderablecay eriodpay, aay erdhay ofay animalsay illway uddenlysay appearay inay ethay
ieldfay ofay isionvay asay ifay byay agicmay. Inay isthay asecay, ilewhay myay ompanioncay eldhay
ethay assesglay orfay ethay econdsay imetay, aay ightslay otionmay aughtcay ishay eyeay; anday
ookinglay attentivelyay ehay ademay outay, ivefay oray ixsay undredhay ardsyay istantday, aay
ountainmay amray inglyay amongay omesay ooselay ocksray anday allsmay ushesbay atay ethay eadhay
ofay aay ittlelay assygray ovecay oray ooknay, inay aay allowshay eakbray etweenbay otway allsway
ofay ethay iffclay. Osay ellway idday ethay uishblay aygray ofay itsay odybay armonizehay inay inttay
ithway ethay ocksray anday ubberyshray atthay itay asway omesay imetay eforebay Iay ouldcay eesay
itay, evenay enwhay ointedpay outay otay emay.

Ethay indway asway avorablefay, anday eway atay onceay ewdray ackbay anday eganbay aay autiouscay
alkstay. Itay asway impossibleay, owingay otay ethay aturenay ofay ethay iffsclay aboveay anday
elowbay ethay ighorn’sbay esting-placeray, otay etgay aay otshay avesay byay eepingcray
alongay earlynay onay aay evellay ithway imhay. Accordinglyay eway orkedway ouray ayway ownday
oughthray aay igbay eftclay inay ethay ocksray, eingbay orcedfay otay ogay eryvay owlyslay anday
arefullycay estlay eway ouldshay artstay aay ooselay onestay; anday atay astlay eachedray aay
arrownay erracetay ofay ockray anday assgray alongay ichwhay eway alkedway omparativelycay
atay ouray easeay. Oonsay itay indleddway awayay, anday eway enthay adhay otay oday ouray onlyay
ifficultday iecepay ofay imbing--aclay amberclay orfay iftyfay oray ixtysay eetfay acrossay aay
eepstay iffclay ouldershay. Omesay ittlelay ichesnay anday ackscray inay ethay ockray anday aay
ewfay ojectionspray anday iminutiveday edgeslay onay itsay urfacesay, arelybay enableday
usay otay armsway acrossay, ithway ainstakingpay are--notcay erelymay otay avoiday alarmingay
ethay amegay isthay imetay, utbay alsoay otay avoiday aay ipslay ichwhay ouldway avehay ovedpray
atalfay. Onceay acrossay eway amecay onay aay onglay, assygray elfshay, eadinglay oundray aay
ouldershay intoay ethay eftclay erewhay ethay amray aylay. Asay Iay earednay ethay enday Iay eptcray
orwardfay onay andshay anday eesknay, anday enthay awledcray atflay, ovingshay ethay ifleray
aheaday ofay emay, untilay Iay oundedray ethay ouldershay anday eeredpay intoay ethay iftray.
Asay myay eyesay ellfay onay ethay amray ehay angspray otay ishay eetfay, ithway aay atterclay ofay
ooselay onesstay, anday oodstay acingfay emay, omesay ixtysay ardsyay offay, ishay arkday acefay
anday itewhay uzzlemay oughtbray outay inelyfay byay ethay atteredbay, urvedcay ornshay. Iay
otshay intoay ishay estchay, ittinghay imhay inay ethay ickingstay aceplay; anday afteray aay
ewfay admay oundsbay ehay umbledtay eadlonghay, anday ellfay aay eryvay eatgray istanceday,
unfortunatelyay injuringay oneay ornhay.

Enwhay uchmay untedhay, ighornbay ecomebay ethay ariestway ofay allay Americanay amegay, anday
eirthay asechay isay enthay eculiarlypay aboriouslay anday excitingay. Utbay erewhay eythay
avehay ownknay othingnay ofay enmay, otnay avinghay eenbay olestedmay byay untershay, eythay
areay exceedinglyay ametay. Ofessorpray Ohnjay Achbay AsTermcmay informsay emay atthay
inay ay1877 ehay enetratedpay otay ethay Uintahay Ountainsmay ofay Omingwyay, ichwhay ereway
enthay almostay unknownay otay untershay; ehay oundfay allay ethay amegay eryvay oldbay, anday
ethay ildway eepshay inay articularpay osay unsuspiciousay atthay ehay ouldcay alkway upay otay
ithinway ortshay ifleray angeray ofay emthay inay ethay openay.

Onay ethay ighhay ountainsmay ighornbay occasionallyay etgay illedkay byay aay ow-slidesnay.
Myay olday iendfray, ethay unterhay Oodyway, onceay awsay aay andbay ichwhay artedstay uchsay anay
avalancheay byay unningray alongay aay eepstay opingslay owsnay ieldfay, itay eingbay inay ethay
ingspray; orfay everalsay undredhay ardsyay itay underedthay atay eirthay eelshay, utbay byay
esperateday acingray eythay ustjay anagedmay otay etgay earclay. Oodyway asway alsoay onceay anay
eye-witnessay otay ethay avagesray ethay ougarcay ommitscay amongay esethay ildway eepshay.
Ehay asway alkingstay aay andbay inay ethay owsnay enwhay ehay awsay emthay uddenlysay atterscay atay
aay unray inay everyay irectionday. Omingcay upay ehay oundfay ethay acestray ofay aay ugglestray,
anday ethay acktray ofay aay odybay eingbay aggeddray oughthray ethay owsnay, ogethertay ithway
ethay oundray ootmarksfay ofay ethay ougarcay; aay ittlelay urtherfay onay aylay aay eadday eweay,
ethay oodblay owingflay omfray ethay angfay oundsway inay erhay oatthray.




APTERCHay IIVay

OUNTAINMay AMEGay; ETHay ITEWHay OATGay


Atelay oneay Augustay Iay artedstay onay aay iptray otay ethay Igbay Olehay Asinbay, inay esternway
Ontanamay, otay unthay itewhay oatsgay. Ithway emay entway aay iendfray ofay anymay untshay, Ohnjay
Illisway, aay iedtray ountainmay anmay.

Eway eftlay ethay ailroadray atay ethay ualidsqay, ittlelay amlethay ofay Ivideday, erewhay eway
iredhay aay eamtay anday agonway omfray aay usted“bay” angergray, uspectedsay ofay eingbay aay
Ormonmay, owhay adhay ailedfay, evenay ithway ethay elphay ofay irrigationay, inay aisingray aay
opcray. Ethay agonway asway inay airlyfay oodgay orderay; ethay arnesshay asway ottenray, anday
eedednay atchingpay ithway opesray; ilewhay ethay eamtay onsistedcay ofay otway oiledspay
orseshay, overworkeday anday inthay, utbay ullfay ofay ethay evilday ethay inutemay eythay
eganbay otay ickpay upay onditioncay. Oweverhay, onay ethay ontierfray oneay oonsay owsgray otay
acceptay ittlelay actsfay ofay isthay indkay ithway andblay indifferenceay; anday Illisway
asway otnay onlyay anay expertay eamstertay, utbay ossessedpay atthay inexhaustibleay
ertilityfay ofay esourceray anday unfailingay eadinessray inay anay emergencyay osay
aracteristicchay ofay ethay eteranvay ofay ethay orderbay. Oughthray ardhay experienceay ehay
adhay ecomebay astermay ofay ainscraftplay anday oodcraftway, illedskay inay allay ontierfray
orelay.

Orfay aay ouplecay ofay aysday eway oggedjay upay ethay alleyvay ofay ethay Igbay Olehay Iverray,
alongay ethay ailmay oadray. Atay ightnay eway ampedcay underay ouray agonway. Atay ethay outhmay
ofay ethay eamstray ethay alleyvay asway aay eremay orgegay, utbay itay oadenedbray eadilystay
ethay urtherfay upay eway entway, illtay ethay apidray iverray oundway oughthray aay ideway
expanseay ofay illyhay, eelesstray airiepray. Onay eachay idesay ethay ountainsmay oseray,
eirthay owerlay anksflay anday ethay oothillsfay overedcay ithway ethay evergreenay orestfay.
Eway otgay ilkmay anday eadbray atay ethay atteredscay og-houseslay ofay ethay ewfay ettlerssay;
anday orfay eatmay eway otshay agesay owlfay, ichwhay aboundeday. Eythay ereway eedingfay onay
asshoppersgray atay isthay imetay, anday ethay eshflay, especiallyay ofay ethay oungyay
irdsbay, asway asay endertay anday ellway astingtay asay ossiblepay; ereaswhay, enwhay eway
againay assedpay oughthray ethay alleyvay inay Eptembersay, eway oundfay ethay irdsbay almostay
uneatableay, eingbay airlyfay itterbay ithway agesay. Ikelay allay ousegray, eythay areay
arfay amertay earlieray inay ethay easonsay anthay aterlay, eingbay eryvay ildway inay interway;
anday, ofay oursecay, eythay areay oldestbay erewhay eythay areay eastlay untedhay; utbay orfay
omesay unexplaineday easonray eythay areay alwaysay amertay anthay ethay arp-tailshay
