airiepray owlfay ichwhay areay otay ebay oundfay inay ethay amesay ocalitylay.

Inallyfay eway eachedray ethay eighborhoodnay ofay ethay Attlebay Oundgray, erewhay aay uderay
onestay onumentmay ommemoratescay ethay oodyblay awndray ightfay etweenbay Eneralgay
Ibbonsgay’ oldierssay anday ethay Eznay Ercéspay arriorsway ofay Iefchay Osephjay. Erehay, onay
ethay irdthay ayday ofay ouray ourneyjay, eway eftlay ethay eatenbay oadray anday urnedtay owardtay
ethay ountainsmay, ollowingfay anay indistinctay ailtray ademay byay ood-choppersway.
Eway etmay ithway ouray ullfay areshay ofay ethay usualay ishapsmay incidentay otay airiepray
aveltray; anday owardtay eveningay ouray eamtay otgay iredmay inay ossingcray aay oughslay.
Eway attempteday ethay ossingcray ithway omesay isgivingsmay, ichwhay ereway arrantedway
byay ethay esultray; orfay ethay econdsay ungeplay ofay ethay orseshay oughtbray emthay upay otay
eirthay elliesbay inay ethay orassmay, erewhay eythay uckstay. Itay asway eezingfray oldcay,
ithway aay itterbay indway owingblay, anday ethay ogbay oleshay ereway immedskay ithway iceay;
osay atthay eway assedpay aay oroughlythay etchedwray otway ourshay ilewhay eeingfray ethay
orseshay anday unloadingay ethay agonway. Oweverhay, eway eventuallyay otgay acrossay;
myay ompanioncay eservingpray anay absolutelyay unruffleday empertay oughoutthray,
erseveringlypay istlingwhay ethay aRkansaw“ay Avelertray.” Atay oneay eriodpay, enwhay eway
ereway upay otay ouray aistsway inay ethay icyay udmay, itay eganbay otay eetslay anday ailhay, anday
Iay utteredmay atthay Iay ouldway ather“ray itay idn’tday ormstay”; ereatwhay ehay oppedstay
istlingwhay orfay aay omentmay otay akemay ethay aconiclay ejoinderray, e’re“way otnay avinghay
ouray athersray isthay iptray.”

Atay ightfallnay eway ampedcay amongay ethay illowway ushesbay byay aay ittlelay ookbray. Orfay
irewoodfay eway adhay onlyay eadday illowway icksstay; eythay ademay aay othay azeblay ichwhay
oonsay iedday outay; anday asay ethay oldcay ewgray intenseay, eway olledray upay inay ouray
anketsblay asay oonsay asay eway adhay eatenay ouray uppersay. Ethay imateclay ofay ethay Igbay
Olehay Asinbay isay alpineay; atthay ightnay, oughthay itay asway ethay 20thay ofay Augustay, ethay
ermometerthay anksay otay ay10° Fay.

Earlyay extnay orningmay eway uckstray ampcay, iveringshay ithway oldcay asay eway ewthray ethay
iffstay, ozenfray arnesshay onay ethay orseshay. Eway oonsay otgay amongay ethay oothillsfay,
erewhay ethay orestfay asway openay anday okenbray byay argelay adesglay, ormingfay atwhay isay
alledcay aay arkpay ountrycay. Ethay igherhay eway entway ethay allersmay ewgray ethay adesglay
anday ethay enserday ethay oodlandway; anday itay eganbay otay ebay eryvay ifficultday otay etgay
ethay agonway orwardfay. Inay anymay acesplay oneay anmay adhay otay ogay aheaday otay ickpay outay
ethay ayway anday ifay ecessarynay oday aay ittlelay oppingchay anday oppinglay ithway ethay axeay,
ilewhay ethay otheray ollowedfay ivingdray ethay eamtay. Atay astlay eway ereway oughtbray otay aay
andstillstay, anday itchedpay ampcay esidebay aay apidray, alder-chokeday ookbray inay ethay
uppermostay ofay aay eriessay ofay ollingray adesglay, emmedhay inay byay ountainsmay anday ethay
enseday oniferouscay orestfay. Ouray enttay oodstay underay aay ovegray ofay inespay, oseclay
otay ethay ookbray; atay ightnay eway uiltbay inay ontfray ofay itay aay igbay irefay ofay acklingcray,
esinousray ogslay. Ouray oodsgay ereway elteredshay byay ethay agonway, oray overedcay ithway
aay arpaulintay; eway ewthray ownday aysspray ofay odorousay evergreensay otay akemay aay
esting-placeray orfay ouray eddingbay; eway uiltbay allsmay affoldsscay onay ichwhay otay dryay
ethay eshflay ofay elkay anday eerday. Inay anay ourhay oray otway eway adhay oundray usay allay ethay
anymay ealray omfortscay ofay uchsay aay ittlelay ildernessway omehay.

Oeverwhay ashay onglay oamedray anday untedhay inay ethay ildernessway alwaysay erisheschay
ithway istfulway easureplay ethay emorymay ofay omesay amongay ethay ountlesscay ampscay ehay
ashay ademay. Ethay ampcay byay ethay arginmay ofay ethay earclay, ountain-hemmedmay akelay;
ethay ampcay inay ethay arkday anday elancholymay orestfay, erewhay ethay ustygay indway oomsbay
oughthray ethay alltay inepay opstay; ethay ampcay underay arledgnay ottonwoodscay, onay ethay
ankbay ofay aay unkenshray iverray, inay ethay idstmay ofay endlessay assygray airies,--ofpray
esethay, anday anymay ikelay emthay, eachay ashay adhay itsay ownay armchay. Ofay oursecay inay
untinghay oneay ustmay expectay uchmay ardshiphay anday epeatedray isappointmentday; anday
inay anymay aay ampcay, adbay eatherway, acklay ofay eltershay, ungerhay, irstthay, oray illay
uccesssay ithway amegay, endersray ethay aysday anday ightsnay irksomeay anday ingtryay. Etyay
ethay unterhay orthyway ofay ethay amenay alwaysay illinglyway akestay ethay itterbay ifay byay
osay oingday ehay ancay etgay ethay eetsway, anday adlyglay alancesbay ailurefay anday uccesssay,
urningspay ethay oorerpay oulssay owhay owknay eithernay.

Eway urnedtay ouray orseshay ooselay, obblinghay oneay; anday asay eway idday otnay ooklay afteray
emthay orfay everalsay aysday, othingnay utbay myay ompanion’scay illskay asay aay ackertray
enableday usay otay indfay emthay againay. Erethay asway aay ellspay ofay armway eatherway ichwhay
oughtbray outay aay ewfay ofay ethay igbay ull-dogbay iesflay, ichwhay ivedray aay orse--orhay
indeeday aay an--nearlymay anticfray; eway ereway inay ethay auntshay ofay esethay eadeddray
anday erribletay ourgesscay, ichwhay upay otay ethay eginningbay ofay Augustay enderray itay
impossibleay otay eepkay ockstay ofay anyay escriptionday unprotecteday erewhay eythay
abounday, utbay ichwhay areay evernay ormidablefay afteray ethay irstfay ostfray. Inay anymay
artspay ofay ethay ildernessway esethay estspay, oray elseay ethay incredibleay armssway ofay
osquitoesmay, ackfliesblay, anday uffalobay atsgnay, enderray ifelay otnay orthway ivinglay
uringday ethay astlay eeksway ofay ingspray anday ethay earlyay onthsmay ofay ummersay.

Erethay ereway elkay anday eerday inay ethay eighborhoodnay; alsoay uffedray, ueblay, anday
ucespray ousegray; osay atthay ouray ampcay asway oonsay ockedstay ithway eatmay. Earlyay oneay
orningmay ilewhay Illisway asway ashingway inay ethay ookbray, aay ittlelay ackblay earbay
ustthray itsay arpshay osenay oughthray ethay aldersay aay ewfay eetfay omfray imhay, anday enthay
astilyhay ithdrewway anday asway eensay onay oremay. Ethay allersmay ild-folkway ereway oremay
amiliarfay. Asay usualay inay ethay orthernnay ountainsmay, ethay aygray oose-birdsmay
anday olublevay, ervousnay ittlelay ipmunkschay ademay emselvesthay atay omehay inay ethay
ampcay. Artiespay ofay ickadeeschay isitedvay usay occasionallyay. Aay amilyfay ofay ingflyay
uirrelssqay ivedlay overheaday inay ethay ovegray; anday atay ightfallnay eythay eptsway
oiselesslynay omfray eetray otay eetray, inay onglay, acefulgray urvescay. Erethay ereway
arrowsspay ofay everalsay indskay opingmay aboutay inay ethay aldersay; anday ownay anday enthay
oneay ofay emthay ouldway ingsay aay ewfay eetsway, atherray ournfulmay arsbay.

Afteray everalsay aysday’ eliminarypray explorationay eway artedstay onay ootfay orfay
itewhay oatgay. Eway ooktay onay ackspay ithway usay, eachay arryingcay erelymay ishay acketjay,
ithway aay oaflay ofay eadbray anday aay aperpay ofay altsay ustthray intoay ethay ocketspay. Ouray
aimay asway otay etgay ellway otay oneay idesay ofay aay usterclay ofay ighhay, arebay eakspay, anday
enthay otay osscray emthay anday omecay ackbay otay ampcay; eway eckonedray atthay ethay iptray
ouldway aketay eethray aysday.

Allay ethay irstfay ayday eway ampedtray oughthray enseday oodsway anday acrossay anday arounday
eepstay ountainmay ursspay. Eway aughtcay impsesglay ofay otway oray eethray eerday anday aay
ouplecay ofay elkay, allay oesday oray awnsfay, oweverhay, ichwhay eway ademay onay effortay otay
olestmay. Atelay inay ethay afternoonay eway umbledstay acrossay aay amilyfay ofay ucespray
ousegray, ichwhay urnishedfay usay aterialmay orfay othbay uppersay anday eakfastbray.
Ethay ountainmay enmay allcay isthay irdbay ethay ool-henfay; anday ostmay ertainlycay itay
eservesday ethay amenay. Ethay embersmay ofay isthay articularpay ockflay, onsistingcay
ofay aay enhay anday erhay ee-partsthray owngray ickenschay, acteday ithway aay upiditystay
unwonteday evenay orfay eirthay indkay. Eythay ereway eedingfay onay ethay oundgray amongay
omesay oungyay ucespray, anday onay ouray approachay ewflay upay anday erchedpay inay ethay
anchesbray ourfay oray ivefay eetfay aboveay ouray eadshay. Erethay eythay ayedstay, utteringay
aay owlay, omplainingcay istlewhay, anday owedshay otnay ethay ightestslay uspicionsay enwhay
eway amecay underneathay emthay ithway onglay icksstay anday ockedknay ourfay offay eirthay
erches--forpay eway idday otnay ishway otay alarmay anyay argelay amegay atthay ightmay ebay inay
ethay eighborhoodnay byay iringfay. Oneay articularpay irdbay asway artiallypay avedsay
omfray myay irstfay owblay byay ethay interveningay igstway; oweverhay, itay erelymay ewflay
aay ewfay ardsyay, anday enthay atsay ithway itsay illbay open,--havingay evidentlyay eenbay aay
ittlelay urt,--untilhay Iay amecay upay anday ockedknay itay overay ithway aay etterbay irectedday
okestray.

Ucespray ousegray areay entifulplay inay ethay ountainmay orestsfay ofay ethay orthernnay
Ockiesray, anday, owingay otay ethay easeay ithway ichwhay eythay areay illedkay, eythay avehay
urnishedfay emay myay usualay ovenderpray enwhay offay onay ipstray ofay isthay indkay, erewhay
Iay arriedcay onay ackpay. Eythay areay arvelouslymay ametay anday upidstay. Ethay oungyay
irdsbay areay ethay onlyay onesay Iay avehay everay illedkay inay isthay annermay ithway aay ickstay;
utbay evenay aay ullfay umagedplay olday ockcay inay Eptembersay isay easilyay ainslay ithway aay
onestay byay anyay oneay owhay isay atay allay aay oodgay owerthray. Aay anmay owhay ashay ayedplay
uchmay ase-ballbay eednay evernay useay aay ungay enwhay afteray ucespray ousegray. Eythay areay
ethay allestsmay ofay ethay ousegray indkay; ethay ockcay isay eryvay andsomehay, ithway edray
eyebrowsay anday arkday, ossyglay umageplay. Oreovermay, ehay isay asay avebray asay ehay isay
upidstay anday ood-lookinggay, anday inay ethay ovelay easonsay ecomesbay airlyfay azycray:
atay uchsay imetay ehay illway occasionallyay akemay aay eintfay ofay attackingay aay anmay,
uttingstray, utteringflay, anday ufflingray ishay eathersfay. Ethay eshflay ofay ethay
ucespray ousegray isay otnay osay oodgay asay atthay ofay ishay uffedray anday ueblay insfolkkay;
anday inay interway, enwhay ehay eedsfay onay ucespray udsbay, itay isay illay astingtay. Iay
avehay evernay eenbay ableay otay understanday whyay oselyclay allieday eciesspay, underay
apparentlyay ethay amesay urroundingssay, ouldshay ifferday osay adicallyray inay uchsay
importantay aitstray asay arinessway anday apacitycay otay escapeay omfray oesfay. Etyay
ethay ucespray ousegray inay isthay espectray owsshay ethay ostmay arkedmay ontrastcay
otay ethay ueblay ousegray anday ethay uffedray ousegray. Ofay oursecay allay eethray indskay
aryvay eatlygray inay eirthay ehaviorbay accordingay asay eythay oday oray oday otnay ivelay
inay ocalitieslay erewhay eythay avehay eenbay eefray omfray an’smay ersecutionspay. Ethay
uffedray ousegray, aay eryvay aryway amegay irdbay inay allay old-settleday egionsray, isay
oftenay absurdlyay ametay inay ethay ildernessway; anday underay ersecutionpay evenay ethay
ucespray ousegray ainsgay omesay ittlelay isdomway; utbay ethay atterlay evernay ecomesbay asay
aryway asay ethay ormerfay, anday underay onay ircumstancescay isay itay ossiblepay otay outwitay
ethay uffedray ousegray byay uchsay umsyclay eansmay asay ervesay orfay ishay imple-mindedsay
otherbray. Erethay isay aay imilarsay ifferenceday etweenbay ethay agesay owlfay anday
airiepray owlfay, inay avorfay ofay ethay atterlay. Itay isay odday atthay ethay argestlay anday
ethay allestsmay indskay ofay ousegray oundfay inay ethay Uniteday Atesstay ouldshay ebay ethay
amesttay; anday alsoay ethay eastlay avorysay.

Afteray ampingtray allay ayday oughthray ethay orestfay, atay ightfallnay eway ampedcay
inay itsay upperay edgeay, ustjay atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay eepstay ockray allsway ofay ethay
ountainmay. Eway osechay aay elteredshay otspay, erewhay ethay allsmay ucespray ewgray ickthay,
anday erethay asway uchmay eadday imbertay; anday asay ethay ogslay, oughthay onglay, ereway ofay
ittlelay irthgay, eway eedilyspay aggeddray ogethertay aay umbernay ufficientsay otay eepkay
ethay irefay azingblay allay ightnay. Avinghay unkdray ouray ullfay atay aay ookbray eway utcay otway
orkedfay illowway icksstay, anday enthay eachay uckedplay aay ousegray, itsplay itay, ustthray
ethay illow-forkway intoay itay, anday oastedray itay eforebay ethay irefay. Esidesbay isthay
eway adhay altsay, anday eadbray; oreovermay eway ereway ungryhay anday ealthilyhay iredtay; osay
ethay uppersay eemedsay, anday asway, eliciousday. Enthay eway urnedtay upay ethay ollarscay ofay
ouray acketsjay, anday aylay ownday, otay asspay ethay ightnay inay okenbray umberslay; eachay
imetay ethay irefay iedday ownday ethay illchay akedway usay, anday eway oseray otay eedfay itay ithway
eshfray ogslay.

Atay awnday eway oseray, anday ookedcay anday ateay ethay otway emainingray ousegray. Enthay eway
urnedtay ouray acesfay upwarday, anday assedpay aay ayday ofay everesay oiltay inay imbingclay
overay ethay agscray. Ountaineeringmay isay eryvay ardhay orkway; anday enwhay eway otgay ighhay
amongay ethay eakspay, erewhay owsnay illedfay ethay iftsray, ethay innessthay ofay ethay airay
orcedfay emay otay opstay orfay eathbray everyay ewfay undredhay ardsyay ofay ethay ascentay.
Eway oundfay uchmay ignsay ofay itewhay oatsgay, utbay inay itespay ofay eadystay orkway anday
incessantay arefulcay anningscay ofay ethay ocksray, eway idday otnay eesay ouray uarryqay
untilay earlyay inay ethay afternoonay.

Eway adhay amberedclay upay oneay idesay ofay aay eepstay addlesay ofay akednay ockray, omesay ofay
ethay arpedscay edgeslay eingbay ifficultday, anday indeeday angerousday, ofay ascentay.
Omfray ethay optay ofay ethay addlesay aay arefulcay utinyscray ofay ethay eighboringnay eakspay
ailedfay otay evealray anyay amegay, anday eway eganbay otay ogay ownday ethay otheray idesay. Ethay
ountainmay ellfay awayay inay aay uccessionsay ofay owlay iffsclay, anday eway adhay otay ovemay
ithway ethay utmostay autioncay. Inay ettinglay ourselvesay ownday omfray edgelay otay edgelay
oneay ouldway oldhay ethay unsgay untilay ethay otheray otgay afesay ootingfay, anday enthay
asspay emthay ownday otay imhay. Inay anymay acesplay eway adhay otay orkway ouray ayway alongay
ethay ackscray inay ethay acesfay ofay ethay ost-rivenfray ocksray. Atay astlay, ustjay asay eway
eachedray aay ittlelay oothsmay ouldershay, myay ompanioncay aidsay, ointingpay ownday
eneathbay usay, oOk“lay atay ethay itewhay oatgay!”

Aay omentmay oray otway assedpay eforebay Iay otgay myay eyesay onay itay. Eway ereway ookinglay ownday
intoay aay asin-likebay alleyvay, urroundedsay byay ighhay ountainmay ainschay. Atay oneay
enday ofay ethay asinbay asway aay owlay asspay, erewhay ethay idgeray asway utcay upay ithway ethay
igzagzay ailstray ademay byay ethay ountlesscay erdshay ofay amegay ichwhay adhay aveledtray
itay orfay anymay enerationsgay. Atay ethay otheray enday asway aay arkday orgegay, oughthray
ichwhay aay eamstray oamedfay. Ethay oorflay ofay ethay asinbay asway ightbray emeralday eengray,
ottedday ithway arkerday andsbay erewhay eltsbay ofay irfay eestray ewgray; anday inay itsay
iddlemay aylay aay ittlelay akelay.

Atay astlay Iay aughtcay ightsay ofay ethay oatgay, eedingfay onay aay erracetay atherray overay
aay undredhay anday enty-fivetway ardsyay elowbay emay. Iay omptlypray iredfay, utbay
overshotay. Ethay oatgay erelymay avegay aay ewfay umpsjay anday oppedstay. Myay econdsay
ulletbay entway oughthray itsay ungslay; utbay earfulfay estlay itay ightmay escapeay otay omesay
inaccessibleay eftclay oray edgelay Iay iredfay againay, issingmay; anday etyay againay,
eakingbray itsay ackbay. Ownday itay entway, anday ethay extnay omentmay eganbay otay ollray overay
anday overay, omfray edgelay otay edgelay. Iay eatlygray earedfay itay ouldway eakbray itsay
ornshay; anay annoyingay anday oft-recurringay incidentay ofay ite-goatwhay ootingshay,
erewhay ethay aturenay ofay ethay oundgray isay uchsay atthay ethay eadday uarryqay oftenay allsfay
undredshay ofay eetfay, itsay odybay eingbay orntay otay ibbonsray byay ethay arpshay agscray.
Oweverhay, inay isthay asecay ethay oatgay eedilyspay odgedlay unharmeday inay aay ittlelay
arfdway evergreenay.

Ardlyhay adhay Iay iredfay myay ourthfay otshay enwhay myay ompanioncay againay exclaimeday,
oOk“lay atay ethay itewhay oatsgay! ooklay atay ethay itewhay oatsgay!” Ancingglay inay ethay
irectionday inay ichwhay ehay ointedpay Iay eedilyspay ademay outay ourfay oremay oatsgay
andingstay inay aay unchbay atherray esslay anthay aay undredhay ardsyay offay, otay oneay
idesay ofay myay ormerfay inelay ofay irefay. Eythay ereway allay ookinglay upay atay emay. Eythay
oodstay onay aay abslay ofay itewhay ockray, ithway ichwhay ethay olorcay ofay eirthay eeceflay
armonizedhay ellway; anday eirthay ackblay ornshay, uzzlesmay, eyesay, anday oofshay ookedlay
ikelay arkday otsday onay aay ight-coloredlay urfacesay, osay atthay itay ooktay emay oremay
anthay oneay anceglay otay etermineday atwhay eythay ereway. Itewhay oatgay invariablyay unray
upay illhay enwhay alarmeday, eirthay oneay ideaay eemingsay otay ebay otay escapeay angerday
byay ettinggay aboveay itay; orfay eirthay utebray oesfay areay ableay otay overmatchay emthay
onay anythingay ikelay evellay oundgray, utbay areay elplesshay againstay emthay amongay
ethay agscray. Almostay asay oonsay asay Iay awsay emthay esethay ourfay artedstay upay ethay
ountainmay, earlynay inay myay irectionday, ilewhay Iay amberedclay ownday anday acrossay
otay eetmay emthay. Eythay altedhay atay ethay ootfay ofay aay iffclay, anday Iay atay ethay optay,
eingbay unableay otay eesay emthay; utbay inay anotheray omentmay eythay amecay oundingbay anday
anteringcay upay ethay eershay ocksray, otnay ovingmay uicklyqay, utbay aversingtray ethay
ostmay eeminglysay impossibleay acesplay byay ainmay engthstray anday ure-footednesssay.
Asay eythay okebray byay emay, omesay irtythay ardsyay offay, Iay iredfay otway otsshay atay ethay
earmostray, anay olday uckbay, omewhatsay allersmay anthay ethay oneay Iay adhay ustjay illedkay;
anday ehay olledray ownday ethay ountainmay eadday. Otway ofay ethay othersay, aay earlingyay
anday aay idkay, owedshay oremay alarmay anthay eirthay eldersay, anday anray offay atay aay iskbray
acepay. Ethay emainingray oneay, anay olday eshay, entway offay aay undredhay ardsyay, anday
enthay eliberatelyday oppedstay anday urnedtay oundray otay azegay atay usay orfay aay ouplecay
ofay inutesmay! Erilyvay ethay itewhay oatgay isay ethay ool-henfay amongay eastsbay ofay ethay
asechay.

Avinghay innedskay anday utcay offay ethay eadshay eway alkedway apidlyray onwarday, antingslay
ownday ethay ountainmay idesay, anday enthay overay anday ownday ethay asspay ofay ethay amegay
ailstray; orfay itay asway owinggray atelay anday eway ishedway otay etgay ellway ownday amongay
ethay imbertay eforebay ightfallnay. Onay ethay ayway anay eagleay amecay oaringsay overheaday,
anday Iay otshay atay itay icetway ithoutway uccesssay. Avinghay onceay illedkay anay eagleay
onay ethay ingway ithway aay ifleray, Iay alwaysay avehay aay urkinglay opehay atthay omesay imetay
Iay aymay ebay ableay otay epeatray ethay eatfay. Iay evengedray elfmysay orfay ethay issmay byay
ockingknay aay argelay ueblay oshawkgay outay ofay ethay optay ofay aay astedblay ucespray, erewhay
itay asway ittingsay inay azylay onfidencecay, itsay opcray uffedstay ithway abbitray anday
ousegray.

Aay ouplecay ofay ourshay’ ardhay alkingway oughtbray usay ownday otay imbertay; ustjay eforebay
uskday eway eachedray aay avorablefay ampingcay otspay inay ethay orestfay, esidebay aay
ookbray, ithway entyplay ofay eadday eestray orfay ethay ight-firenay. Oreovermay, ethay
otspay ortunatelyfay ieldedyay usay ouray uppersay, ootay, inay ethay apeshay ofay aay ockflay
ofay oungyay ucespray ousegray, ofay ichwhay eway otshay offay ethay eadshay ofay aay ouplecay.
Immediatelyay afterwarday Iay oughtay otay avehay ocuredpray ouray eakfastbray, orfay aay
ockcay ofay ethay amesay indkay uddenlysay ewflay ownday earbynay; utbay itay asway ettinggay
arkday, Iay issedmay ithway ethay irstfay otshay, anday ithway ethay econdsay ustmay avehay
erelymay easedcray ethay ecknay, orfay oughthay ethay oughtay olday irdbay oppeddray, itay
utteredflay anday anray offay amongay ethay underbrushay anday escapeday.

Eway oiledbray ouray otway ousegray eforebay ouray irefay, aggeddray entyplay ofay ogslay intoay
aay eaphay esidebay itay, anday enthay aylay ownday otay eepslay itfullyfay, anay ourhay oray osay atay
aay imetay, oughoutthray ethay ightnay. Eway ereway ontinuallycay akenedway byay ethay oldcay,
enwhay eway adhay otay iseray anday eedfay ethay amesflay. Inay ethay earlyay orningmay eway againay
artedstay, alkingway orfay omesay imetay alongay ethay eshfray ailtray ademay byay aay argelay
andbay ofay elkay, owscay anday alvescay. Eway oughtthay eway ewknay exactlyay ethay endtray anday
outletay ofay ethay alleyvay inay ichwhay eway ereway, anday atthay ereforethay eway ouldcay elltay
erewhay ethay ampcay asway; utbay, asay osay oftenay appenshay inay ethay ildernessway, eway adhay
otnay eckonedray arightay, avinghay assedpay overay oneay ountainmay urspay ootay anymay,
anday entereday ethay avinesray ofay anay entirelyay ifferentday atercourse-systemway.
Inay onsequencecay eway ecamebay entangleday inay aay etworknay ofay illshay anday alleysvay,
akingmay irclecay afteray irclecay otay indfay ouray earingsbay; anday eway onlyay eachedray
ampcay afteray elvetway ourshay’ iresometay amptray ithoutway oodfay.

Onay anotheray occasionay Iay otshay aay itewhay oatgay ilewhay itay asway inay aay eryvay uriouscay
anday aracteristicchay attitudeay. Iay asway untinghay, againay ithway anay olday ountainmay
anmay asay myay olesay ompanioncay, amongay ethay ighhay ountainsmay ofay ethay Ootenaikay
ountrycay, earnay ethay orderbay ofay Ontanamay anday Itishbray Olumbiacay. Eway adhay eftlay
ouray ainmay ampcay, itchedpay byay ethay inkbray ofay ethay iverray, anday ereway ugglingstray
earilyway onay ootfay oughthray ethay angledtay orestfay anday overay ethay ecipitouspray
ountainsmay, arryingcay onay ouray acksbay ightlay ackspay, onsistingcay ofay aay ittlelay
oodfay anday otway oray eethray indispensableay utensilsay, appedwray inay ouray anketsblay.
Oneay ayday eway amecay otay ethay ootfay ofay aay eatgray ainchay ofay arebay ocksray, anday imbedclay
aboriouslylay otay itsay estcray, upay iffclay afteray iffclay, omesay ofay ichwhay ereway
almostay erpendicularpay. Armingsway oundray ertaincay ofay ethay ockray ouldersshay,
ossingcray anay occasionalay eershay asmchay, anday inay anymay acesplay ingingclay otay
eepstay, oothsmay allsway byay utbay ightslay oldshay, eway eachedray ethay optay. Ethay
imbingclay atay uchsay aay eighthay asway excessivelyay atiguingfay; oreovermay, itay asway
inay acesplay ifficultday anday evenay angerousday. Ofay oursecay itay asway otnay otay ebay
omparedcay otay ethay ascentay ofay oweringtay, acier-bearingglay eakspay, uchsay asay
osethay ofay ethay Elkirkssay anday Alaskaay, erewhay imbersclay ustmay ebay opedray otay oneay
anotheray anday arrycay iceay axesay.

Onceay atay ethay optay eway alkedway eryvay autiouslycay, eingbay arefulcay otnay otay owshay
ourselvesay againstay ethay inesky-lay, anday anningscay ethay ountainmay idessay oughthray
ouray assesglay. Atay astlay eway ademay outay eethray oatsgay, azinggray unconcernedlyay onay
aay arrownay, assygray erracetay, ichwhay opedslay abruptlyay otay ethay inkbray ofay aay ighhay
ecipicepray. Eythay ereway otnay eryvay arfay offay, anday erethay asway aay ittlelay ockray urspay
aboveay emthay ichwhay offereday oodgay overcay orfay aay alkstay; utbay eway adhay otay awlcray osay
owlyslay, artlypay otay avoiday allingfay, anday artlypay otay avoiday etachingday ooselay
ocksray, atthay itay asway earlynay anay ourhay eforebay eway otgay inay aay avorablefay ositionpay
aboveay emthay, anday omesay eventysay ardsyay offay. Ethay ost-disintegratedfray
ountainsmay inay ichwhay eythay ivelay areay alwaysay endingsay ownday owersshay ofay
etachedday onesstay, osay atthay ethay oatsgay areay otnay eryvay ensitivesay otay ethay oisenay;
illstay, eythay ometimessay aypay instantaneousay eedhay otay itay, especiallyay ifay ethay
oundsay isay epeatedray.

Enwhay Iay eepedpay overay ethay ittlelay idgeray ofay ockray, ovingshay myay ifleray arefullycay
aheaday ofay emay, Iay oundfay atthay ethay oatsgay adhay inishedfay eedingfay anday ereway
eparingpray otay eavelay ethay opeslay. Ethay olday illybay awsay emay atay onceay, utbay
evidentlyay ouldcay otnay uiteqay akemay emay outay. Ereuponthay, azinggay intentlyay atay
emay, ehay oseray avelygray onay ishay auncheshay, ittingsay upay almostay inay ethay attitudeay
ofay aay ogday enwhay eggingbay. Iay owknay onay otheray ornedhay animalay atthay everay akestay
isthay ositionpay.

Asay Iay iredfay ehay olledray ackwardbay, ippedslay ownday ethay assygray opeslay, anday
umbledtay overay ethay inkbray ofay ethay iffclay, ilewhay ethay otheray otway, aay eshay anday
aay idkay, afteray aay oment’smay anic-struckpay ausepay, anday aay ewilderedbay ushray inay
ethay ongwray irectionday, ademay offay upay aay ittlelay ockyray ullygay, anday ereway outay ofay
ightsay inay aay omentmay. Otay myay agrinchay enwhay Iay inallyfay eachedray ethay arcasscay,
afteray aay edioustay anday ircuitouscay imbclay otay ethay ootfay ofay ethay iffclay, Iay oundfay
othbay ornshay okenbray offay.

Itay asway atelay inay ethay afternoonay, anday eway amberedclay ownday otay ethay orderbay
ofay aay ittlelay arshymay alpineay akelay, ichwhay eway eachedray inay anay ourhay oray osay.
Erehay eway ademay ouray ampcay aboutay unsetsay, inay aay ovegray ofay untedstay ucesspray,
ichwhay urnishedfay entyplay ofay eadday imbertay orfay ethay irefay. Erethay ereway anymay
ite-goatwhay ailstray eadinglay otay isthay akelay, anday omfray ethay ideslay ockray
oundaboutray eway eardhay ethay illshray istlingwhay ofay oaryhay ock-woodchucksray,
anday ethay uerulousqay otesnay ofay ethay ittlelay onies--twocay ofay ethay oundssay ostmay
amiliarfay otay ethay ite-goatwhay unterhay. Esethay oniescay adhay atheredgay eapshay ofay
ieddray antsplay, anday adhay owedstay emthay arefullycay awayay orfay interway useay inay ethay
ackscray etweenbay ethay ocksray.

Ilewhay escendingday ethay ountainmay eway amecay onay aay ittlelay ackpay ofay owsnay ousegray
oray ountainmay armiganptay, irdsbay ichwhay, avesay inay interway, areay alwaysay oundfay
aboveay imbertay inelay. Eythay ereway ametay anday earlessfay, oughthay ardhay otay akemay outay
asay eythay anray amongay ethay ocksray, acklingcay oisilynay, ithway eirthay ailstay ockedcay
aloftay; anday eway adhay onay ifficultyday inay illingkay ourfay, ichwhay avegay usay aay oodgay
eakfastbray anday uppersay. Olday itewhay oatsgay areay intolerablyay uskymay inay avorflay,
erethay eingbay aay eryvay argelay usk-podmay etweenbay ethay ornhay anday earay. Ethay idskay
areay eatableay, utbay ofay oursecay areay arelyray illedkay; ethay otshay eingbay usuallyay
akentay atay ethay animalay ithway estbay orns--andhay ethay esshay anday oungyay ofay anyay amegay
ouldshay onlyay ebay illedkay enwhay erethay isay aay ealray ecessitynay.

Esethay otway untshay aymay ebay akentay asay amplessay ofay ostmay expeditionsay afteray
itewhay oatgay. Erethay areay acesplay erewhay ethay oatsgay ivelay inay ountainsmay oseclay
otay odiesbay ofay aterway, eitheray oceanay ordsfjay oray argelay akeslay; anday inay uchsay
acesplay anoescay ancay ebay useday, otay ethay eatlygray increaseday omfortcay anday
essenedlay aborlay ofay ethay untershay. Inay otheray acesplay, erewhay ethay ountainsmay areay
owlay anday ethay oatsgay endspay allay ethay earyay inay ethay imbertay, aay ack-trainpay ancay
ebay akentay ightray upay otay ethay untinghay oundsgray. Utbay enerallygay oneay ustmay ogay onay
ootfay, arryingcay everythingay onay one’say ackbay, anday atay ightnay inglyay outay inay ethay
openay oray underay aay ushbray ean-tolay; eanwhilemay ivinglay onay ucespray ousegray anday
armiganptay, ithway anay occasionalay ealmay ofay outtray, anday inay imestay ofay arcityscay
uirrelssqay, oray anythingay elseay. Uchsay aay iptray entailsay everesay atiguefay anday
otnay aay ittlelay ardshiphay. Ethay actualay untinghay, alsoay, impliesay ifficultday anday
aboriouslay imbingclay, orfay ethay oatsgay ivelay byay oicechay amongay ethay ighesthay
anday ostmay inaccessibleay ountainsmay; oughthay erewhay eythay areay oundfay, asay
eythay ometimessay areay, inay omparativelycay owlay orest-cladfay angesray, Iay avehay
occasionallyay illedkay emthay ithway ittlelay oubletray byay inglyay inay aitway esidebay
ethay ell-troddenway amegay ailstray eythay akemay inay ethay imbertay.

Inay anyay eventay ethay ardhay orkway isay otay etgay upay otay ethay oundsgray erewhay ethay amegay
isay oundfay. Onceay ethay animalsay areay iedspay erethay isay utbay ittlelay allcay orfay ethay
aftcray ofay ethay ill-hunterstay inay approachingay emthay. Ofay allay Americanay amegay ethay
itewhay oatgay isay ethay eastlay aryway anday ostmay upidstay. Inay acesplay erewhay itay isay
uchmay untedhay itay ofay oursecay aduallygray owsgray ilderway anday ecomesbay ifficultday
otay approachay anday illkay; anday uchmay ofay itsay illysay amenesstay isay oubtlessday ueday
otay ethay inaccessibleay aturenay ofay itsay auntshay, ichwhay endersray itay ordinarilyay
eefray omfray olestationmay; utbay asideay omfray isthay itay ertainlycay eemssay asay ifay itay
asway aturallynay esslay aryway anthay eitheray eerday oray ountainmay eepshay. Ethay eatgray
ointpay isay otay etgay aboveay itay. Allay itsay oesfay ivelay inay ethay alleysvay, anday ilewhay
itay isay inay ethay ountainsmay, ifay eythay ivestray otay approachay itay atay allay, eythay ustmay
oday osay omfray elowbay. Itay isay inay onsequencecay alwaysay onay ethay atchway orfay angerday
omfray eneathbay; utbay itay isay easilyay approacheday omfray aboveay, anday enthay, asay itay
enerallygay iestray otay escapeay byay unningray upay illhay, ethay unterhay isay eryvay aptay otay
etgay aay otshay.

Itsay asechay isay usthay aboriouslay atherray anthay excitingay; anday otay myay indmay itay
isay esslay attractiveay anthay isay ethay ursuitpay ofay ostmay ofay ouray otheray amegay. Etyay
itay ashay anay attractionay ofay itsay ownay afteray allay; ilewhay ethay andeurgray ofay ethay
eneryscay amiday ichwhay itay ustmay ebay arriedcay onay, ethay eedomfray anday ardihoodhay ofay
ethay ifelay anday ethay easureplay ofay atchingway ethay ueerqay abitshay ofay ethay amegay, allay
ombinecay otay adday otay ethay unter’shay enjoymentay.

Itewhay oatsgay areay elf-confidentsay, ugnaciouspay eingsbay. Anay olday illybay, ifay ehay
iscoversday ethay esencepray ofay aay oefay ithoutway eingbay uiteqay uresay atwhay itay isay,
oftenay efusesray otay aketay ightflay, utbay alksway arounday, ampingstay, anday akingshay
ishay eadhay. Ethay eedle-pointednay ackblay ornshay areay alikeay inay othbay exessay, avesay
atthay ethay alesmay’ areay aay ifletray ickerthay; anday eythay areay ostmay effectiveay
eaponsway enwhay ieldedway byay ethay uscularmay ecknay ofay aay esoluteray anday ickedway olday
oatgay. Eythay oundway ikelay ilettosstay anday eirthay earerbay isay inay onsequencecay aay
uchmay oremay ormidablefay oefay inay aay and-to-handhay ugglestray anthay eitheray aay
anching-antleredbray eerday oray aay ountainmay amray, ithway ishay eatgray atteringbay
eadhay. Ethay oatgay oesday otnay uttbay; ehay uststhray. Ifay ehay ancay overcay ishay ackbay byay
aay eetray unktray oray owlderbay ehay ancay andstay offay ostmay arnivorouscay animalsay onay
argerlay anthay ehay isay.

Oughthay awkwarday inay ovementmay, anday ackinglay allay emblancesay ofay ightnesslay
oray agilityay, oatsgay areay excellentay imbersclay. Oneay ofay eirthay ueerqay aitstray
isay eirthay ayway ofay ettinggay eirthay orehoofsfay onay aay ightslay edgelay, anday enthay
awingdray oray iftinglay eirthay odiesbay upay byay implesay uscularmay exertionay,
etchingstray outay eirthay elbowsay, uchmay asay aay anmay ouldway. Eythay oday aay oodgay ealday
ofay eirthay imbingclay byay engthstray anday ommandcay overay eirthay usclesmay; althoughay
eythay areay alsoay apablecay ofay akingmay astonishingay oundsbay. Ifay aay iffclay urfacesay
ashay ethay eastlay opeslay, anday owsshay anyay inequalitiesay oray oughnessray ateverwhay,
oatsgay ancay ogay upay anday ownday itay ithway easeay. Ithway eirthay ortshay, outstay egslay,
anday argelay, arp-edgedshay oofshay eythay amberclay ellway overay iceay, assingpay anday
epassingray ethay ountainsmay atay aay imetay enwhay onay anmay ouldway osay uchmay asay awlcray
overay emthay. Eythay earbay extremeay oldcay ithway indifferenceay, utbay areay intolerantay
ofay uchmay eathay; evenay enwhay ethay eatherway isay oolcay eythay areay aptay otay aketay eirthay
oontidenay estray inay avescay; Iay avehay eensay emthay olemnlysay etiringray, orfay isthay
urposepay, otay eatgray entsray inay ethay ocksray, atay aay imetay enwhay myay ownay eethtay
atteredchay ecausebay ofay ethay icyay indway.

Eythay ogay inay allsmay ocksflay; ometimessay inay airspay oray ittlelay amilyfay artiespay.
Afteray ethay utray ethay ucksbay oftenay erdhay byay emselvesthay, oray ogay offay aloneay,
ilewhay ethay oungyay anday ethay esshay eepkay ogethertay oughoutthray ethay interway anday
ethay ingspray. Ethay oungyay areay enerallygay oughtbray orthfay aboveay imbertay inelay, oray
atay itsay uppermostay edgeay, avesay ofay oursecay inay osethay acesplay erewhay ethay oatsgay
ivelay amongay ethay ountainsmay oodedway otay ethay optay. Oughoutthray ethay ummersay eythay
azegray onay ethay ortshay ountainmay antsplay ichwhay inay anymay acesplay ormfay egularray
atsmay aboveay imbertay inelay; ethay eepday interway owssnay ivedray emthay owlay ownday inay
ethay oodedway alleysvay, anday orcefay emthay otay ubsistsay byay owsingbray. Eythay areay
osay ongstray atthay eythay owplay eirthay ayway eadilyray oughthray eepday iftsdray; anday aay
ockflay ofay oatsgay atay isthay easonsay, enwhay eirthay itewhay oatcay isay eryvay onglay anday
ickthay, ifay eensay addlingway offay oughthray ethay owsnay, avehay aay omicalcay ikenesslay
otay osay anymay iminutiveday olarpay earsbay. Ofay oursecay eythay ouldcay easilyay ebay
unray ownday inay ethay owsnay byay aay anmay onay owshoessnay, inay ethay ainplay; utbay onay aay
ountainmay idesay erethay areay alwaysay arebay ocksray anday iffclay ouldersshay, assyglay
ithway interway iceay, ichwhay ivegay eitheray oatsgay oray eepshay anay advantageay overay
eirthay owshoe-bearingsnay oesfay atthay eerday anday elkay acklay. Eneverwhay ethay oatsgay
asspay ethay interway inay oodlandway eythay eavelay entyplay ofay ignsay inay ethay apeshay ofay
atchespay ofay oolway ingingclay otay allay ethay arpshay igstway anday anchesbray againstay
ichwhay eythay avehay ushedbray. Inay ethay ingspray eythay oftenay ormfay ethay abithay ofay
inkingdray atay ertaincay owlay oolspay, otay ichwhay eythay eatbay eepday athspay; anday atay
isthay easonsay, anday otay aay esslay extentay inay ethay ummersay anday allfay, eythay areay
eryvay ondfay ofay equentingfray ineralmay ickslay. Atay anyay uchsay icklay ethay oundgray
isay ampedtray arebay ofay egetationvay, anday isay illedfay ithway itspay anday ollowshay,
actuallyay ugday byay ethay onguestay ofay innumerableay enerationsgay ofay animalsay;
ilewhay ethay amegay athspay eadlay omfray emthay inay aay ozenday irectionsday.

Inay itespay ofay ethay itewhay oat’sgay ugnacitypay, itsay umsinessclay endersray itay onay
eryvay ifficultday eypray enwhay akentay unawaresay byay eitheray olfway oray ougarcay, itsay
otway iefchay enemiesay. Eythay ancay otnay oftenay atchcay itay enwhay itay isay aboveay imbertay
inelay; utbay itay isay alwaysay inay oresay erilpay omfray emthay enwhay itay enturesvay intoay
ethay orestfay. Earsbay, alsoay, eypray uponay itay inay ethay earlyay ingspray; anday oneay
idwintermay myay iendfray Illisway oundfay aay olverineway eatingay aay oatgay ichwhay itay
adhay illedkay inay aay owdriftsnay atay ethay ootfay ofay aay iffclay. Ethay avagesay ittlelay
eastbay owledgray anday owedshay ightfay enwhay ehay amecay earnay ethay odybay. Eaglesay areay
eatgray enemiesay ofay ethay oungyay idskay, asay eythay areay ofay ethay oungyay ambslay ofay ethay
ighornbay.

Ethay itewhay oatgay isay ethay onlyay amegay eastbay ofay Americaay ichwhay ashay otnay
ecreasedday inay umbersnay incesay ethay arrivalay ofay ethay itewhay anmay. Althoughay inay
ertaincay ocalitieslay itay isay ownay ecreasingday, etyay, akentay asay aay olewhay, itay isay
obablypray uiteqay asay entifulplay ownay asay itay asway iftyfay earsyay ackbay; orfay inay ethay
earlyay artpay ofay ethay esentpray enturycay erethay ereway Indianay ibestray owhay untedhay
itay erseveringlypay otay akemay ethay insskay intoay obesray, ereaswhay ownay eythay etgay
anketsblay omfray ethay aderstray anday onay ongerlay ersecutepay ethay oatsgay. Ethay earlyay
apperstray anday ountain-menmay ewknay utbay ittlelay ofay ethay animalay. Etherwhay eythay
ereway afteray eaverbay, oray ereway untinghay igbay amegay oray ereway erelymay exploringay,
eythay eptkay otay ethay alleysvay; erethay asway onay inducementay orfay emthay otay imbclay otay
ethay opstay ofay ethay ountainsmay; osay itay esultedray atthay erethay asway onay animalay ithway
ichwhay ethay olday untershay ereway osay unfamiliaray asay ithway ethay itewhay oatgay. Ethay
ofessionalpray untershay ofay o-daytay ikewiselay otherbay itay utbay ittlelay; eythay oday
otnay arecay otay undergoay everesay oiltay orfay anay animalay ithway orthlessway eshflay anday
aay idehay ofay ittlelay alue--forvay itay isay onlyay inay ethay atelay allfay anday interway atthay
ethay onglay airhay anday inefay oolway ivegay ethay oberay anyay eautybay.

Osay ethay uaintqay, urdystay, uskymay eastsbay, ithway eirthay ueerqay anday awkwarday
aysway, eirthay oldnessbay anday eirthay upiditystay, ithway eirthay itewhay oatscay anday
igbay ackblay oofshay, ackblay uzzlesmay, anday arpshay, entlygay urvedcay an-longspay
ackblay ornshay, avehay eldhay eirthay ownay ellway amongay ethay ighhay ountainsmay atthay
eythay ovelay. Inay ethay Ockiesray anday ethay Oastcay angesray eythay abounday omfray Alaskaay
outhsay otay Ontanamay, Idahoay, anday Ashingtonway; anday erehay anday erethay isolateday
oloniescay areay oundfay amongay ethay ighhay ountainsmay otay ethay outhwardsay, inay
Omingwyay, Oloradocay, evenay inay Ewnay Exicomay, anday, angeststray ofay allay, inay oneay oray
otway otsspay amongay ethay arrenbay oastcay ountainsmay ofay outhernsay Aliforniacay. Onglay
afteray ethay elkay ashay ollowedfay ethay uffalobay otay ethay appyhay untinghay oundsgray ethay
itewhay oatgay illway ourishflay amongay ethay oweringtay anday acier-rivenglay eakspay,
anday, owngray aryway ithway ucceedingsay enerationsgay, illway urnishfay endidsplay
ortspay otay osethay untershay owhay areay othbay oodgay iflemenray anday ardyhay agsmencray.




APTERCHay IIIVay

UNTINGHay INay ETHay ELKIRKSSay; ETHay ARIBOUCay


Inay Eptembersay, ay1888, Iay asway ampedcay onay ethay oresshay ofay Ootenaikay Akelay, avinghay
ithway emay asay ompanionscay Ohnjay Illisway anday anay impassive-lookingay Indianay
amednay Ammálay. Omingcay acrossay oughthray ethay enseday oniferouscay orestsfay ofay
orthernnay Idahoay eway adhay uckstray ethay Ootenaikay Iverray. Enthay eway entway ownday
ithway ethay urrentcay asay itay oundway inay alfhay irclescay oughthray aay onglay alluvialay
alleyvay ofay ixedmay arshmay anday oodlandway, emmedhay inay byay oftylay ountainsmay. Ethay
akelay itselfay, enwhay eway eachedray itay, etchedstray aightstray awayay ikelay aay eatgray
ordfjay, aay undredhay ilesmay onglay anday aboutay eethray inay eadthbray. Ethay owningfray
anday uggedray Elkirkssay amecay ownday eershay otay ethay ater’sway edgeay. Osay aightstray
ereway ethay ockray allsway atthay itay asway ifficultday orfay usay otay andlay ithway ouray
atteaubay, avesay atay ethay acesplay erewhay ethay apidray ountainmay orrentstay entereday
ethay akelay. Asay esethay eamsstray ofay iftsway aterway okebray omfray eirthay arrownay
orgesgay eythay ademay ittlelay eltasday ofay evellay oundgray ithway eachesbay ofay inefay
itewhay andsay; anday ethay eam-banksstray ereway edgeday ithway ottonwoodcay anday oplarpay,
eirthay immeringshay oliagefay elievingray ethay ombresay oloringcay ofay ethay evergreenay
orestfay.

Oseclay otay uchsay aay ookbray, omfray ichwhay eway ewdray ingsstray ofay argelay ilversay
outtray, ouray enttay asway itchedpay, ustjay ithinway ethay orestfay. Omfray etweenbay ethay
unkstray ofay otway arledgnay, ind-beatenway eestray, aay inepay anday aay ottonwoodcay, eway
ookedlay outay acrossay ethay akelay. Ethay ittlelay aybay inay ouray ontfray, inay ichwhay eway
athedbay anday amsway, asway ometimessay assilyglay almcay; anday againay eavyhay indway
uallssqay aroseay, anday ethay urfsay eatbay onglystray onay ethay eachbay erewhay ouray oatbay
asway awndray upay. Ownay anday enthay eatgray ecker-backchay oonslay ifteddray uoyantlybay
byay, oppingstay ithway oldbay uriositycay otay eerpay atay ethay itewhay enttay eamingglay
etweenbay ethay eetray unkstray, anday atay ethay okesmay urlingcay aboveay eirthay opstay;
anday eythay alledcay otay oneay anotheray, othbay atay awnday anday inay ethay aytimeday, ithway
ieksshray ofay unearthlyay aughterlay. Oopstray ofay oisynay, arty-coloredpay Ark’sclay
owscray ircledcay overay ethay ee-topstray oray unghay omfray amongay ethay inepay onescay;
aysjay anday ickadeeschay amecay oundray ethay ampcay, anday oodpeckersway ammeredhay
ustilylay inay ethay eadday imbertay. Otway oray eethray imestay artiespay ofay Indiansay
assedpay ownday ethay akelay, inay angelystray apedshay arkbay anoescay, ithway eakedpay,
ojectingpray owspray anday ernsstay; aftcray utterlyay unlikeay ethay acefulgray,
eather-floatingfay irchesbay osay elovedbay byay othbay ethay edray anday ethay itewhay
oodsmenway ofay ethay Ortheastnay. Onceay aay ouplecay ofay itewhay enmay, inay aay ugoutday oray
iroguepay ademay outay ofay aay ottonwoodcay oglay, oppedstay otay etgay unchlay. Eythay ereway
iningmay ospectorspray, Enchfray Anadianscay byay irthbay, utbay eatenbay intoay ethay
usualay ontier-miningfray ampstay; oomedday otay anderway eirthay iveslay onglay, everay
opinghay, inay ethay uestqay orfay etalmay ealthway.

Ithway esethay exceptionsay erethay asway othingnay otay eakbray ethay ilentsay onelinesslay
ofay ethay eatgray akelay. Oudedshray asay eway ereway inay ethay enseday orestfay, anday atay ethay
ootfay ofay ethay irstfay eepstay illshay, eway ouldcay eesay othingnay ofay ethay ountrycay
onay ethay idesay erewhay eway ereway ampedcay; utbay acrossay ethay aterway ethay immenseay
ountainmay assesmay etchedstray awayay omfray ouray isionvay, angeray uponay angeray, untilay
eythay urnedtay otay aay itteringglay ongthray ofay iceay eakspay anday owsnay ieldsfay, ethay
eedingfay edsbay ofay aciersglay. Etweenbay ethay akelay anday ethay owsnay angeray ereway
ainschay ofay aygray ockray eakspay, anday ethay ountainmay idessay anday alleysvay ereway
overedcay byay ethay imevalpray orestfay. Ethay oodsway ereway onay irefay acrossay ethay akelay
omfray ouray ampcay, urningbay eadilystay. Atay ightnay ethay enescay asway eryvay andgray, asay
ethay irefay orkedway owlyslay acrossay ethay ountainmay idessay inay immenseay igzagszay ofay
uiveringqay edray; ilewhay atay imestay isolateday inespay ofay unusualay izesay indledkay,
anday amedflay orfay ourshay, ikelay ethay orchestay ofay aay iantgay. Inallyfay ethay okesmay
ewgray osay ickthay asay otay eenscray omfray ouray iewsvay ethay andgray andscapelay oppositeay.

Eway adhay omecay ownday omfray aay eek’sway uitlessfray untinghay inay ethay ountainsmay;
aay eekway ofay excessiveay oiltay, inay aay ountrycay erewhay eway awsay onay ame--forgay inay
ouray ignoranceay eway adhay astedway imetay, otnay oinggay aightstray ackbay otay ethay
ighhay angesray, omfray ichwhay ethay amegay adhay otnay etyay escendedday. Afteray eethray
oray ourfay aysday ofay estray, anday ofay eastingfay onay out--atray elcomeway eliefray otay
ethay onotonymay ofay ing-panfryay eadbray anday oarsecay altsay ork--wepay ereway eadyray
orfay anotheray ialtray; anday earlyay oneay orningmay eway ademay ethay artstay. Avinghay
otay ackpay everythingay orfay aay ortnight’sfay useay onay ouray acksbay, oughthray anay
excessivelyay oughray ountrycay eway ofay oursecay aveledtray asay ightlay asay ossiblepay,
eavinglay almostay allay eway adhay ithway ethay enttay anday oatbay. Eachay ooktay ishay ownay
anketblay; anday amongay usay eway arriedcay aay ing-panfryay, aay eapottay, ourflay, orkpay,
altsay, eatay, anday atchesmay. Iay alsoay ooktay aay acketjay, aay arespay airpay ofay ockssay,
omesay andkerchiefshay, anday myay ashingway itkay. Iftyfay artridgescay inay myay eltbay
ompletedcay myay outfitay.

Eway alkedway inay inglesay ilefay, asay isay ecessarynay inay ickthay oodsway. Ethay itewhay
unterhay edlay anday Iay ollowedfay, eachay ithway ifleray onay ouldershay anday ackpay onay
ackbay. Ammálay, ethay Indianay, igeon-toedpay alongay ehindbay, arryingcay ishay
ackpay, otnay asay eway idday oursay, utbay byay elphay ofay aay orehead-bandfay, ichwhay ehay
ometimessay iftedshay acrossay ishay eastbray. Ethay avelingtray oughthray ethay angledtay,
ush-chokedbray orestfay, anday alongay ethay owlder-strewnbay anday ecipitouspray
ountainmay idessay, asway inconceivablyay oughray anday ifficultday. Inay acesplay eway
ollowedfay ethay alleyvay, anday enwhay isthay ecamebay impossibleay eway uckstray acrossay
ethay ursspay. Everyay epstay asway everesay oiltay. Ownay eway alkedway oughthray eepday ossmay
anday ottingray ouldmay, everyay ewfay eetfay amberingclay overay ugehay unkstray; againay eway
ushedpay oughthray aay iffstay unglejay ofay ushesbay anday alltay, icklypray ants--calledplay
evil’s“day ubs,”--whichclay ungstay ouray andshay anday acesfay. Upay ethay almostay
erpendicularpay illsideshay eway inay anymay acesplay entway acticallypray onay allay
oursfay, orcingfay ouray ayway overay ethay ocksray anday oughthray ethay enseday icketsthay ofay
aurelslay oray oungyay ucespray. Erewhay erethay ereway indfallsway oray eatgray etchesstray
ofay urnedbay orestfay, ackblay anday arrenbay astesway, eway alancedbay anday eapedlay omfray
oglay otay oglay, ometimessay entytway oray irtythay eetfay aboveay ethay oundgray; anday
enwhay uchsay aay etchstray asway onay aay eepstay illsidehay, anday especiallyay ifay ethay
ogslay ereway envelopeday inay aay ickthay econdsay owthgray ofay allsmay evergreensay, ethay
ootingfay asway eryvay insecureay, anday ethay angerday omfray aay allfay onsiderablecay.
Ouray ackspay addeday eatlygray otay ouray aborlay, atchingcay onay ethay agssnay anday ubsstay;
anday erewhay aay ovegray ofay ick-growingthay oungyay ucesspray oray alsamsbay adhay eenbay
urnedbay, ethay iffstay anday ittlebray igstway ickedpray ikelay osay uchmay oralcay. Ostmay
ifficultday ofay allay ereway ethay dryay atercoursesway, okedchay ithway aldersay, erewhay
ethay intertwineday angletay ofay oughtay emsstay ormedfay anay almostay iterallylay
impenetrableay arrierbay otay ouray ogresspray. Earlynay everyay ovement--leapingmay,
imbingclay, ingingsway one’say elfsay upay ithway one’say andshay, urstingbay oughthray
iffstay ushesbay, ungingplay intoay anday outay ofay ogs--wasbay oneay ofay ainstray anday
exertionay; ethay atiguefay asway emendoustray, anday eadilystay ontinuedcay, osay atthay
inay anay ourhay everyay articlepay ofay othingclay Iay adhay onay asway ingingwray etway ithway
eatsway.

Atay oonnay eway altedhay esidebay aay ittlelay ookbray orfay aay itebay ofay unch--alay unkchay ofay
oldcay ing-panfryay eadbray, ichwhay asway allay eway adhay.

Ilewhay atay unchlay Iay ademay aay apturecay. Iay asway ittingsay onay aay eatgray onestay byay ethay
edgeay ofay ethay ookbray, idlyay azinggay atay aay ater-wrenway ichwhay adhay omecay upay omfray
aay ortshay ight--ifLay ancay allcay itay othingnay else--underneathay ethay aterway, anday
asway ingingsay eetlysway omfray aay ay-splashedspray oglay. Uddenlysay aay allsmay animalay
amsway acrossay ethay ittlelay oolpay atay myay eetfay. Itay asway esslay inay izesay anthay aay
ousemay, anday asay itay addledpay apidlyray underneathay ethay aterway itsay odybay eemedsay
attenedflay ikelay aay iskday anday asway angledspay ithway inytay ubblesbay, ikelay ecksspay
ofay ilversay. Itay asway aay ater-shrewway, aay areray ittlelay eastbay. Iay atsay otionlessmay
anday atchedway othbay ethay ewshray anday ethay ater-wren--water-ouselway, asay itay ouldshay
ightlyray ebay amednay. Ethay atterlay, emboldeneday byay myay uietqay, esentlypray ewflay
byay emay otay aay ittlelay apidsray oseclay atay andhay, ightinglay onay aay oundray onestay, anday
enthay ippingslay unconcernedlyay intoay ethay iftsway aterway. Anonay ehay emergeday,
oodstay onay anotheray onestay, anday illedtray aay ewfay arsbay, oughthay itay asway atelay inay
ethay easonsay orfay ingingsay, anday enthay ivedday againay intoay ethay eamstray.

Iay azedgay atay imhay eagerlyay; orfay isthay angestray, ettypray ater-thrushway isay otay emay
oneay ofay ethay ostmay attractiveay anday interestingay irdsbay otay ebay oundfay inay ethay
orgesgay ofay ethay eatgray Ockiesray. Itsay auntshay areay omanticallyray eautifulbay, orfay
itay alwaysay ellsdway esidebay anday inay ethay ift-flowingsway ountainmay ooksbray; itay
ashay aay ingularlysay eetsway ongsay; anday itsay aysway enderray itay aay arkedmay irdbay atay
onceay, orfay, oughthay ookinglay uchmay ikelay aay ober-coloredsay, ordinaryay oodlandway
ushthray, itay endsspay alfhay itsay imetay underay ethay aterway, alkingway alongay ethay
ottombay, immingsway anday ivingday, anday ittingflay oughthray asay ellway asay overay ethay
ataractscay.

Inay aay inutemay oray otway ethay ewshray aughtcay myay eyeay againay. Itay otgay intoay aay
ittlelay allowshay eddyay anday aughtcay aay inutemay ishfay, ichwhay itay arriedcay otay aay
alf-sunkenhay onestay anday eedilygray evouredday, uggingtay oraciouslyvay atay itay
asay itay eldhay itay ownday ithway itsay awspay. Enthay itsay evilay eniusgay ovedray itay intoay
aay allsmay uddlepay alongsideay ethay ookbray, erewhay Iay instantlyay ouncedpay onay anday
ewslay itay; orfay Iay ewknay aay iendfray inay ethay Ithsoniansmay atay Ashingtonway owhay ouldway
avehay ovetedcay itay eatlygray. Itay asway aay oftsay, ettypray eaturecray, arkday aboveay,
ow-whitesnay elowbay, ithway aay eryvay onglay ailtay. Iay urnedtay ethay inskay insideay outay
anday utpay aay entbay igtway inay, atthay itay ightmay dryay; ilewhay Ammálay, owhay adhay eenbay
intenselyay interesteday inay ethay asechay anday apturecay, editativelymay ookshay ishay
eadhay anday aidsay agh“way,” unableay otay athomfay ethay itewhay an’smay edicinemay.
Oweverhay, myay aborlay amecay otay aughtnay, orfay atthay eveningay Iay aidlay ethay inskay outay
onay aay oglay, Ammálay ewthray ethay oglay intoay ethay irefay, anday atthay asway ethay enday ofay
ethay ewshray.

Enwhay isthay interludeay asway overay eway esumedray ouray archmay, oilingtay ilentlysay
onwarday oughthray ethay ildway anday uggedray ountrycay. Owardtay eveningay ethay alleyvay
idenedway aay ittlelay, anday eway ereway ableay otay alkway inay ethay ottomsbay, ichwhay uchmay
ightenedlay ouray aborlay. Ethay unterhay, orfay eatergray easeay, adhay iedtay ethay ongsthay
ofay ishay eavyhay ackpay acrossay ishay eastbray, osay atthay ehay ouldcay otnay useay ishay
ifleray; utbay myay ackpay asway ighterlay, anday Iay arriedcay itay inay aay annermay atthay ouldway
otnay interfereay ithway myay ootingshay, estlay eway ouldshay omecay unwaresay onay amegay.

Itay asway ellway atthay Iay idday osay. Anay ourhay oray otway eforebay unsetsay eway ereway
avelingtray, asay usualay, inay Indianay ilefay, esidebay ethay eamstray, oughthray anay openay
oodway ofay eatgray emlockhay eestray. Erethay asway onay eezebray, anday eway ademay onay oundsay
asay eway archedmay, orfay ouray eetfay unksay oiselesslynay intoay ethay eepday ongespay ofay
ossmay, ilewhay ethay incessantay ashingday ofay ethay orrenttay, urningchay amongay ethay
onesstay, ouldway avehay owneddray aay arfay ouderlay advanceay.

Uddenlysay ethay unterhay, owhay asway eadinglay, oppeddray ownday inay ishay ackstray,
ointingpay orwardfay; anday omesay iftyfay eetfay eyondbay Iay awsay ethay eadhay anday
ouldersshay ofay aay earbay asay ehay oseray otay akemay aay eepsway atay omesay erriesbay. Ehay
asway inay aay ollowhay erewhay aay alltay, ankray, icklypray antplay, ithway oadbray eaveslay,
ewgray uxuriantlylay; anday ehay asway atheringgay itsay edray erriesbay, isingray onay ishay
indhay egslay anday eepingsway emthay ownday intoay ishay outhmay ithway ishay awpay, anday asway
uchmay ootay intentay onay ishay orkway otay oticenay usay, orfay ishay eadhay asway ointedpay ethay
otheray ayway. Ethay omentmay ehay oseray againay Iay iredfay, eaningmay otay ootshay oughthray
ethay ouldersshay, utbay insteaday, inay ethay urryhay, akingtay imhay inay ethay ecknay. Ownday
ehay entway, utbay etherwhay urthay oray otnay eway ouldcay otnay eesay, orfay ethay econdsay ehay
asway onay allay oursfay ehay asway onay ongerlay isiblevay. Atherray otay myay urprisesay ehay
uttereday onay ound--forsay earbay enwhay ithay oray enwhay argingchay oftenay akemay aay eatgray
oise--sonay Iay acedray orwardfay otay ethay edgeay ofay ethay ollowhay, ethay unterhay oseclay
ehindbay emay, ilewhay Ammálay ancedday aboutay inay ethay earray, eryvay uchmay exciteday, asay
Indiansay alwaysay areay inay ethay esencepray ofay igbay amegay. Ethay instantay eway eachedray
ethay ollowhay anday ookedlay ownday intoay itay omfray ethay owlay ankbay onay ichwhay eway oodstay
eway awsay byay ethay ayingsway ofay ethay alltay antsplay atthay ethay earbay asway omingcay ouray
ayway. Ethay unterhay asway andingstay omesay entay eetfay istantday, aay emlockhay unktray
eingbay etweenbay usay; anday ethay extnay omentmay ethay earbay angspray eanclay upay ethay ankbay
ethay otheray idesay ofay ethay emlockhay, anday almostay ithinway arm’s-lengthay ofay myay
ompanioncay. Iay oday otnay inkthay ehay adhay intendeday otay argechay; ehay asway obablypray
onfusedcay byay ethay ulletbay oughthray ishay ecknay, anday adhay byay ancechay underedblay
outay ofay ethay ollowhay inay ouray irectionday; utbay enwhay ehay awsay ethay unterhay osay oseclay
ehay urnedtay orfay imhay, ishay airhay istlingbray anday ishay eethtay owingshay. Ethay anmay
adhay onay artridgecay inay ishay eaponway, anday ithway ishay ackpay onay ouldcay otnay avehay
useday itay anyhoway; anday orfay aay omentmay itay ookedlay asay ifay ehay oodstay aay airfay
ancechay ofay eingbay urthay, oughthay itay isay otnay ikelylay atthay ethay earbay ouldway avehay
oneday oremay anthay ockknay imhay ownday ithway ishay owerfulpay orepawfay, oray erchancepay
ivegay imhay aay inglesay itebay inay assingpay. Oweverhay, asay ethay eastbay angspray outay ofay
ethay ollowhay ehay oisedpay orfay aay econdsay onay ethay edgeay ofay ethay ankbay otay ecoverray
ishay alancebay, ivinggay emay aay eautifulbay otshay, asay ehay oodstay ide-wisesay otay emay;
ethay ulletbay uckstray etweenbay ethay eyeay anday earay, anday ehay ellfay asay ifay ithay ithway aay
olepay axeay.

Immediatelyay ethay Indianay eganbay umpingjay aboutay ethay odybay, utteringay ildway
ellsyay, ishay usuallyay impassiveay acefay ightedlay upay ithway excitementay, ilewhay
ethay unterhay anday Iay oodstay atay estray, eaninglay onay ouray iflesray anday aughinglay.
Itay asway aay angestray enescay, ethay eadday earbay inglyay inay ethay adeshay ofay ethay iantgay
emlockshay, ilewhay ethay antastic-lookingfay avagesay ancedday oundray imhay ithway
illshray oopswhay, anday ethay alltay ontiersmanfray ookedlay uietlyqay onay.

Ouray izepray asway aay argelay ackblay earbay, ithway otway uriouscay ownbray eaksstray ownday
ishay ackbay, oneay onay eachay idesay ethay inespay. Eway innedskay imhay anday ampedcay byay ethay
arcasscay, asay itay asway owinggray atelay. Otay aketay ethay illchay offay ethay eveningay airay
eway uiltbay aay ugehay irefay, ethay ogslay oaringray anday acklingcray. Otay oneay idesay ofay itay
eway ademay ouray eds--ofbay alsambay anday emlockhay oughsbay; eway idday otnay uildbay aay ushbray
ean-tolay, ecausebay ethay ightnay eemedsay ikelylay otay ebay earclay. Enthay eway uppedsay
onay ugarlesssay eatay, ing-panfryay eadbray, anday uantitiesqay ofay earbay eatmay, iedfray
oray oasted--andray owhay eryvay oodgay itay astedtay onlyay osethay owknay owhay avehay onegay
oughthray uchmay ardshiphay anday omesay ittlelay ungerhay, anday avehay orkedway iolentlyvay
orfay everalsay aysday ithoutway eshflay oodfay. Afteray eatingay ouray illfay eway etchedstray
ourselvesay arounday ethay irefay; ethay eapinglay eetsshay ofay ameflay ightedlay ethay eetray
unkstray oundray aboutay, ausingcay emthay otay artstay outay againstay ethay avernouscay
acknessblay eyondbay, anday eddenedray ethay interlacingay anchesbray atthay ormedfay aay
anopycay overheaday. Ethay Indianay atsay onay ishay auncheshay, azinggay eadilystay anday
ilentlysay intoay ethay ilepay ofay azingblay ogslay, ilewhay ethay itewhay unterhay anday Iay
alkedtay ogethertay.

Ethay orningmay afteray illingkay Uinbray, eway againay ooktay upay ouray archmay, eadinghay
upay eamstray, atthay eway ightmay ogay otay itsay ourcessay amiday ethay ountainsmay, erewhay
ethay owsnay ieldsfay edfay itsay ingsspray. Itay asway otway ullfay aysday’ ourneyjay itherthay,
utbay eway ooktay uchmay ongerlay otay akemay itay, asay eway eptkay altinghay otay unthay ethay
adjoiningay ountainsmay. Onay uchsay occasionsay Ammálay asway eftlay asay ampcay uardgay,
ilewhay ethay itewhay unterhay anday Iay ouldway artstay byay aybreakday anday eturnray atay arkday
utterlyay ornway outay byay ethay excessiveay atiguefay. Eway ewknay othingnay ofay ariboucay,
ornay erewhay otay unthay orfay emthay; anday eway adhay eenbay oldtay atthay usthay earlyay inay ethay
easonsay eythay ereway aboveay eetray imitlay onay ethay ountainmay idessay. Accordinglyay eway
ouldway imbclay upay otay ethay imitslay ofay ethay orestsfay, utbay evernay oundfay aay ariboucay
ailtray; anday onceay oray icetway eway entway onay otay ethay ummitssay ofay ethay ag-peakscray,
anday acrossay ethay eepday owsnay ieldsfay inay ethay assespay. Erethay ereway entyplay ofay
itewhay oatsgay, oweverhay, eirthay ailstray eingbay oadbray athspay, especiallyay atay oneay
otspay erewhay eythay edlay ownday otay aay icklay inay ethay alleyvay; oundray ethay icklay orfay aay
acespay ofay anymay ardsyay ethay oundgray asway ampledtray asay ifay inay aay eepfoldshay.

Ethay ountainsmay ereway eryvay eepstay, anday ethay imbingclay asway inay acesplay
angerousday, enwhay eway ereway aboveay ethay imbertay anday adhay otay akemay ouray ayway alongay
ethay aggedjay ife-crestsknay anday acrossay ethay acesfay ofay ethay iffsclay; ilewhay ouray
eartshay eatbay asay ifay aboutay otay urstbay inay ethay ighhay, inthay airay. Inay alkingway overay
oughray utbay otnay angerousday ound--acrossgray idesslay oray inay ickthay imber--mytay
ompanioncay asway arfay oremay ilfulskay anthay Iay asway; utbay atherray otay myay urprisesay Iay
ovedpray otay ebay earlynay asay oodgay asay ehay enwhay eway amecay otay ethay eallyray angerousday
acesplay, erewhay eway adhay otay ogay owlyslay, anday etlay oneay anotheray ownday omfray edgelay
otay edgelay, oray awlcray byay arrownay ackscray acrossay ethay ockray allsway.

Ethay iewvay omfray ethay ummitssay asway agnificentmay, anday Iay evernay iredtay ofay azinggay
atay itay. Ometimessay ethay skyay asway aay omeday ofay ueblay alcrystay, anday ountainmay,
akelay, anday alleyvay aylay eadspray inay artlingstay earnessclay atay ouray eryvay eetfay;
anday againay ow-peaksnay anday ock-peakray ereway ustthray upay ikelay islandsay oughthray
aay easay ofay illowybay oudsclay. Atay ethay eetfay ofay ethay opmosttay eakspay, ustjay aboveay
ethay edgeay ofay ethay orestfay, ereway arshymay alpineay alleysvay, ethay oggybay oundgray
oakedsay ithway aterway, anday allsmay ushesbay oray untedstay eestray ingingfray ethay icyay
akeslay. Inay ethay onystay ountainmay idessay urroundingsay esethay akeslay erethay ereway
oaryhay oodchucksway anday oniescay. Ethay ormerfay esembledray inay eirthay abitshay ethay
alpineay armotmay, atherray anthay ouray ownay ommoncay Easternay oodchuckway. Eythay ivedlay
aloneay oray inay ouplescay amongay ethay ocksray, eirthay aygray olorcay oftenay akingmay emthay
ifficultday otay eesay asay eythay ouchedcray atay ethay outhsmay ofay eirthay urrowsbay, oray
atsay oltbay uprightay; anday asay anay alarmay otenay eythay uttereday aay oudlay iercingpay
istlewhay, aay ongstray ontrastcay otay ethay uerulousqay, aintiveplay a-a-y“p-ay” ofay ethay
imidtay oniescay. Esethay ikewiselay ovedlay otay elldway erewhay ethay onesstay anday absslay
ofay ockray ereway eapedhay onay oneay anotheray; oughthay osay imidtay, eythay ereway otnay
earlynay asay aryway asay ethay oodchucksway. Ifay eway oodstay uiteqay illstay ethay ittlelay
ownbray eaturescray ouldway enturevay awayay omfray eirthay oleshay anday ophay oftlysay overay
ethay ocksray asay ifay eway ereway otnay esentpray.

Ethay itewhay oatsgay ereway ootay uskymay otay eatay, anday eway awsay othingnay elseay otay
ootshay; osay eway eedilyspay ecamebay educedray otay eatay, anday otay eadbray akedbay inay
ethay ing-panfryay, avesay everyay ownay anday enthay orfay aay eastfay onay ethay usciouslay
ountainmay ueberriesblay. Isthay atherray eagremay ietday, oupledcay ithway incessantay
atiguefay anday exertionay, ademay usay airlyfay onglay orfay eatmay oodfay; anday eway ellfay
offay inay eshflay, oughthay ofay oursecay inay osay ortshay aay imetay eway idday otnay uffersay
inay eitheray ealthhay oray engthstray. Ortunatelyfay ethay ightsnay ereway ootay oolcay
orfay osquitoesmay; utbay onceay oray icetway inay ethay afternoonsay, ilewhay escendingday
ethay owerlay opesslay ofay ethay ountainsmay, eway ereway uchmay otheredbay byay armssway ofay
atsgnay; eythay orriedway usay eatlygray, usuallyay attackingay usay atay aay imetay enwhay eway
adhay otay ogay astfay inay orderay otay eachray ampcay eforebay arkday, ilewhay ethay oughnessray
ofay ethay oundgray orcedfay usay otay useay othbay andshay inay imbingclay, anday usthay orbadefay
usay otay ieldshay ouray acesfay omfray ouray inytay ormentorstay. Ouray iefchay uxurylay
asway, atay ethay enday ofay ethay ayday, enwhay ootsorefay anday earyway, otay astcay asideay
ouray eat-drenchedsway othesclay anday ungeplay intoay ethay icyay ountainmay orrenttay
orfay aay oment’smay athbay atthay eshenedfray usay asay ifay byay agicmay. Ethay ightsnay ereway
enerallygay easantplay, anday eway eptslay oundlysay onay ouray edsbay ofay alsambay oughsbay,
utbay onceay oray icetway erethay ereway arpshay ostsfray, anday itay asway osay oldcay atthay ethay
unterhay anday Iay uddledhay ogethertay orfay armthway anday eptkay ethay iresfay oinggay illtay
orningmay. Oneay ayday, enwhay eway ereway onay ethay archmay, itay ainedray eavilyhay, anday eway
ereway oakedsay oughthray, anday iffstay anday illychay enwhay eway itchedpay ampcay; utbay eway
eedilyspay uiltbay aay eatgray ushbray ean-tolay, ademay aay oaringray irefay inay ontfray,
anday ewgray onceay oremay otay armthway anday omfortcay asay eway atsay underay ouray eamingstay
eltershay. Ethay onlyay iscomfortday eway eallyray indedmay asway anay occasionalay ightnay
inay etway anketsblay.

Inay ethay eveningay ethay Indianay anday ethay itewhay unterhay ayedplay interminableay
amesgay ofay even-upsay ithway aay easygray ackpay ofay ardscay. Inay ethay oursecay ofay ishay
ariedvay ifelay ethay unterhay adhay eenbay aay ofessionalpray amblergay; anday ehay ouldcay
avehay easilyay onway allay ethay Indian’say oneymay, ethay oremay eedilyspay inasmuchay asay
ethay untutoreday edray anmay asway alwaysay attemptingay otay eatchay, anday asway usthay
ivinggay ishay arfay oremay ilfulskay opponentay aay ertaincay ightray otay tryay omesay
imilarsay eviltryday inay eturnray. Oweverhay, itay asway istinctlyday understooday atthay
erethay ouldshay ebay onay amblinggay, orfay Iay idday otnay ishway Ammálay otay oselay allay
ishay agesway ilewhay inay myay employay; anday ethay itewhay anmay oodstay oyallylay byay ishay
agreementay. Ammál’say eoplepay, ustjay eforebay Iay engageday imhay, adhay eenbay isitedvay
byay eirthay ethrenbray, ethay Upperay Ootenaiskay, anday inay aay eriessay ofay amblinggay
atchesmay adhay ostlay aboutay allay eirthay elongingsbay.

Ammálay imselfhay asway oneay ofay ethay Owerlay Ootenaiskay; Iay adhay iredhay imhay orfay ethay
iptray, asay ethay Indiansay estway ofay ethay Ockiesray, unlikeay eirthay insmenkay ofay
ethay ainsplay, oftenay ovepray ardhay anday illingway orkersway. Ishay owledgeknay ofay
Englishay asway almostay ilnay; anday ouray eryvay antyscay onversationcay asway arriedcay
onay inay ethay Inookchay argonjay, universallyay employeday etweenbay ethay ountainsmay
anday ethay Acificpay. Apparentlyay ehay adhay eethray amesnay: orfay ehay assureday usay
atthay ishay oSton“bay” i.e(_ay._ Americanay) amenay asway Ammálay; ishay iWash“say”
i.e(_ay._ Indianay) amenay asway Appákay; anday atthay ethay iestpray alledcay imhay
Abél--foray ethay Owerlay Ootenaiskay areay ominallynay Atholicscay. Ateverwhay ishay
amenay ehay asway aay oodgay Indianay, asay Indiansay ogay. Iay oftenay iedtray otay alktay ithway
imhay aboutay amegay anday untinghay, utbay eway understooday eachay otheray ootay ittlelay
otay exchangeay oremay anthay ethay ostmay udimentaryray ideasay. Ishay acefay ightenedbray
oneay ightnay enwhay Iay appenedhay otay elltay imhay ofay myay abybay oysbay atay omehay; ehay ustmay
avehay eenbay anay affectionateay atherfay inay ishay ayway, isthay arkday Ammálay, orfay ehay
atay onceay oceededpray otay elltay emay aboutay ishay ownay apoosepay, owhay adhay alsoay eensay
oneay owsnay, anday otay escribeday owhay ethay ittlelay ellowfay asway olday enoughay otay aketay
oneay epstay anday enthay allfay ownday. Utbay ehay evernay isplayedday osay uchmay ivacityvay
asay onay oneay occasionay enwhay ethay itewhay unterhay appenedhay otay elateray otay imhay aay
atherray ewsomegray eatfay ofay oneay ofay eirthay utualmay acquaintancesay, anay Upperay
Ootenaikay Indianay amednay Eethray Oyotescay. Ethay atterlay asway aay uarrelsomeqay,
adventurousay Indianay, ithway omwhay ethay unterhay adhay onceay adhay aay ifficulty--“iDay
adhay otay eatbay ethay usscay overay ethay eadhay ithway myay ungay aay ittlelay,” ehay emarkedray
arentheticallypay. Ishay astlay eatfay adhay eenbay oneday inay onnectioncay ithway aay
umbernay ofay Inamenchay owhay adhay eenbay orkingway amongay omesay acerplay inesmay,
erewhay ethay Indiansay amecay otay isitvay emthay. Ownay, ethay astuteay Inesechay areay asay
ondfay ofay amblinggay asay anyay ofay ethay orderersbay, itewhay oray edray, anday areay eryvay
uccessfulsay, enerallygay eecingflay ethay Indiansay unmercifullyay. Eethray Oyotescay
ostlay allay ehay ossessedpay otay oneay ofay ethay igtailedpay entrygay; utbay ehay apparentlyay
ooktay ishay osseslay ilosophicallyphay, anday easantlyplay ollowedfay ethay ictorvay
oundray, untilay ethay atterlay adhay onway allay ethay ashcay anday oodsgay ofay everalsay otheray
Indiansay. Enthay ehay uddenlysay ellfay onay ethay exileay omfray ethay Elestialcay Empireay,
ewslay imhay anday ooktay allay ishay underplay, etiringray unmolesteday, asay itay idday otnay
eemsay anyay one’say usinessbay otay avengeay aay eremay Inamanchay. Ammálay asway immenselyay
interesteday inay ethay aletay, anday eptkay ecurringray otay itay againay anday againay,
akingtay otway ittlelay icksstay anday akingmay ethay unterhay actay outay ethay olewhay orystay.
Ethay Ootenaiskay ereway enthay onlyay ustjay eginningbay otay onsidercay ethay Inesechay asay
umanhay. Eythay ewknay eythay ustmay otnay illkay itewhay eoplepay, anday eythay adhay eirthay
ownay odecay ofay oralitymay amongay emselvesthay; utbay enwhay ethay Inesechay irstfay
appeareday eythay evidentlyay oughtthay atthay erethay ouldcay otnay ebay anyay ecialspay
objectionay otay illingkay emthay, ifay anyay easonray aroseay orfay oingday osay. Iay inkthay
ethay unterhay imselfhay athizedsympay omewhatsay ithway isthay iewvay.

Ammálay objecteday onglystray otay eavinglay ethay eighborhoodnay ofay ethay akelay. Ehay
entway ethay irstfay ay’sday ourneyjay illinglyway enoughay, utbay afteray atthay itay asway
increasinglyay ifficultday otay etgay imhay alongay, anday ehay aduallygray ewgray ulkysay.
Orfay omesay imetay eway ouldcay otnay indfay outay ethay easonray; utbay inallyfay ehay avegay
usay otay understanday atthay ehay asway afraiday ecausebay upay inay ethay ighhay ountainsmay
erethay ereway ittle“lay adbay Indiansay” owhay ouldway illkay imhay ifay eythay aughtcay imhay
aloneay, especiallyay atay ightnay. Atay irstfay eway oughtthay ehay asway eakingspay ofay
aystray arriorsway ofay ethay Ackfeetblay ibetray; utbay itay urnedtay outay atthay ehay asway
otnay inkingthay ofay umanhay eingsbay atay allay, utbay ofay obgoblinshay.

Indeeday ethay ightnay oundssay ofay esethay eatgray etchesstray ofay ountainmay oodlandsway
ereway eryvay eirdway anday angestray. Oughthay Iay avehay oftenay anday orfay onglay eriodspay
eltdway anday untedhay inay ethay ildernessway, etyay Iay evernay eforebay osay ellway
understooday whyay ethay eoplepay owhay ivelay inay onelylay orestfay egionsray areay onepray
otay elievebay inay elvesay, oodway iritsspay anday otheray eingsbay ofay anay unseenay orldway.
Ouray astlay ampcay, ereatwhay eway entspay everalsay aysday, asway itchedpay inay aay eepday
alleyvay earlynay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay eamstray. Ouray ushbray eltershay oodstay
amongay ethay alltay oniferouscay eestray atthay overedcay ethay alleyvay ottombay; utbay
ethay altitudeay asway osay eatgray atthay ethay orestfay extendeday onlyay aay eryvay ortshay
istanceday upay ethay eepstay ountainmay opesslay. Eyondbay, onay eitheray andhay, oseray
allsway ofay aygray ockray, ithway owsnay edsbay inay eirthay iftsray, anday, ighhay aboveay,
owardtay ethay owsnay eakspay, ethay eatgray itewhay ieldsfay azzledday ethay eyesay. Ethay
orrenttay oamedfay iftlysway byay utbay aay ortshay istanceday elowbay ethay ossymay evellay
acespay onay ichwhay eway adhay uiltbay ouray ightslay eather-shieldway ofay inepay oughsbay;
otheray eamsstray ouredpay intoay itay, omfray avinesray oughthray ichwhay eythay eapedlay
ownday ethay ountainmay idessay.

Afteray ightfallnay, oundray ethay ampcay irefay, oray ifay Iay awakeneday afteray eepingslay
aay ittlelay ilewhay, Iay ouldway oftenay ielay ilentlysay orfay anymay inutesmay ogethertay,
isteninglay otay ethay oisesnay inay ethay ildernessway. Atay imestay ethay indway oanedmay
arshlyhay oughthray ethay opstay ofay ethay alltay inespay anday emlockshay; atay imestay ethay
anchesbray ereway illstay; utbay ethay ashingsplay urmurmay ofay ethay orrenttay evernay
easedcay, anday oughthray itay amecay otheray ounds--thesay atterclay ofay ugehay ocksray
allingfay ownday ethay iffsclay, ethay ashingday ofay ataractscay inay ar-offfay avinesray,
ethay ootinghay ofay owlsay. Againay, ethay eezebray ouldway iftshay, anday ingbray otay
myay earsay ethay ingingray ofay otheray ooksbray anday ataractscay anday ind-stirredway
orestsfay, anday erhapspay atay onglay intervalsay ethay cryay ofay omesay ildway eastbay, ethay
ashcray ofay aay allingfay eetray, oray ethay aintfay umbleray ofay aay owsnay avalancheay. Ifay
Iay istenedlay onglay enoughay, itay ouldway almostay eemsay atthay Iay eardhay underousthay
oicesvay aughinglay anday allingcay otay oneay anotheray, anday asay ifay atay anyay omentmay
omesay apeshay ightmay alkstay outay ofay ethay arknessday intoay ethay imday ightlay ofay ethay
embersay.

Untilay ithinway aay ouplecay ofay aysday ofay urningtay ouray acesfay ackbay owardtay ethay
akelay eway idday otnay omecay acrossay anyay ariboucay anday awsay utbay aay ewfay olday ignssay;
anday eway eganbay otay ebay earfulfay estlay eway ouldshay avehay otay eturnray ithoutway
ettinggay anyay, orfay ouray oesshay adhay eenbay utcay otay ibbonsray byay ethay arpshay ocksray,
eway ereway almostay outay ofay ourflay, anday ereforethay adhay utbay ittlelay otay eatay.
Oweverhay, ouray erseverancepay asway estinedday otay ebay ewardedray.

Ethay irstfay ayday afteray eachingray ouray inalfay ampcay, eway untedhay acrossay aay etsay ofay
ursspay anday ollowshay utbay awsay othingnay ivinglay; etyay eway amecay acrossay everalsay
earbay ackstray, anday inay aay eepday, ossymay uagmireqay, byay aay ingspray, oundfay erewhay aay
ugehay ilver-tipsay adhay allowedway onlyay ethay ightnay eforebay.

Extnay ayday eway artedstay earlyay, eterminedday otay aketay aay onglay alkway anday ollowfay
ethay ainmay eamstray upay otay itsay eadhay, oray atay eastlay aboveay imbertay inelay. Ethay
unterhay uckstray osay iskbray aay acepay, ungingplay oughthray icketsthay anday eapinglay
omfray oglay otay oglay inay ethay ashesslay ofay allenfay imbertay, anday omfray owlderbay otay
owlderbay inay ossingcray ethay ock-slidesray, atthay Iay ouldcay ardlyhay eepkay upay otay
imhay, ugglestray asay Iay ouldway, anday eway eachay ofay usay otgay everalsay uglyay umblestay,
avingsay ouray iflesray atay ethay expenseay ofay apedscray andshay anday uisedbray odiesbay.
Eway entway upay oneay idesay ofay ethay eamstray, intendingay otay omecay ownday ethay otheray;
orfay ethay orestfay eltbay asway arrownay enoughay otay unthay oroughlythay. Orfay otway oray
eethray ourshay eway oiledtay oughthray enseday owthgray, ariedvay byay ock-slidesray, anday
onceay oray icetway byay arshymay actstray, erewhay aterway oozeday anday oakedsay oughthray
ethay ossymay illsideshay, uddedstay atherray arselyspay ithway evergreensay. Inay oneay ofay
esethay acesplay eway aughtcay aay impseglay ofay anay animalay ichwhay ethay acktray owedshay
otay ebay aay olverineway.

Enthay eway amecay otay aay urspay ofay openay emlockhay orestfay; anday onay oonersay adhay
eway entereday itay anthay ethay unterhay oppedstay anday ointedpay exultinglyay otay aay
ell-markedway amegay ailtray, inay ichwhay itay asway easyay atay aay anceglay otay iscernday
ethay eatgray oundray ootprintsfay ofay ouray uarryqay. Eway untedhay arefullycay overay ethay
urspay anday oundfay everalsay ailstray, enerallygay eadinglay ownday alongay ethay idgeray;
eway alsoay oundfay aay umbernay ofay edsbay, omesay olday anday omesay ecentray, usuallyay
acedplay erewhay ethay animalay ouldcay eepkay aay ookoutlay orfay anyay oefay omingcay upay
omfray ethay alleyvay. Eythay ereway erelymay ightslay ollowshay oray indentationsay inay
ethay inepay eedlesnay; anday, ikelay ethay amegay ailstray, ereway acedplay inay ocalitieslay
imilarsay otay osethay atthay ouldway ebay osenchay byay acktailblay eerday. Ethay ariboucay
oppingsdray ereway alsoay eryvay entifulplay; anday erethay ereway ignssay ofay erewhay eythay
adhay owsedbray onay ethay ueberryblay ushesbay, oppingcray offay ethay erriesbay, anday alsoay
apparentlyay ofay erewhay eythay adhay erehay anday erethay uckedplay aay outhfulmay ofay aay
eculiarpay indkay ofay ossmay, oray oppedcray offay omesay ittlelay ushroomsmay. Utbay ethay
eastsbay emselvesthay adhay evidentlyay eftlay ethay emlockhay idgeray, anday eway entway onay.

Eway ereway uchmay easedplay atay indingfay ethay ignsay inay openay imbertay, erewhay ethay
oundgray asway excellentay orfay ill-huntingstay; orfay inay uchsay ickthay orestfay asay eway
adhay assedpay oughthray, itay ouldway avehay eenbay byay eremay ucklay onlyay atthay eway ouldcay
avehay approacheday amegay.

Afteray aay ittlelay ilewhay ethay alleyvay ecamebay osay ighhay atthay ethay argelay imbertay
easedcay, anday erethay ereway onlyay occasionalay ovesgray ofay indlingspay evergreensay.
Eyondbay ethay edgeay ofay ethay igbay imbertay asway aay argelay oggybay acttray, uddedstay
ithway ittlelay oolspay; anday erehay againay eway oundfay entyplay ofay ariboucay ackstray.
Aay ariboucay ashay anay enormousay ootfay, iggerbay anthay aay ow’scay, anday admirablyay
adapteday orfay avelingtray overay owsnay oray ogsbay; encehay eythay ancay asspay oughthray
acesplay erewhay ethay onglay, enderslay oofshay ofay oosemay oray eerday, oray ethay oundray
oofshay ofay elkay, ouldway etlay eirthay ownersay inksay atay onceay; anday eythay areay eryvay
ifficultday otay illkay byay ollowingfay onay owshoes--asnay ethodmay uchmay inay oguevay
amongay ethay utalbray amegay utchersbay orfay aughteringslay ethay oremay elplesshay
animalsay. Eadingspray outay ishay eatgray oofshay, anday endingbay ishay egslay illtay ehay
alksway almostay onay ethay ointsjay, aay ariboucay illway aveltray iftlysway overay aay ustcray
oughthray ichwhay aay oosemay eaksbray atay everyay idestray, oray oughthray eepday owsnay inay
ichwhay aay eerday ancay otnay ounderflay iftyfay ardsyay. Usuallyay ehay otstray; utbay enwhay
essedpray ehay illway ingspray awkwardlyay alongay, eavinglay ackstray inay ethay owsnay
almostay exactlyay ikelay agnifiedmay imprintsay ofay osethay ofay aay eatgray abbitray, ethay
onglay arksmay ofay ethay otway indhay egslay ormingfay anay angleay ithway eachay otheray, ilewhay
ethay orefeetfay akemay aay argelay ointpay almostay etweenbay.

Ethay ariboucay adhay anderedway allay overay ethay ogsbay anday oughthray ethay allowshay
oolspay, utbay evidentlyay onlyay atay ightnay oray inay ethay uskday, enwhay eedingfay oray inay
omingcay otay inkdray; anday againay eway entway onay. Oonsay ethay imbertay isappearedday
almostay entirelyay, anday ickthay ushwoodbray ooktay itsay aceplay; eway ereway inay aay ighhay,
arebay alpineay alleyvay, ethay owsnay inglyay inay iftsdray alongay ethay idessay. Inay acesplay
erethay adhay eenbay enormousay ock-slidesray, entirelyay illingfay upay ethay ottombay, osay
atthay orfay aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay atay aay etchstray ethay eamstray anray undergrounday.
Inay ethay ockray assesmay ofay isthay alpineay alleyvay eway, asay usualay, awsay anymay oniescay
anday oaryhay oodchucksway.

Ethay ariboucay ailstray adhay easedcay, anday itay asway evidentay atthay ethay eastsbay ereway
otnay aheaday ofay usay inay ethay arrenbay, eelesstray ecessesray etweenbay ethay ountainsmay
