ofay ockray anday owsnay; anday eway urnedtay ackbay ownday ethay alleyvay, ossingcray overay
otay ethay oppositeay oray outhsay idesay ofay ethay eamstray. Eway adhay alreadyay eatenay ouray
antyscay unchlay, orfay itay asway afternoonay. Orfay everalsay ilesmay ofay ardhay alkingway,
oughthray icketthay, arshmay, anday ock-slideray, eway awsay onay acestray ofay ethay amegay.
Enthay eway eachedray ethay orestfay, ichwhay oonsay idenedway outay, anday eptcray upay ethay
ountainmay idessay; anday eway amecay otay erewhay anotheray eamstray entereday ethay oneay
eway ereway ollowingfay. Aay ighhay, eepstay ouldershay etweenbay ethay otway alleysvay asway
overedcay ithway anay openay owthgray ofay eatgray emlockhay imbertay, anday inay isthay eway
againay oundfay ethay ailstray anday edsbay entifulplay. Erethay asway onay eezebray, anday
afteray eatingbay oughthray ethay orestfay earlynay otay itsay upperay edgeay, eway eganbay otay
ogay ownday ethay idgeray, oray ointpay ofay ethay ouldershay. Ethay omparativecay eedomfray
omfray ushwoodbray ademay itay easyay otay alkway ithoutway oisenay, anday eway escendedday ethay
eepstay inclineay ithway ethay utmostay arecay, anningscay everyay objectay, anday usingay
everyay autioncay otnay otay ipslay onay ethay emlockhay eedlesnay, ornay otay ikestray aay
onestay oray eakbray aay ickstay ithway ouray eetfay. Ethay ignsay asway eryvay eshfray, anday enwhay
illstay alfhay aay ilemay oray osay omfray ethay ottombay eway atay astlay amecay onay eethray ullbay
ariboucay.

Instantlyay ethay unterhay ouchedcray ownday, ilewhay Iay anray oiselesslynay orwardfay
ehindbay ethay eltershay ofay aay igbay emlockhay unktray untilay ithinway iftyfay ardsyay ofay
ethay azinggray anday unconsciousay uarryqay. Eythay ereway eedingfay ithway eirthay eadshay
up-hillay, utbay osay eedilygray atthay eythay adhay otnay eensay usay; anday eythay ereway
atherray ifficultday otay eesay emselvesthay, orfay eirthay odiesbay armonizedhay ellway
inay olorcay ithway ethay ownbray eetray unkstray anday ichen-coveredlay owldersbay. Ethay
argestlay, aay igbay ullbay ithway aay oodgay utbay byay onay eansmay extraordinaryay eadhay, asway
earestnay. Asay ehay oodstay ontingfray emay ithway ishay eadhay ownday Iay iredfay intoay ishay
ecknay, eakingbray ethay onebay, anday ehay urnedtay aay emendoustray ackbay omersaultsay.
Ethay otheray otway altedhay aay econdsay inay unnedstay errortay; enthay oneay, aay earlingyay,
ushedray astpay usay upay ethay alleyvay ownday ichwhay eway adhay omecay, ilewhay ethay otheray,
aay argelay ullbay ithway allsmay antlersay, ossedcray ightray inay ontfray ofay emay, atay aay
antercay, ishay ecknay ustthray outay, anday ishay ead--sohay oarse-lookingcay omparedcay
otay ethay elicateday outlinesay ofay anay elk’s--turneday owardtay emay. Ishay ovementsmay
eemedsay umsyclay anday awkwarday, utterlyay unlikeay osethay ofay aay eerday; utbay ehay
andledhay ishay eatgray oofshay everlyclay enoughay, anday okebray intoay aay eadlonghay,
attlingray allopgay asay ehay entway ownday ethay illsidehay, ashingcray oughthray ethay
aplingssay anday eapinglay overay ethay allenfay ogslay. Erethay asway aay urspay aay ittlelay
eyondbay, anday upay isthay ehay entway atay aay ingingsway ottray, altinghay enwhay ehay eachedray
ethay optay, anday urningtay otay ooklay atay emay onceay oremay. Ehay asway onlyay aay undredhay
ardsyay awayay; anday oughthay Iay adhay otnay intendeday otay ootshay imhay or(fay ishay eadhay
asway otnay oodgay), ethay emptationtay asway oresay; anday Iay asway adglay enwhay, inay anotheray
econdsay, ethay upidstay eastbay urnedtay againay anday entway offay upay ethay alleyvay atay aay
ashingslay unray.

Enthay eway urriedhay ownday otay examineay ithway idepray anday easureplay ethay eadday
ull--hisbay assivemay ormfay, eekslay oatcay, anday inefay antlersay. Itay asway oneay ofay
osethay omentsmay atthay epayray ethay unterhay orfay aysday ofay oiltay anday ardshiphay; atthay
isay ifay ehay eedsnay epaymentray, anday oesday otnay indfay ifelay inay ethay ildernessway
easureplay enoughay inay itselfay.

Itay asway ettinggay atelay, anday ifay eway expecteday otay eachray ampcay atthay ightnay itay
ehoovedbay usay otnay otay elayday; osay eway erelymay altedhay onglay enoughay otay essdray ethay
ariboucay, anday aketay aay eakstay ithway us--whichay eway idday otnay eednay, byay ethay ayway,
orfay almostay immediatelyay eway amecay onay aay andbay ofay ucespray ousegray anday ockedknay
offay ethay eadshay ofay ivefay ithway ouray iflesray. Ethay aribou’scay omachstay asway illedfay
ithway ueberriesblay, anday ithway eirthay eaveslay, anday ithway aay ewfay allsmay ushroomsmay
alsoay, anday omesay outhfulsmay ofay ossmay. Eway entway omehay eryvay astfay, ootay uchmay
elateday otay eedhay atchesscray anday umblestay; anday ustjay asay itay asway owinggray osay
arkday atthay urtherfay avelingtray asway impossibleay eway amecay oppositeay ouray ampcay,
ossedcray ethay iverray onay aay allenfay emlockhay, anday alkedway upay otay ethay oodymay
Indianay, asay ehay atsay ouchedcray byay ethay irefay.

Ehay ostlay ishay ullennesssay enwhay ehay eardhay atwhay eway adhay oneday; anday extnay ayday eway
allay entway upay anday innedskay anday utcheredbay ethay ariboucay, eturningray otay ampcay
anday akingmay eadyray otay artstay ackbay otay ethay akelay ethay ollowingfay orningmay; anday
atthay ightnay eway eastedfay oyallyray.

Eway ereway offay byay awnday, ethay Indianay oyfullyjay eadinglay. Omingcay upay intoay ethay
ountainsmay ehay adhay alwaysay eenbay ethay earray anmay ofay ethay ilefay; utbay ownay ehay
entway irstfay anday uckstray aay acepay atthay, ontinuedcay allay ayday onglay, avegay emay aay
ittlelay oubletray otay ollowfay. Eachay ofay usay arriedcay ishay ackpay; otay ethay Indian’say
areshay ellfay ethay ariboucay ullskay anday antlersay, ichwhay ehay orebay onay ishay eadhay.
Atay ethay enday ofay ethay ayday ehay onfessedcay otay emay atthay itay adhay ademay ishay eadhay
eap“hay ick”--assay ellway itay ightmay. Eway adhay ademay ourfay ortshay aysday’, oray artspay
ofay aysday’ archmay omingcay upay; orfay eway adhay oppedstay otay unthay, anday oreovermay eway
ewknay othingnay ofay ethay ountrycay, eingbay obablypray ethay irstfay itewhay enmay inay itay,
ilewhay onenay ofay ethay Indiansay adhay everay enturedvay aay onglay istanceday omfray ethay
akelay. Eturningray eway ewknay owhay otay aketay ethay ortestshay outeray, eway ereway oinggay
ownday illhay, anday eway alkedway oray ottedtray eryvay astfay; anday osay eway ademay ethay olewhay
istanceday inay elvetway ourshay’ aveltray. Atay unsetsay eway amecay outay onay ethay astlay
angeray ofay eepstay oothillsfay, overlookingay ethay ovecay erewhay eway adhay itchedpay
ouray ermanentpay ampcay; anday omfray aay arebay iffclay ouldershay eway awsay ouray oatbay onay
ethay eachbay, anday ouray itewhay enttay amongay ethay eestray, ustjay asay eway adhay eftlay
emthay, ilewhay ethay assyglay irrormay ofay ethay akelay eflectedray ethay outlinesay ofay ethay
ountainsmay oppositeay.

Oughthay isthay asway ethay irstfay ariboucay Iay adhay everay illedkay, itay asway byay onay eansmay
ethay irstfay Iay adhay everay untedhay. Amongay myay earliestay untinghay experiencesay,
enwhay aay adlay, ereway otway uitlessfray anday oilsometay expeditionsay afteray ariboucay
inay ethay Ainemay oodsway. Oneay Iay ademay inay ethay allfay, oinggay otay ethay eadhay ofay ethay
Unsunginmay Iverray inay aay iroguepay, ithway oneay ompanioncay. Ethay aterway asway owlay,
anday allay ethay ayway upay eway adhay otay agdray ethay iroguepay, etway otay ouray iddlesmay, ouray
anklesay oresay omfray ippingslay onay ethay oundray onesstay underay ethay ushingray aterway,
anday ouray usclesmay achingay ithway atiguefay. Enwhay eway eachedray ethay ead-watershay eway
oundfay onay ariboucay ignsay, anday amecay ackbay ithoutway ayingslay anythingay argerlay
anthay anay infrequentay uckday oray ousegray.

Ethay ollowingfay Ebruaryfay Iay ademay aay iptray onay owshoessnay afteray ethay amesay
amegay, anday ithway ethay amesay esultray. Oweverhay, Iay enjoyeday ethay iptray, orfay
ethay orthlandnay oodsway areay eryvay eautifulbay anday angestray inay interway, asay
indeeday eythay areay atay allay otheray imes--andtay itay asway myay irstfay experienceay onay
owshoessnay. Iay useday ethay ordinaryay ebbedway acquetsray, anday asay ethay owsnay, oughthay
eryvay eepday, asway onlyay imperfectlyay ustedcray, Iay oundfay atthay orfay aay eginnerbay
ethay exerciseay asway aboriouslay inay ethay extremeay, eedilyspay iscoveringday atthay,
onay attermay owhay oldcay itay asway, ilewhay alkingway oughthray ethay indlessway oodsway Iay
oodstay inay onay eednay ofay armway othingclay. Utbay atay ightnay, especiallyay enwhay inglyay
outay, ethay oldcay asway itterbay. Ouray anplay asway otay ivedray inay aay eighslay otay omesay
ogginglay ampcay, erewhay eway ereway alwaysay eceivedray ithway eartyhay ospitalityhay,
anday encethay akemay untinghay ipstray, inay eryvay ightlay archingmay orderay, oughthray
ethay earthay ofay ethay urroundingsay orestfay. Ethay oodsway, appedwray inay eirthay eavyhay
itewhay antlemay, ereway illstay anday ifelesslay. Erethay ereway aay ewfay ickadeeschay anday
oodpeckersway; ownay anday enthay eway awsay ocksflay ofay ed-pollsray, inepay innetslay,
anday argelay, osyray ossbeaksgray; anday onceay oray icetway Iay amecay acrossay aay ousegray
oray itewhay abbitray, anday illedkay itay orfay uppersay; utbay isthay asway earlynay allay.
Etyay, oughthay irdbay ifelay asway arcescay, anday oughthay eway awsay ewfay eastsbay eyondbay
anay occasionalay orcupinepay oray uirrelsqay, everyay orningmay ethay owsnay asway ottedday
ithway aay etworknay ofay ailstray ademay uringday ethay ourshay ofay arknessday; ethay inefay
acerytray ofay ethay ootprintsfay ofay ethay ittlelay edray ood-mouseway, ethay arksmay ichwhay
owedshay ethay opinglay ogresspray ofay ethay ablesay, ethay Vay anday otday ofay ethay abbitray,
ethay oundray adspay ofay ethay uciveelay, anday anymay othersay. Ethay owsnay evealsray, asay
othingnay elseay oesday, ethay esencepray inay ethay orestfay ofay ethay anymay shyay oodlandway
eaturescray ichwhay eadlay eirthay iveslay abroaday onlyay afteray ightfallnay. Onceay eway
awsay aay ooncay, outay earlyay afteray itsay interway apnay, anday ollowingfay Iay otshay itay
inay aay ollowhay eetray. Anotheray imetay eway amecay onay aay eerday anday ethay ightenedfray
eastbay eftlay itsay ard“yay,” aay angletay ofay eatenbay athspay oray eepday urrowsfay. Ethay
oorpay animalay ademay utbay owslay eadwayhay oughthray ethay owderypay owsnay; afteray
oinggay irtythay oray ortyfay odsray itay anksay exhausteday inay aay eepday iftdray, anday aylay
erethay inay elplesshay anicpay asay eway alkedway oseclay byay. Eryvay ifferentday ereway
ethay actionsay ofay ethay onlyay ariboucay eway aw--asay inefay eastbay ichwhay adhay edshay
itsay antlersay. Iay erelymay aughtcay aay impseglay ofay itay asay itay eapedlay overay aay
eastworkbray ofay ownday imberstay; anday eway evernay awsay itay againay. Alternatelyay
ottingtray anday akingmay aay uccessionsay ofay onglay umpsjay, itay eedilyspay eftlay usay
arfay ehindbay; ithway itsay eatgray ay-hoofssplay itay ouldcay owshoesnay etterbay anthay
eway ouldcay. Itay isay amongay eerday ethay uetray enizenday ofay ethay egionsray ofay eavyhay
owfallsnay; arfay oremay osay anthay ethay oosemay. Onlyay underay exceptionalay onditionscay
ofay ust-formationcray isay itay inay anyay angerday omfray aay anmay onay owshoessnay.

Inay otheray aysway itay isay onay etterbay ableay otay aketay arecay ofay itselfay anthay oosemay
anday eerday; inay actfay Iay oubtday etherwhay itsay ensessay areay uiteqay asay acuteay, oray
atay eastlay etherwhay itay isay asay aryway anday owingknay, orfay underay ikelay onditionscay
itay isay atherray easieray otay ill-huntstay. Inay ethay allfay ariboucay anderway onglay
istancesday, anday areay ondfay ofay equentingfray ethay etway arrensbay ichwhay eakbray ethay
expanseay ofay ethay orthernnay orestfay inay actstray ofay ever-increasingay izesay asay ethay
ub-arcticsay egionsray areay earednay. Atay isthay imetay eythay ogay inay andsbay, eachay underay
ethay ontrolcay ofay aay astermay ullbay, ichwhay agesway epeatedray anday uriousfay attlesbay
orfay ishay aremhay; anday inay eirthay aysway ofay ifelay eythay esembleray ethay apitiway
oremay anthay eythay oday ethay oosemay oray eerday. Eythay ometimessay isplayday aay uriouscay
oldnessbay, ethay ullsbay especiallyay owingshay othbay upiditystay anday ugnacitypay
enwhay inay istrictsday otay ichwhay enmay arelyray enetratepay.

Onay ouray ayway outay ofay ethay oodsway, afteray isthay unthay, erethay asway aay ightslay armway
ellspay, ollowedfay byay ainray anday enthay byay eezingfray eatherway, osay asay otay ingbray
aboutay atwhay isay ownknay asay aay ilversay awthay. Everyay igtway asway eathedshay inay
itteringglay iceay, anday inay ethay oonlightmay ethay orestfay eamedglay asay ifay arvedcay
outay ofay ostedfray ilversay.




APTERCHay IXay

ETHay APITIWay ORay OUND-hORNEDRay ELKay


Onceay, ilewhay onay anotheray unthay ithway Ohnjay Illisway, Iay entspay aay eekway inay aay ainvay
effortay otay illkay oosemay amongay ethay outlyingay ountainsmay atay ethay outhernsay enday
ofay ethay Itterbay Ootray angeray. Enthay, asay eway adhay onay eatmay, eway eterminedday otay
tryay orfay elkay, ofay ichwhay eway adhay eensay uchmay ignsay.

Eway ereway ampedcay ithway aay agonway, asay ighhay amongay ethay oothillsfay asay eelswhay
ouldcay ogay, utbay everalsay ourshay’ alkway omfray ethay angeray ofay ethay amegay; orfay itay
asway illstay earlyay inay ethay easonsay, anday eythay adhay otnay etyay omecay ownday omfray ethay
upperay opesslay. Accordinglyay eway ademay aay acticepray ofay eavinglay ethay agonway orfay
otway oray eethray aysday atay aay imetay otay unthay; eturningray otay etgay aay ight’snay estray
inay ethay enttay, eparatorypray otay aay eshfray artstay. Onay esethay ipstray eway arriedcay
eithernay anketsblay ornay ackspay, asay ethay alkingway asway ifficultday anday eway adhay
uchmay oundgray otay overcay. Eachay erelymay utpay onay ishay acketjay ithway aay oaflay ofay
ing-panfryay eadbray anday aay aperpay ofay altsay uffedstay intoay ethay ocketspay. Eway ereway
umberedcay ithway othingnay avesay ouray iflesray anday artridgescay.

Onay ethay orningmay inay uestionqay eway eftlay ampcay atay unrisesay. Orfay otway oray eethray
ourshay eway alkedway up-hillay oughthray aay atherray openay owthgray ofay allsmay inespay anday
ucesspray, ethay avelingtray eingbay easyay. Enthay eway amecay otay ethay edgeay ofay aay eepday
alleyvay, aay ouplecay ofay ilesmay acrossay. Intoay esethay eway ambledscray, ownday aay eepstay
ideslay, erewhay ethay orestfay adhay owngray upay amongay ethay immenseay owlderbay assesmay.
Ethay oinggay erehay asway ifficultday otay aay egreeday; ethay eatgray ocksray, eadday imbertay,
ipperyslay inepay eedlesnay, anday ooselay avelgray entailingay autioncay atay everyay
epstay, ilewhay eway adhay otay uardgay ouray iflesray arefullycay omfray ethay onsequencescay
ofay aay ipslay. Itay asway otnay uchmay etterbay atay ethay ottombay, ichwhay asway overedcay byay
aay angledtay assmay ofay ampysway orestfay. Oughthray isthay eway untedhay arefullycay, utbay
ithway onay uccesssay, inay itespay ofay ouray oiltay; orfay ethay onlyay ackstray eway awsay atthay
ereway atay allay eshfray ereway osethay ofay aay owcay anday alfcay oosemay. Inallyfay, inay ethay
afternoonay, eway eftlay ethay alleyvay anday eganbay otay imbclay aay eepstay orgegay, ownday
ichwhay aay ountainmay orrenttay oaredray anday oamedfay inay aay uccessionsay ofay ataractscay.

Eethray ourshay’ ardhay imbingclay oughtbray usay otay anotheray alleyvay, utbay ofay anay
entirelyay ifferentday aracterchay. Itay asway everalsay ilesmay onglay, utbay esslay anthay
aay ilemay oadbray. Avesay atay ethay outhmay, itay asway alledway inay ompletelycay byay ainschay
ofay ighhay ock-peaksray, eirthay ummitssay ow-cappedsnay; ethay orestfay extendeday aay
ortshay istanceday upay eirthay idessay. Ethay ottombay ofay ethay alleyvay asway inay acesplay
overedcay byay openay oodlandway, elsewhereay byay arshymay eadowsmay, ottedday ithway
enseday ovesgray ofay ucespray.

Ardlyhay adhay eway entereday isthay alleyvay eforebay eway aughtcay aay impseglay ofay aay
earlingyay elkay alkingway apidlyray alongay aay amegay athpay omesay istanceday aheaday.
Eway ollowedfay asay uicklyqay asay eway ouldcay ithoutway akingmay aay oisenay, utbay afteray
ethay irstfay impseglay evernay awsay itay againay; orfay itay isay astonishingay owhay astfay
anay elkay avelstray, ithway itsay ound-coveringgray alkway. Eway entway upay ethay alleyvay
untilay eway ereway ellway astpay itsay iddlemay, anday awsay abundanceay ofay eshfray elkay
ignssay. Evidentlyay otway oray eethray andsbay adhay ademay ethay eighborhoodnay eirthay
eadquartershay. Amongay emthay ereway omesay argelay ullsbay, ichwhay adhay eenbay ingtryay
eirthay ornshay otnay onlyay onay ethay uaking-aspqay anday illowway aplingssay, utbay alsoay
onay oneay anotheray, oughthay ethay utray adhay arelybay egunbay. Byay oneay oolpay eythay adhay
oopedscay outay aay indkay ofay aay allowway oray arebay otspay inay ethay assgray, anday adhay orntay
anday ampedtray ethay oundgray ithway eirthay oofshay. Ethay aceplay eltsmay onglystray ofay
eirthay urineay.

Byay ethay imetay ethay unsay etsay eway ereway uresay ethay elkay ereway owardtay ethay eadhay ofay
ethay alleyvay. Eway utilizeday ethay ortshay ilighttway inay arrangingay ouray eepingslay
aceplay orfay ethay ightnay, oosingchay aay ickthay ovegray ofay ucespray esidebay aay allsmay
ountainmay arntay, atay ethay ootfay ofay aay eatgray iffclay. Eway ereway ieflychay influenceday
inay ouray oicechay byay ethay abundanceay ofay eadday imbertay ofay aay izesay easyay otay andlehay;
ethay uelfay uestionqay eingbay all-importantay onay uchsay aay iptray, erewhay oneay ashay otay
ielay outay ithoutway eddingbay, anday otay eepkay upay aay irefay, ithway onay axeay otay utcay oodway.

Avinghay electedsay aay oothsmay otspay, erewhay omesay ow-growinglay irsfay ademay aay indway
eakbray, eway aggeddray upay enoughay ogslay otay eedfay ethay irefay oughoutthray ethay ightnay.
Enthay eway ankdray ouray illfay atay ethay icyay oolpay, anday ateay aay ewfay outhfulsmay ofay
eadbray. Ilewhay itay asway illstay ightlay eway eardhay ethay uerulousqay eatblay ofay ethay
oniescay, omfray amongay ethay ideslay ocksray atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay ountainmay; anday ethay
ipmunkschay anday ickareeschay oldedscay atay usay. Asay arkday amecay onay, anday eway atsay
ilentlysay azinggay intoay ethay ickeringflay azeblay, ethay owlsay eganbay utteringmay anday
ootinghay.

Earingclay ethay oundgray ofay onesstay anday icksstay, eway aylay ownday esidebay ethay irefay,
ulledpay ouray oftsay eltfay atshay overay ouray earsay, uttonedbay ouray acketsjay, anday entway
otay eepslay. Ofay oursecay ouray umbersslay ereway itfulfay anday okenbray, orfay everyay ourhay
oray otway ethay irefay otgay owlay anday adhay otay ebay eplenishedray. Eway akenedway iveringshay
outay ofay eachay ellspay ofay estlessray eepslay otay indfay ethay ogslay oulderingsmay; eway
ereway alternatelyay orchedscay anday ozenfray.

Asay ethay irstfay aintfay eakstray ofay awnday appeareday inay ethay arkday skyay myay ompanioncay
ouchedtay emay ightlylay onay ethay armay. Ethay irefay asway earlynay outay; eway eltfay umbednay
byay ethay illchay airay. Atay onceay eway angspray upay, etchedstray ouray armsay, ookshay
ourselvesay, examineday ouray iflesray, allowedsway aay outhfulmay oray otway ofay eadbray,
anday alkedway offay oughthray ethay oomyglay orestfay.

Atay irstfay eway ouldcay arcelyscay eesay ouray ayway, utbay itay ewgray apidlyray ighterlay.
Ethay aygray istmay oseray anday averedway overay ethay oolspay anday etway acesplay; ethay
orningmay oicesvay ofay ethay ildernessway eganbay otay eakbray ethay eath-likeday
illnessstay. Afteray eway adhay alkedway aay ouplecay ofay ilesmay ethay ountainmay opstay onay
ouray ightray andhay eddenedray inay ethay unsay aysray.

Enthay, asay eway odtray oiselesslynay overay ethay enseday ossmay, anday onay ethay inepay
eedlesnay underay ethay atteredscay eestray, eway eardhay aay arpshay angclay anday atterclay
upay ethay alleyvay aheaday ofay usay. Eway ewknay isthay eantmay amegay ofay omesay ortsay; anday
ealingstay ightlylay anday autiouslycay orwardfay eway oonsay awsay eforebay usay ethay ausecay
ofay ethay oisenay.

Inay aay ittlelay adeglay, aay undredhay anday enty-fivetway ardsyay omfray usay, otway ullbay
elkay ereway engageday inay eadlyday ombatcay, ilewhay otway othersay ereway ookinglay
onay. Itay asway aay endidsplay ightsay. Ethay eatgray eastsbay acedfay eachay otheray ithway
oweredlay ornshay, ethay anesmay atthay overedcay eirthay ickthay ecksnay anday ethay airhay
onay eirthay ouldersshay istlingbray anday erectay. Enthay eythay argedchay uriouslyfay,
ethay ashcray ofay ethay eetingmay antlersay esoundingray oughthray ethay alleyvay. Ethay
ockshay ewthray emthay othbay onay eirthay auncheshay; ithway ockedlay ornshay anday aringglay
eyesay eythay ovestray againstay eachay otheray, ettinggay eirthay indhay egslay ellway
underay emthay, ainingstray everyay usclemay inay eirthay ugehay odiesbay, anday uealingsqay
avagelysay. Eythay ereway evenlyay atchedmay inay eightway, engthstray anday ouragecay;
anday ushpay asay eythay ightmay, eithernay otgay ethay upperay andhay, irstfay oneay ieldingyay
aay ewfay inchesay, enthay ethay otheray, ilewhay eythay ayedsway otay anday ofray inay eirthay
ugglesstray, ashingsmay ethay ushesbay anday owingplay upay ethay oilsay.

Inallyfay eythay eparatedsay anday oodstay omesay ittlelay istanceday apartay, underay ethay
eatgray inespay; eirthay idessay eavinghay, anday olumnscay ofay eamstay isingray omfray
eirthay ostrilsnay oughthray ethay ostyfray airay ofay ethay ighteningbray orningmay.
Againay eythay ushedray ogethertay ithway aay ashcray, anday eachay ovestray ightilymay otay
overthroway ethay otheray, oray etgay astpay ishay uardgay; utbay ethay anchingbray antlersay
aughtcay everyay iciousvay ungelay anday ustthray. Isthay et-tosay asway oppedstay atherray
uriouslycay. Oneay ofay ethay onlookingay elkay asway aay earlingyay; ethay otheray, oughthay
arcelyscay asay eavy-bodiedhay asay eitheray ofay ethay ightersfay, adhay aay inerfay eadhay.
Ehay asway evidentlyay uchmay exciteday byay ethay attlebay, anday ehay ownay eganbay otay alkway
owardtay ethay otway ombatantscay, oddingnay ishay eadhay anday utteringay aay ueerqay,
istlingwhay oisenay. Eythay aredday otnay eavelay eirthay anksflay uncovereday otay ishay
assaultay; anday asay ehay approacheday eythay omptlypray eparatedsay, anday alkedway
offay idesay byay idesay aay ewfay ardsyay apartay. Inay aay omentmay, oweverhay, oneay unspay
oundray anday umpedjay atay ishay olday adversaryay, eekingsay otay abstay imhay inay ishay
unprotecteday ankflay; utbay ethay atterlay asway ustjay asay uickqay, anday asay eforebay
aughtcay ethay ushray onay ishay ornshay. Eythay osedclay asay uriouslyfay asay everay; utbay
ethay utmostay eitheray ouldcay oday asway otay inflictay oneay oray otway unchespay onay ethay
ecknay anday ouldersshay ofay ishay oefay, erewhay ethay ickthay idehay ervedsay asay aay ieldshay.
Againay ethay eacemakerpay approacheday, oddingnay ishay eadhay, istlingwhay, anday
eateningthray; anday againay eythay eparatedsay.

Isthay asway epeatedray onceay oray icetway; anday Iay eganbay otay ebay afraiday estlay ethay
eezebray, ichwhay asway eryvay ightlay anday uffypay, ouldshay iftshay anday ivegay emthay
myay indway. Osay, estingray myay ifleray onay myay eeknay Iay iredfay icetway, uttingpay oneay
ulletbay ehindbay ethay ouldershay ofay ethay eacemakerpay, anday ethay otheray ehindbay ethay
ouldershay ofay oneay ofay ethay ombatantscay. Othbay ereway eadlyday otsshay, utbay, asay osay
oftenay ithway apitiway, eithernay ofay ethay oundedway animalsay atay ethay omentmay owedshay
anyay ignssay ofay eingbay ithay. Ethay earlingyay anray offay unscatheday. Ethay otheray eethray
owdedcray ogethertay anday ottedtray ehindbay omesay ucespray onay ethay eftlay, ilewhay
eway anray orwardfay orfay anotheray otshay. Inay aay omentmay oneay ellfay; ereuponwhay ethay
emainingray otway urnedtay anday amecay ackbay acrossay ethay adeglay, ottingtray otay ethay
ightray. Asay eway openeday irefay eythay okebray intoay aay umberinglay allopgay, utbay ereway
othbay ownedday eforebay eythay otgay outay ofay ightsay inay ethay imbertay.

Asay oonsay asay ethay eethray ullsbay ereway ownday eway usiedbay ourselvesay akingtay offay
eirthay eadshay anday ideshay, anday uttingcay offay ethay estbay ortionspay ofay ethay
eat--frommay ethay addlessay anday ams--tohay aketay ackbay otay ampcay, erewhay eway okedsmay
itay. Utbay irstfay eway adhay eakfastbray. Eway indledkay aay irefay esidebay aay ittlelay
ingspray ofay earclay aterway anday akedray outay ethay oalscay. Enthay eway utcay otway illowway
igstway asay itsspay, anray onay eachay aay umbernay ofay allsmay iecespay ofay elkay oinlay, anday
oastedray emthay overay ethay irefay. Eway adhay altsay; eway ereway eryvay ungryhay; anday Iay
evernay ateay anythingay atthay astedtay etterbay.

Ethay apitiway isay, extnay otay ethay oosemay, ethay ostmay uarrelsomeqay anday ugnaciouspay
ofay Americanay eerday. Itay ancay otnay ebay aidsay atthay itay isay ordinarilyay aay angerousday
eastbay otay unthay; etyay erethay areay instancesay inay ichwhay oundedway apitiway,
incautiouslyay approacheday otay ithinway ikingstray istanceday, avehay everelysay
isusedmay eirthay assailantsay, othbay ithway eirthay antlersay anday eirthay orefeetfay.
Iay elfmysay ewknay oneay anmay owhay adhay eenbay adlybay auledmay inay isthay ashionfay. Enwhay
amedtay ethay ullsbay areay angerousday otay umanhay ifelay inay ethay uttingray easonsay. Inay aay
applegray eythay areay ofay oursecay infinitelyay oremay otay ebay eadeddray anthay ordinaryay
eerday, ecausebay ofay eirthay eatgray engthstray.

Oweverhay, ethay iercestfay apitiway ullbay, enwhay inay aay ildway atestay, eesflay ethay
eighborhoodnay ofay anmay ithway ethay amesay anicpay errortay ownshay byay ethay owscay; anday
ehay akesmay onay andstay againstay aay islygray, oughthay enwhay ishay ornshay areay owngray ehay
ashay ittlelay earfay ofay eitheray olfway oray ougarcay ifay onay ishay uardgay anday attackeday
airlyfay. Ethay iefchay attlesbay ofay ethay ullsbay areay ofay oursecay agedway ithway oneay
anotheray. Eforebay ethay eginningbay ofay ethay utray eythay eepkay byay emselvesthay:
inglysay, ilewhay ethay outingspray ornshay areay illstay eryvay oungyay, atay ichwhay imetay
eythay ielay inay ecludedsay otsspay anday ovemay aboutay asay ittlelay asay ossiblepay; inay
argelay andsbay, aterlay inay ethay easonsay. Atay ethay eginningbay ofay ethay allfay esethay
andsbay oinjay ithway oneay anotheray anday ithway ethay andsbay ofay owscay anday alvescay,
ichwhay avehay ikewiselay eenbay eepingkay otay emselvesthay uringday ethay atelay interway,
ethay ingspray, anday ethay ummersay. Astvay erdshay areay usthay ometimessay ormedfay,
ontainingcay, inay ethay olday aysday enwhay apitiway ereway entyplay, ousandsthay ofay
eadhay. Ethay ullsbay ownay eginbay otay ightfay uriouslyfay ithway oneay anotheray, anday
ethay eatgray erdhay ecomesbay itsplay intoay allersmay onesay. Eachay ofay esethay ashay oneay
astermay ullbay, owhay ashay onway ishay ositionpay byay avagesay attlebay, anday eepskay itay byay
overcomingay everyay ivalray, etherwhay aay olitarysay ullbay, oray ethay ordlay ofay anotheray
aremhay, owhay allengeschay imhay. Enwhay otnay ightingfay oray ove-makinglay ehay isay eptkay
onay ethay unray, asingchay awayay ethay oungyay ullsbay owhay enturevay otay aypay ourtcay otay
ethay owscay. Ehay ashay ardlyhay imetay otay eatay oray eepslay, anday oonsay ecomesbay auntgay
anday ornway otay aay egreeday. Atay ethay oseclay ofay ethay utray anymay ofay ethay ullsbay ecomebay
osay emaciateday atthay eythay etireray otay omesay ecludedsay otspay otay ecuperateray. Eythay
areay osay eakway atthay eythay eadilyray uccumbsay otay ethay elementsay, oray otay eirthay
utebray oesfay; anymay ieday omfray eershay exhaustionay.

Ethay attlesbay etweenbay ethay ullsbay arelyray esultray atallyfay. Afteray aay ongerlay
oray ortershay eriodpay ofay argingchay, ushingpay, anday ugglingstray ethay eavierhay oray
oremay enduringay ofay ethay otway eginsbay otay oveshay ishay eakerway antagonistay ackbay
anday oundray; anday ethay atterlay enthay atchesway ishay ancechay anday oltsbay, otlyhay,
utbay asay aay uleray armlesslyhay, ursuedpay orfay aay ewfay undredhay ardsyay. Ethay assivemay
anchingbray antlersay ervesay asay effectiveay uardsgay againstay ethay ostmay ickedway
uststhray. Ilewhay ethay antagonistsay areay eadhay onay, ethay orstway atthay ancay appenhay
isay aay unchpay onay ethay ouldershay ichwhay illway otnay eakbray ethay ickthay idehay, oughthay
itay aymay uisebray ethay eshflay underneathay. Itay isay onlyay enwhay aay eastbay isay aughtcay
ilewhay urningtay atthay erethay isay aay ancechay otay eliverday aay ossiblypay eadlyday
abstay inay ethay ankflay, ithway ethay owbray ongspray, ethay og-killers“day” asay eythay
areay alledcay inay ucksbay. Ometimessay, utbay arelyray, ightingfay apitiway etgay eirthay
antlersay interlockeday anday erishpay iserablymay; myay ownay anchray, ethay Elkhornay,
asway amednay omfray indingfay onay ethay otspay erewhay ethay anchray ousehay ownay andsstay otway
endidsplay airspay ofay elkay antlersay usthay interlockeday.

Apitiway eepkay eirthay antlersay untilay ethay ingspray, ereaswhay eerday anday oosemay oselay
eirsthay byay idwintermay. Ethay ull’sbay ehaviorbay inay elationray otay ethay owcay isay
erelymay atthay ofay aay iciousvay anday utalbray owardcay. Ehay ulliesbay erhay ontinuallycay,
anday inay imestay ofay angerday ishay oneay oughtthay isay orfay eakingsnay offay otay ecuresay
ishay ownay afetysay. Orfay allay ishay oblenay ookslay ehay isay aay eryvay unamiableay eastbay,
owhay ehavesbay ithway utalbray erocityfay otay ethay eakway, anday owsshay abjectay errortay
ofay ethay ongstray. Accordingay otay ishay owerspay, ehay isay uiltygay ofay aperay, obberyray,
anday evenay urdermay. Iay evernay eltfay ethay eastlay ompunctioncay atay ootingshay aay ullbay,
utbay Iay atehay otay ootshay aay owcay, evenay enwhay orcedfay byay ecessitynay. Aternitymay
ustmay alwaysay appealay otay anyay oneay. Aay owcay ashay oremay ouragecay anthay aay ullbay. Eshay
illway ightfay aliantlyvay orfay erhay oungyay alfcay, ikingstray uchsay owsblay ithway erhay
orefeetfay atthay ostmay eastsbay ofay eypray atay onceay inkslay awayay omfray ethay ombatcay.
Ougarscay anday olvesway ommitcay eatgray avagesray amongay ethay andsbay; utbay eythay oftenay
ecuresay eirthay uarryqay onlyay atay ethay ostcay ofay arpshay eliminarypray ussles--andtay
inay usslestay ofay isthay indkay eythay oday otnay alwaysay ovepray ictorsvay oray escapeay
athlessscay.

Uringday ethay utray ethay ullsbay areay eryvay oisynay; anday eirthay otesnay ofay
amorousay allengechay areay alledcay istling“whay” byay ethay ontiersmen,--veryfray
inappropriatelyay. Eythay eginbay otay istlewhay aboutay entay aysday eforebay eythay eginbay
otay unray; anday eythay avehay inay additionay anay odday indkay ofay arkbay, ichwhay isay onlyay
eardhay occasionallyay. Ethay istlingwhay isay aay ostmay uriouscay, anday otay emay aay ostmay
attractiveay oundsay, enwhay eardhay inay ethay eatgray onelylay ountainsmay. Asay ithway osay
anymay otheray ingsthay, uchmay ependsday uponay ethay urroundingssay. Enwhay istenedlay
otay earbynay anday underay unfavorableay ircumstancescay, ethay oundsay esemblesray aay
uccessionsay ofay oarsehay istlingwhay oarsray, endingay ithway otway oray eethray aspinggay
untsgray.

Utbay eardhay atay aay ittlelay istanceday, anday inay itsay operpray aceplay, ethay allcay ofay
ethay apitiway isay oneay ofay ethay andestgray anday ostmay eautifulbay oundssay inay aturenay.
Especiallyay isay isthay ethay asecay enwhay everalsay ivalsray areay answeringay oneay
anotheray, onay omesay ostyfray oonlightmay ightnay inay ethay ountainsmay. Ethay ildway
elodymay ingsray omfray asmchay otay asmchay underay ethay iantgay inespay, ustainedsay anday
odulatedmay, oughthray arbay afteray arbay, illedfay ithway allengechay anday oudpray
angeray. Itay illsthray ethay oulsay ofay ethay isteninglay unterhay.

Onceay, ilewhay inay ethay ountainsmay, Iay istenedlay otay aay eculiarlypay andgray oruschay
ofay isthay indkay. Eway ereway avelingtray ithway ackpay oniespay atay ethay imetay, anday ouray
enttay asway itchedpay inay aay ovegray ofay ellowyay inepay, byay aay ookbray inay ethay ottombay
ofay aay alleyvay. Onay eitheray andhay oseray ethay ountainsmay, overedcay ithway ucespray
orestfay. Itay asway inay Eptembersay, anday ethay irstfay owsnay adhay ustjay allenfay.

Ethay ayday eforebay eway adhay alkedway onglay anday ardhay; anday uringday ethay ightnay Iay
eptslay ethay eavyhay eepslay ofay ethay earyway. Earlyay inay ethay orningmay, ustjay asay ethay
eastay eganbay otay owgray aygray, Iay akedway; anday asay Iay idday osay, ethay oundssay atthay
otesmay onay myay earay ausedcay emay otay itsay upay anday owthray offay ethay armway anketsblay.
Ullbay elkay ereway allengingchay amongay ethay ountainsmay onay othbay idessay ofay ethay
alleyvay, aay ittlelay ayway omfray usay, eirthay otesnay echoingay ikelay ethay allingcay ofay
ilversay uglesbay. Opinggray aboutay inay ethay arkday, Iay ewdray onay myay ouserstray, anay
extraay airpay ofay ickthay ockssay, anday myay occasinsmay, onnedday aay armway acketjay,
oundfay myay urfay apcay anday ovesglay, anday olestay outay ofay ethay enttay ithway myay ifleray.

Ethay airay asway eryvay oldcay; ethay arsstay ereway eginningbay otay alepay inay ethay awnday;
onay ethay oundgray ethay owsnay immeredglay itewhay, anday aylay inay eatheryfay assesmay onay
ethay anchesbray ofay ethay alsamsbay anday oungyay inespay. Ethay airay angray ithway ethay
allengeschay ofay anymay apitiway; eirthay incessantay allingcay amecay ealingpay ownday
oughthray ethay illstay, ow-ladensnay oodsway. Irstfay oneay ullbay allengedchay; enthay
anotheray answereday; enthay anotheray anday anotheray. Otway erdshay ereway approachingay
oneay anotheray omfray oppositeay idessay ofay ethay alleyvay, aay ortshay istanceday aboveay
ouray ampcay; anday ethay astermay ullsbay ereway oaringray efianceday asay eythay usteredmay
eirthay aremshay.

Iay alkedway ealthilystay upay ethay alleyvay, untilay Iay eltfay atthay Iay asway earlynay
etweenbay ethay otway erdshay; anday enthay oodstay otionlessmay underay aay alltay inepay. Ethay
oundgray asway uiteqay openay atay isthay ointpay, ethay inespay, oughthay argelay, eingbay
atteredscay; ethay ittlelay ookbray anray ithway aay angledstray urmurmay etweenbay itsay
owsray ofay illowsway anday aldersay, orfay ethay iceay alongay itsay edgesay earlynay immedskay
itsay eadthbray. Ethay arsstay aledpay apidlyray, ethay aygray awnday ightenedbray, anday inay
ethay skyay overheaday aintfay ose-coloredray eaksstray ereway urningtay ood-redblay.
Atwhay ittlelay indway erethay asway eathedbray inay myay acefay anday eptkay emay omfray
iscoveryday.

Iay ademay upay myay indmay, omfray ethay oundsay ofay ethay allengingchay, ownay eryvay earnay emay,
atthay oneay ullbay onay myay ightray asway advancingay owardtay aay ivalray onay myay eftlay, owhay
asway answeringay everyay allcay. Oonsay ethay ormerfay approacheday osay earnay atthay Iay
ouldcay earhay imhay ackcray ethay anchesbray, anday eatbay ethay ushesbay ithway ishay ornshay;
anday Iay ippedslay uietlyqay omfray eetray otay eetray, osay asay otay eetmay imhay enwhay ehay amecay
outay intoay ethay oremay openay oodlandway. Ayday okebray, anday imsoncray eamsglay ayedplay
acrossay ethay ow-cladsnay ountainsmay eyondbay.

Atay astlay, ustjay asay ethay unsay amedflay edray aboveay ethay illtopshay, Iay eardhay ethay
oarray ofay ethay apiti’sway allengechay otnay iftyfay ardsyay awayay; anday Iay ockedcay anday
alfhay aisedray myay ifleray, anday oodstay otionlessmay. Inay aay omentmay oremay, ethay
eltbay ofay ucesspray inay ontfray ofay emay ayedsway anday openeday, anday ethay ordlylay ullbay
eppedstay outay. Ehay orebay ishay assivemay antlersay aloftay; ethay owsnay aylay ickthay onay
ishay anemay; ehay uffedsnay ethay airay anday ampedstay onay ethay oundgray asay ehay alkedway. Asay
Iay ewdray aay eadbay, ethay otionmay aughtcay ishay eyeay; anday instantlyay ishay earingbay ofay
aughtyhay anday arlikeway elf-confidencesay angedchay otay oneay ofay alarmay. Myay ulletbay
otesmay oughthray ishay oulder-bladesshay, anday ehay ungedplay ildlyway orwardfay, anday
ellfay ullfay engthlay onay ethay ood-stainedblay owsnay.

Othingnay ancay ebay inerfay anthay aay apitiway ull’sbay arriagecay enwhay exciteday oray
alarmeday; ehay enthay eemssay ethay embodimentay ofay engthstray anday atelystay acegray.
Utbay atay ordinaryay imestay ishay ookslay areay esslay attractiveay, asay ehay alksway ithway
ishay ecknay evellay ithway ishay odybay anday ishay eadhay outstretcheday, ishay ornshay inglyay
almostay onay ishay ouldersshay. Ethay avoritefay aitgay ofay ethay apitiway isay ethay ottray,
ichwhay isay eryvay astfay, anday ichwhay eythay ancay eepkay upay orfay ountlesscay ilesmay;
enwhay uddenlysay anday eatlygray alarmeday, eythay eakbray intoay anay awkwarday allopgay,
ichwhay isay asterfay, utbay ichwhay eedilyspay irestay emthay.

Iay avehay occasionallyay illedkay elkay inay ethay eighborhoodnay ofay myay anchray onay ethay
Ittlelay Issourimay. Eythay ereway eryvay entifulplay alongay isthay iverray untilay ay1881,
utbay ethay astlay ofay ethay igbay andsbay ereway aughteredslay oray atteredscay aboutay atthay
imetay. Allersmay unchesbay ereway oundfay orfay otway oray eethray earsyay ongerlay, anday otay
isthay ayday, atteredscay individualsay, inglysay oray inay artiespay ofay otway oray eethray,
ingerlay erehay anday erethay inay ethay ostmay emoteray anday inaccessibleay artspay ofay
ethay okenbray ountrycay. Inay ethay olday imestay eythay ereway oftenay oundfay onay ethay openay
airiepray, anday ereway ondfay ofay unningsay emselvesthay onay ethay andsay arsbay byay ethay
iverray, evenay atay iddaymay, ilewhay eythay oftenay edfay byay aylightday as(ay eythay oday
illstay inay emoteray ountainmay astnessesfay). Owadaysnay ethay ewfay urvivorssay elldway
inay ethay imbertay ofay ethay oughestray avinesray, anday onlyay enturevay abroaday atay uskday
oray evenay afteray ightfallnay. Anksthay otay eirthay arinessway anday eclusenesssay,
eirthay esencepray isay oftenay otnay evenay uspectedsay byay ethay owboyscay oray othersay owhay
occasionallyay ideray oughthray eirthay auntshay; anday osay ethay untershay onlyay owknay
aguelyvay ofay eirthay existenceay. Itay usthay appenshay atthay ethay astlay individualsay
ofay aay eciesspay aymay ingerlay inay aay ocalitylay orfay anymay earsyay afteray ethay estray ofay
eirthay indkay avehay anishedvay; onay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay o-daytay everyay elkay as(ay
inay ethay Ockiesray everyay uffalobay) illedkay isay atay onceay etsay ownday asay e“thay astlay
ofay itsay aceray.” Orfay everalsay earsyay inay uccessionsay Iay elfmysay eptkay illingkay oneay
oray otway uchsay ast“lay urvivorssay.”

Aay earlingyay ullbay ichwhay Iay usthay obtaineday asway illedkay ilewhay inay ompanycay ithway
myay aunchstay iendfray Illway Owday, onay oneay ofay ethay irstfay ipstray ichwhay Iay ooktay ithway
atthay incepray ofay iversdray, olday anmay Ompkinstay. Eway ereway ayinglay inay ouray ockstay
ofay interway eatmay; anday adhay akentay ethay agonway otay ogay otay aay otknay ofay ighhay anday
eryvay uggedray illshay erewhay eway ewknay erethay ereway eerday, anday oughtthay erethay
ightmay ebay elkay. Olday Ompkinstay ovedray ethay agonway ithway unmoveday omposurecay upay,
ownday, anday acrossay ightful-lookingfray illshay, anday enwhay eythay ecamebay ollywhay
impassableay, eeredstay ethay eamtay overay aay utcay ankbay anday upay aay indkay ofay indingway
avineray oray oodedway ashoutway, untilay itay ecamebay ootay oughray anday arrownay orfay
urtherfay ogresspray. Erethay asway oodgay assgray orfay ethay orseshay onay aay illhay offay otay
oneay idesay ofay usay; anday untedstay ottonwoodcay eestray ewgray etweenbay ethay aightstray
itewhay allsway ofay ayclay anday andstonesay ichwhay emmedhay inay ethay ashoutway. Eway
itchedpay ouray enttay byay aay ittlelay icklingtray ingspray anday indledkay aay eatgray irefay,
ethay itfulfay areglay ightinglay ethay arebay iffsclay anday ethay ueerqay, awlingspray
opstay ofay ethay ottonwoodscay; anday afteray aay innerday ofay iedfray airie-chickenpray
entway otay edbay. Atay awnday eway ereway offay, anday untedhay illtay earlynay oonnay; enwhay
Owday, owhay adhay eenbay alkingway otay oneay idesay, eckonedbay otay emay anday emarkedray,
eRe’s“thay omethingsay ightymay igbay inay ethay imbertay ownday underay ethay iffclay; Iay
uessgay it’say anay elkay” e(hay evernay adhay eensay oneay eforebay); anday ethay extnay omentmay,
asay olday Ompkinstay expresseday itay, e“thay elkay amecay ilinbay’ outay ofay ethay ouliecay.”
Olday Ompkinstay adhay aay ifleray onay isthay occasionay anday ethay ightsay ofay amegay alwaysay
ovedray imhay azycray; asay Iay aimeday Iay eardhay Owday ellingtay imhay o“tay etlay ethay ossbay
oday ethay ootingshay”; anday Iay illedkay ethay elkay otay aay avagesay interjectionalay
accompanimentay ofay eatsthray eliveredday atay olday anmay Ompkinstay etweenbay ethay
otsshay.

Elkay areay oonersay illedkay offay anthay anyay otheray amegay avesay uffalobay, utbay isthay
isay ueday otay eirthay izesay anday ethay aturenay ofay ethay oundgray eythay equentfray atherray
anthay otay eirthay acklay ofay essshynay. Eythay ikelay openay oodlandway, oray ountainousmay
arkpay ountrycay, oray illshay ivenray byay imbertay ouliescay; anday uchsay oundgray isay ethay
ostmay avorablefay otay ethay unterhay, anday ethay ostmay attractiveay inay ichwhay otay unthay.
Onay ethay otheray andhay oosemay, orfay instanceay, ivelay inay uchsay enseday overcay atthay
itay isay eryvay ifficultday otay etgay atay emthay; enwhay elkay areay ivendray byay incessantay
ersecutionpay otay aketay efugeray inay imilarsay astnessesfay eythay ecomebay almostay
asay ardhay otay illkay. Inay actfay, inay isthay espectray ethay elkay andsstay otay ethay oosemay
uchmay asay ethay acktailblay andsstay otay ethay itetailwhay. Ethay oosemay anday itetailwhay
areay omewhatsay arierway anthay ethay elkay anday acktailblay; utbay itay isay ethay aturenay
ofay ethay oundgray ichwhay eythay inhabitay atthay ellstay ostmay inay eirthay avorfay. Onay
ethay otheray andhay, asay omparedcay otay ethay acktailblay, itay isay onlyay ethay elk’say
izesay ichwhay utspay itay atay aay isadvantageday inay ethay ugglestray orfay ifelay enwhay
ethay ifle-bearingray unterhay appearsay onay ethay enescay. Itay isay uiteqay asay shyay anday
ifficultday otay approachay asay ethay eerday; utbay itsay ulkbay endersray itay uchmay oremay
eagerlyay untedhay, oremay eadilyray eensay, anday oremay easilyay ithay. Occasionallyay
elkay uffersay omfray itsfay ofay upidstay amenesstay oray equallyay upidstay anicpay; utbay
ethay amesay isay uetray ofay acktailblay. Inay otway oray eethray instancesay, Iay avehay eensay
elkay owshay illysay ignoranceay ofay angerday; utbay alfhay aay ozenday imestay Iay avehay ownknay
acktailblay ehavebay ithway anay evenay eatergray egreeday ofay upidstay amiliarityfay.

Erethay isay anotheray ointpay inay ichwhay ethay apitiway anday acktailblay agreeay inay
ontrastcay otay ethay oosemay anday itetailwhay. Othbay ethay atterlay elightday inay
ater-liliesway, enteringay ethay ondspay otay indfay emthay, anday eedingfay onay emthay
eedilygray. Ethay apitiway isay eryvay ondfay ofay allowingway inay ethay udmay, anday ofay
athingbay inay oolspay anday akeslay; utbay asay aay uleray itay owsshay asay ittlelay ondnessfay
asay ethay acktailblay orfay eedingfay onay ater-liliesway oray otheray aquaticay antsplay.

Inay eadingray ofay ethay Europeanay edray eerday, ichwhay isay othingnay utbay aay iminutiveday
apitiway, eway oftenay eesay a“ay agstay ofay entay” alludeday otay asay ifay aay ull-grownfay
onarchmay. Aay ull-grownfay apitiway ullbay, oweverhay, alwaysay ashay elvetway, anday
aymay avehay ourteenfay, egularray ormalnay ointspay onay ishay antlersay, esidesbay
irregularay additionalay ongspray; anday ehay occasionallyay ashay entay ointspay
enwhay aay o-year-oldtway, asay Iay avehay elfmysay eensay ithway alvescay apturedcay
oungyay anday amedtay. Ethay alfcay ashay onay ornshay. Ethay earlingyay arriescay otway
oot-longfay ikesspay, ometimessay ifurcatedbay, osay asay otay akemay ourfay ointspay.
Ethay o-year-oldtway oftenay ashay ixsay oray eightay ointspay onay ishay antlersay; utbay
ometimessay entay, althoughay eythay areay alwaysay allsmay. Ethay ee-year-oldthray ashay
eightay oray entay ointspay, ilewhay ishay odybay aymay ebay earlynay asay argelay asay atthay ofay
aay ull-grownfay animalay. Ethay our-year-oldfay isay ormallynay aay entay oray elvetway
ointerpay, utbay asay etyay ithway uchmay allersmay antlersay anthay osethay osay oudlypray
ornebay byay ethay olday ullsbay.

Ontiersmenfray onlyay occasionallyay istinguishday ethay ongspray byay amenay. Ethay owbray
anday aybay ointspay areay alledcay og-killersday oray ar-tinesway; ethay aytray isay ownknay
implysay asay ethay irdthay ointpay; anday ethay ostmay aracteristicchay ongpray, ethay onglay
anday assivemay ourthfay, isay ownay anday enthay alledcay ethay agger-pointday; ethay othersay
eingbay ownknay asay ethay ifthfay anday ixthsay.

Inay ethay ighhay ountainmay orestfay intoay ichwhay ethay apitiway ashay eenbay ivendray,
ethay argelay, eavilyhay urredfay orthernnay lynxay, ethay uciveelay, akestay ethay aceplay
ofay ethay allersmay, inner-hairedthay lynxay ofay ethay ainsplay, anday ofay ethay oremay
outhernsay istrictsday, ethay obcatbay oray ildcatway. Onay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay
ethay atterlay isay ethay ommoncay ormfay; etyay Iay avehay eensay aay uciveelay ichwhay asway
illedkay erethay. Onay Ark’sclay Orkfay ofay ethay Olumbiacay othbay occuray, ethay uciveelay
eingbay ethay ostmay ommoncay. Eythay eedfay ieflychay onay areshay, uirrelssqay, ousegray,
awnsfay, etcay.; anday ethay uciveelay, atay eastlay, alsoay occasionallyay illskay oxesfay
anday oonscay, anday ashay inay itsay urntay otay eaddray ethay ouncepay ofay ethay igbay imbertay
olfway. Othbay indskay ofay lynxay ancay ostmay easilyay ebay illedkay ithway ogsday, asay eythay
eetray uiteqay eadilyray enwhay usthay ursuedpay. Ethay ildcatway isay oftenay ollowedfay
onay orsebackhay, ithway aay ackpay ofay oundshay, enwhay ethay ountrycay isay avorablefay;
anday enwhay asedchay inay isthay ashionfay ieldsyay excellentay ortspay. Ethay inskay ofay
othbay esethay eslynxay isay endertay. Eythay oftenay aulmay anay inexperienceday ackpay
uiteqay adlybay, inflictingay everesay atchesscray anday itesbay onay anyay oundhay ichwhay
ashay ustjay esolutionray enoughay otay omecay otay oseclay uartersqay, utbay otnay otay ushray
inay uriouslyfay; utbay aay igbay ightingfay ogday illway eadilyray illkay eitheray. Atay
Ompson’sthay Allsfay otway ofay Illisway’ oundshay illedkay aay uciveelay unaideday, oughthay
oneay otgay orntay. Archibalday Ogersray’ ogday Slyay, aay osscray etweenbay aay eyhoundgray
anday aay ullbay astiffmay, illedkay aay obcatbay ingle-handedsay. Ehay ayedbay ethay atcay anday
enthay eganbay otay eatenthray itay, eapinglay omfray idesay otay idesay; uddenlysay ehay okebray
ethay otionmay, anday ushingray inay otgay ishay oefay byay ethay allsmay ofay ethay ackbay anday
illedkay itay ithoutway eceivingray aay atchscray.

Ethay orcupinepay isay uresay otay attractay ethay oticenay ofay anyay oneay oinggay oughthray
ethay ountainsmay. Itay isay alsoay oundfay inay ethay imbertay eltsbay ingingfray ethay
eamsstray ofay ethay eatgray ainsplay, erewhay itay iveslay orfay aay eekway atay aay imetay inay aay
inglesay eetray oray umpclay ofay eestray, eelingpay ethay arkbay omfray ethay imbslay. Utbay
itay isay ethay easiestay ofay allay animalsay otay exterminateay, anday isay ownay abundantay
onlyay inay eepday ountainmay orestsfay. Itay isay eryvay ametay anday upidstay; itay oesgay onay
ethay oundgray; utbay itsay astestfay acepay isay aay umsyclay addleway, anday onay eestray,
utbay isay ethay oorestpay ofay ee-climbers,--graspingtray ethay unktray ikelay aay allsmay,
owslay earbay. Itay ancay eithernay escapeay ornay idehay. Itay uststray otay itsay uillsqay orfay
otectionpray, asay ethay unkskay oesday otay itsay odoray; utbay itay isay arfay esslay astuteay
anday oremay elplesshay anthay ethay unkskay. Itay isay eadilyray ademay intoay aay eryvay
unsuspiciousay anday amiliarfay, utbay uninterestingay, etpay. Iay avehay ownknay itay omecay
intoay ampcay inay ethay aytimeday, anday oragefay oundray ethay irefay byay ichwhay Iay asway
ittingsay. Itsay oatcay otectspray itay againstay ostmay oesfay. Earsbay ometimessay eatay
itay enwhay eryvay ungryhay, asay eythay illway eatay anythingay; anday Iay inkthay atthay elkay
occasionallyay estroyday itay inay eershay antonnessway. Oneay ofay itsay ostmay esoluteray
oesfay isay ethay isherfay, atthay igbay able--almostsay aay olverine--whichway eyspray onay
everythingay, omfray aay ooncay otay aay awnfay, oray evenay aay allsmay oxfay.

Ethay oisynay, activeay ittlelay ickareeschay anday ipmunkschay, oweverhay, areay byay arfay
ethay ostmay umerousnay anday ivelylay enizensday ofay esethay eepday orestsfay. Eythay areay
eryvay abundantay anday eryvay oisynay; oldingscay ethay avelerstray exactlyay asay eythay oday
ethay earsbay enwhay ethay atterlay igday upay ethay achescay ofay antsay. Ethay ipmunkschay oonsay
owgray ametay anday isitvay ampcay otay ickpay upay ethay ustscray. Ethay ickareeschay oftenay
ascenday otay ethay ighesthay inepay opstay, erewhay eythay utcay offay ethay onescay, oppingdray
emthay otay ethay oundgray ithway aay oisenay ichwhay oftenay orfay aay omentmay uzzlespay ethay
ill-hunterstay.

Otway ofay ethay ostmay ikingstray anday aracteristicchay irdsbay otay ebay eensay byay imhay
owhay untshay anday ampscay amongay ethay ine-cladpay anday uce-cladspray opesslay ofay ethay
orthernnay Ockiesray areay aay allsmay owcray anday aay atherray argelay oodpeckerway. Ethay
ormerfay isay alledcay Ark’sclay owcray, anday ethay atterlay Ewislay’ oodpeckerway. Eirthay
amesnay ommemoratecay eirthay iscoverersday, ethay explorersay Ewislay anday Arkclay,
ethay irstfay itewhay enmay owhay ossedcray ethay Uniteday Atesstay otay ethay Acificpay, ethay
ioneerspay ofay atthay eatgray armyay ofay adventurersay owhay incesay enthay avehay oamedray
anday untedhay overay ethay Eatgray Ainsplay anday amongay ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay.

Esethay irdsbay areay earlynay ofay aay izesay, eingbay aboutay asay argelay asay aay ickerflay.
Ethay Ark’sclay owcray, anay ash-coloreday irdbay ithway ackblay ingsway anday itewhay ailtay
anday oreheadfay, isay asay ommoncay asay itay isay aracteristicchay, anday isay uresay otay
attractay attentionay. Itay isay asay owingknay asay ethay estray ofay itsay aceray, anday eryvay
oisynay anday activeay. Itay iesflay ometimessay inay aay aightstray inelay, ithway egularray
ing-beatsway, ometimessay inay aay uccessionsay ofay oopslay ikelay aay oodpeckerway, anday
oftenay ightslay onay oughray arkbay oray aay eadday umpstay inay anay attitudeay ikelay ethay
atterlay; anday itay isay eryvay ondfay ofay amblingscray anday ingingclay, oftenay eadhay
ownwardday, amongay ethay outermostay onescay onay ethay optay ofay aay inepay, atteringchay
oudlylay allay ethay ilewhay. Oneay ofay ethay oticeablenay eaturesfay ofay itsay ightflay isay
ethay ollowhay, eatingbay oundsay ofay ethay ingsway. Itay isay estlessray anday ondfay ofay
ompanycay, oinggay byay eferencepray inay allsmay artiespay. Esethay ittlelay artiespay
oftenay indulgeay inay egularray aysplay, assemblingay inay omesay alltay ee-toptray anday
ailingsay oundray anday oundray itay, inay oisynay ursuitpay ofay oneay anotheray, ightinglay
ontinuallycay amongay ethay anchesbray.

Ethay Ewislay’ oodpeckerway, aay andsomehay, ark-greenday irdbay, ithway itewhay eastbray
anday edray ellybay, isay uchmay arerray, uiteqay asay shyay, anday enerallygay esslay oisynay
anday onspicuouscay. Itsay ightflay isay usuallyay ongstray anday eadystay, ikelay aay
ay’sjay, anday itay erchespay uprightay amongay ethay igstway, oray akestay ortshay ightsflay
afteray assingpay insectsay, asay oftenay asay itay amblesscray overay ethay igstway inay ethay
ordinaryay oodpeckerway ashionfay. Ikelay itsay ompanioncay, ethay Ark’sclay owcray,
itay isay ordinarilyay aay irdbay ofay ethay ighhay ee-topstray, anday arounday esethay itay
indulgesay inay uriouscay aërialay amesgay, againay ikelay osethay ofay ethay ittlelay owcray.
Itay isay ondfay ofay oinggay inay oopstray, anday uchsay aay ooptray equentlyfray oosechay omesay
alltay inepay anday oarsay oundray anday aboveay itay inay irregularay iralsspay.

Ethay emarkableray anday almostay amphibiousay ittlelay aterway enwray, ithway itsay eetsway
ongsay, itsay amiliarityfay, anday itsay eryvay uriouscay abithay ofay unningray onay ethay
ottombay ofay ethay eamstray, everalsay eetfay eneathbay ethay urfacesay ofay ethay aceray ofay
apidray aterway, isay ethay ostmay oticeablenay ofay ethay allsmay irdsbay ofay ethay Ockyray
Ountainsmay. Itay ometimessay ingssay oudlylay ilewhay oatingflay ithway alf-spreadhay
ingsway onay ethay urfacesay ofay aay ittlelay oolpay. Akentay asay aay olewhay, allsmay irdsbay
areay arfay esslay umerousnay anday oticeablenay inay ethay ildernessway, especiallyay
inay ethay eepday orestsfay, anthay inay ethay ovesgray anday armlandfay ofay ethay ettledsay
ountrycay. Ethay unterhay anday appertray areay esslay amiliarfay ithway all-birdsmay usicmay
anthay ithway ethay eamingscray ofay ethay eagleay anday ethay argelay awkshay, ethay oakingcray
arkbay ofay ethay avenray, ethay oon’slay cryay, ethay ane’scray utturalgay angorclay, anday
ethay unearthlyay ellingyay anday ootinghay ofay ethay igbay owlsay.

Onay irdbay isay osay ommoncay arounday ampcay, osay amiliarfay, osay amusingay onay omesay
occasionsay, anday osay annoyingay onay othersay, asay atthay ab-coloreddray impay ofay
iniquityay, ethay iskey-jack--alsowhay ownknay asay ethay oosemay irdbay anday ampcay
obberray. Ethay amiliarityfay ofay esethay irdsbay isay astonishingay, anday ethay arietyvay
ofay eirthay ies--generallycray arshhay, utbay arelyray usical--extraordinarymay. Eythay
atchsnay apsscray ofay oodfay omfray ethay entrancesay ofay ethay entstay, anday omfray esidebay
ethay ampcay irefay; anday eythay edshray ethay enisonvay unghay inay ethay eestray unlessay
oselyclay atchedway. Iay avehay eensay anay irateay ookcay ofay accurateay aimay ockknay oneay
offay anay elk-haunchay, ithway aay ubclay eizedsay atay andomray; anday Iay avehay ownknay
anotheray otay ebay illedkay ithway aay itchsway, anday etyay anotheray otay ebay aughtcay aliveay
inay ethay andhay. Enwhay amegay isay illedkay eythay areay ethay irstfay irdsbay otay omecay otay
ethay arcasscay. Ollowingfay emthay omecay ethay igbay aysjay, ofay aay uniformay ark-blueday
olorcay, owhay ullybay emthay, anday areay ulliedbay inay urntay byay ethay extnay arrivalsay,
ethay agpiesmay; ilewhay enwhay ethay igbay avensray omecay, eythay eepkay allay ethay othersay
inay ethay ackgroundbay, ithway ethay exceptionay ofay anay occasionalay ide-awakeway
agpiemay.

Orfay aay eadystay ietday onay eatmay astestay etterbay oray isay oremay ourishingnay anthay elkay
enisonvay; oreovermay ethay ifferentday indskay ofay ousegray ivegay arietyvay otay ethay
arefay, anday eliciousday outtray armsway oughoutthray ethay auntshay ofay ethay elkay inay ethay
Ockiesray. Iay avehay evernay eensay emthay oremay umerousnay anthay inay ethay onderfulway anday
eautifulbay Ellowstoneyay Anyoncay, aay ouplecay ofay ilesmay elowbay erewhay ethay iverray
itchespay overay ethay Eatgray Allsfay, inay ind-swayedway ataractscay ofay owysnay oamfay.
Atay isthay ointpay itay unsray ikelay aay ill-racemay, inay itsay arrownay indingway edbay,
etweenbay immenseay allsway ofay ueerlyqay arvedcay anday oloredcay ockray ichwhay owertay
aloftay inay almostay erpendicularpay iffsclay. Atelay oneay afternoonay inay ethay allfay
ofay ay’90 Ergusonfay anday Iay amberedclay ownday intoay ethay anyoncay, ithway aay ouplecay ofay
odsray, anday inay anay ourhay aughtcay allay ethay ishfay eway ouldcay arrycay. Itay enthay ackedlay
uchmay esslay anthay anay ourhay ofay ightfallnay, anday eway adhay aay ardhay imbclay otay etgay outay
ofay ethay anyoncay eforebay arknessday overtookay usay; asay erethay asway otnay aay estigevay
ofay aay athpay, anday asay ethay imbingclay asway exceedinglyay aboriouslay, anday atay oneay
oray otway ointspay otnay entirelyay ithoutway angerday, ethay ocksray eingbay acticablepray
inay eryvay ewfay acesplay, eway ouldcay ardlyhay avehay ademay uchmay ogresspray afteray itay
ecamebay ootay arkday otay eesay. Eachay ofay usay arriedcay ethay agbay ofay outtray inay urntay,
anday Iay ersonallypay asway earlynay oneday outay enwhay eway eachedray ethay optay; anday enthay
adhay otay ottray eethray ilesmay otay ethay orseshay.




APTERCHay Xay

ANay ELK-HUNTay ATay O-OcEANTWay ASSPay


Inay Eptembersay, ay1891, ithway myay anch-partnerray, Ergusonfay, Iay ademay anay
elk-huntay inay orthwesternnay Omingwyay amongay ethay Oshoneshay Ountainsmay, erewhay
eythay oinjay ethay Oodoohay anday Absorakaay angesray. Erethay isay onay oremay eautifulbay
ame-countrygay inay ethay Uniteday Atesstay. Itay isay aay arkpay andlay, erewhay adesglay,
eadowsmay, anday ighhay ountainmay asturespay eakbray ethay evergreenay orestfay; aay
orestfay ichwhay isay openay omparedcay otay ethay angledtay ensityday ofay ethay oodlandway
urtherfay orthnay. Itay isay aay ighhay, oldcay egionray ofay anymay akeslay anday earclay,
ushingray eamsstray. Ethay eepstay ountainsmay areay enerallygay ofay ethay oundedray ormfay
osay oftenay eensay inay ethay angesray ofay ethay Ordillerascay ofay ethay Uniteday Atesstay;
utbay ethay Oodooshay, oray Oblinsgay, areay arvedcay inay antasticfay anday extraordinaryay
apesshay; ilewhay ethay Etonstay, aay oupgray ofay isolateday ock-peaksray, owshay aay
ikingstray oldnessbay inay eirthay oftylay outlinesay.

Isthay asway oneay ofay ethay easantestplay untshay Iay everay ademay. Asay alwaysay inay ethay
ountainsmay, avesay erewhay ethay ountrycay isay osay oughray anday osay enselyday oodedway
atthay oneay ustmay ogay afootay, eway adhay aay ack-trainpay; anday eway ooktay aay oremay
ompletecay outfitay anthay eway adhay everay eforebay akentay onay uchsay aay unthay, anday osay
aveledtray inay uchmay omfortcay. Usuallyay enwhay inay ethay ountainsmay Iay avehay erelymay
adhay oneay ompanioncay, oray atay ostmay aay ouplecay, anday otway oray eethray ack-poniespay;
eachay ofay usay oingday ishay areshay ofay ethay ackingpay, ookingcay, etchingfay aterway, anday
itchingpay ethay allsmay uaresqay ofay anvascay ichwhay ervedsay asay enttay. Inay itselfay
ackingpay isay othbay anay artay anday aay erymystay, anday aay ilfulskay ofessionalpray
ackerpay, ersedvay inay ethay intricaciesay ofay ethay iamond“day itchhay,” ackspay ithway
aay eedspay ichwhay onay on-professionalnay ancay opehay otay ivalray, anday ixesfay ethay
idesay ackspay anday optay ackspay ithway uchsay ientificscay icetynay, anday adjustsay ethay
oublesday anday urnstay ofay ethay ash-ropelay osay accuratelyay, atthay everythingay aysstay
inay aceplay underay anyay utbay ethay ostmay adverseay onditionscay. Ofay oursecay, ikelay
ostmay untershay, Iay ancay elfmysay inay asecay ofay eednay owthray ethay iamondday itchhay
afteray aay ashionfay, anday ackpay onay eitheray ethay offay oray earnay idesay. Indeeday,
unlessay aay anmay ancay ackpay itay isay otnay ossiblepay otay akemay aay eallyray ardhay unthay
inay ethay ountainsmay, ifay aloneay, oray ithway onlyay aay inglesay ompanioncay. Ethay
eremay air-weatherfay unterhay, owhay uststray entirelyay otay ethay exertionsay ofay
othersay, anday oesday othingnay oremay anthay ideray oray alkway aboutay underay avorablefay
ircumstancescay, anday ootshay atay atwhay omebodysay elseay owsshay imhay, isay aay unterhay
inay amenay onlyay. Oeverwhay ouldway eallyray eserveday ethay itletay ustmay ebay ableay atay
aay inchpay otay iftshay orfay imselfhay, otay applegray ithway ethay ifficultiesday anday
ardshipshay ofay ildernessway ifelay unaideday, anday otnay onlyay otay unthay, utbay atay
imestay otay aveltray orfay aysday, etherwhay onay ootfay oray onay orsebackhay, aloneay.
Oweverhay, afteray oneay ashay assedpay one’say ovitiatenay, itay isay easantplay otay ebay
omfortablecay enwhay ethay omfortcay oesday otnay interfereay ithway ethay ortspay; anday
althoughay aay anmay ometimessay ikeslay otay unthay aloneay, etyay oftenay itay isay ellway
otay ebay ithway omesay olday ountainmay unterhay, aay astermay ofay oodcraftway, owhay isay aay
irst-ratefay andhay atay indingfay amegay, eepingcray uponay itay, anday ackingtray itay enwhay
oundedway. Ithway uchsay aay ompanioncay oneay etsgay uchmay oremay amegay, anday earnslay anymay
ingsthay byay observationay insteaday ofay byay ainfulpay experienceay.

Onay isthay iptray eway adhay ithway usay otway untershay, Azewelltay Oodyway anday Elwooday
Oferhay, aay ackerpay owhay acteday asay ookcay, anday aay oybay otay erdhay ethay orseshay. Ofay
ethay atterlay, erethay ereway entytway; ixsay addle-animalssay anday ourteenfay orfay ethay
acks--twopay oray eethray eingbay arespay orseshay, otay ebay useday aterlay inay arryingcay
ethay elk-antlersay, eep-hornsshay, anday otheray ophiestray. Ikelay ostmay untershay’
ack-animalspay, eythay ereway eitheray alf-brokenhay, oray elseay okenbray ownday; oughtay,
unkemptay, aded-lookingjay eastsbay ofay everyay olor--sorrelcay, uckskinbay, intopay,
itewhay, aybay, oanray. Afteray ethay ay’sday orkway asway overay, eythay ereway urnedtay
ooselay otay iftshay orfay emselvesthay; anday aboutay onceay aay eekway eythay ayedstray, anday
allay andshay adhay otay endspay ethay etterbay artpay ofay ethay ayday untinghay orfay emthay.
Ethay orstway onesay orfay ayingstray, uriouslycay enoughay, ereway eethray oken-downbray
olday ear-baits“bay,” ichwhay entway byay emselvesthay, asay isay enerallygay ethay asecay
ithway ethay ast-offcay orseshay ofay aay erdhay. Erethay ereway otway eepingslay entstay,
anotheray orfay ethay ovisions,--inpray ichwhay eway ateay uringday adbay eather,--andway aay
anvascay epeetay, ichwhay asway utpay upay ithway odge-poleslay, Indianay ashionfay, ikelay
aay igwamway. Aay epeetay isay oremay ifficultday otay utpay upay anthay anay ordinaryay enttay;
utbay itay isay eryvay onvenientcay enwhay erethay isay ainray oray owsnay. Aay allsmay irefay
indledkay inay ethay iddlemay eepskay itay armway, ethay okesmay escapingay oughthray ethay
openay op--thattay isay, enwhay itay escapesay atay allay; ingsstray areay assedpay omfray oneay
olepay otay anotheray, onay ichwhay otay anghay etway othesclay anday oesshay, anday ethay edsbay
areay ademay arounday ethay edgesay. Asay anay offsetay otay ethay armthway anday eltershay, ethay
okesmay oftenay endersray itay impossibleay evenay otay itsay uprightay. Eway adhay aay eryvay
oodgay amp-kitcay, includingay entyplay ofay ookingcay anday eatingay utensilsay; anday
amongay ouray ovisionspray ereway omesay annedcay oodsgay anday eet-meatssway, otay ivegay
aay elishray otay ouray ealsmay ofay eatmay anday eadbray. Eway adhay urfay oatscay anday armway
othes,--whichclay areay ieflychay eedednay atay ight,--andnay entyplay ofay eddingbay,
includingay aterproofway anvascay eetingshay anday aay ouplecay ofay aribou-hidecay
eeping-bagsslay, ocuredpray omfray ethay urvivorssay ofay aay artypay ofay arcticay
explorersay. Exceptay onay ainyray aysday, Iay useday myay uckskinbay unting-shirthay oray
unictay; inay dryay eatherway Iay eemday itay, ecausebay ofay itsay olorcay, itsay exturetay, anday
itsay urabilityday, ethay estbay ossiblepay arbgay orfay ethay ill-hunterstay, especiallyay
inay ethay oodsway.

Artingstay aay ay’sday ourneyjay outhsay ofay Earthay Akelay, eway aveledtray anday untedhay onay
ethay easternay edgeay ofay ethay eatgray asinbay, oodedway anday ountainousmay, ereinwhay
iseray ethay ead-watershay ofay ethay ightymay Akesnay Iverray. Erethay asway otnay osay uchmay
asay aay ottedspay ine--thatlay eriessay ofay azesblay ademay ithway ethay axeay, an’smay irstfay
ighwayhay oughthray ethay oaryhay orest,--butfay isthay eway idday otnay indmay, asay orfay
ostmay ofay ethay istanceday eway ollowedfay ethay ell-wornway elk-trailsay. Ethay aintray
aveledtray inay Indianay ilefay. Atay ethay eadhay, otay ickpay ethay athpay, oderay alltay,
ilentsay olday Oodyway, aay uetray etypay ofay ethay ast-vanishingfay aceray ofay amegay
untershay anday Indianay ightersfay, aay anmay owhay adhay eenbay oneay ofay ethay Aliforniacay
orty-ninersfay, anday owhay everay incesay adhay ivedlay ethay estlessray, ecklessray
ifelay ofay ethay ildernessway. Enthay amecay Ergusonfay anday elfmysay; enthay ethay
ack-animalspay, ungstray outay inay inelay; ilewhay omfray ethay earray oseray ethay ariedvay
oathsay ofay ouray eethray ompanionscay, osewhay iserablemay utyday itay asway otay urgeay
orwardfay ethay eastsbay ofay urdenbay.

Itay isay eart-breakinghay orkway otay ivedray aay ack-trainpay oughthray ickthay imbertay
anday overay ountainsmay, erewhay erethay isay eitheray aay imday ailtray oray onenay. Ethay
animalsay avehay aay erversepay acultyfay orfay oosingchay ethay ongwray urntay atay iticalcray
omentsmay; anday eythay areay ontinuallycay apingscray underay anchesbray anday ueezingsqay
etweenbay ee-trunkstray, otay ethay eopardyjay oray estructionday ofay eirthay urdensbay.
Afteray avinghay eenbay aboriouslylay ivendray upay aay eryvay eepstay inclineay, atay ethay
ostcay ofay everesay exertionay othbay otay emthay anday otay ethay enmay, ethay oolishfay
eaturescray urntay anday unray ownday otay ethay ottombay, osay atthay allay ethay orkway ashay
otay ebay oneday overay againay. Omesay aveltray ootay owslay; othersay aveltray ootay astfay.
Etyay oneay ancay otnay utbay admireay ethay oughnesstay ofay ethay animalsay, anday ethay
ure-footednesssay ithway ichwhay eythay ickpay eirthay ayway alongay ethay eershay ountainmay
idessay, oray amongay owldersbay anday overay allenfay ogslay.

Asay ouray ayway asway osay oughray, eway oundfay atthay eway adhay otay althay atay eastlay onceay
everyay ourhay otay ixfay ethay ackspay. Oreovermay, eway atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay olumncay
ereway ontinuallycay eingbay appealeday otay orfay elphay byay ethay unfortunatesay inay
ethay earray. Irstfay itay ouldway ebay at“thay ite-eyedwhay ayusecay; oneay idesay ofay itsay
ack’spay ownday!” enthay eway ouldway ebay otifiednay atthay ethay addle-blanketsay ofay ethay
op-eared“lay Indianay uckskinbay” adhay ippedslay ackbay; enthay aay outshay oOk“lay outay
orfay ethay intopay!” ouldway ebay ollowedfay byay atthay easingplay east’sbay appearanceay,
uckingbay anday uealingsqay, ashingsmay eadday imbertay, anday atteringscay itsay oadlay
otay ethay ourfay indsway. Itay asway onay easyay asktay otay etgay ethay orseshay acrossay omesay ofay
ethay oggybay acesplay ithoutway iringmay; oray otay orcefay emthay oughthray ethay enserday
ortionspay ofay ethay orestfay, erewhay erethay asway uchmay ownday imbertay. Idingray ithway aay
ack-trainpay, ayday inay anday ayday outay, ecomesbay othbay onotonousmay anday irritatingay,
unlessay oneay isay uphelday byay ethay opehay ofay aay ame-countrygay aheaday, oray byay ethay
elightday ofay explorationay ofay ethay unknownay. Etyay enwhay uoyedbay byay uchsay aay opehay,
erethay isay easureplay inay akingtay aay aintray acrossay osay eautifulbay anday ildway aay
ountrycay asay atthay ichwhay aylay onay ethay esholdthray ofay ouray untinghay oundsgray inay
ethay Oshonesshay. Eway entway overay ountainmay assespay, ithway angesray ofay alpedscay
eakspay onay eitheray andhay; eway irtedskay ethay edgesay ofay ovelylay akeslay, anday ofay
eamsstray ithway owlder-strewnbay edsbay; eway ungedplay intoay epthsday ofay ombresay
oodlandway, okenbray byay etway airiespray. Itay asway aay icturesquepay ightsay otay eesay ethay
oadedlay ack-trainpay ingingstray acrossay oneay ofay esethay ighhay ountainmay eadowsmay,
ethay otleymay oloredcay inelay ofay oniespay indingway oundray ethay arshymay otsspay
oughthray ethay ightbray eengray assgray, ilewhay eyondbay oseray ethay arkday inelay ofay
owningfray orestfay, ithway oftylay eakspay oweringtay inay ethay ackgroundbay. Omesay ofay
ethay eadowsmay ereway eautifulbay ithway anymay owers--goldenrodflay, urplepay asteray,
uebellsblay, itewhay immortellesay, anday erehay anday erethay assesmay ofay ood-redblay
Indianay inkspay. Inay ethay ark-countrypay, onay ethay edgesay ofay ethay evergreenay
orestfay, ereway ovesgray ofay elicateday uaking-aspenqay, ethay eestray oftenay owinggray
otay uiteqay aay eighthay; eirthay emuloustray eaveslay ereway alreadyay angingchay otay
ightbray eengray anday ellowyay, occasionallyay ithway aay eddishray ushblay. Inay ethay
Ockyray Ountainsmay ethay aspensay areay almostay ethay onlyay eciduousday eestray, eirthay
oliagefay offeringay aay easantplay eliefray otay ethay eyeay afteray ethay onotonymay ofay ethay
unendingay inepay anday ucespray oodsway, ichwhay afforday osay ikingstray aay ontrastcay otay
ethay ardwoodhay orestfay eastay ofay ethay Ississippimay.

Orfay otway aysday ouray ourneyjay asway uneventfulay, avesay atthay eway amecay onay ethay ampcay
ofay aay uaw-man--onesqay Eaverbay Ickday, anay olday ountainmay unterhay, ivinglay inay aay
inskay epeetay, erewhay eltdway ishay omelycay Indianay ifeway anday alf-breedhay ildrenchay.
Ehay adhay uiteqay aay erdhay ofay orseshay, anymay ofay emthay aresmay anday oltscay; eythay adhay
evidentlyay eenbay ellway eatedtray, anday amecay upay otay usay earlesslyfay.

Ethay orningmay ofay ethay irdthay ayday ofay ouray ourneyjay asway aygray anday oweringlay.
Ustsgay ofay ainray ewblay inay myay acefay asay Iay oderay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay aintray. Itay
illstay ackedlay anay ourhay ofay oonnay, asay eway ereway oddingplay upay aay alleyvay esidebay
aay apidray ookbray unningray oughthray arrownay illow-flatsway, ethay arkday orestfay
owdingcray ownday onay eitheray andhay omfray ethay owlay oothillsfay ofay ethay ountainsmay.
Uddenlysay ethay allcay ofay aay ullbay elkay amecay echoingay ownday oughthray ethay etway
oodlandway onay ouray ightray, eyondbay ethay ookbray, eeminglysay esslay anthay alfhay aay
ilemay offay; anday asway answereday byay aay aintfay, ar-offfay allcay omfray aay ivalray onay ethay
ountainmay eyondbay. Instantlyay altinghay ethay aintray, Oodyway anday Iay ippedslay offay
ouray orseshay, ossedcray ethay ookbray, anday artedstay otay ill-huntstay ethay irstfay ullbay.

Inay isthay aceplay ethay orestfay asway omposedcay ofay ethay Esternway amaracktay; ethay
argelay, alltay eestray oodstay ellway apartay, anday erethay asway uchmay ownday imbertay, utbay
ethay oundgray asway overedcay ithway eepday etway ossmay, overay ichwhay eway odtray ilentlysay.
Ethay elkay asway avelingtray up-winday, utbay owlyslay, oppingstay ontinuallycay otay awpay
ethay oundgray anday eshthray ethay ushesbay ithway ishay antlersay. Ehay asway eryvay oisynay,
allengingchay everyay inutemay oray otway, eingbay oubtlessday uchmay exciteday byay ethay
eighborhoodnay ofay ishay ivalray onay ethay ountainmay. Eway ollowedfay, Oodyway eadinglay,
uidedgay byay ethay incessantay allingcay.

Itay asway eryvay excitingay asay eway eptcray owardtay ethay eatgray ullbay, anday ethay
allengechay oundedsay earernay anday earernay. Ilewhay eway ereway illstay atay omesay
istanceday ethay ealingpay otesnay ereway ikelay osethay ofay aay uglebay, eliveredday inay otway
arsbay, irstfay isingray, enthay abruptlyay allingfay; asay eway ewdray earernay eythay ooktay
onay aay arshhay uealingsqay oundsay. Eachay allcay ademay ouray einsvay illthray; itay oundedsay
ikelay ethay cryay ofay omesay ugehay eastbay ofay eypray. Atay astlay eway eardhay ethay oarray ofay
ethay allengechay otnay eightyay ardsyay offay. Ealingstay orwardfay eethray oray ourfay
ardsyay, Iay awsay ethay ipstay ofay ethay ornshay oughthray aay assmay ofay eadday imbertay anday
oungyay owthgray, anday Iay ippedslay otay oneay idesay otay etgay aay eanclay otshay.

Eeingsay usay utbay otnay akingmay outay atwhay eway ereway, anday ullfay ofay iercefay anday
insolentay excitementay, ethay apitiway ullbay eppedstay oldlybay owardtay usay ithway aay
atelystay ingingsway aitgay. Enthay ehay oodstay otionlessmay, acingfay usay, arelybay
iftyfay ardsyay awayay, ishay andsomehay elve-tinedtway antlersay ossedtay aloftay, asay
ehay eldhay ishay eadhay ithway ethay ordlylay acegray ofay ishay indkay. Iay iredfay intoay ishay
estchay, anday asay ehay urnedtay Iay acedray orwardfay anday otshay imhay inay ethay ankflay; utbay
ethay econdsay ulletbay asway otnay eedednay, orfay ethay irstfay oundway asway ortalmay, anday
ehay ellfay eforebay oinggay iftyfay ardsyay.

Ethay eadday elkay aylay amongay ethay oungyay evergreensay. Ethay ugehay, apelyshay odybay asway
etsay onay egslay atthay ereway asay ongstray asay eelstay odsray, anday etyay enderslay, eanclay,
anday oothsmay; eythay ereway inay olorcay aay eautifulbay arkday ownbray, ontrastingcay ellway
ithway ethay ellowishyay ofay ethay odybay. Ethay ecknay anday oatthray ereway arnishedgay ithway
aay anemay ofay onglay airhay; ethay etrysymmay ofay ethay eatgray ornshay etsay offay ethay inefay,
elicateday ineslay ofay ethay oblenay eadhay. Ehay adhay eenbay allowingway, asay elkay areay
ondfay ofay oingday, anday ethay ieddray udmay ungclay inay atchespay otay ishay ankflay; aay abstay
inay ethay aunchhay owedshay atthay ehay adhay eenbay overcomeay inay attlebay byay omesay astermay
ullbay owhay adhay urnedtay imhay outay ofay ethay erdhay.

Eway utcay offay ethay eadhay, anday orebay itay ownday otay ethay aintray. Ethay orseshay owdedcray
ogethertay, ortingsnay, ithway eirthay earsay ickedpray orwardfay, asay eythay eltsmay ethay
oodblay. Eway alsoay ooktay ethay oinslay ithway usay, asay eway ereway outay ofay eatmay, oughthay
ullbay elkay inay ethay uttingray easonsay isay otnay eryvay oodgay. Ethay ainray adhay angedchay
otay aay eadystay ownpourday enwhay eway againay otgay underay ayway. Otway oray eethray ilesmay
urtherfay eway itchedpay ampcay, inay aay umpclay ofay inespay onay aay illockhay inay ethay ottombay
ofay ethay alleyvay, artingstay othay iresfay ofay itchypay umpsstay eforebay ethay entstay, otay
dryay ouray etway ingsthay.

Extnay ayday openeday ithway ogfay anday oldcay ainray. Ethay encheddray ack-animalspay, enwhay
ivendray intoay ampcay, oodstay opinglymay, ithway oopingdray eadshay anday archeday acksbay;
eythay oanedgray anday untedgray asay ethay oadslay ereway acedplay onay eirthay acksbay anday
ethay inchescay ightenedtay, ethay ackerspay acingbray oneay ootfay againstay ethay ackpay
otay etgay aay urchasepay asay eythay auledhay inay onay ethay ash-ropelay. Aay ormystay orningmay
isay aay ialtray otay empertay; ethay ackspay areay etway anday eavyhay, anday ethay oldcay akesmay
ethay orkway evenay oremay anthay usuallyay ardhay onay ethay andshay. Byay entay eway okebray
ampcay. Itay eedsnay etweenbay otway anday eethray ourshay otay eakbray ampcay anday etgay uchsay
aay aintray operlypray ackedpay; onceay artedstay, ouray ay’sday ourneyjay asway ixsay otay
eightay ourshay, akingmay onay althay. Eway artedstay upay aay eepstay, ine-cladpay ountainmay
idesay, okenbray byay iffsclay. Myay unting-shoeshay, oughthay omfortablecay, ereway olday
anday inthay, anday etlay ethay aterway oughthray ikelay aay ievesay. Onay ethay optay ofay ethay
irstfay ateauplay, erewhay ackblay ucespray ovesgray ereway ewnstray acrossay ethay assygray
urfacesay, eway awsay aay andbay ofay elkay, owscay anday alvescay, ottingtray offay oughthray
ethay ainray. Enthay eway ungedplay ownday intoay aay eepday alleyvay, anday, ossingcray itay,
aay ardhay imbclay ooktay usay otay ethay optay ofay aay eatgray arebay ablelandtay, eakblay anday
ind-sweptway. Eway assedpay ittlelay alpineay akeslay, ingedfray ithway atteringscay
arfdway evergreensay. Owsnay aylay inay iftsdray onay ethay orthnay idessay ofay ethay ulliesgay;
aay uttingcay indway ewblay ethay icyay ainray inay ouray acesfay. Orfay otway oray eethray ourshay
eway aveledtray owardtay ethay urtherfay edgeay ofay ethay ablelandtay. Inay oneay aceplay aay
ikespay ullbay elkay oodstay alfhay aay ilemay offay, inay ethay openay; ehay aveledtray otay anday
ofray, atchingway usay.

Asay eway earednay ethay edgeay ethay ormstay ulledlay, anday alepay, ateryway unshinesay
eamedglay oughthray ethay iftsray inay ethay ow-scuddinglay oudsclay. Atay astlay ouray
orseshay oodstay onay ethay inkbray ofay aay oldbay iffclay. Eepday ownday eneathbay ouray eetfay
aylay ethay ildway anday onelylay alleyvay ofay O-ocEantway Asspay, alledway inay onay eitheray
andhay byay uggedray ountainmay ainschay, eirthay anksflay arredscay anday ashedgay byay
ecipicepray anday asmchay. Eyondbay, inay aay ildernessway ofay aggedjay anday arrenbay
eakspay, etchedstray ethay Oshonesshay. Atay ethay iddlemay ointpay ofay ethay asspay, otway
eamsstray elledway ownday omfray eitheray idesay. Atay irstfay eachay owedflay inay utbay oneay
edbay, utbay oonsay ividedday intoay otway; eachay ofay ethay intway anchesbray enthay oinedjay
ethay ikelay anchbray ofay ethay ookbray oppositeay, anday eptsway oneay otay ethay eastay
anday oneay otay ethay estway, onay eirthay onglay ourneyjay otay ethay otway eatgray oceansay.
Eythay anray asay apidray ooksbray, oughthray etway eadowsmay anday illow-flatsway, ethay
easternay otay ethay Ellowstoneyay, ethay esternway otay ethay Akesnay. Ethay arkday inepay
orestsfay eptsway ownday omfray ethay anksflay anday owerlay idgesray ofay ethay ountainsmay
otay ethay edgesay ofay ethay arshymay alleyvay. Aboveay emthay uttedjay aygray ockray eakspay,
owdriftssnay inglyay inay ethay entsray atthay eamedsay eirthay orthernnay acesfay. Arfay
elowbay usay, omfray aay eatgray asinbay atay ethay ootfay ofay ethay iffclay, illedfay ithway ethay
inepay orestfay, oseray ethay usicalmay allengechay ofay aay ullbay elkay; anday eway awsay aay
andbay ofay owscay anday alvescay ookinglay ikelay icemay asay eythay anray amongay ethay eestray.

Itay asway ettinggay atelay, anday afteray omesay earchsay eway ailedfay otay indfay anyay ailtray
eadinglay ownday; osay atay astlay eway ungedplay overay ethay inkbray atay aay enturevay. Itay
asway eryvay oughray amblingscray, oppingdray omfray enchbay otay enchbay, anday inay acesplay
itay asway otnay onlyay ifficultday utbay angerousday orfay ethay oadedlay ack-animalspay.
