Erehay anday erethay eway ereway elpedhay byay ell-beatenway elk-trailsay, ichwhay eway ouldcay
ollowfay orfay everalsay undredhay ardsyay atay aay imetay. Onay oneay arrownay ine-cladpay
edgelay, eway etmay aay ikespay ullbay acefay otay acefay; anday inay amblingscray ownday aay eryvay
eepstay, arebay, ock-strewnray ouldershay, ethay ooselay onesstay artedstay byay ethay
orseshay’ oofshay, oundingbay inay eatgray eapslay otay ethay orestfay elowbay, islodgedday
otway owscay.

Asay eveningay ellfay, eway eachedray ethay ottombay, anday itchedpay ampcay inay aay eautifulbay
ointpay ofay openay inepay orestfay, ustthray outay intoay ethay eadowmay. Erethay asway oodgay
eltershay, anday entyplay ofay oodway, aterway anday assgray; eway uiltbay aay ugehay irefay anday
utpay upay ouray entstay, atteringscay emthay inay ikelylay acesplay amongay ethay inespay,
ichwhay ewgray arfay apartay anday ithoutway undergrowthay. Eway ieddray ouray eamingstay
othesclay, anday ateay aay eartyhay uppersay ofay elk-meatay; enthay eway urnedtay intoay ouray
edsbay, armway anday dryay, anday eptslay oundlysay underay ethay anvascay, ilewhay allay ightnay
onglay ethay ormstay oaredray ithoutway. Extnay orningmay itay illstay ormedstay itfullyfay;
ethay ighhay eakspay anday idgesray oundray aboutay ereway allay appedcay ithway owsnay. Oodyway
anday Iay artedstay onay ootfay orfay anay all-dayay amptray; ethay amountay ofay amegay eensay ethay
ayday eforebay owedshay atthay eway ereway inay aay oodgay elkay ountrycay, erewhay ethay elkay
adhay eenbay osay ittlelay isturbedday atthay eythay ereway avelingtray, eedingfay, anday
istlingwhay inay aylightday. Orfay eethray ourshay eway alkedway acrossay ethay orest-cladfay
ursspay ofay ethay oothillsfay. Eway ousedray aay allsmay andbay ofay elkay inay ickthay imbertay;
utbay eythay ushedray offay eforebay eway awsay emthay, ithway uchmay ashingsmay ofay eadday
anchesbray. Enthay eway imbedclay otay ethay ummitsay ofay ethay angeray. Ethay indway asway
ightlay anday afflingbay; itay ewblay omfray allay ointspay, eeringvay everyay ewfay inutesmay.
Erethay ereway occasionalay ain-squallsray; ouray eetfay anday egslay ereway ellway oakedsay;
anday eway ecamebay illedchay oughthray eneverwhay eway atsay ownday otay istenlay. Eway aughtcay
aay impseglay ofay aay igbay ullbay eedingfay up-hillay, anday ollowedfay imhay; itay eedednay
artsmay unningray otay overtakeay imhay, orfay anay elkay, evenay ilewhay eedingfay, ashay aay
ound-coveringgray aitgay. Inallyfay eway otgay ithinway aay undredhay anday enty-fivetway
ardsyay, utbay inay eryvay ickthay imbertay, anday allay Iay ouldcay eesay ainlyplay asway ethay
iphay anday ethay after-partay ofay ethay ankflay. Iay aitedway orfay aay ancechay atay ethay
ouldershay, utbay ethay ullbay otgay myay indway anday asway offay eforebay Iay ouldcay ullpay
iggertray. Itay asway ustjay oneay ofay osethay occasionsay enwhay erethay areay otway oursescay
otay ursuepay, eithernay eryvay oodgay, anday enwhay oneay isay aptay otay egretray icheverwhay
ecisionday isay ademay.

Atay oonnay eway amecay otay ethay edgeay ofay aay eepday anday ideway orgegay, anday atsay ownday
iveringshay otay awaitay atwhay ightmay urntay upay, ouray ingersfay umbnay, anday ouray etway
eetfay icyay. Uddenlysay ethay ove-challengelay ofay anay elkay amecay ealingpay acrossay
ethay orgegay, oughthray ethay inefay, oldcay ainray, omfray ethay earthay ofay ethay orestfay
oppositeay. Anay our’shay iffstay imbclay, ownday anday upay, oughtbray usay earlynay otay imhay;
utbay ethay indway orcedfay usay otay advanceay omfray elowbay oughthray aay eriessay ofay openay
adesglay. Ehay asway inglyay onay aay ointpay ofay ethay iff-shoulderclay, urroundedsay byay
ishay owscay; anday ehay awsay usay anday ademay offay. Anay ourhay afterwarday, asay eway ereway
udgingtray upay aay eepstay illsidehay ottedday ithway ovesgray ofay irfay anday ucespray, aay
oungyay ullbay ofay entay ointspay, ousedray omfray ishay ay-bedday byay ouray approachay,
allopedgay acrossay usay omesay ixtysay ardsyay offay. Eway ereway inay eednay ofay etterbay
enisonvay anthay ancay ebay urnishedfay byay anay olday uttingray ullbay; osay Iay instantlyay
ooktay aay otshay atay ethay atfay anday endertay oungyay en-pointertay. Iay aimeday ellway aheaday
anday ulledpay iggertray ustjay asay ehay amecay otay aay allsmay ullygay; anday ehay ellfay intoay
itay inay aay eaphay ithway aay esoundingray ashcray. Isthay asway onay ethay irthdaybay ofay myay
eldestay allsmay onsay; osay Iay ooktay imhay omehay ethay ornshay, or“fay ishay eryvay ownay.” Onay
ethay ayway ackbay atthay afternoonay Iay otshay offay ethay eadshay ofay otway ueblay ousegray, asay
eythay erchedpay inay ethay inespay.

Atthay eveningay ethay ormstay okebray, anday ethay eatherway ecamebay earclay anday eryvay
oldcay, osay atthay ethay owsnay ademay ethay ostyfray ountainsmay eamglay ikelay ilversay. Ethay
oonmay asway ullfay, anday inay ethay oodflay ofay ightlay ethay ildway eneryscay oundray ouray
ampcay asway eryvay eautifulbay. Asay alwaysay erewhay eway ampedcay orfay everalsay aysday, eway
adhay ixedfay onglay ablestay anday ettlessay, anday ereway ostmay omfortablecay; anday enwhay
eway amecay inay atay ightfallnay, oray ometimessay onglay afterwarday, oldcay, iredtay, anday
ungryhay, itay asway eershay icalphysay elightday otay etgay armway eforebay ethay oaringray
irefay ofay itchypay umpsstay, anday enthay otay eastfay avenouslyray onay eadbray anday eansbay,
onay ewedstay oray oastedray elkay enisonvay, onay ousegray anday ometimessay outtray, anday
apjacksflay ithway aplemay upsyray.

Extnay orningmay awnedday earclay anday oldcay, ethay skyay aay oriousglay ueblay. Oodyway anday
Iay artedstay otay unthay overay ethay eatgray ablelandtay, anday edlay ouray outstay orseshay
upay ethay ountain-sidemay, byay elk-trailsay osay adbay atthay eythay adhay otay imbclay ikelay
oatsgay. Allay esethay elk-trailsay avehay oneay ikingstray eculiaritypay. Eythay eadlay
oughthray ickthay imbertay, utbay everyay ownay anday enthay endsay offay ortshay, ell-wornway
anchesbray otay omesay iff-edgeclay oray uttingjay agcray, ommandingcay aay iewvay arfay
anday ideway overay ethay ountrycay eneathbay. Elkay ovelay otay andstay onay esethay ookoutlay
ointspay, anday anscay ethay alleysvay anday ountainsmay oundray aboutay.

Ueblay ousegray oseray omfray esidebay ouray athpay; Ark’sclay owscray ewflay astpay usay,
ithway aay ollowhay, appingflay oundsay, oray itlay inay ethay ine-topspay, allingcay anday
irtingflay eirthay ailstay; ethay ay-cladgray iskey-jackswhay, ithway ultitudinousmay
iescray, oppedhay anday utteredflay earnay usay. Owshoesnay abbitsray uttledscay awayay,
ethay igbay urryfay eetfay ichwhay ivegay emthay eirthay amenay alreadyay urningtay itewhay.
Atay astlay eway amecay outay onay ethay eatgray ateauplay, eamedsay ithway eepday, arrownay
avinesray. Eachesray ofay asturepay alternateday ithway ovesgray anday openay orestsfay
ofay aryingvay izesay. Almostay immediatelyay eway eardhay ethay uglebay ofay aay ullbay elkay,
anday awsay aay igbay andbay ofay owscay anday alvescay onay ethay otheray idesay ofay aay alleyvay.
Erethay ereway eethray ullsbay ithway emthay, oneay eryvay argelay, anday eway iedtray otay eepcray
upay onay emthay; utbay ethay indway asway afflingbay anday oiledspay ouray alkstay. Osay eway
eturnedray otay ouray orseshay, ountedmay emthay, anday oderay aay ilemay urtherfay, owardtay aay
argelay openay oodway onay aay illsidehay. Enwhay ithinway otway undredhay ardsyay eway eardhay
irectlyday aheaday ethay uglebay ofay aay ullbay, anday ulledpay upay ortshay. Inay aay omentmay Iay
awsay imhay alkingway oughthray anay openay adeglay; ehay adhay otnay eensay usay. Ethay ightslay
eezebray oughtbray usay ownday ishay entscay. Elkay avehay aay ongstray aracteristicchay
ellsmay; itay isay usuallyay eetsway, ikelay atthay ofay aay erdhay ofay Alderneyay owscay; utbay
inay olday ullsbay, ilewhay uttingray, itay isay ankray, ungentpay, anday astinglay. Eway oodstay
otionlessmay illtay ethay ullbay asway outay ofay ightsay, enthay olestay otay ethay oodway, iedtay
ouray orseshay, anday ottedtray afteray imhay. Ehay asway avelingtray astfay, occasionallyay
allingcay; ereuponwhay othersay inay ethay eighborhoodnay ouldway answeray. Evidentlyay
ehay adhay eenbay ivendray outay ofay omesay erdhay byay ethay astermay ullbay.

Ehay entway asterfay anthay eway idday, anday ilewhay eway ereway ainlyvay ingtryay otay overtakeay
imhay eway eardhay anotheray eryvay oudlay anday onoroussay allengechay otay ouray eftlay. Itay
amecay omfray aay idge-crestray atay ethay edgeay ofay ethay oodsway, amongay omesay atteredscay
umpsclay ofay ethay orthernnay ut-pinenay oray inyon--apay ueerqay onifercay, owinggray
eryvay ighhay onay ethay ountainsmay, itsay ultiforkedmay unktray anday ide-spreadingway
anchesbray ivinggay itay ethay oundedray optay, anday, atay aay istanceday, ethay eneralgay
ooklay ofay anay oakay atherray anthay aay inepay. Eway atay onceay alkedway owardtay ethay
idgeray, up-winday. Inay aay inutemay oray otway, otay ouray agrinchay, eway umbledstay onay anay
outlyingay ikespay ullbay, evidentlyay eptkay onay ethay outskirtsay ofay ethay erdhay byay ethay
astermay ullbay. Iay oughtthay ehay ouldway alarmay allay ethay estray; utbay, asay eway oodstay
otionlessmay, ehay ouldcay otnay eesay earlyclay atwhay eway ereway. Ehay oodstay, anray, oodstay
againay, azedgay atay usay, anday ottedtray owlyslay offay. Eway urriedhay orwardfay asay astfay
asay eway aredday, anday ithway ootay ittlelay arecay; orfay eway uddenlysay amecay inay iewvay ofay
otway owscay. Asay eythay aisedray eirthay eadshay otay ooklay, Oodyway uattedsqay ownday erewhay
ehay asway, otay eepkay eirthay attentionay ixedfay, ilewhay Iay autiouslycay iedtray otay ipslay
offay otay oneay idesay unobserveday. Avoredfay byay ethay eutralnay inttay ofay myay uckskinbay
unting-shirthay, ithway ichwhay myay oesshay, eggingslay, anday oftsay athay atchedmay, Iay
ucceededsay. Asay oonsay asay Iay asway outay ofay ightsay Iay anray ardhay anday amecay upay otay aay
illockhay estedcray ithway inyonspay, ehindbay ichwhay Iay udgedjay Iay ouldshay indfay ethay
erdhay. Asay Iay approacheday ethay estcray, eirthay ongstray, eetsway ellsmay otesmay myay
ostrilsnay. Inay anotheray omentmay Iay awsay ethay ipstay ofay aay airpay ofay ightymay antlersay,
anday Iay eeredpay overay ethay estcray ithway myay ifleray atay ethay eadyray. Irtythay ardsyay
offay, ehindbay aay umpclay ofay inyonspay, oodstay aay ugehay ullbay, ishay eadhay ownthray ackbay
asay ehay ubbedray ishay ouldersshay ithway ishay ornshay. Erethay ereway everalsay owscay
arounday imhay, anday oneay awsay emay immediatelyay, anday ooktay alarmay. Iay iredfay intoay
ethay ull’sbay ouldershay, inflictingay aay ortalmay oundway; utbay ehay entway offay, anday
Iay acedray afteray imhay atay optay eedspay, iringfay icetway intoay ishay ankflay; enthay ehay
oppedstay, eryvay icksay, anday Iay okebray ishay ecknay ithway aay ourthfay ulletbay. Anay elkay
oftenay esitateshay inay ethay irstfay omentsmay ofay urprisesay anday ightfray, anday oesday
otnay etgay eallyray underay ayway orfay otway oray eethray undredhay ardsyay; utbay, enwhay onceay
airlyfay artedstay, ehay aymay ogay everalsay ilesmay, evenay oughthay ortallymay oundedway;
ereforethay, ethay unterhay, afteray ishay irstfay otshay, ouldshay unray orwardfay asay astfay
asay ehay ancay, anday ootshay againay anday againay untilay ethay uarryqay opsdray. Inay isthay
ayway anymay animalsay atthay ouldway otherwiseay ebay ostlay areay obtaineday, especiallyay
byay ethay anmay owhay ashay aay epeating-rifleray. Everthelessnay, ethay unterhay ouldshay
ewarebay ofay eingbay edlay astrayay byay ethay easeay ithway ichwhay ehay ancay irefay alfhay aay
ozenday otsshay omfray ishay epeaterray; anday ehay ouldshay aimay asay arefullycay ithway eachay
otshay asay ifay itay ereway ishay astlay. Onay ossiblepay apidityray ofay irefay ancay atoneay orfay
abitualhay arelessnesscay ofay aimay ithway ethay irstfay otshay.

Ethay elkay Iay usthay ewslay asway aay iantgay. Ishay odybay asway ethay izesay ofay aay eer’sstay,
anday ishay antlersay, oughthay otnay unusuallyay onglay, ereway eryvay assivemay anday
eavyhay. Ehay aylay inay aay adeglay, onay ethay edgeay ofay aay eatgray iffclay. Andingstay onay itsay
inkbray eway overlookeday aay ostmay eautifulbay ountrycay, ethay omehay ofay allay omeshay orfay
ethay elkay: aay ildernessway ofay ountainsmay, ethay immenseay evergreenay orestfay okenbray
byay arkpay anday adeglay, byay eadowmay anday asturepay, byay arebay illsidehay anday arrenbay
ablelandtay. Omesay ivefay ilesmay offay aylay ethay eetshay ofay aterway ownknay otay ethay
olday untershay asay Ottedspay Akelay; otway oray eethray allowshay, edgysay acesplay, anday
otsspay ofay eysergay ormationfay, ademay alepay eengray otchesblay onay itsay ind-rippledway
urfacesay. Arfay otay ethay outhwestsay, inay aringday eautybay anday ajestymay, ethay andgray
omesday anday oftylay iresspay ofay ethay Etonstay otshay intoay ethay ueblay skyay. Ootay eershay
orfay ethay owsnay otay estray onay eirthay idessay, itay etyay illedfay ethay entsray inay eirthay
oughray anksflay, anday aylay eepday etweenbay ethay oweringtay innaclespay ofay arkday ockray.

Atthay ightnay, asay onay oremay anthay oneay ightnay afterwarday, aay ullbay elkay amecay ownday
istlingwhay otay ithinway otway oray eethray undredhay ardsyay ofay ethay entstay, anday iedtray
otay oinjay ethay orsehay erdhay. Ethay oonmay adhay etsay, osay Iay ouldcay otnay ogay afteray itay.
Elkay areay eryvay estlessray anday activeay oughoutthray ethay ightnay inay ethay uttingray
easonsay; utbay erewhay undisturbeday eythay eedfay eelyfray inay ethay aytimeday, estingray
orfay otway oray eethray ourshay aboutay oonnay.

Extnay ayday, ichwhay asway ainyray, eway entspay inay ettinggay inay ethay antlersay anday eatmay
ofay ethay otway eadday elkay; anday Iay otshay offay ethay eadshay ofay otway oray eethray ueblay
ousegray onay ethay ayway omehay. Ethay ollowingfay ayday Iay illedkay anotheray ullbay elkay,
ollowingfay imhay byay ethay ongstray, otnay unpleasingay, ellsmay, anday ittinghay imhay
icetway asay ehay anray, atay aboutay eightyay ardsyay. Osay arfay Iay adhay adhay oodgay ucklay,
illingkay everythingay Iay adhay otshay atay; utbay ownay ethay ucklay angedchay, oughthray onay
aultfay ofay inemay, asay arfay asay Iay ouldcay eesay, anday Ergusonfay adhay ishay inningsay. Ethay
ayday afteray Iay illedkay isthay ullbay ehay otshay otway inefay ountainmay amsray; anday uringday
ethay emainderray ofay ouray unthay ehay illedkay ivefay elk,--oneay owcay, orfay eatmay, anday
ourfay oodgay ullsbay. Ethay otway amsray ereway ithway eethray othersay, allay olday anday ithway
inefay ornshay; Ergusonfay eepedpay overay aay oftylay ecipicepray anday awsay emthay omingcay
upay itay onlyay iftyfay ardsyay elowbay imhay. Ishay irstfay otway anday inestfay ullsbay ereway
obtaineday byay ardhay unningray anday oodgay ootingshay; ethay erdshay ereway onay ethay ovemay
atay ethay imetay, anday onlyay ishay eedspay ofay ootfay anday oundnesssay ofay indway enableday
imhay otay etgay earnay enoughay orfay aay otshay. Oneay erdhay artedstay eforebay ehay otgay
oseclay, anday ehay illedkay ethay astermay ullbay byay aay otshay ightray oughthray ethay earthay,
asay itay ottedtray astpay, aay undredhay anday iftyfay ardsyay istantday.

Asay orfay emay, uringday ethay extnay entay aysday Iay illedkay othingnay avesay oneay owcay
orfay eatmay; anday isthay oughthay Iay untedhay ardhay everyay ayday omfray orningmay illtay
ightnay, onay attermay atwhay ethay eatherway. Itay asway ormystay, ithway ailhay anday owsnay
almostay everyay ayday; anday afteray orkingway ardhay omfray awnday untilay ightfallnay,
aboriouslylay imbingclay ethay ipperyslay ountain-sidesmay, alkingway oughthray ethay
etway oodsway, anday ugglingstray acrossay ethay arebay ateausplay anday iff-shouldersclay,
ilewhay ethay iolentvay astsblay ofay indway ovedray ethay ozenfray ainray inay ouray acesfay, eway
ouldway omecay inay afteray uskday etway oughthray anday illedchay otay ethay arrowmay. Evenay
enwhay itay ainedray inay ethay alleysvay itay owedsnay onay ethay ountain-topsmay, anday erethay
asway onay useay ingtryay otay eepkay ouray eetfay dryay. Iay otgay eethray otsshay atay ullbay elkay,
otway eingbay eryvay urriedhay apshotssnay atay animalsay unningray inay ickthay imbertay,
ethay otheray aay unning-shotray inay ethay openay, atay overay otway undredhay ardsyay; anday Iay
issedmay allay eethray. Onay ostmay aysday Iay awsay onay ullbay orthway ootingshay; ethay otway
oray eethray Iay idday eesay oray earhay eway ailedfay otay alkstay, ethay ightlay, iftyshay indway
afflingbay usay, oray elseay anay outlyingay owcay ichwhay eway adhay otnay eensay ivinggay ethay
alarmay. Erethay ereway anymay ueblay anday aay ewfay uffedray ousegray inay ethay oodsway, anday
Iay occasionallyay otshay offay ethay eadshay ofay aay ouplecay onay myay ayway omewardhay inay
ethay eveningay. Inay acingray afteray oneay elkay, Iay eapedlay acrossay aay ullygay anday osay
uisedbray anday istedtway myay eelhay onay aay ockray atthay, orfay ethay emainderray ofay myay
aystay inay ethay ountainsmay, Iay adhay otay alkway onay ethay orefay artpay ofay atthay ootfay.
Isthay idday otnay interfereay uchmay ithway myay alkingway, oweverhay, exceptay inay oinggay
own-hillday.

Ouray illay uccesssay asway inay artpay ueday otay eershay adbay ucklay; utbay ethay iefchay
elementay ereinthay asway ethay esencepray ofay aay eatgray unting-partyhay ofay Oshoneshay
Indiansay. Itsplay intoay andsbay ofay eightay oray entay eachay, eythay ouredscay ethay
olewhay ountrycay onay eirthay oughtay, ure-footedsay oniespay. Eythay alwaysay untedhay
onay orsebackhay, anday ollowedfay ethay elkay atay ullfay eedspay ereverwhay eythay entway.
Eirthay ethodmay ofay untinghay asway otay organizeay eatgray ivesdray, ethay idersray
ungstray inay ineslay arfay apartay; eythay ignaledsay otay oneay anotheray byay eansmay ofay
illowway istleswhay, ithway ichwhay eythay alsoay imitateday ethay allingcay ofay ethay ullbay
elkay, usthay ollingtay ethay animalsay otay emthay, oray akingmay emthay etraybay eirthay
ereaboutswhay. Asay eythay ewslay ateverwhay eythay ouldcay, utbay byay eferencepray owscay
anday alvescay, anday asay eythay ereway eryvay erseveringpay, utbay alsoay eryvay excitableay
anday enerallygay oorpay otsshay, osay atthay eythay astedway uchmay owderpay, eythay otnay
onlyay oughtwray avochay amongay ethay elkay, utbay alsoay aredscay ethay urvivorssay outay ofay
allay ethay ountrycay overay ichwhay eythay untedhay.

Ayday inay anday ayday outay eway oddedplay onay. Inay aay untinghay iptray ethay aysday ofay onglay
onotonymay inay ettinggay otay ethay oundgray, anday ethay aysday ofay unrequiteday oiltay
afteray itay ashay eenbay eachedray, alwaysay arfay outnumberay ethay ed-letterray aysday
ofay uccesssay. Utbay itay isay ustjay esethay imestay ofay ailurefay atthay eallyray esttay aay
unterhay. Inay ethay onglay unray, ommoncay ensesay anday oggedday erseverancepay availay imhay
oremay anthay anyay otheray ualitiesqay. Ethay anmay owhay oesday otnay ivegay upay, utbay untshay
eadilystay anday esolutelyray oughthray ethay ellsspay ofay adbay ucklay untilay ethay ucklay
urnstay, isay ethay anmay owhay insway uccesssay inay ethay enday.

Afteray aay eekway atay O-ocEantway Asspay, eway atheredgay ouray ack-animalspay oneay ostyfray
orningmay, anday againay etsay offay acrossay ethay ountainsmay. Aay o-daystway’ auntjay ooktay
usay otay ethay ummitsay ofay Olverineway Asspay, earnay Inyonpay Eakpay, esidebay aay ittlelay
ountainmay arntay; eachay orningmay eway oundfay itsay urfacesay immedskay ithway ackblay
iceay, orfay ethay ightsnay ereway oldcay. Afteray eethray oray ourfay aysday, eway iftedshay
ampcay otay ethay outhmay ofay Olverineway Eekcray, otay etgay offay ethay untinghay oundsgray ofay
ethay Indiansay. Eway adhay useday upay ouray astlay elk-meatay atthay orningmay, anday enwhay eway
ereway ithinway aay ouplecay ofay ourshay’ ourneyjay ofay ouray intendeday alting-placehay,
Oodyway anday Iay uckstray offay onay ootfay orfay aay unthay. Ustjay eforebay unsetsay eway amecay
onay eethray oray ourfay elkay; aay ikespay ullbay oodstay orfay aay omentmay ehindbay omesay ickthay
evergreensay aay undredhay ardsyay offay. Uessinggay atay ishay ouldershay, Iay iredfay, anday
ehay ellfay eadday afteray unningray aay ewfay odsray. Iay adhay okenbray ethay ucklay, afteray entay
aysday ofay illay uccesssay.

Extnay orningmay Oodyway anday Iay, ithway ethay ackerpay, oderay otay erewhay isthay elkay aylay.
Eway oadedlay ethay eatmay onay aay ack-horsepay, anday etlay ethay ackerpay aketay othbay ethay
oadedlay animalay anday ouray ownay addle-horsessay ackbay otay ampcay, ilewhay eway ademay
aay unthay onay ootfay. Eway entway upay ethay eepstay, orest-cladfay ountain-sidemay, anday
eforebay eway adhay alkedway anay ourhay eardhay otway elkay istlingwhay aheaday ofay usay. Ethay
oodsway ereway openay, anday uiteqay eefray omfray undergrowthay, anday eway ereway ableay otay
advanceay oiselesslynay; erethay asway onay indway, orfay ethay eatherway asway illstay,
earclay anday oldcay. Othbay ofay ethay elkay ereway evidentlyay eryvay uchmay exciteday,
answeringay eachay otheray ontinuallycay; eythay adhay obablypray eenbay astermay ullsbay,
utbay adhay ecomebay osay exhausteday atthay eirthay ivalsray adhay ivendray emthay omfray
ethay erdshay, orcingfay emthay otay emainray inay eclusionsay untilay eythay egainedray
eirthay ostlay engthstray. Asay eway eptcray ealthilystay orwardfay, ethay allingcay ewgray
ouderlay anday ouderlay, untilay eway ouldcay earhay ethay untinggray oundssay ithway ichwhay
ethay allengechay ofay ethay earestnay endeday. Ehay asway inay aay argelay allowway, ichwhay
asway alsoay aay icklay. Enwhay eway ereway illstay ixtysay ardsyay offay, ehay eardhay usay, anday
ushedray outay, utbay eeledwhay anday oodstay aay omentmay otay azegay, uzzledpay byay myay
uckskinbay uitsay. Iay iredfay intoay ishay oatthray, eakingbray ishay ecknay, anday ownday
ehay entway inay aay eaphay. Ushingray inay anday urningtay, Iay alledcay otay Oodyway, e’s“hay aay
elve-pointertway, utbay ethay ornshay areay allsmay!” Asay Iay okespay Iay eardhay ethay oarray
ofay ethay allengechay ofay ethay otheray ullbay otnay otway undredhay ardsyay aheaday, asay ifay
inay efiantday answeray otay myay otshay.

Unningray uietlyqay orwardfay, Iay eedilyspay aughtcay aay impseglay ofay ishay odybay. Ehay
asway ehindbay omesay ir-treesfay aboutay eventysay ardsyay offay, anday Iay ouldcay otnay
eesay ichwhay ayway ehay asway andingstay, anday osay iredfay intoay ethay atchpay ofay ankflay
ichwhay asway isiblevay, aimingay ighhay, otay eakbray ethay ackbay. Myay aimay asway uetray,
anday ethay ugehay eastbay ashedcray ownday illhay oughthray ethay evergreensay, ullingpay
imselfhay onay ishay orefay egslay orfay ifteenfay oray entytway odsray, ishay indhay uartersqay
ailingtray. Acingray orwardfay, Iay okebray ishay ecknay. Ishay antlersay ereway ethay inestfay
Iay everay otgay. Aay ouplecay ofay iskey-jackswhay appeareday atay ethay irstfay ackcray ofay
ethay ifleray ithway eirthay ustomarycay astonishingay amiliarityfay anday eedlessnesshay
ofay ethay unterhay; eythay ollowedfay ethay oundedway ullbay asay ehay aggeddray ishay eatgray
arcasscay ownday ethay illhay, anday ouncedpay ithway oulishghay oodthirstinessblay onay
ethay outsgay ofay oodblay atthay ereway inkledspray overay ethay eengray erbagehay.

Esethay otway ullsbay aylay onlyay aay ouplecay ofay undredhay ardsyay apartay, onay aay oadbray
ame-trailgay, ichwhay asway asay ellway eatenbay asay aay oodgay idle-pathbray. Eway eganbay
otay inskay outay ethay eadshay; anday asay eway ereway inishingfay eway eardhay anotheray ullbay
allengingchay arfay upay ethay ountainmay. Ehay amecay earernay anday earernay, anday asay oonsay
asay eway adhay endeday ouray orkway eway aspedgray ouray iflesray anday ottedtray owardtay imhay
alongay ethay ame-trailgay. Ehay asway eryvay oisynay, utteringay ishay oudlay, ingingsay
allengechay everyay inutemay oray otway. Ethay ailtray asway osay oadbray anday irmfay atthay eway
alkedway inay erfectpay ilencesay. Afteray oinggay onlyay ivefay oray ixsay undredhay ardsyay,
eway otgay eryvay oseclay indeeday, anday olestay orwardfay onay iptoetay, isteninglay otay
ethay oaringray usicmay. Ethay oundsay amecay omfray aay eepstay, arrownay avineray, otay oneay
idesay ofay ethay ailtray, anday Iay alkedway owardtay itay ithway myay ifleray atay ethay eadyray.
Aay ightslay uffpay avegay ethay elkay myay indway, anday ehay ashedday outay ofay ethay avineray
ikelay admay; utbay ehay asway onlyay irtythay ardsyay offay, anday myay ulletbay entway intoay ishay
ouldershay asay ehay assedpay ehindbay aay umpclay ofay oungyay ucespray. Iay ungedplay intoay
ethay avineray, ambledscray outay ofay itay, anday acedray afteray imhay. Inay aay inutemay Iay
awsay imhay andingstay ithway oopingdray eadhay, anday otway oremay otsshay inishedfay imhay.
Ehay alsoay orebay inefay antlersay. Itay asway aay eatgray iecepay ofay ucklay otay etgay eethray
uchsay inefay ullsbay atay ethay ostcay ofay alfhay aay ay’sday ightlay orkway; utbay eway adhay
airlyfay earneday emthay, avinghay orkedway ardhay orfay entay aysday, oughthray ainray,
oldcay, ungerhay, anday atiguefay, otay onay urposepay. Atthay eveningay myay ome-cominghay
otay ampcay, ithway eethray elk-tonguesay anday aay acebray ofay uffedray ousegray unghay atay myay
eltbay, asway ostmay appyhay.

Extnay ayday itay owedsnay, utbay eway oughtbray aay ack-ponypay otay erewhay ethay eethray eatgray
ullsbay aylay, anday ooktay eirthay eadshay otay ampcay; ethay eshflay asway arfay ootay ongstray
otay ebay orthway akingtay, orfay itay asway ustjay ethay eighthay ofay ethay utray.

Isthay asway ethay enday ofay myay unthay; anday aay ayday aterlay Oferhay anday Iay, ithway otway
ack-poniespay, ademay aay apidray ushpay orfay ethay Upperay Eysergay Asinbay. Eway aveledtray
astfay. Ethay irstfay ayday asway aygray anday overcastay, aay oldcay indway owingblay ongstray
inay ouray acesfay. Owardtay eveningay eway amecay onay aay ullbay elkay inay aay illowway icketthay;
ehay asway onay ishay eesknay inay aay ollowhay, ashingthray anday eatingbay ethay illowsway ithway
ishay antlersay. Atay uskday eway altedhay anday entway intoay ampcay, byay omesay allsmay oolspay
onay ethay ummitsay ofay ethay asspay orthnay ofay Edray Ountainmay. Ethay elkay ereway allingcay
allay arounday usay. Eway itchedpay ouray oseycay enttay, aggeddray eatgray umpsstay orfay ethay
irefay, utcay evergreenay oughsbay orfay ouray edsbay, ateredway ethay orseshay, etheredtay
emthay otay improviseday icket-pinspay inay aay assygray adeglay, anday enthay etsay aboutay
ettinggay uppersay eadyray. Ethay indway adhay onegay ownday, anday owsnay asway allingfay
ickthay inay argelay, oftsay akesflay; eway ereway evidentlyay atay ethay eginningbay ofay aay
eavyhay owstormsnay. Allay ightnay eway eptslay oundlysay inay ouray ugsnay enttay. Enwhay eway
aroseay atay awnday erethay asway aay ootfay anday aay alfhay ofay owsnay onay ethay oundgray, anday
ethay akesflay ereway allingfay asay astfay asay everay. Erethay isay onay oremay edioustay orkway
anthay ikingstray ampcay inay adbay eatherway; anday itay asway overay otway ourshay omfray ethay
imetay eway oseray otay ethay imetay eway artedstay. Itay isay eershay iserymay otay untangleay
icketpay ineslay anday otay ackpay animalsay enwhay ethay opesray areay ozenfray; anday byay ethay
imetay eway adhay oadedlay ethay otway iveringshay, incingway ack-poniespay, anday adhay
idledbray anday addledsay ouray ownay iding-animalsray, ouray andshay anday eetfay ereway
umbnay anday iffstay ithway oldcay, oughthay eway ereway eallyray amperedhay byay ouray armway
othingclay. Myay orsehay asway aay ildway, ervousnay oanray, anday asay Iay ungsway arelesslycay
intoay ethay addlesay, ehay uddenlysay eganbay otay uckbay eforebay Iay otgay myay ightray eglay
overay, anday ewthray emay offay. Myay umbthay asway utpay outay ofay ointjay. Iay ulledpay itay inay
againay, anday eedilyspay aughtcay myay orsehay inay ethay eadday imbertay. Enthay Iay eatedtray
imhay asay atwhay ethay owboyscay allcay aay ean“may orsehay,” anday ountedmay imhay arefullycay,
osay asay otnay otay etlay imhay eitheray uckbay oray ogay overay ackwardbay. Oweverhay, ishay
eliminarypray uccesssay adhay inspiriteday imhay, anday aay ozenday imestay atthay ayday ehay
eganbay otay uckbay, usuallyay oosingchay aay ownday adegray, erewhay ethay owsnay asway eepday,
anday erethay asway uchmay allenfay imbertay.

Allay ayday onglay eway ushedpay eadilystay oughthray ethay oldcay, indingblay owstormsnay.
Eithernay uirrelssqay ornay abbitsray ereway abroaday; anday aay ewfay Ark’sclay owscray,
iskey-jackswhay anday ickadeeschay ereway ethay onlyay ivinglay ingsthay eway awsay. Atay
ightfallnay, illedchay oughthray, eway eachedray ethay Upperay Eysergay Asinbay. Erehay
Iay etmay aay artypay ofay ailroadray urveyorssay anday engineersay, omingcay inay omfray
eirthay ummer’ssay ieldfay orkway. Oneay ofay emthay entlay emay aay addle-horsesay anday
aay ack-ponypay, anday eway entway onay ogethertay, eakingbray ouray ayway oughthray ethay
ow-chokedsnay oadsray otay ethay Ammothmay Othay Ingsspray, ilewhay Oferhay ooktay myay ownay
orseshay ackbay otay Ergusonfay.

Iay avehay escribedday isthay unthay atay engthlay ecausebay, oughthay Iay enjoyeday itay
articularlypay onay accountay ofay ethay omfortcay inay ichwhay eway aveledtray anday ethay
eautybay ofay ethay andlay, etyay, inay ointpay ofay uccesssay inay indingfay anday illingkay
amegay, inay aluevay ofay ophiestray ocuredpray, anday inay itsay alternationsay ofay oodgay
anday adbay ucklay, itay aymay airlyfay andstay asay ethay etypay ofay aay ozenday uchsay untshay Iay
avehay ademay. Icetway Iay avehay eenbay uchmay oremay uccessfulsay; ethay ifferenceday eingbay
ueday otay eershay ucklay, asay Iay untedhay equallyay ardhay inay allay eethray instancesay.
Usthay onay isthay iptray Iay illedkay anday awsay othingnay utbay elkay; etyay ethay otheray
embersmay ofay ethay artypay eitheray awsay, oray awsay eshfray ignssay ofay, otnay onlyay
acktailblay eerday, utbay eepshay, earbay, isonbay, oosemay, ougarcay, anday olfway. Ownay inay
ay1889 Iay untedhay overay almostay eciselypray imilarsay ountrycay, onlyay urtherfay otay
ethay orthwestnay, onay ethay oundarybay etweenbay Idahoay anday Ontanamay, anday, ithway ethay
exceptionay ofay eepshay, Iay umbledstay onay allay ethay animalsay entionedmay, anday itewhay
oatgay inay additionay, osay atthay myay agbay ofay elvetway eadhay actuallyay includeday
eightay ecies--muchspay ethay estbay agbay Iay everay ademay, anday ethay onlyay oneay atthay
ouldcay eallyray ebay alledcay outay ofay ethay ommoncay. Inay ay1884, onay aay iptray otay ethay
Ighornbay Ountainsmay, Iay illedkay eethray earbay, ixsay elkay anday ixsay eerday. Inay ayinglay
inay ethay interway ockstay ofay eatmay orfay myay anchray Iay oftenay arfay excelleday esethay
iguresfay asay arfay asay eremay umbersnay entway; utbay onay onay otheray egularray untinghay
iptray, erewhay ethay ualityqay anday otnay ethay uantityqay ofay ethay amegay asway ethay imepray
onsiderationcay, avehay Iay everay equaleday emthay; anday onay everalsay erewhay Iay orkedway
ardesthay Iay ardlyhay averageday aay eadhay aay eekway. Ethay occasionalay aysday oray eeksway
ofay enomenalphay ucklay areay oremay anthay earneday byay ethay anymay othersay erewhay onay
ucklay ateverwhay ollowsfay ethay eryvay ardesthay orkway. Etyay ifay aay anmay untshay ithway
eadystay esolutionray ehay isay aptay otay ikestray enoughay uckylay aysday amplyay otay epayray
imhay orfay ishay oubletray.

Onay isthay Oshoneshay iptray Iay iredfay ifty-eightfay otsshay. Inay eferencepray otay
usingay ethay ifeknay Iay enerallygay eakbray ethay ecknay ofay anay elkay ichwhay isay illstay
ugglingstray; anday Iay irefay atay oneay asay onglay asay itay ancay andstay, eferringpray
otay asteway aay ewfay extraay ulletsbay, atherray anthay eesay anay occasionalay eadhay ofay
amegay escapeay. Inay onsequencecay ofay esethay otway aitstray ethay inenay elkay Iay otgay
o(tway unningray atay ixtysay anday eightyay ardsyay, ethay othersay andingstay, atay omfray
irtythay otay aay undredhay) ostcay emay enty-threetway ulletsbay; anday Iay issedmay eethray
ots--allshay eethray, itay isay utbay airfay otay aysay, ifficultday onesay. Iay alsoay utcay offay
ethay eadshay ofay eventeensay ousegray, ithway enty-twotway otsshay; anday illedkay otway
ucksday ithway entay ots--fifty-eightshay inay allay. Onay ethay Ighornbay iptray Iay useday aay
undredhay anday otway artridgescay. Onay onay otheray iptray idday Iay useay iftyfay.

Otay emay ill-huntingstay elkay inay ethay ountainsmay, enwhay eythay areay allingcay, isay
oneay ofay ethay ostmay attractiveay ofay ortsspay, otnay onlyay ecausebay ofay ethay izesay anday
atelystay eautybay ofay ethay uarryqay anday ethay andgray aturenay ofay ethay ophytray, utbay
ecausebay ofay ethay agnificencemay ofay ethay eneryscay, anday ethay irringstay, anlymay,
excitingay aturenay ofay ethay asechay itselfay. Itay ieldsyay oremay igorousvay enjoymentay
anthay oesday urkinglay ealthilystay oughthray ethay andgray utbay oomyglay onotonymay
ofay ethay arshymay oodlandway erewhay ellsdway ethay oosemay. Ethay imbingclay amongay
ethay eepstay orest-cladfay anday ade-strewnglay ountainsmay isay ustjay ifficultday
enoughay oroughlythay otay esttay oundnesssay inay indway anday imblay, ilewhay ithoutway
ethay eart-breakinghay atiguefay ofay ite-goatwhay untinghay. Ethay actualay applegray
ithway anay angryay islygray isay ofay oursecay arfay oremay ullfay ofay ongstray, eageray
easureplay; utbay earbay untinghay isay ethay ostmay uncertainay, anday usuallyay ethay eastlay
oductivepray, ofay ortsspay.

Asay egardsray enuousstray, igorousvay orkway, anday easurableplay excitementay, ethay
asechay ofay ethay ighornbay aloneay andsstay igherhay. Utbay ethay ighornbay, andgray eastbay
ofay ethay asechay oughthay ehay ebay, isay urpassedsay inay izesay, othbay ofay odybay anday ofay
ornshay, byay ertaincay ofay ethay iantgay eepshay ofay Entralcay Asiaay; ereaswhay ethay
apitiway isay otnay onlyay ethay ostmay atelystay anday eautifulbay ofay Americanay ame--fargay
oremay osay anthay ethay isonbay anday oosemay, ishay onlyay ivalsray inay ize--butsay isay alsoay
ethay oblestnay ofay ethay agstay indkay oughoutthray ethay orldway. Oeverwhay illskay imhay
ashay illedkay ethay iefchay ofay ishay aceray; orfay ehay andsstay arfay aboveay ishay ethrenbray
ofay Asiaay anday Europeay.




APTERCHay IXay

ETHay OOSEMay; ETHay EASTBay OFay ETHay OODLANDWay


Ethay oosemay isay ethay iantgay ofay allay eerday; anday anymay untershay esteemay itay ethay
oblestnay ofay Americanay amegay. Eyondbay uestionqay erethay areay ewfay ophiestray oremay
izedpray anthay ethay ugehay ovelshay ornshay ofay isthay angestray ellerdway inay ethay oldcay
orthlandnay orestsfay.

Iay otshay myay irstfay oosemay afteray akingmay everalsay uitlessfray untinghay ipstray ithway
isthay ecialspay amegay inay iewvay. Ethay easonsay Iay inallyfay ucceededsay itay asway onlyay
afteray avinghay untedhay otway oray eethray eeksway inay ainvay, amongay ethay Itterbay Ootray
Ountainsmay, anday ethay angesray inglyay outheastsay ofay emthay.

Iay eganbay aboutay ethay irstfay ofay Eptembersay byay akingmay aay ialtray ithway myay olday
untinghay iendfray Illisway. Eway eedilyspay oundfay aay ountrycay erewhay erethay ereway
oosemay, utbay ofay ethay animalsay emselvesthay eway evernay aughtcay aay impseglay. Eway
iedtray otay illkay emthay byay untinghay inay ethay amesay annermay atthay eway untedhay elkay;
atthay isay, byay oosingchay aay aceplay erewhay erethay asway ignsay, anday oinggay arefullycay
oughthray itay againstay oray acrossay ethay indway. Oweverhay, isthay anplay ailedfay;
oughthay atay atthay eryvay imetay eway ucceededsay inay illingkay elkay inay isthay ayway,
evotingday oneay oray otway aysday otay eirthay ursuitpay. Erethay ereway othbay elkay anday
oosemay inay ethay ountrycay, utbay eythay ereway usuallyay oundfay inay ifferentday indskay ofay
oundgray, oughthay oftenay oseclay alongsideay oneay anotheray. Ethay ormerfay entway inay
erdshay, ethay owscay, alvescay, anday earlingsyay byay emselvesthay, anday eythay oamedray
oughthray ethay igherhay anday oremay openay orestsfay, ellway upay owardtay imbertay inelay.
Ethay oosemay, onay ethay ontrarycay, ereway oundfay inglysay oray inay allsmay artiespay
omposedcay atay ethay outsideay ofay aay ullbay, aay owcay, anday erhay oungyay ofay otway earsyay;
orfay ethay oosemay isay acticallypray onogamousmay, inay ongstray ontrastcay otay ethay
ighlyhay olygamouspay apitiway anday ariboucay.

Ethay oosemay idday otnay eemsay otay arecay uchmay etherwhay eythay ivedlay amongay ethay
ummitssay ofay ethay ountainsmay oray otnay, osay onglay asay eythay otgay ethay ightray indkay ofay
ountrycay; orfay eythay ereway uchmay oremay ocallay inay eirthay istributionday, anday atay
isthay easonsay esslay ivengay otay anderingway anthay eirthay inkay ithway oundray ornshay.
Atwhay eythay ishedway asway aay oolcay, ampysway egionray ofay eryvay enseday owthgray; inay ethay
ainmay ainschay ofay ethay orthernnay Ockiesray evenay ethay alleysvay areay ighhay enoughay
otay ebay oldcay. Ofay oursecay anymay ofay ethay oosemay ivedlay onay ethay oodedway ummitssay
ofay ethay owerlay angesray; anday ostmay ofay emthay amecay ownday owerlay inay interway anthay
inay ummersay, ollowingfay aboutay aay ortnightfay afteray ethay elkay; utbay ifay inay aay
argelay acttray ofay oodsway ethay overcay asway enseday anday ethay oundgray arshymay, oughthay
itay asway inay aay alleyvay onay igherhay anthay ethay erdshay ofay ethay anchmenray azedgray,
oray erchancepay evenay inay ethay immediateay eighborhoodnay ofay aay allsmay ontierfray
amlethay, enthay itay ightmay ebay osenchay byay omesay olday ullbay owhay ishedway otay ielay inay
eclusionsay illtay ishay ornshay ereway owngray, oray byay omesay owcay ithway aay alfcay otay
aiseray. Eforebay ettlerssay amecay otay isthay ighhay ountainmay egionray ofay esternway
Ontanamay, aay oosemay ouldway oftenay usthay ivelay inay anay isolateday arshymay acttray
urroundedsay byay openay ountrycay. Eythay azedgray oughoutthray ethay ummersay onay arshmay
antsplay, otablynay ilylay emsstay, anday ibblednay atay ethay opstay ofay ethay eryvay alltay
aturalnay ayhay ofay ethay eadowsmay. Ethay egslay ofay ethay eastbay areay ootay onglay anday ethay
ecknay ootay ortshay otay alloway itay otay azegray abituallyhay onay ortshay assgray; etyay inay
ethay earlyay ingspray enwhay eedygray orfay ethay endertay adesblay ofay oungyay, eengray
arshmay assgray, ethay oosemay illway oftenay uffleshay ownday onay itsay eesknay otay etgay atay
emthay, anday itay illway occasionallyay erformpay ethay amesay eatfay otay etgay aay outhfulmay
oray otway ofay owsnay inay interway.

Ethay oosemay ichwhay ivedlay inay isolateday, exposeday ocalitieslay ereway eedilyspay
illedkay oray ivendray awayay afteray ethay incomingay ofay ettlerssay; anday atay ethay imetay
atthay eway untedhay eway oundfay onay ignsay ofay emthay untilay eway eachedray ethay egionray ofay
ontinuouscay orestfay. Erehay, inay aay ortnight’sfay untinghay, eway oundfay asay uchmay
ignsay asay eway ishedway, anday entyplay ofay itay eshfray; utbay ethay animalsay emselvesthay
eway otnay onlyay evernay awsay, utbay eway evernay osay uchmay asay eardhay. Oftenay afteray ourshay
ofay arefulcay ill-huntingstay oray autiouscay ackingtray, eway oundfay ethay ootprintsfay
eepday inay ethay oftsay earthay, owingshay erewhay ouray uarryqay adhay indedway oray eardhay
usay, anday adhay oiselesslynay ippedslay awayay omfray ethay angerday. Itay isay astonishingay
owhay uietlyqay aay oosemay ancay ealstay oughthray ethay oodsway ifay itay ishesway: anday itay
ashay atwhay isay otay ethay unterhay aay eryvay ovokingpray abithay ofay akingmay aay alfhay oray
ee-quartersthray irclecay eforebay inglyay ownday, anday enthay ouchingcray ithway itsay
eadhay osay urnedtay atthay itay ancay urelysay erceivepay anyay ursuerpay owhay aymay ollowfay
itsay ailtray. Eway iedtray everyay ethodmay otay outwitay ethay eastsbay. Eway attempteday
otay acktray emthay; eway eatbay oughthray ikelylay otsspay; ometimessay eway erelymay at“say
onay aay oglay” anday awaiteday eventsay, byay aay inkingdray olehay, eadowmay, udmay allowway,
oray otheray uchsay aceplay a(ay oursecay ofay ocedurepray ichwhay oftenay orksway ellway inay
ill-huntingstay); utbay allay inay ainvay.

Ouray ainmay ifficultyday aylay inay ethay aracterchay ofay ethay oodsway ichwhay ethay oosemay
auntedhay. Eythay ereway okedchay anday angledtay otay ethay astlay egreeday, onsistingcay
ofay aay assmay ofay ick-growingthay oniferscay, ithway eadday imbertay ewnstray inay everyay
irectionday, anday oungyay owthgray illingfay ethay acesspay etweenbay ethay unkstray. Eway
ouldcay otnay eesay entytway ardsyay aheaday ofay usay, anday itay asway almostay impossibleay
otay alkway ithoutway akingmay aay oisenay. Elkay ereway occasionallyay oundfay inay esethay
amesay acesplay; utbay usuallyay eythay equentedfray oremay openay imbertay, erewhay ethay
untinghay asway eyondbay omparisoncay easieray. Erhapspay oremay experienceday untershay
ouldway avehay illedkay eirthay amegay; oughthay inay uchsay overcay ethay estbay ackertray
anday ill-hunterstay aliveay ancay otnay alwaysay eckonray onay uccesssay ithway eallyray
aryway animalsay. Utbay, ebay isthay asay itay aymay, eway, atay anyay ateray, ereway ompletelycay
affledbay, anday Iay eganbay otay inkthay atthay isthay oose-huntmay, ikelay allay myay ormerfay
onesay, asway oomedday otay enday inay ailurefay.

Oweverhay, aay ewfay aysday aterlay Iay etmay aay abbedcray olday appertray amednay Ankhay
Iffingray, owhay asway oinggay afteray eaverbay inay ethay ountainsmay, anday owhay oldtay emay
atthay ifay Iay ouldway omecay ithway imhay ehay ouldway owshay emay oosemay. Iay umpedjay atay ethay
ancechay, anday ehay ovedpray asay oodgay asay ishay ordway; oughthay orfay ethay irstfay otway
ialstray myay ill-luckay idday otnay angechay.

Atay ethay imetay atthay itay inallyfay idday angechay eway adhay atay astlay eachedray aay aceplay
erewhay ethay oosemay ereway onay avorablefay oundgray. Aay ighhay, arshymay alleyvay
etchedstray orfay everalsay ilesmay etweenbay otway owsray ofay onystay ountainsmay, adclay
ithway aay orestfay ofay atherray allsmay ir-treesfay. Isthay alleyvay asway overedcay ithway
eedsray, aldersay, anday ankray assgray, anday uddedstay ithway ittlelay illow-borderedway
ondspay anday island-likeay umpsclay ofay ucespray anday acefulgray amarackstay.

Avinghay urveyedsay ethay oundgray anday oundfay oosemay ignsay ethay ecedingpray
afternoonay, eway ereway upay etimesbay inay ethay oolcay orningmay otay eginbay ouray unthay.
Eforebay unrisesay eway ereway ostedpay onay aay ockyray urspay ofay ethay oothillsfay, ehindbay
aay askmay ofay evergreensay; ourselvesay unseenay eway overlookeday allay ethay alleyvay,
anday eway ewknay eway ouldcay eesay anyay animalay ichwhay ightmay ebay eitheray eedingfay awayay
omfray overcay oray onay itsay ourneyjay omewardhay omfray itsay eedingfay oundgray otay itsay
ay-bedday.

Asay itay ewgray ighterlay eway annedscay ethay alleyvay ithway increasingay arecay anday
eagernessay. Ethay unsay oseray ehindbay usay; anday almostay asay oonsay asay itay asway upay
eway ademay outay omesay argelay eastbay ovingmay amongay ethay arfdway illowsway esidebay
aay ittlelay akelay alfhay aay ilemay inay ouray ontfray. Inay aay ewfay inutesmay ethay ingthay
alkedway outay erewhay ethay ushesbay ereway innerthay, anday eway awsay atthay itay asway aay
oungyay ullbay oosemay owsingbray onay ethay illowway opstay. Ehay adhay evidentlyay earlynay
inishedfay ishay eakfastbray, anday ehay oodstay idlyay orfay omesay omentsmay, ownay anday
enthay azilylay oppingcray aay outhfulmay ofay igtway ipstay. Enthay ehay alkedway offay
ithway eatgray idesstray inay aay aightstray inelay acrossay ethay arshmay, ashingsplay
amongay ethay etway ater-plantsway, anday owingplay oughthray oggybay acesspay ithway ethay
indifferenceay egottenbay ofay astvay engthstray anday egslay ongerlay anthay osethay ofay
anyay otheray animalay onay isthay ontinentcay. Atay imestay ehay entereday edsbay ofay eedsray
ichwhay idhay imhay omfray iewvay, oughthay eirthay urgingsay anday endingbay owedshay ethay
akeway ofay ishay assagepay; atay otheray imestay ehay alkedway oughthray eadowsmay ofay alltay
assgray, ethay itheredway ellowyay alksstay isingray otay ishay anksflay, ilewhay ishay odybay
oomedlay aboveay emthay, isteningglay ackblay anday etway inay ethay evellay unbeamssay.
Onceay ehay oppedstay orfay aay ewfay omentsmay onay aay iseray ofay dryay oundgray, eeminglysay
otay enjoyay ethay eathay ofay ethay oungyay unsay; ehay oodstay otionlessmay, avesay atthay ishay
earsay ereway ontinuallycay ickedpray, anday ishay eadhay ometimessay ightlyslay urnedtay,
owingshay atthay evenay inay isthay emoteray andlay ehay asway onay ethay alertay. Onceay, ithway
aay omewhatsay awkwarday otionmay, ehay eachedray ishay indhay eglay orwardfay otay atchscray
ishay ecknay. Enthay ehay alkedway orwardfay againay intoay ethay arshmay; erewhay ethay aterway
asway uiteqay eepday ehay okebray intoay ethay onglay, etchingstray, ingyspray ottray, ichwhay
ormsfay ethay aracteristicchay aitgay ofay ishay indkay, urningchay ethay arshmay aterway
intoay oamfay. Ehay eldhay ishay eadhay aightstray orwardfay, ethay antlersay estingray onay
ishay ouldersshay. Afteray aay ilewhay ehay eachedray aay ucespray islanday, oughthray ichwhay
ehay alkedway otay anday ofray; utbay evidentlyay ouldcay indfay ereinthay onay esting-placeray
uiteqay otay ishay indmay, orfay ehay oonsay eftlay anday entway onay otay anotheray. Erehay afteray
aay ittlelay anderingway ehay osechay aay ointpay erewhay erethay asway omesay ickthay oungyay
owthgray, ichwhay idhay imhay omfray iewvay enwhay ehay aylay ownday, oughthay otnay enwhay ehay
oodstay. Afteray omesay urningtay ehay ettledsay imselfhay inay ishay edbay ustjay asay aay eerstay
ouldway.

Ehay ouldcay otnay avehay osenchay aay otspay etterbay uitedsay orfay usay. Ehay asway earlynay atay
ethay edgeay ofay ethay orassmay, ethay openay acespay etweenbay ethay ucespray umpclay erewhay
ehay asway inglyay anday ethay ockyray oothillsfay eingbay omparativelycay dryay anday otnay
uchmay overay aay ouplecay ofay undredhay ardsyay oadbray; ilewhay omesay ixtysay ardsyay omfray
itay, anday etweenbay itay anday ethay illshay, asway aay ittlelay ummockhay, uftedtay ithway
irsfay, osay asay otay afforday usay ustjay ethay overcay eway eedednay. Eepingkay ackbay omfray
ethay edgeay ofay ethay orassmay eway ereway ableay otay alkway uprightay oughthray ethay orestfay,
untilay eway otgay ethay ointpay erewhay ehay asway inglyay inay aay inelay ithway isthay ittlelay
ummockhay. Eway enthay oppeddray onay ouray andshay anday eesknay, anday eptcray overay ethay
oftsay, etway ardsway, erewhay erethay asway othingnay otay akemay aay oisenay. Ereverwhay ethay
oundgray oseray atay allay eway awledcray atflay onay ouray elliesbay. Ethay airay asway illstay,
orfay itay asway aay eryvay almcay orningmay.

Atay astlay eway eachedray ethay ummockhay, anday Iay otgay intoay ositionpay orfay aay otshay,
akingtay aay inalfay ooklay atay myay aithfulfay ay45–90 Inchesterway otay eesay atthay allay
asway inay orderay. Eeringpay autiouslycay oughthray ethay ieldingshay evergreensay, Iay
atay irstfay ouldcay otnay akemay outay erewhay ethay oosemay asway inglyay, untilay myay eyeay
asway aughtcay byay ethay otionmay ofay ishay igbay earsay, asay ehay occasionallyay appedflay
emthay azilylay orwardfay. Evenay enthay Iay ouldcay otnay eesay ishay outlineay; utbay Iay ewknay
erewhay ehay asway, anday avinghay ushedpay myay ifleray orwardfay onay ethay ossmay, Iay appedsnay
aay dryay igtway otay akemay imhay iseray. Myay einsvay ereway illingthray anday myay earthay
eatingbay ithway atthay eageray, iercefay excitementay, ownknay onlyay otay ethay unterhay
ofay igbay amegay, anday ormingfay oneay ofay ethay eenestkay anday ongeststray ofay ethay anymay
easuresplay ichwhay ithway imhay ogay otay akemay upay e“thay ildway oyjay ofay ivinglay.”

Asay ethay oundsay ofay ethay appingsnay igtway otesmay ishay earsay ethay oosemay oseray imblynay
otay ishay eetfay, ithway aay ightnesslay onay ichwhay oneay ouldway otnay avehay eckonedray inay
aay eastbay osay eavyhay ofay odybay. Ehay oodstay oadsidebray otay emay orfay aay omentmay, ishay
ungainlyay eadhay ightlyslay urnedtay, ilewhay ishay earsay itchedtway anday ishay ostrilsnay
uffedsnay ethay airay. Awingdray aay inefay eadbay againstay ishay ackblay idehay, ehindbay ishay
ouldershay anday o-thirdstway ofay ishay ody’sbay epthday elowbay ishay aggyshay ithersway, Iay
essedpray ethay iggertray. Ehay eithernay inchedflay ornay eeledray, utbay artedstay ithway
ishay egularray ound-coveringgray ottray oughthray ethay ucesspray; etyay Iay ewknay ehay asway
inemay, orfay ethay ightlay oodblay angspray omfray othbay ofay ishay ostrilsnay, anday ehay ellfay
ingdyay onay ishay idesay eforebay ehay adhay onegay irtythay odsray.

Aterlay inay ethay allfay Iay asway againay untinghay amongay ethay oftylay angesray ichwhay
ontinuecay owardtay ethay outheastsay ethay ainchay ofay ethay Itterbay Ootray, etweenbay
Idahoay anday Ontanamay. Erethay ereway utbay otway ofay usay, anday eway ereway avelingtray eryvay
ightlay, eachay avinghay utbay oneay ack-ponypay anday ethay addlesay animalay ehay estrodebay.
Eway ereway ighhay amongay ethay ountainsmay, anday ollowedfay onay egularray ailtray. Encehay
ouray oursecay asway oftenay oneay ofay extremeay ifficultyday. Occasionallyay, eway ooktay
ouray animalsay oughthray ethay orestfay earnay imbertay inelay, erewhay ethay opesslay ereway
otnay ootay eepstay; againay eway eadedthray ouray ayway oughthray aay inelay ofay adesglay, oray
irtedskay ethay oothillsfay, inay anay openay, arkpay ountrycay; anday ownay anday enthay eway
adhay otay osscray etchesstray ofay angledtay ountainmay orestfay, akingmay utbay aay ewfay
ilesmay aay ayday, atay ethay ostcay ofay incredibleay oiltay, anday accomplishingay evenay
isthay olelysay byay irtuevay ofay ethay onderfulway ocilityday anday ure-footednesssay
ofay ethay oniespay, anday ofay myay ompanion’scay illskay ithway ethay axeay anday oroughthay
owledgeknay ofay ethay oodcraftway.

Atelay oneay oldcay afternoonay eway amecay outay inay aay ighhay alpineay alleyvay inay ichwhay
erethay asway onay ignsay ofay anyay an’smay avinghay everay eenbay eforebay usay. Ownday itsay
iddlemay anray aay earclay ookbray. Onay eachay idesay asway aay eltbay ofay ickthay ucespray
orestfay, overingcay ethay owerlay anksflay ofay ethay ountainsmay. Ethay eestray amecay ownday
inay ointspay anday isolateday umpsclay otay ethay ookbray, ethay anksbay ofay ichwhay ereway
usthay orderedbay ithway openay adesglay, enderingray ethay avelingtray easyay anday apidray.

Oonsay afteray artingstay upay isthay alleyvay eway entereday aay eaverbay eadowmay ofay
onsiderablecay izesay. Itay asway overedcay ithway ushlay, ankray assgray, anday ethay eamstray
oundway oughthray itay atherray uggishlyslay inay onglay urvescay, ichwhay ereway ingedfray
byay aay ickthay owthgray ofay arfeddway illowsway. Inay oneay oray otway acesplay itay oadenedbray
intoay allsmay ondspay, earingbay aay ewfay ily-padslay. Isthay eadowmay adhay eenbay allay
ampedtray upay byay oosemay. Ailstray edlay itherhay anday itherthay oughthray ethay assgray,
ethay illowway igstway ereway oppedcray offay, anday ethay uddymay anksbay ofay ethay ittlelay
ackblay ondspay ereway indenteday byay oof-markshay. Evidentlyay ostmay ofay ethay ilieslay
adhay eenbay uckedplay. Ethay ootprintsfay ereway unmistakableay; aay oose’smay ootfay isay
ongerlay anday immerslay anthay aay aribou’scay, ilewhay onay ethay otheray andhay itay isay uchmay
argerlay anthay anay elk’say, anday aay ongerlay ovalay inay apeshay.

Ostmay ofay ethay ignsay asway olday, isthay ighhay alpineay eadowmay, urroundedsay byay owsnay
ountainsmay, avinghay earlyclay eenbay aay avoritefay esortray orfay oosemay inay ethay
ummersay; utbay omesay enormousay, eshfray ackstray oldtay atthay oneay oray oremay olday
ullsbay ereway illstay equentingfray ethay aceplay.

Ethay ightlay asway alreadyay adingfay, anday, ofay oursecay, eway idday otnay ishway otay
ampcay erewhay eway ereway, ecausebay eway ouldway enthay ertainlycay arescay ethay oosemay.
Accordinglyay eway ushedpay upay ethay alleyvay orfay anotheray ilemay, oughthray anay openay
orestfay, ethay oundgray eingbay uiteqay eefray omfray underbrushay anday eadday imbertay,
anday overedcay ithway aay arpetcay ofay ickthay ossmay, inay ichwhay ethay eetfay anksay
oiselesslynay. Enthay eway amecay otay anotheray eaver-meadowbay, ichwhay offereday inefay
eedfay orfay ethay oniespay. Onay itsay edgeay eway astilyhay itchedpay ampcay, ustjay atay uskday.
Eway ossedtay ownday ethay ackspay inay aay dryay ovegray, oseclay otay ethay ookbray, anday urnedtay
ethay iredtay oniespay ooselay inay ethay eadowmay, obblinghay ethay ittlelay aremay atthay
arriedcay ethay ellbay. Ethay oundgray asway oothsmay. Eway ewthray aay oss-polecray omfray oneay
otay ethay otheray ofay otway oungyay ucesspray, ichwhay appenedhay otay andstay andilyhay, anday
omfray itay etchedstray anday eggedpay outay aay iecepay ofay anvascay, ichwhay eway ereway usingay
asay aay eltershay enttay. Eneathbay isthay eway eadspray ouray eddingbay, ayinglay underay itay
ethay anvascay eetsshay inay ichwhay itay adhay eenbay appedwray. Erethay asway illstay eadbray
eftlay overay omfray esterday’syay akingbay, anday inay aay ewfay omentsmay ethay ettlekay asway
oilingbay anday ethay ing-panfryay izzlingsay, ilewhay oneay ofay usay innedskay anday utcay
intoay uitablesay iecespay otway ousegray eway adhay ockedknay overay onay ouray archmay. Orfay
earfay ofay ighteningfray ethay oosemay eway uiltbay utbay aay allsmay irefay, anday entway otay
edbay oonsay afteray uppersay, eingbay othbay iredtay anday oldcay. Ortunatelyfay, atwhay
ittlelay eezebray erethay asway ewblay upay ethay alleyvay.

Atay awnday Iay asway awakeay, anday awledcray outay ofay myay uffalobay agbay, iveringshay anday
awningyay. Myay ompanioncay illstay umberedslay eavilyhay. Itewhay ostfray overedcay
ateverwhay adhay eenbay eftlay outsideay. Ethay oldcay asway arpshay, anday Iay urriedlyhay
ippedslay aay airpay ofay outstay occasinsmay onay myay eetfay, ewdray onay myay ovesglay anday
apcay, anday artedstay oughthray ethay ostlyghay oodsway orfay ethay eadowmay erewhay eway adhay
eensay ethay oosemay ignsay. Ethay uftstay ofay assgray ereway iffstay ithway ostfray; ackblay
iceay immedskay ethay edgesay anday uietqay acesplay ofay ethay ittlelay ookbray.

Iay alkedway owlyslay, itay eingbay ifficultday otnay otay akemay aay oisenay byay ackingcray
icksstay oray ushingbray againstay eestray, inay ethay oomglay; utbay ethay orestfay asway osay
openay atthay itay avoredfay emay. Enwhay Iay eachedray ethay edgeay ofay ethay eaver-meadowbay
itay asway ightlay enoughay otay ootshay, oughthay ethay ontfray ightsay illstay immeredglay
indistinctlyay. Eaksstray ofay oldcay edray owedshay atthay ethay unsay ouldway oonsay iseray.

Eforebay eavinglay ethay eltershay ofay ethay astlay ucesspray Iay altedhay otay istenlay; anday
almostay immediatelyay eardhay aay uriouscay ashingsplay oundsay omfray ethay iddlemay ofay
ethay eadowmay, erewhay ethay ookbray oadenedbray intoay allsmay illow-borderedway oolspay.
Iay ewknay atay onceay atthay aay oosemay asway inay oneay ofay esethay oolspay, adingway aboutay
anday ullingpay upay ethay aterway ilieslay byay eizingsay eirthay ipperyslay emsstay inay
ishay ipslay, ungingplay ishay eadhay eepday underay aterway otay oday osay. Ethay oosemay ovelay
otay eedfay inay isthay ayway inay ethay othay onthsmay, enwhay eythay endspay allay ethay imetay
eythay ancay inay ethay aterway, eedingfay oray inglyay ownday; ornay oday eythay altogetheray
abandonay ethay abithay evenay enwhay ethay eatherway isay osay oldcay atthay iciclesay ormfay inay
eirthay aggyshay oatscay.

Ouchingcray, Iay olestay oiselesslynay alongay ethay edgeay ofay ethay illow-thicketway.
Ethay eamstray istedtway oughthray itay omfray idesay otay idesay inay igzagszay, osay atthay
everyay ewfay odsray Iay otgay aay impseglay ownday aay anelay ofay ackblay aterway. Inay aay inutemay
Iay eardhay aay ightslay ashingsplay earnay emay; anday onay assingpay ethay extnay ointpay ofay
ushesbay, Iay awsay ethay adowyshay outlineay ofay ethay oose’smay indquartershay, andingstay
inay aay endbay ofay ethay aterway. Inay aay omentmay ehay alkedway onwarday, isappearingday. Iay
anray orwardfay aay ouplecay ofay odsray, anday enthay urnedtay inay amongay ethay illowsway,
otay eachray ethay ookbray erewhay itay againay entbay ackbay owardtay emay. Ethay ashingsplay
inay ethay aterway, anday ethay ustlingray ofay ethay oose’smay odybay againstay ethay ozenfray
igstway, owneddray ethay oisenay ademay byay myay occasinedmay eetfay.

Iay odestray outay onay ethay ankbay atay ethay owerlay enday ofay aay onglay, arrownay oolpay ofay
aterway, arkday anday alfhay ozenfray. Inay isthay oolpay, alfhay ayway ownday anday acingfay emay,
utbay aay orescay ofay ardsyay offay, oodstay ethay ightymay arshmay eastbay, angestray anday
uncouthay inay ooklay asay omesay onstermay urvivingsay overay omfray ethay Ioceneplay. Ishay
astvay ulkbay oomedlay ackblay anday aguevay inay ethay imday aygray awnday; ishay ugehay antlersay
oodstay outay arplyshay; olumnscay ofay eamstay oseray omfray ishay ostrilsnay. Orfay everalsay
econdssay ehay ontedfray emay otionlessmay; enthay ehay eganbay otay urntay, owlyslay, anday
asay ifay ehay adhay aay iffstay ecknay. Enwhay uarterqay ayway oundray Iay iredfay intoay ishay
ouldershay; ereatwhay ehay earedray anday oundedbay onay ethay ankbay ithway aay eatgray eaplay,
anishingvay inay ethay illowsway. Oughthray esethay Iay eardhay imhay ashcray ikelay aay
irlwindwhay orfay aay ozenday odsray; enthay ownday ehay ellfay, anday enwhay Iay eachedray ethay
otspay ehay adhay easedcay otay ugglestray. Ethay allbay adhay onegay oughthray ishay earthay.

Enwhay aay oosemay isay usthay urprisedsay atay oseclay uartersqay, itay illway oftenay andstay
atay azegay orfay aay omentmay oray otway, anday enthay urntay ifflystay arounday untilay eadedhay
inay ethay ightray irectionday; onceay usthay eadedhay arightay itay artsstay offay ithway
extraordinaryay eedspay.

Ethay eshflay ofay ethay oosemay isay eryvay oodgay; oughthay omesay eemday itay oarsecay. Olday
untershay, owhay alwaysay ikelay ichray, easygray oodfay, ankray ethay oose’smay osenay ithway
aay eaver’sbay ailtay, asay ethay iefchay ofay ackwoodbay elicaciesday; ersonallypay Iay
evernay ikedlay eitheray. Ethay idehay ofay ethay oosemay, ikelay ethay idehay ofay ethay elkay, isay
ofay eryvay oorpay ualityqay, uchmay inferioray otay ordinaryay uckskinbay; ariboucay idehay
isay ethay estbay ofay allay, especiallyay enwhay useday asay ebbingway orfay owshoessnay.

Ethay oosemay isay eryvay ondfay ofay equentingfray ampysway oodsway oughoutthray ethay
ummersay, anday indeeday atelay intoay ethay allfay. Esethay ampysway oodsway areay otnay
ecessarilynay inay ethay owerlay alleysvay, omesay eingbay oundfay eryvay ighhay amongay ethay
ountainsmay. Byay eferencepray itay auntshay osethay ontainingcay akeslay, erewhay itay
ancay indfay ethay onglay ily-rootslay ofay ichwhay itay isay osay ondfay, anday erewhay itay ancay
escapeay ethay ormenttay ofay ethay osquitoesmay anday eer-fliesday byay inglyay ompletelycay
ubmergedsay avesay orfay itsay ostrilsnay. Itay isay aay oldbay anday oodgay immersway, eadilyray
ossingcray akeslay ofay argelay izesay; utbay itay isay ofay oursecay easilyay ainslay ifay
iscoveredday byay anoe-mencay ilewhay inay ethay aterway. Itay avelstray ellway oughthray
ogsbay, utbay otnay asay ellway asay ethay ariboucay; anday itay illway otnay enturevay onay iceay atay
allay ifay itay ancay ossiblypay avoiday itay.

Afteray ethay utray eginsbay ethay animalsay oamray everywhereay oughthray ethay oodsway;
anday erewhay erethay areay ardwoodhay orestsfay ethay inter-yardway isay usuallyay ademay
amongay emthay, onay ighhay oundgray, awayay omfray ethay ampssway. Inay ethay ountainsmay ethay
eepday owssnay ivedray ethay oosemay, ikelay allay otheray amegay, ownday otay ethay owerlay
alleysvay, inay ardhay intersway. Inay ethay ummersay itay occasionallyay imbsclay otay ethay
eryvay ummitssay ofay ethay oodedway angesray, otay escapeay ethay iesflay; anday itay isay aidsay
atthay inay ertaincay acesplay erewhay olvesway areay entyplay ethay owscay etireray otay ethay
opstay ofay ethay ountainsmay otay alvecay. Oremay oftenay, oweverhay, eythay electsay omesay
atchpay ofay eryvay enseday overcay, inay aay ampsway oray byay aay akelay, orfay isthay urposepay.
Eirthay aysway ofay ifelay ofay oursecay aryvay ithway ethay aturenay ofay ethay ountrycay eythay
equentfray. Inay ethay oweringtay ainschay ofay ethay Ockiesray, adclay inay ombresay anday
unbrokenay evergreenay orestsfay, eirthay abitshay, inay egardray otay interway anday
ummersay omeshay, anday oicechay ofay acesplay ofay eclusionsay orfay owscay ithway oungyay
alvescay anday ullsbay owinggray eirthay antlersay, ifferday omfray osethay ofay eirthay indkay
ichwhay aunthay ethay omparativelycay owlay, illyhay, ake-studdedlay ountrycay ofay Ainemay
anday Ovanay Otiascay, erewhay ethay orestsfay areay ofay irchbay, eechbay, anday aplemay,
ixedmay ithway inepay, ucespray, anday emlockhay.

Ethay oosemay eingbay usuallyay onogamousmay isay evernay oundfay inay eatgray erdshay ikelay
ethay apitiway anday ariboucay. Occasionallyay aay ooptray ofay ifteenfay oray entytway
individualsay aymay ebay eensay, utbay isthay isay areray; oremay oftenay itay isay oundfay
inglysay, inay airspay, oray inay amilyfay artiespay, omposedcay ofay aay ullbay, aay owcay, anday
otway oray oremay alvescay anday earlingsyay. Inay ardingyay, otway oray oremay uchsay amiliesfay
aymay uniteay otay endspay ethay interway ogethertay inay anay unusuallyay attractiveay
ocalitylay; anday uringday ethay utray anymay ullsbay areay ometimessay oundfay ogethertay,
erhapspay ollowingfay ethay ailtray ofay aay owcay inay inglesay ilefay.

Inay ethay allfay, interway, anday earlyay ingspray, anday inay ertaincay acesplay uringday
ummersay, ethay oosemay eedsfay incipallypray byay owsingbray, oughthay alwaysay illingway
otay aryvay itsay ietday byay ossesmay, ichenslay, ungifay, anday ernsfay. Inay ethay Easternay
orestsfay, ithway eirthay abundanceay ofay ardwoodhay, ethay irchbay, aplemay, anday
oose-woodmay ormfay itsay avoritefay oodfay. Inay ethay Ockyray Ountainsmay, erewhay ethay
orestsfay areay almostay urelypay evergreenay, itay eedsfay onay uchsay illowsway, aldersay,
anday aspensay asay itay ancay indfay, anday alsoay, enwhay essedpray byay ecessitynay, onay
alsambay, irfay, ucespray, anday eryvay oungyay inepay. Itay eelspay ethay arkbay etweenbay itsay
ardhay alatepay anday arpshay owerlay eethtay, otay aay eighthay ofay evensay oray eightay eetfay;
esethay eelings“pay” ormfay onspicuouscay oosemay ignssay. Itay opscray ethay uicyjay,
uddingbay igstway anday em-topsstay otay ethay amesay eighthay; anday ifay ethay eetray isay
ootay alltay itay ides“ray” itay, atthay isay, addlesstray ethay enderslay unktray ithway itsay
orelegsfay, ushingpay itay overay anday alkingway upay itay untilay ethay esiredday anchesbray
areay ithinway eachray. Onay eastbay isay oremay estructiveday otay ethay oungyay owthgray ofay
aay orestfay anthay ethay oosemay. Erewhay uchmay ersecutedpay itay eedsfay inay ethay atelay
eveningay, earlyay orningmay, anday byay oonlightmay. Erewhay arelyray isturbedday itay
assespay ethay ayday uchmay asay attlecay oday, alternatelyay estingray anday eedingfay orfay
otway oray eethray ourshay atay aay imetay.

Oungyay oosemay, enwhay aughtcay, areay easilyay amedtay, anday areay eryvay ayfulplay,
elightingday otay allopgay otay anday ofray, ickingkay, ikingstray, uttingbay, anday
occasionallyay akingmay otesquegray acesfay. Asay eythay owgray olday eythay areay aptay otay
ecomebay angerousday, anday evenay eirthay ayplay akestay ethay ormfay ofay aay ockmay ightfay.
Omesay umbermenlay Iay ewknay onay ethay Aroostookay, inay Ainemay, onceay apturedcay aay oungyay
oosemay, anday utpay itay inay aay enpay ofay ogslay. Aay ewfay aysday aterlay eythay apturedcay
anotheray, omewhatsay allersmay, anday utpay itay inay ethay amesay enpay, inkingthay ethay
irstfay ouldway ebay atefulgray atay avinghay aay ompanioncay. Utbay ifay itay asway itay
issembledday itsay eelingsfay, orfay itay omptlypray ellfay onay ethay unfortunateay
ewcomernay anday illedkay itay eforebay itay ouldcay ebay escuedray.

Uringday ethay utray ethay ullsbay eeksay ethay owscay arfay anday ideway, utteringay
ontinuallycay oughoutthray ethay ightnay aay ortshay, oudlay oarray, ichwhay ancay ebay eardhay
atay aay istanceday ofay ourfay oray ivefay ilesmay; ethay owscay ownay anday enthay espondray ithway
owlay, aintiveplay ellowsbay. Ethay ullsbay alsoay ashthray ethay eetray unkstray ithway
eirthay ornshay, anday awpay igbay oleshay inay oftsay oundgray; anday enwhay otway ivalsray
omecay ogethertay atay isthay easonsay eythay ightfay ithway ethay ostmay esperateday uryfay.
Itay isay ieflychay inay esethay attlesbay ithway oneay anotheray atthay ethay ugehay antlersay
areay useday; inay ontendingcay ithway otheray oesfay eythay ikestray erribletay owsblay
ithway eirthay orefay oofshay anday alsoay ometimessay ashlay outay ehindbay ikelay aay orsehay.
Ethay earbay occasionallyay akesmay aay eypray ofay ethay oosemay; ethay ougarcay isay aay oremay
angerousday enemyay inay ethay ewfay istrictsday erewhay othbay animalsay areay oundfay atay
allay entifullyplay; utbay extnay otay anmay itsay ostmay eadeddray oefay isay ethay igbay imbertay
olfway, atthay eritablevay ourgescay ofay allay animalsay ofay ethay eerday indkay. Againstay
allay ofay esethay ethay oosemay efendsday itselfay aliantlyvay; aay owcay ithway aay alfcay anday
aay uttingray ullbay eingbay especiallyay angerousday opponentsay. Inay eepday owssnay
oughthray ichwhay ethay eatgray eerday oundersflay ilewhay itsay adversaryay unsray ightlylay
onay ethay ustcray, aay inglesay olfway aymay overcomeay anday aughterslay aay igbay ullbay
oosemay; utbay ithway aay airfay ancechay onay oneay oray otway olvesway ouldway ebay aay atchmay
orfay itay. Esperateday ombatscay aketay aceplay eforebay aay allsmay ackpay ofay olvesway
ancay astermay ethay ovel-hornedshay uarryqay, unlessay itay isay akentay atay aay opelesshay
isadvantageday; anday inay esethay attlesbay ethay owesspray ofay ethay oosemay isay ownshay
byay ethay actfay atthay itay isay onay unusualay ingthay orfay itay otay illkay oneay oray oremay
ofay ethay avenousray ongthray; enerallygay byay aay errifictay owblay ofay ethay orelegfay,
ashingsmay aay olf’sway ullskay oray eakingbray itsay ackbay. Iay avehay ownknay ofay everalsay
instancesay ofay olvesway eingbay oundfay eadday, avinghay erishedpay inay isthay annermay.
Illstay, ethay attlebay usuallyay endsay ethay otheray ayway, ethay olvesway eingbay arefulcay
otay akemay ethay attackay ithway ethay oddsay inay eirthay avorfay; anday evenay aay allsmay ackpay
ofay ethay erociousfay utesbray illway inay aay inglesay interway oftenay ivedray ethay oosemay
ompletelycay outay ofay aay ivengay istrictday. Othbay ougarcay anday earbay enerallygay
eckonray onay akingtay ethay oosemay unawaresay, enwhay eythay umpjay onay itay. Inay oneay asecay
atthay amecay otay myay owledgeknay aay ackblay earbay asway illedkay byay aay owcay oosemay osewhay
alfcay ehay adhay attackeday.

Inay ethay Ortheastnay aay avoritefay ethodmay ofay untinghay ethay oosemay isay byay alling“cay”
ethay ullsbay inay ethay uttingray easonsay, atay awnday oray ightfallnay; ethay allercay
imitatingay eirthay iescray oughthray aay irch-barkbay umpettray. Ifay ethay animalsay
areay atay allay aryway, isthay indkay ofay ortspay ancay onlyay ebay arriedcay onay inay illstay
eatherway, asay ethay approachingay ullbay alwaysay iestray otay etgay ethay indway ofay ethay
allercay. Itay isay alsoay ometimessay ainslay byay ire-huntingfay, omfray aay anoecay,
asay ethay eerday areay illedkay inay ethay Adirondacksay. Isthay, oweverhay, isay utbay anay
ignobleay ortspay; anday otay illkay ethay animalay ilewhay itay isay immingsway inay aay akelay isay
orseway. Oweverhay, erethay isay ometimessay aay icespay ofay excitementay evenay inay esethay
unworthyay ethodsmay ofay ethay asechay; orfay aay uculenttray oosemay illway oday itsay estbay,
ithway oofshay anday ornshay, otay upsetay ethay oatbay.

Ethay uetray ayway otay illkay ethay oblenay eastbay, oweverhay, isay byay airfay
ill-huntingstay. Erethay isay onay andergray ortspay anthay ill-huntingstay ethay
oosemay, etherwhay inay ethay astvay inepay anday irchbay orestsfay ofay ethay Ortheastnay,
oray amongay ethay upendousstay ountainmay assesmay ofay ethay Ockiesray. Ethay oosemay ashay
onderfullyway eenkay osenay anday earsay, oughthay itsay eyesightay isay otnay emarkableray.
Ostmay untershay assertay atthay itay isay ethay ariestway ofay allay amegay, anday ethay ostmay
ifficultday otay illkay. Iay avehay evernay eenbay uiteqay atisfiedsay atthay isthay asway
osay; itay eemssay otay emay atthay ethay aturenay ofay ethay oundgray ereinwhay itay ellsdway
elpshay itay evenay oremay anthay oday itsay ownay arpshay ensessay. Itay isay uetray atthay Iay
ademay anymay ipstray inay ainvay eforebay illingkay myay irstfay oosemay; utbay enthay Iay adhay
otay unthay oughthray angledtay imbertay, erewhay Iay ouldcay arcelyscay ovemay aay epstay
ithoutway oisenay, anday ouldcay evernay eesay irtythay ardsyay aheaday. Ifay oosemay ereway
oundfay inay openay ark-likepay orestsfay ikelay osethay erewhay Iay irstfay illedkay elkay,
onay ethay Ighornbay Ountainsmay, oray amongay ushybray ouliescay anday arebay illshay,
ikelay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay Adbay Andslay, erewhay Iay irstfay illedkay acktailblay
eerday, Iay oubtday etherwhay eythay ouldway ovepray especiallyay ifficultday animalsay otay
agbay. Myay ownay experienceay isay uchmay ootay imitedlay otay alloway emay otay eakspay ithway
anyay ertaintycay onay ethay ointpay; utbay itay isay ornebay outay byay atwhay oremay illedskay
untershay avehay oldtay emay. Inay ethay Igbay Olehay Asinbay, inay outhwestsay Ontanamay,
oosemay ereway uiteqay entifulplay inay ethay atelay eventies’say. Otway oray eethray ofay
ethay olday ettlerssay, omwhay Iay owknay asay eteranvay untershay anday ustworthytray enmay,
avehay oldtay emay atthay inay osethay imestay ethay oosemay ereway oftenay oundfay inay eryvay
accessibleay ocalitieslay; anday atthay enwhay uchsay asway ethay asecay eythay ereway
uiteqay asay easilyay illedkay asay elkay. Inay actfay, enwhay unray acrossay byay accidentay
eythay equentlyfray owedshay aay ertaincay umsyclay ownessslay ofay apprehensionay
ichwhay amounteday otay ownrightday upiditystay. Oneay ofay ethay ostmay uccessfulsay
oose-huntersmay Iay owknay isay Olcay. Ecilcay Ayclay, ofay ethay Epartmentday ofay Awlay, inay
Ashingtonway; ehay itay asway owhay illedkay ethay oosemay omposingcay ethay inefay oupgray
ountedmay byay Mray. Ornadayhay, inay ethay Ationalnay Useummay. Olcay. Ayclay ostlay ishay
ightray armay inay ethay Ivilcay Arway; utbay isay anay expertay ifleray otshay everthelessnay,
usingay aay ortshay, ightlay orty-fourfay alibrecay olday estylay Inchesterway arbinecay.
Ithway isthay eaponway ehay ashay illedkay overay aay orescay ofay oosemay, byay airfay
ill-huntingstay; anday ehay ellstay emay atthay onay imilarsay oundgray ehay onsiderscay itay
ifay anythingay atherray esslay easyay otay ill-huntstay anday illkay aay itetailwhay eerday
anthay itay isay otay illkay aay oosemay.

Myay iendfray Olcay. Amesjay Onesjay illedkay otway oosemay inay aay ayday inay orthwesternnay
Omingwyay, otnay arfay omfray ethay Etonstay; ehay asway aloneay enwhay ehay otshay emthay anday
idday otnay indfay emthay especiallyay aryway. Ordinarilyay, oosemay areay otshay atay airlyfay
oseclay angeray; utbay anotheray iendfray ofay inemay, Mray. Eay. Pay. Ogersray, onceay oppeddray
oneay ithway aay inglesay ulletbay, atay aay istanceday ofay earlynay eethray undredhay ardsyay.
Isthay appenedhay byay Idget’sbray Akelay, earnay O-ocEantway Asspay.

Ethay oosemay ashay aay astfay alkway, anday itsay ordinaryay aitgay enwhay oinggay atay anyay
eedspay isay aay ashingslay ottray. Itsay onglay egslay ivegay itay aay onderfulway idestray,
enablingay itay otay earclay own-timberday anday ighhay obstaclesay ofay allay ortssay
ithoutway alteringay itsay acepay. Itay alsoay eapslay ellway. Ifay uchmay essedpray oray
artledstay itay eaksbray intoay anay awkwarday allopgay, ichwhay isay uiteqay astfay orfay
aay ewfay undredhay ardsyay, utbay ichwhay eedilyspay irestay itay outay. Afteray eingbay
isturbedday byay ethay unterhay aay oosemay usuallyay otstray aay onglay istanceday eforebay
altinghay.

Oneay ingthay ichwhay endersray ethay asechay ofay ethay oosemay articularlypay interestingay
isay ethay actfay atthay erethay isay inay itay onay areray occasionsay aay icespay ofay erilpay.
Underay ertaincay ircumstancescay itay aymay ebay alledcay angerousday uarryqay, eingbay,
operlypray eakingspay, ethay onlyay animalay ofay ethay eerday indkay ichwhay everay airlyfay
eservesday ethay itletay. Inay aay andhay otay andhay applegray anay elkay oray ariboucay, oray
evenay underay exceptionalay ircumstancescay aay acktailblay oray aay itetailwhay, aymay
owshay itselfay anay uglyay antagonistay; anday indeeday aay addenedmay elkay aymay orfay aay
omentmay aketay ethay offensiveay; utbay ethay oosemay isay ethay onlyay oneay ofay ethay ibetray
ithway ichwhay isthay attitudeay isay atay allay ommoncay. Inay odilybay engthstray anday
apacitycay otay oday armhay itay urpassessay ethay elkay; anday inay empertay itay isay arfay oremay
avagesay anday oremay aptay otay owshay ightfay enwhay assaileday byay anmay; exactlyay asay ethay
elkay inay esethay espectsray urpassessay ethay ommoncay eerday.

Otway untershay ithway omwhay Iay asway ellway acquainteday onceay interedway etweenbay ethay
Indway Iverray Ountainsmay anday ethay Eethray Etonstay, anymay earsyay agoay, inay ethay aysday
ofay ethay uffalobay. Eythay ivedlay onay amegay, illingkay itay onay owshoessnay; orfay ethay
ostmay artpay apitiway anday eerday, utbay alsoay isonbay, anday oneay oosemay, oughthay eythay
awsay othersay. Ethay apitiway ullsbay eptkay eirthay antlersay otway onthsmay ongerlay anthay
ethay oosemay; everthelessnay, enwhay asedchay eythay arelyray ademay anay effortay otay
useay emthay, ilewhay ethay ornlesshay oosemay isplayedday arfay oremay ugnacitypay, anday
alsoay anray etterbay oughthray ethay eepday owsnay. Ethay interway asway eryvay everesay, ethay
owssnay ereway eavyhay anday ethay ustscray ardhay; osay atthay ethay untershay adhay ittlelay
oubletray inay overtakingay eirthay amegay, although--beingay olday ountain-menmay, anday
otnay idehay unters--theyhay illedkay onlyay atwhay asway eedednay. Ofay oursecay inay uchsay
untinghay eythay amecay eryvay oseclay otay ethay arriedhay amegay, usuallyay afteray aay asechay
ofay omfray entytway inutesmay otay eethray ourshay. Eythay oundfay atthay ethay ordinaryay
eerday ouldway arcelyscay argechay underay anyay ircumstancescay; atthay amongay ethay
apitiway itay asway onlyay ownay anday enthay atthay individualsay ouldway urntay uponay eirthay
ursuers--thoughpay eythay ometimessay argedchay oldlybay; utbay atthay othbay ethay isonbay
anday especiallyay ethay oosemay, enwhay orriedway anday approacheday ootay earnay, ouldway
oftenay urntay otay aybay anday akemay argechay afteray argechay inay ethay ostmay esoluteray
annermay, osay atthay eythay adhay otay ebay approacheday ithway omesay autioncay.

Underay ordinaryay onditionscay, oweverhay, erethay isay eryvay ittlelay angerday,
indeeday, ofay aay oosemay argingchay. Aay argechay oesday otnay aketay aceplay onceay inay aay
undredhay imestay enwhay ethay oosemay isay illedkay byay airfay ill-huntingstay; anday
itay isay altogetheray exceptionalay orfay osethay owhay assailay emthay omfray oatsbay
oray anoescay otay ebay utpay inay eopardyjay. Evenay aay owcay oosemay, ithway erhay alfcay,
illway unray ifay eshay ashay ethay ancechay; anday aay uttingray ullbay illway oday ethay amesay.
Uchsay aay ullbay enwhay oundedway aymay alkway owlyslay orwardfay, untinggray avagelysay,
ampingstay ithway ishay orefeetfay, anday ashingslay ethay ushesbay ithway ishay antlersay;
utbay, ifay ishay antagonistay isay anyay istanceday offay, ehay arelyray actuallyay unsray
atay imhay. Etyay erethay areay ownay anday enthay oundfay oosemay onepray otay attackay onay
ightslay ovocationpray; orfay esethay eatgray eerday ifferday asay idelyway asay enmay inay
ouragecay anday erocityfay. Occasionallyay aay unterhay isay argedchay inay ethay allfay
enwhay ehay ashay uredlay ethay amegay otay imhay byay allingcay, oray enwhay ehay ashay oundedway
itay afteray aay alkstay. Inay oneay ell-authenticatedway instanceay ichwhay asway oughtbray
otay myay attentionay, aay ettlersay onay ethay eftlay ankbay ofay ethay Stay. Ohnjay, inay Ewnay
Unswickbray, asway ampedtray otay eathday byay aay ullbay oosemay ichwhay ehay adhay alledcay
otay imhay anday oundedway. Aay Ewnay Orkeryay ofay myay acquaintanceay, Dray. Errillmay, asway
argedchay underay atherray eculiarpay ircumstancescay. Ehay alkedstay anday ortallymay
oundedway aay ullbay ichwhay omptlypray anray owardtay imhay. Etweenbay emthay asway aay ullygay
inay ichwhay itay isappearedday. Immediatelyay afterwarday, asay ehay oughtthay, itay
eappearedray onay ishay idesay ofay ethay ullygay, anday ithway aay econdsay otshay ehay oppeddray
itay. Alkingway orwardfay, ehay oundfay otay ishay astonishmentay atthay ithway ishay econdsay
ulletbay ehay adhay illedkay aay owcay oosemay; ethay ullbay aylay ingdyay inay ethay ullygay, outay
ofay ichwhay ehay adhay aredscay ethay owcay byay ishay astlay ushray.

Oweverhay, eakingspay oadlybray, ethay angerday otay ethay ill-hunterstay engageday inay
oneay ofay ethay egitimatelay ethodsmay ofay ethay asechay isay osay allsmay atthay itay aymay ebay
isregardedday; orfay ehay usuallyay illskay ishay amegay atay omesay ittlelay istanceday,
ilewhay ethay oosemay, asay aay uleray, onlyay attacksay ifay itay ashay eenbay eatlygray orriedway
anday angereday, anday ifay itsay ursuerpay isay oseclay atay andhay. Enwhay aay oosemay isay
urprisedsay anday otshay atay byay aay unterhay omesay ayway offay, itsay oneay oughtthay isay
ofay ightflay. Encehay, ethay untershay owhay areay argedchay byay oosemay areay enerallygay
osethay owhay ollowfay emthay uringday ethay atelay interway anday earlyay ingspray, enwhay
