ethay animalsay avehay ardedyay anday ancay ebay illedkay onay owshoes--bysnay usting“cray,”
asay itay isay ermedtay, aay eryvay estructiveday, anday oftenay aay eryvay unsportsmanlikeay
eciesspay ofay asechay.

Ifay ethay owfallsnay isay eryvay ightlay, oosemay oday otnay ardyay atay allay; utbay inay aay ardhay
interway eythay eginbay otay akemay eirthay ardsyay inay Ecemberday. Aay ard“yay” isay otnay,
asay omesay eoplepay eemsay otay upposesay, aay ampled-downtray acespay, ithway efiniteday
oundariesbay; ethay ermtay erelymay enotesday ethay otspay ichwhay aay oosemay ashay osenchay
orfay itsay interway omehay, oosingchay itay ecausebay itay ontainscay entyplay ofay owsebray
inay ethay apeshay ofay oungyay eestray anday aplingssay, anday erhapspay alsoay ecausebay
itay isay elteredshay otay omesay extentay omfray ethay iercefay indsway anday eaviesthay
owdriftssnay. Ethay animalay avelstray otay anday ofray acrossay isthay acespay inay aightstray
ineslay anday irregularay irclescay afteray oodfay, eadingtray inay itsay ownay ootstepsfay,
erewhay acticablepray. Asay ethay owsnay eadilystay eepensday, esethay ineslay ofay
aveltray ecomebay eatenbay athspay. Erethay esultsray inallyfay aay acespay alfhay aay ilemay
uare--sometimessqay oremay, ometimessay eryvay uchmay esslay, accordingay otay ethay aylay
ofay ethay andlay, anday ethay umbernay ofay oosemay ardingyay ogether--wheretay ethay eepday
owsnay isay eamedsay inay everyay irectionday byay aay etworknay ofay arrownay athspay alongay
ichwhay aay oosemay ancay aveltray atay eedspay, itsay ackbay evellay ithway ethay owsnay oundray
aboutay. Ometimessay, enwhay oosemay areay eryvay entifulplay, anymay ofay esethay ardsyay
ielay osay oseclay ogethertay atthay ethay eastsbay ancay eadilyray akemay eirthay ayway omfray
oneay otay anotheray. Enwhay uchsay isay ethay asecay, ethay ostmay expertay owshoersnay, underay
ethay ostmay avorablefay onditionscay, ancay otnay overtakeay emthay, orfay eythay ancay
enthay aveltray eryvay astfay oughthray ethay athspay, eepingkay eirthay aitgay allay ayday.
Inay ethay earlyay ecadesday ofay ethay esentpray enturycay, ethay irstfay ettlerssay inay
Aroostookay Ountycay, Ainemay, ilewhay oose-huntingmay inay interway, ereway equentlyfray
affledbay inay isthay annermay.

Enwhay untershay approachay anay isolateday ardyay ethay oosemay immediatelyay eavelay itay
anday unray offay oughthray ethay owsnay. Ifay erethay isay onay ustcray, anday ifay eirthay onglay
egslay ancay eachray ethay oundgray, ethay owsnay itselfay impedesay emthay utbay ittlelay,
ecausebay ofay eirthay astvay engthstray anday enduranceay. Owdriftssnay ichwhay enderray
anay ordinaryay eerday absolutelyay elplesshay, anday ingbray evenay anay elkay otay aay
andstillstay, offeray onay impedimentay ateverwhay otay aay oosemay. Ifay, asay appenshay
eryvay arelyray, ethay ooselay owsnay isay ofay uchsay epthday atthay evenay ethay ilt-likestay
egslay ofay ethay oosemay ancay otnay ouchtay olidsay earthay, itay oundersflay anday ugglesstray
orwardfay orfay aay ittlelay imetay, anday enthay inkssay exhausteday; orfay aay ariboucay isay
ethay onlyay argelay animalay ichwhay ancay aveltray underay uchsay onditionscay. Ifay erethay
ebay aay ustcray, evenay oughthay ethay owsnay isay otnay emarkablyray eepday, ethay aborlay ofay
ethay oosemay isay astlyvay increaseday, asay itay eaksbray oughthray atay everyay epstay,
uttingcay itsay egslay anday exhaustingay itselfay. Aay ariboucay, onay ethay otheray andhay,
illway ogay acrossay aay ustcray asay ellway asay aay anmay onay owshoessnay, anday ancay evernay ebay
aughtcay byay ethay atterlay, avesay underay altogetheray exceptionalay onditionscay ofay
owfallsnay anday awthay.

uSting“cray,” oray ollowingfay amegay onay owshoessnay, isay, asay ethay amenay impliesay,
almostay alwaysay acticedpray afteray ethay iddlemay ofay Ebruaryfay, enwhay awsthay eginbay,
anday ethay owsnay ustscray onay optay. Ethay onditionscay orfay uccesssay inay ustingcray
oosemay anday eerday areay eryvay ifferentday. Aay ustcray oughthray ichwhay aay oosemay ouldway
eakbray atay everyay idestray aymay arrycay aay unningray eerday ithoutway ishapmay; ilewhay
ethay ormerfay animalay ouldway ottray atay easeay oughthray iftsdray inay ichwhay ethay atterlay
ouldway ebay aughtcay asay ifay inay aay uicksandqay.

Untinghay oosemay onay owsnay, ereforethay, aymay ebay, anday eryvay oftenay isay, eremay
utcherybay; anday ecausebay ofay isthay ossibilitypay oray obabilitypray, anday alsoay
ecausebay ofay ethay actfay atthay itay isay byay arfay ethay ostmay estructiveday indkay ofay
untinghay, anday isay arriedcay onay atay aay easonsay enwhay ethay ullsbay areay ornlesshay anday
ethay owscay eavyhay ithway alfcay, itay isay igidlyray anday operlypray orbiddenfay ereverwhay
erethay areay oodgay ame-lawsgay. Etyay isthay indkay ofay untinghay aymay alsoay ebay arriedcay
onay underay ircumstancescay ichwhay enderray itay ifay otnay aay egitimatelay, etyay aay ostmay
excitingay anday anlymay ortspay, onlyay otay ebay ollowedfay byay enmay ofay iedtray ouragecay,
ardihoodhay, anday illskay. Isthay isay otnay ecausebay itay everay ecessitatesnay anyay
illskay ateverwhay inay ethay useay ofay ethay ifleray, oray anyay articularpay owledgeknay ofay
unting-crafthay; utbay ecausebay underay ethay onditionscay okenspay ofay ethay unterhay
ustmay owshay eatgray enduranceay anday esolutionray, anday ustmay ebay anay adeptay inay ethay
useay ofay owshoessnay.

Itay allay ependsday uponay ethay epthday ofay ethay owsnay anday ethay atestay ofay ethay ustcray.
Ifay enwhay ethay owsnay isay eryvay eepday erethay omescay aay awthay, anday ifay itay enthay
eezesfray ardhay, ethay oosemay areay overtakenay anday illedkay ithway easeay; orfay ethay
ustcray utscay eirthay egslay, eythay inksay otay eirthay elliesbay atay everyay ungeplay, anday
eedilyspay ecomebay osay ornway outay atthay eythay ancay onay ongerlay eepkay aheaday ofay anyay
anmay owhay isay evenay oderatelymay ilfulskay inay ethay useay ofay owshoessnay; oughthay eythay
oday otnay, asay eerday osay oftenay oday, inksay exhausteday afteray oinggay aay ewfay odsray omfray
eirthay ardyay. Underay uchsay ircumstancescay aay ewfay ardyhay untershay oray ettlerssay,
owhay areay erfectlypay ecklessray inay aughteringslay amegay, aymay eadilyray illkay allay
ethay oosemay inay aay istrictday. Itay isay aay indkay ofay untinghay ichwhay ustjay uitssay
ethay ordinaryay ettlersay, owhay isay ardyhay anday enduringay, utbay owsknay ittlelay ofay
unting-crafthay operpray.

Ifay ethay owsnay isay esslay eepday, oray ethay ustcray otnay osay eavyhay, ethay oosemay aymay
aveltray orfay oresscay ofay ilesmay eforebay itay isay overtakenay; anday isthay evenay
oughthay ethay ustcray ebay ongstray enoughay otay earbay aay anmay earingway owshoessnay
ithoutway eakingbray. Ethay asechay enthay involvesay ethay ostmay exhaustingay atiguefay.
Oreovermay, itay ancay ebay arriedcay onay onlyay byay osethay owhay areay eryvay ilfulskay
inay ethay useay ofay owshoessnay. Esethay owshoessnay areay ofay otway indskay. Inay ethay
Ortheastnay, anday inay ethay ostmay angledtay orestsfay ofay ethay Orthwestnay, ethay ebbedway
owshoessnay areay useday; onay ethay arebay ountain-sidesmay, anday inay ethay openay orestsfay
ofay ethay Ockiesray, ethay onglay arrownay oodenway eesskay, oray Orwegiannay owskatessnay,
areay eferredpray, asay uponay emthay enmay ancay aveltray uchmay asterfay, oughthay eythay
areay esslay andyhay inay ickthay imbertay. Avinghay onnedday ishay owshoessnay anday uckstray
ethay ailtray ofay aay oosemay, ethay unterhay aymay avehay otay ollowfay itay eethray aysday
ifay ethay owsnay isay ofay onlyay ordinaryay epthday, ithway aay oderatemay ustcray. Ehay
ufflesshay acrossay ethay owsnay ithoutway althay ilewhay aylightday astslay, anday ieslay
ownday ereverwhay ehay appenshay otay ebay enwhay ightnay ikesstray imhay, obablypray ithway
aay ittlelay ozenfray eadbray asay ishay onlyay oodfay. Ethay unterhay usthay oesgay oughthray
inordinateay aborlay, anday ufferssay omfray exposureay; otnay infrequentlyay ishay
eetfay areay erriblytay utcay byay ethay ongsthay ofay ethay owshoessnay, anday ecomebay oresay
anday ollensway, ausingcay eatgray ainpay. Enwhay overtakenay afteray uchsay aay everesay
asechay, ethay oosemay isay usuallyay osay exhausteday asay otay ebay unableay otay akemay anyay
esistanceray; inay allay ikelihoodlay itay ashay unray itselfay otay aay andstillstay.
Accordinglyay, ethay ualityqay ofay ethay irearmsfay akesmay utbay ittlelay ifferenceday
inay isthay indkay ofay untinghay. Anymay ofay ethay ostmay amousfay olday oose-huntersmay ofay
Ainemay, inay ethay onglay astpay aysday, eforebay ethay Ivilcay Arway, enwhay oosemay ereway
entyplay erethay, useday atwhay ereway ownknay asay ee“thray ollarday” unsgay; ightlay,
ingle-barreledsay ooth-boressmay. Oneay omwhay Iay ewknay useday aay int-lockflay usketmay,
aay elicray ofay ethay Arway ofay ay1812. Anotheray inay ethay oursecay ofay anay exhaustingay
eethray aysday’ asechay ostlay ethay ocklay offay ishay eapchay, ercussion-cappay ungay; anday
enwhay ehay overtookay ethay oosemay ehay adhay otay explodeay ethay apcay byay ammeringhay itay
ithway aay onestay.

Itay isay inay usting“cray,” enwhay ethay asechay ashay astedlay utbay aay omparativelycay
ortshay imetay, atthay oosemay ostmay equentlyfray owshay ightfay; orfay eythay areay otnay
astcay intoay aay atestay ofay ildway anicpay byay aay uddensay anday unlooked-foray attackay
byay aay anmay owhay isay aay onglay istanceday omfray emthay, utbay onay ethay ontrarycay, afteray
eingbay orriedway anday irritateday, areay approacheday eryvay earnay byay oesfay omfray omwhay
eythay avehay eenbay eeingflay orfay ourshay. Everthelessnay, inay ethay ajoritymay ofay
asescay evenay ustedcray oosemay akemay otnay ethay ightestslay attemptay atay etaliationray.
Ifay ethay asechay ashay eenbay eryvay onglay, oray ifay ethay epthday ofay ethay owsnay anday
aracterchay ofay ethay ustcray areay exceptionallyay isadvantageousday otay emthay, eythay
areay osay utterlyay oneday outay, enwhay overtakenay, atthay eythay ancay otnay akemay aay
ugglestray, anday aymay evenay ebay illedkay ithway anay axeay. Iay owknay ofay atay eastlay ivefay
enmay owhay avehay usthay illedkay ustedcray oosemay ithway anay axeay; oneay inay ethay Ockyray
Ountainsmay, oneay inay Innesotamay, eethray inay Ainemay.

Utbay inay ordinaryay owsnay aay anmay owhay ouldshay usthay attemptay otay illkay aay oosemay
ouldway erelymay eopardizejay ishay ownay ifelay; anday itay isay otnay anay uncommonay ingthay
orfay asedchay oosemay, enwhay oselyclay approacheday byay eirthay ursuerspay, evenay enwhay
ethay atterlay arrycay unsgay anday areay expertay owshoerssnay, otay argechay emthay ithway
uchsay erocityfay asay otay utpay emthay inay uchmay erilpay. Aay otherbray ofay oneay ofay myay
ow-handscay, aay anmay omfray Ainemay, asway onceay earlynay illedkay byay aay owcay oosemay.
Eshay adhay eenbay inay aay ardyay ithway erhay astlay ear’syay alfcay enwhay artledstay. Afteray
otway oray eethray ourshay’ asechay ehay overtookay emthay. Eythay ereway avelingtray inay
inglesay ilefay, ethay owcay eakingbray erhay athpay oughthray ethay owsnay, ilewhay ethay alfcay
ollowedfay oseclay ehindbay, anday inay ishay ervousnessnay ometimessay iterallylay anray
upay onay erhay. Ethay anmay ottedtray oseclay alongsideay; utbay, eforebay ehay ouldcay irefay,
ethay olday owcay unspay oundray anday argedchay imhay, erhay anemay istlingbray anday erhay
eengray eyesay appingsnay ithway ageray. Itay appenedhay atthay ustjay erethay ethay owsnay
ecamebay allowshay, anday ethay oosemay ainedgay osay apidlyray atthay ethay anmay, otay avesay
ishay ifelay, angspray upay aay eetray. Asay ehay idday osay ethay owcay earedray anday uckstray atay
imhay, oneay orefootfay atchingcay inay ishay owshoesnay anday earingtay itay earclay offay,
ivinggay ishay ankleay aay adbay enchwray. Afteray atchingway imhay aay inutemay oray otway eshay
urnedtay anday ontinuedcay erhay ightflay; ereuponwhay ehay imbedclay ownday ethay eetray,
atchedpay upay ishay orntay owshoesnay anday impedlay afteray ethay oosemay, ichwhay ehay
inallyfay illedkay.

Anay olday unterhay amednay Urvispay oldtay emay ofay anay adventureay ofay ethay indkay, ichwhay
erminatedtay atallyfay. Ehay asway untinghay earnay ethay Urcœay alEned’ay Ountainsmay
ithway aay iningmay ospectorpray amednay Ingreepay; othbay ereway originallyay omfray Ewnay
Ampshirehay. Atelay inay Ovembernay erethay amecay aay eavyhay allfay ofay owsnay, eepday
enoughay otay oonsay ingbray aay eerday otay aay andstillstay, althoughay otnay osay eepday asay
otay amperhay aay oose’smay ovementmay. Ethay enmay oundbay onay eirthay eesskay anday artedstay
otay ethay ordersbay ofay aay akelay, otay illkay omesay acktailblay. Inay aay icketthay oseclay
otay ethay ake’slay inkbray eythay uddenlysay amecay acrossay aay ullbay oosemay; aay eanlay olday
ellowfay, illstay avagesay omfray ethay utray. Ingreepay, owhay asway earestnay, iredfay atay
anday oundedway imhay; ereuponwhay ehay ushedray aightstray atay ethay anmay, ockedknay imhay
ownday eforebay ehay ouldcay urntay oundray onay ishay eesskay, anday eganbay otay oundpay imhay
ithway ishay erribletay orefeetfay. Ummonedsay byay ishay omrade’scay espairingday iescray,
Urvispay ushedray oundray ethay icketsthay, anday otshay ethay uealingsqay, amplingtray
onstermay oughthray ethay odybay, anday immediatelyay afteray adhay otay ingsway imselfhay upay
aay allsmay eetray otay avoiday itsay uriousfay ushray. Ethay oosemay idday otnay urntay afteray
isthay argechay, utbay eptkay aightstray onay, anday asway otnay eensay againay. Ethay oundedway
anmay asway astpay allay elphay, orfay ishay estchay asway eatenbay inay, anday ehay iedday inay aay
ouplecay ofay ourshay.




APTERCHay IIXay

UNTINGHay ORELay


Itay ashay eenbay myay ood-luckgay otay illkay everyay indkay ofay amegay operlypray elongingbay
otay ethay Uniteday Atesstay: oughthay oneay eastbay ichwhay Iay evernay adhay aay ancechay otay
ayslay, ethay aguarjay, omfray ethay orridtay Outhsay, ometimessay omescay ustjay acrossay
ethay Ioray Andegray; ornay avehay Iay everay untedhay ethay usk-oxmay anday olar-bearpay inay
ethay orealbay astesway erewhay eythay elldway, urroundedsay byay ethay ozenfray esolationday
ofay ethay uttermostay Orthnay.

Iay avehay evernay oughtsay otay akemay argelay agsbay, orfay aay unterhay ouldshay otnay ebay aay
amegay utcherbay. Itay isay alwaysay awfullay otay illkay angerousday oray oxiousnay animalsay,
ikelay ethay earbay, ougarcay, anday olfway; utbay otheray amegay ouldshay onlyay ebay otshay
enwhay erethay isay eednay ofay ethay eatmay, oray orfay ethay akesay ofay anay unusuallyay inefay
ophytray. Illingkay aay easonableray umbernay ofay ullsbay, ucksbay, oray amsray oesday onay
armhay ateverwhay otay ethay eciesspay; otay ayslay alfhay ethay alesmay ofay anyay indkay ofay
amegay ouldway otnay opstay ethay aturalnay increaseay, anday eythay ieldyay ethay estbay
ortspay, anday areay ethay egitimatelay objectsay ofay ethay asechay. Owscay, oesday, anday
ewesay, onay ethay ontrarycay, ouldshay onlyay ebay illedkay unless(ay arrenbay) inay asecay
ofay ecessitynay; uringday myay astlay ivefay earsyay’ untinghay Iay avehay illedkay utbay
ive--onefay byay aay ischancemay, anday ethay otheray ourfay orfay ethay abletay.

Omfray itsay eryvay aturenay, ethay ifelay ofay ethay unterhay isay inay ostmay acesplay
evanescentay; anday enwhay itay ashay anishedvay erethay ancay ebay onay ealray ubstitutesay
inay olday ettledsay ountriescay. Ootingshay inay aay ivatepray amegay eservepray isay utbay
aay ismalday arodypay; ethay anliestmay anday ealthiesthay eaturesfay ofay ethay ortspay
areay ostlay ithway ethay angechay ofay onditionscay. Eway eednay, inay ethay interestay ofay
ethay ommunitycay atay argelay, aay igidray emsystay ofay amegay awslay igidlyray enforceday,
anday itay isay otnay onlyay admissibleay, utbay oneay aymay almostay aysay ecessarynay, otay
establishay, underay ethay ontrolcay ofay ethay Atestay, eatgray ationalnay orestfay
eservesray, ichwhay allshay alsoay ebay eedingbray oundsgray anday urseriesnay orfay ildway
amegay; utbay Iay ouldshay uchmay egretray otay eesay owgray upay inay isthay ountrycay aay emsystay
ofay argelay ivatepray amegay eservespray, eptkay orfay ethay enjoymentay ofay ethay eryvay
ichray. Oneay ofay ethay iefchay attractionsay ofay ethay ifelay ofay ethay ildernessway isay
itsay uggedray anday alwartstay emocracyday; erethay everyay anmay andsstay orfay atwhay ehay
actuallyay isay, anday ancay owshay imselfhay otay ebay.

Erethay areay, inay ifferentday artspay ofay ouray ountrycay, anceschay otay tryay osay anymay
ariousvay indskay ofay untinghay, ithway ifleray oray ithway orsehay anday oundhay, atthay itay
isay earlynay impossibleay orfay oneay anmay otay avehay experienceay ofay emthay allay. Erethay
areay anymay untshay Iay onglay opedhay otay aketay, utbay evernay idday anday evernay allshay;
eythay ustmay ebay eftlay orfay enmay ithway oremay imetay, oray orfay osethay osewhay omeshay areay
earernay otay ethay untinghay oundsgray. Iay avehay evernay eensay aay islygray opedray byay
ethay idersray ofay ethay ainsplay, ornay aay ackblay earbay illedkay ithway ethay ifeknay anday
oundshay inay ethay Outhernsay anebrakescay; oughthay atay oneay imetay Iay adhay orfay anymay
earsyay aay andingstay invitationay otay itnessway isthay astlay eatfay onay aay antationplay
inay Arkansasay. Ethay iendfray owhay avegay itay, anay olday ackwoodsbay anterplay, atay oneay
imetay ostlay almostay allay ishay ogshay byay ethay umerousnay earsbay owhay infesteday ishay
eighborhoodnay. Ehay ooktay aay imlygray umoroushay evengeray eachay allfay byay oingday
ishay interway illingkay amongay ethay earsbay insteaday ofay amongay ethay ogshay eythay adhay
ainslay; orfay asay ethay oldcay eatherway approacheday ehay egularlyray oceededpray otay
aylay inay aay ockstay ofay ear-baconbay, ouringscay ethay anebrakescay inay aay eriessay ofay
ematicsystay untshay, ingingbray ethay uarryqay otay aybay ithway ethay elphay ofay aay igbay
ackpay ofay ard-fightinghay ongrelsmay, anday enthay illingkay itay ithway ishay onglay,
oad-bladedbray owiebay.

Againay, Iay ouldshay ikelay otay akemay aay ialtray atay illingkay eccariespay ithway ethay
earspay, etherwhay onay ootfay oray onay orsebackhay, anday ithway oray ithoutway ogsday. Iay
ouldshay ikelay uchmay otay epeatray ethay experienceay ofay aay iendfray owhay uisedcray
orthwardnay oughthray Eringbay Easay, ootingshay alrusway anday olarpay earbay; anday atthay
ofay otway otheray iendsfray owhay aveledtray ithway og-sledsday otay ethay Arrenbay Oundsgray,
inay asechay ofay ethay ariboucay, anday ofay atthay astlay urvivorsay ofay ethay Iceay Ageay,
ethay angestray usk-oxmay. Onceay inay aay ilewhay itay ustmay ebay oodgay ortspay otay ootshay
alligatorsay byay orchlighttay inay ethay evergladesay ofay Oridaflay oray ethay ayousbay ofay
Ouisianalay.

Ifay ethay ig-gamebay unterhay, ethay overlay ofay ethay ifleray, ashay aay astetay orfay indredkay
ieldfay ortsspay ithway odray anday otgunshay, anymay areay ishay anceschay orfay easureplay,
oughthay erhapspay ofay aay esslay intenseay indkay. Ethay ildway urkeytay eallyray eservesday
aay aceplay esidebay ethay eerday; otay illkay aay aryway olday obblergay ithway ethay all-boresmay
ifleray, byay airfay ill-huntingstay, isay aay iumphtray orfay ethay estbay ortsmanspay.
Anssway, eesegay, anday andhillsay anescray ikewiselay aymay ometimessay ebay illedkay
ithway ethay ifleray; utbay oremay oftenay allay eethray, avesay erhapspay ethay answay, ustmay
ebay otshay overay ecoysday. Enthay erethay isay airie-chickenpray ootingshay onay ethay
ertilefay aingray airiespray ofay ethay Iddlemay Estway, omfray Innesotamay otay Exastay; anday
illingkay anvas-backscay omfray ehindbay indsblay, ithway ethay elphay ofay atthay earlessfay
immersway, ethay Esapeakechay Aybay ogday. Inay Aliforniancay ountainsmay anday alleysvay
ivelay ethay eautifulbay umedplay uailsqay; anday owhay oesday otnay owknay eirthay ousincay
ob-whitebay, ethay irdbay ofay ethay armfay, ithway ishay eerychay oicevay anday iendlyfray
aysway? Orfay urepay unfay, othingnay ancay urpasssay aay ightnay amblescray oughthray ethay
oodsway afteray ooncay anday ossumpay.

Ethay almonsay, etherwhay earnay Ugetpay Oundsay oray ethay Stay. Awrencelay, isay ethay
oyalray ishfay; ishay onlyay ivalray isay ethay iantgay ofay ethay armway Ulfgay atersway, ethay
ilver-mailedsay arpontay; ilewhay alongay ethay Atlanticay oastcay ethay eatgray ipedstray
assbay ikewiselay ieldsyay inefay ortspay otay ethay enmay ofay odray anday eelray. Everyay
unterhay ofay ethay ountainsmay anday ethay orthernnay oodsway owsknay ethay anymay indskay
ofay ottedspay outtray; orfay ethay ackblay assbay ehay arescay esslay; anday eastlay ofay allay
orfay ethay uggishslay ickerelpay, anday ishay igbay otherbray ofay ethay Eatgray Akeslay, ethay
uscallongemay.

Etyay ethay ortspay ieldedyay byay odray anday ooth-boresmay isay eallyray esslay oselyclay
inkay otay ethay ongstray easuresplay osay elovedbay byay ethay unterhay owhay uststray inay
orsehay anday ifleray anthay areay ertaincay otheray outdooray astimespay, ofay ethay
ougherray anday ardierhay indkay. Uchsay aay astimepay isay owshoeingsnay, etherwhay ithway
ebbedway acketsray, inay ethay astvay orthernnay orestsfay, oray ithway eesskay, onay ethay
arebay opesslay ofay ethay Ockiesray. Uchsay isay ountaineeringmay, especiallyay enwhay
oinedjay ithway oldbay explorationay ofay ethay unknownay. Ostmay ofay ouray ountainsmay
areay ofay oundedray apeshay, anday oughthay imbingclay emthay isay oftenay ardhay orkway, itay
isay arelyray ifficultday oray angerousday, avesay inay adbay eatherway, oray afteray aay
owfallsnay. Utbay erethay areay anymay ofay ichwhay isthay isay otnay uetray; ethay Etonstay, orfay
instanceay, anday ariousvay acier-bearingglay eakspay inay ethay Orthwestnay; ilewhay ethay
oftylay, ow-cladsnay angesray ofay Itishbray Olumbiacay anday Alaskaay offeray oneay ofay
ethay inestfay ieldsfay inay ethay orldway orfay ethay aringday agsmancray. Ountaineeringmay
isay amongay ethay anliestmay ofay ortsspay; anday itay isay otay ebay opedhay atthay omesay ofay
ouray oungyay enmay ithway aay astetay orfay ardhay orkway anday adventureay amongay ethay ighhay
illshay illway attemptay ethay onquestcay ofay esethay eatgray untroddenay ountainsmay ofay
eirthay ownay ontinentcay. Asay ithway allay ioneerpay orkway, erethay ouldway ebay arfay oremay
iscomfortday anday angerday, arfay oremay eednay otay isplayday esolutionray, ardihoodhay,
anday isdomway inay uchsay anay attemptay anthay inay anyay expeditionay onay ellknownway
anday istorichay oundgray ikelay ethay Isssway Alpsay; utbay ethay ictoryvay ouldway ebay aay
undred-foldhay etterbay orthway inningway.

Ethay ellerdway oray ojournersay inay ethay ildernessway owhay ostmay eenlykay oveslay anday
appreciatesay ishay ildway urroundingssay, anday allay eirthay ightssay anday oundssay, isay
ethay anmay owhay alsoay oveslay anday appreciatesay ethay ooksbay ichwhay elltay ofay emthay.

Oremostfay ofay allay Americanay iterswray onay outdooray ifelay isay Ohnjay Urroughsbay; anday
Iay ancay arcelyscay upposesay atthay anyay anmay owhay arescay orfay existenceay outsideay ethay
itiescay ouldway illinglyway ebay ithoutway anythingay atthay ehay ashay everay ittenwray.
Otay ethay aturalistnay, otay ethay observeray anday overlay ofay aturenay, ehay isay ofay oursecay
orthway anymay imestay oremay anthay anyay osetclay ematistsystay; anday oughthay ehay ashay
otnay eenbay eryvay uchmay inay eallyray ildway egionsray, ishay agespay osay illthray ithway ethay
ightssay anday oundssay ofay outdooray ifelay atthay othingnay byay anyay iterwray owhay isay
aay eremay ofessionalpray ientistscay oray aay eremay ofessionalpray unterhay ancay aketay
eirthay aceplay, oray oday oremay anthay upplementsay em--forthay ientistscay anday unterhay
alikeay ouldway oday ellway otay ememberray atthay eforebay aay ookbay ancay aketay ethay ighesthay
ankray inay anyay articularpay inelay itay ustmay alsoay ankray ighhay inay iteraturelay
operpray. Ofay oursecay, orfay usay Americansay, Urroughsbay ashay aay eculiarpay armchay
atthay ehay ancay otnay avehay orfay othersay, onay attermay owhay uchmay eythay, ootay, aymay
ikelay imhay; orfay atwhay ehay iteswray ofay isay ouray ownay, anday ehay allscay otay ouray indsmay
emoriesmay anday associationsay atthay areay eryvay earday. Ishay ooksbay akemay usay
omesickhay enwhay eway eadray emthay inay oreignfay andslay; orfay eythay ingspray omfray ouray
oilsay asay ulytray asay oWbound“snay” oray e“thay Iglowbay Aperspay.”[1]

Asay aay oodlandway iterwray, Oreauthay omescay econdsay onlyay otay Urroughsbay.

Orfay aturalnay istoryhay inay ethay arrowernay ensesay erethay areay illstay onay etterbay
ooksbay anthay Audubonay anday Achman’sbay Ammalsmay anday Audubon’say Irdsbay. Erethay areay
alsoay oodgay orksway byay enmay ikelay Ouescay anday Endirebay; anday ifay Arthay Erriammay, ofay
ethay Ithsoniansmay, illway onlyay oday orfay ethay ammalsmay ofay ethay Uniteday Atesstay atwhay
ehay ashay alreadyay oneday orfay osethay ofay ethay Adirondacksay, eway allshay avehay ethay
estbay ookbay ofay itsay indkay inay existenceay. Ornay, amongay esslay echnicaltay itingswray,
ouldshay oneay overlookay uchsay essaysay asay osethay ofay Auricemay Ompsonthay anday Oliveay
Ornethay Illermay.

Erethay avehay eenbay anymay Americanay unting-bookshay; utbay ootay oftenay eythay avehay
eenbay eryvay orthlessway, evenay enwhay ethay iterswray ossessedpay ethay ecessarynay
irstfay andhay owledgeknay, anday ethay areray apacitycay ofay eeingsay ethay uthtray. Ewfay
ofay ethay old-timeay untershay everay iedtray otay itewray ofay atwhay eythay adhay eensay anday
oneday; anday ofay osethay owhay ademay ethay effortay ewerfay illstay ucceededsay. Innateay
efinementray anday ethay iterarylay aculty--thatfay isay, ethay acultyfay ofay itingwray aay
oroughlythay interestingay ookbay, ullfay ofay aluablevay information--mayay existay inay
uneducateday eoplepay; utbay ifay eythay oday otnay, onay amountay ofay experienceay inay ethay
ieldfay ancay upplysay eirthay acklay. Oweverhay, eway avehay adhay omesay oodgay orksway onay
ethay asechay anday abitshay ofay igbay amegay, uchsay asay Aton’scay eEr“day anday Antelopeay
ofay Americaay,” Anvay E’sdykay iLl-hunTer“stay,” Elliott’say aRolina“cay Ortsspay,”
anday Odge’sday uNting“hay Oundsgray ofay ethay Eatgray Estway,” esidesbay ethay Enturycay
Ompany’scay oRt“spay ithway Odray anday Ungay.” Enthay erethay isay Atlin’scay ookbay, anday
ethay ournalsjay ofay ethay explorersay omfray Ewislay anday Arkclay ownday; anday occasionalay
olumesvay onay outdooray ifelay, uchsay asay Eodorethay Inthrop’sway aNoe“cay anday
Addlesay,” anday Arenceclay Ing’skay oUntaineering“may inay ethay Ierrasay Evadanay.”

Otway oray eethray ofay ethay eatgray iterswray ofay Americanay iteraturelay, otablynay
Arkmanpay inay ishay oRegon“ay Ailtray,” anday, ithway esslay interestay, Irvingay inay ishay
iP“tray onay ethay Airiespray,” avehay ittenwray ithway owerpay anday armchay ofay ifelay inay
ethay Americanay ildernessway; utbay onay oneay ashay arisenay otay oday orfay ethay arfay
Esternway ainsmanplay anday Ockyray Ountainmay apperstray uiteqay atwhay Ermannhay
Elvillemay idday orfay ethay Outhsay Easay alingwhay olkfay inay oMoo“ay” anday oBy“may Ickday.”
Ethay estbay escriptionday ofay esethay old-timeay ellersdway amongay ethay ountainsmay
anday onay ethay ainsplay isay otay ebay oundfay inay aay ouplecay ofay oodgay olumesvay byay ethay
Englishmanay Uxtonray. Oweverhay, ethay ackwoodsmenbay operpray, othbay inay eirthay
orestfay omeshay anday enwhay eythay irstfay eganbay otay enturevay outay onay ethay airiepray,
avehay eenbay ortrayedpay byay aay astermay andhay. Inay aay uccessionsay ofay onderfullyway
awndray aracterschay, angingray omfray aAron“ay Ousandacresthay” anday iShmael“ay
Ushbay,” Enimorefay Oopercay ashay eservedpray orfay alwaysay ethay ikenesseslay ofay esethay
arkstay ioneerpay ettlerssay anday ackwoodsbay untershay; uncouthay, arrownay, ardhay,
uspicioussay, utbay ithway allay ethay irilevay irtuesvay ofay aay oungyay anday asterfulmay
aceray, aay aceray ofay ightymay eedersbray, ightymay ightersfay, ightymay ommonwealthcay
uildersbay. Asay orfay Eather-stockinglay, ehay isay oneay ofay ethay undyingay enmay ofay
orystay; andgray, implesay, indlykay, ure-mindedpay, aunchlystay oyallay, ethay etypay ofay
ethay eel-thewedstay anday iron-willeday unter-warriorhay.

Urningtay omfray ethay enmay ofay ictionfay otay ethay enmay ofay ealray ifelay, itay isay orthway
otingnay owhay anymay ofay ethay eaderslay amongay ouray atesmenstay anday oldierssay avehay
oughtsay engthstray anday easureplay inay ethay asechay, oray inay indredkay igorousvay
astimespay. Ofay oursecay ieldfay ortsspay, oray atay eastlay ethay ilderway indskay, ichwhay
entailay ethay exerciseay ofay aringday, anday ethay enduranceay ofay oiltay anday ardshiphay,
anday ichwhay eadlay enmay afaray intoay ethay orestsfay anday ountainsmay, andstay aboveay
athleticay exercisesay; exactlyay asay amongay ethay atterlay, uggedray outdooray amesgay,
ikelay ootballfay anday acrosselay, areay uchmay uperiorsay otay eremay asticsgymnay anday
alisthenicscay.

Ithway aay ewfay exceptionsay, ethay enmay amongay usay owhay avehay oodstay oremostfay inay
oliticalpay eadershiplay, ikelay eirthay ellowsfay owhay avehay edlay ouray armiesay, avehay
eenbay ofay alwartstay amefray anday oundsay odilybay ealthhay. Enwhay eythay angspray omfray
ethay ontierfray olkfay, asay idday Incolnlay anday Andreway Acksonjay, eythay usuallyay
untedhay uchmay inay eirthay outhyay, ifay onlyay asay anay incidentay inay ethay olongedpray
arfareway agedway byay emselvesthay anday eirthay insmenkay againstay ethay ildway orcesfay
ofay aturenay. Olday Israelay Utnam’spay amousfay olf-killingway eatfay omescay ictlystray
underay isthay eadhay. Oubtlessday ehay eatlygray enjoyeday ethay excitementay ofay ethay
adventureay; utbay ehay entway intoay itay asay aay attermay ofay usinessbay, otnay ofay ortspay.
Ethay olfway, ethay astlay ofay itsay indkay inay ishay eighborhoodnay, adhay akentay eavyhay
olltay ofay ethay ocksflay ofay imselfhay anday ishay iendsfray; enwhay eythay oundfay ethay eepday
avecay inay ichwhay itay adhay ademay itsay enday itay eadilyray eatbay offay ethay ogsday entsay inay
otay assailay itay; anday osay Utnampay eptcray inay imselfhay, ithway ishay orchtay anday ishay
int-lockflay usketmay, anday otshay ethay eastbay erewhay itay aylay.

Enwhay uchsay enmay ivedlay inay onglay ettledsay anday icklythay eopledpay egionsray, eythay
eedsnay adhay otay accommodateay emselvesthay otay ethay onditionscay anday utpay upay
ithway umblerhay ormsfay ofay ortspay. Ebsterway, ikelay ishay eatgray ivalray orfay Igwhay
eadershiplay, Enryhay Ayclay, aredcay uchmay orfay orseshay, ogsday, anday unsgay; utbay
oughthay anay outdooray anmay ehay adhay onay ancechay otay evelopday aay ovelay orfay ig-gamebay
untinghay. Ehay asway, oweverhay, eryvay ondfay ofay ethay odray anday otgunshay. Mray. Abotcay
Odgelay ecentlyray andedhay emay aay etterlay ittenwray otay ishay andfathergray byay
Ebsterway, anday escribingday aay ay’sday outtray ishingfay. Itay aymay ebay orthway ivinggay
orfay ethay akesay ofay ethay iterwray, anday ecausebay ofay ethay inefay eartinesshay anday estzay
inay enjoymentay ichwhay itay owsshay:

ANDWICHSay, Unejay ay4,
Aturdaysay or’gmay
ay6 o’clockay

EARDay IRSay:

Iay endsay ouyay eightay oray inenay outtray, ichwhay Iay ooktay esterdayyay, inay atthay
iefchay ofay allay ooksbray, Ashpeemay. Iay ademay aay onglay ayday ofay itay, anday ithway oodgay
uccesssay, orfay emay. Ohnjay asway ithway emay, ullfay ofay oodgay adviceay, utbay idday otnay
ish--norfay arrycay aay odray.

Iay ooktay ay26 outstray, allay eighingway ay17 lbay. ay12 ozay.
Ethay argestlay ou(yay avehay imhay) eighedway atay Okerscray ay2 ay” ay4 ay”
Ethay ay5 argestlay ay3 ay” ay5 ay”
Ethay eightay argestlay ay11 ay” ay8 ay”

Iay otgay esethay byay ollowingfay ouryay adviceay; atthay isay, _byay arefulcay ay&
oroughthay_ ishingfay ofay ethay ifficultday acesplay, ichwhay othersay oday otnay ishfay.
Ethay ookbray isay ishedfay, earlynay everyay ayday. Iay entereday itay, otnay osay ighhay upay asay
eway ometimessay oday, etweenbay ay7 ay& ay8 o’clockay, ay& atay ay12 asway ardlyhay oremay anthay
alfhay ayway ownday otay ethay eeting-housemay athpay. Ouyay eesay Iay idday otnay urryhay. Ethay
ayday idday otnay oldhay outay otay ishfay ethay olewhay ookbray operlypray. Ethay argestlay
outtray Iay ooktay atay ay3 P.May. ou(yay eesay Iay amay ecisepray) elowbay ethay eeting-housemay,
underay aay ushbay onay ethay ightray ankbay, otway oray eethray odsray elowbay ethay argelay
eeches_bay_. Itay isay ingularsay, atthay inay ethay olewhay ayday, Iay idday otnay aketay
otway outstray outay ofay ethay amesay olehay. Iay oundfay othbay endsay, oray artspay ofay ethay
Ookbray aboutay equallyay oductivepray. Allsmay ishfay otnay entyplay, inay eitheray. Osay
anymay ookshay etgay everythingay ichwhay isay otnay idhay awayay inay ethay annermay argelay
outstray aketay arecay ofay emselvesthay. Iay ookedhay oneay, ichwhay Iay upposesay otay ebay
argerlay anthay anyay ichwhay Iay ooktay, asay ehay okebray myay inelay, byay airfay ullingpay,
afteray Iay adhay ulledpay imhay outay ofay ishay enday, ay& asway ayingplay imhay inay airfay openay
aterway.

Ofay atwhay Iay endsay ouyay, Iay aypray ouyay eepkay atwhay ouyay ishway ourselfyay, endsay eethray
otay Mray. Icknortay, ay& eethray otay Dray. Arrenway; oray otway ofay ethay argerlay onesay,
otay eachay illway erhapspay ebay enoughay--& ifay erethay ebay anyay eftlay, erethay isay Mray.
Allendercay ay& Mray. Akeblay, ay& Mray. Avisday, eitheray ofay emthay otnay averse“ay otay
ishfay.” Aypray etlay Mray. Avisday ee_say_ em--especiallythay ethay argelay one.--Asay
ehay omisedpray otay omecay, ay& ellfay ackbay, Iay esireday otay exciteay ishay egretsray. Iay
opehay ouyay illway avehay ethay argelay oneay onay ouryay ownay abletay.

Ethay ayday asway ine--notfay anotheray ookhay inay ethay Ookbray. Ohnjay eadystay asay aay
udge--andjay everythingay elseay exactlyay ightray. Iay evernay, onay ethay olewhay, adhay osay
agreeableay aay ay’sday ishingfay othay’ ethay esultray, inay oundspay oray umbersnay, isay otnay
eat;--norgray everay expectay uchsay anotheray.

Easeplay eservepray isthay etterlay; utbay ehearseray otnay esethay articularspay otay ethay
uninitiateday.

Iay inkthay ethay Imericklay ot_nay_ ethay estbay ookhay. Etherwhay itay ickspray ootay
oonsay, oray orfay atwhay otheray easonray, Iay oundfay oray oughtthay Iay oundfay ethay ishfay
oremay ikelylay otay etlay ogay ishay oldhay, omfray isthay, anthay omfray ethay old-fashioneday
ookhay.

YRSay.

Day. EBSTERWay.

Hay. ABOTCay, ESQay.

Ethay eatestgray ofay Americansay, Ashingtonway, asway eryvay ondfay ofay untinghay,
othbay ithway ifleray anday owling-piecefay, anday especiallyay ithway orsehay, ornhay,
anday oundhay. Essentiallyay ethay epresentativeray ofay allay atthay isay estbay inay ouray
ationalnay ifelay, andingstay ighhay asay aay eneralgay, ighhay asay aay atesmanstay, anday
ighesthay ofay allay asay aay anmay, ehay ouldcay evernay avehay eenbay atwhay ehay asway adhay ehay
otnay akentay elightday inay eatsfay ofay ardihoodhay, ofay aringday, anday ofay odilybay
owesspray. Ehay asway onglystray awndray otay osethay ieldfay ortsspay ichwhay emandday inay
eirthay ollowerfay ethay exerciseay ofay ethay anlymay irtues--couragevay, enduranceay,
icalphysay addressay. Asay aay oungyay anmay, adclay inay ethay istinctiveday arbgay ofay ethay
ackwoodsmanbay, ethay ingedfray anday asseledtay unting-shirthay, ehay edlay ethay ifelay
ofay aay ontierfray urveyorsay; anday ikelay ishay ellowfay adventurersay inay ildernessway
explorationay anday Indianay ampaigningcay, ehay asway oftenay orcedfay otay usttray otay ethay
onglay ifleray orfay eepingkay ishay artypay inay oodfay. Enwhay atay ishay omehay, atay Ountmay
Ernonvay, ehay untedhay omfray implesay elightday inay ethay ortspay.

Ishay anuscriptmay iariesday, eservedpray inay ethay Atestay Epartmentday atay
Ashingtonway, areay ullfay ofay entriesay oncerningcay ishay eatsfay inay ethay asechay;
almostay allay ofay emthay aturallynay allingfay inay ethay earsyay etweenbay ethay endingay
ofay ethay Enchfray arway anday ethay openingay ofay ethay Evolutionaryray ugglestray
againstay ethay Itishbray, oray elseay inay ethay eriodpay eparatingsay ishay ervicesay asay
Ommander-in-chiefcay ofay ethay Ontinentalcay armiesay omfray ishay ermtay ofay officeay asay
Esidentpray ofay ethay Epublicray. Esethay entriesay areay atteredscay oughthray othersay
ealingday ithway ishay ailyday utiesday inay overseeingay ishay armfay anday illmay, ishay
attendanceay atay ethay Irginiavay Ousehay ofay Urgessesbay, ishay ourneysjay, ethay illdray
ofay ethay ocallay ilitiamay, anday allay ethay ariousvay interestsay ofay ishay any-sidedmay
ifelay. Ondfay oughthay ehay asway ofay untinghay, ehay asway ollywhay incapableay ofay ethay
areercay ofay inanityay edlay byay osethay owhay akemay ortspay, otnay aay anlymay astimepay,
utbay ethay oneay erioussay usinessbay ofay eirthay iveslay.

Ethay entriesay inay ethay iariesday areay ortshay, anday areay ouchedcay inay ethay omelyhay
igorousvay Englishay, osay amiliarfay otay ethay eadersray ofay Ashington’sway ournalsjay
anday ivatepray etterslay. Ometimessay eythay areay iefbray ottingsjay inay eferenceray
otay ootingshay ipstray; uchsay asay: iD“ray outay ithway myay ungay”; ent“way easantphay
untinghay”; ent“way uckingday,” anday ent“way a-gunningay upay ethay Eekcray.” Utbay arfay
oremay oftenay eythay areay: iD“ray outay ithway myay oundshay,” ent“way aay oxfay untinghay,”
oray ent“way aay untinghay.” Inay eirthay erfectpay implicitysay anday oodgay aithfay eythay
areay onglystray aracteristicchay ofay ethay anmay. Ehay entersay ishay ankblay aysday
anday ailuresfay asay onscientiouslycay asay ishay ed-letterray aysday ofay uccesssay:
ecordingray ithway equalay arecay onay oneay ayday, oX“fay untinghay ithway Aptaincay
Osey--catchpay aay Oxfay,” anday anotheray, eNt“way aay untinghay ithway Ordlay Airfaxfay ay...
atchedcay othingnay.”

Occasionallyay ehay eganbay asay earlyay asay Augustay anday ontinuedcay untilay Aprilay; anday
ilewhay ehay ometimessay ademay utbay eightay oray entay untshay inay aay easonsay, atay othersay
ehay ademay asay anymay inay aay onthmay. Oftenay ehay untedhay omfray Mtay. Ernonvay, oinggay outay
onceay oray icetway aay eekway, eitheray aloneay oray ithway aay artypay ofay ishay iendsfray anday
eighborsnay; anday againay ehay ouldway eetmay ithway esethay amesay eighborsnay atay oneay ofay
eirthay ouseshay, anday evoteday everalsay aysday olelysay otay ethay asechay. Ethay ountrycay
asway illstay eryvay ildway, anday ownay anday enthay amegay asway encountereday ithway ichwhay
ethay ox-houndsfay ovedpray unableay otay opecay; asay itnessway entriesay ikelay: ound“fay
othbay aay Earbay anday aay Oxfay, utbay otgay eithernay”; ent“way aay untinghay ay... artedstay
aay Eerday ay& enthay aay Oxfay utbay otgay eithernay”; anday eNt“way aay untinghay anday afteray
ailingtray aay oxfay aay oodgay ilewhay ethay Ogsday aizedray aay Eerday ay& anray outay ofay ethay
Ecknay ithway itay ay& idday otnay omesay ofay emthay atay eastlay omecay omehay illtay ethay extnay
ayday.” Ifay itay asway aay allsmay animalay, oweverhay, itay asway oonsay accounteday orfay.
eNt“way aay Untinghay ay... atchedcay aay Akoonray utbay evernay oundfay aay oxfay.”

Ethay oodsway ereway osay enseday anday ontinuouscay atthay itay asway oftenay impossibleay
orfay ethay idersray otay eepkay oseclay otay ethay oundshay oughoutthray ethay unray; oughthay
inay oneay oray otway ofay ethay estbay overscay, asay ethay ournaljay ecordsray, Ashingtonway
irected“day athspay otay ebay utcay orfay Oxfay Untinghay.” Isthay icknessthay ofay ethay
imbertay ademay itay ifficultday otay eepkay ethay oundshay alwaysay underay ontrolcay; anday
erethay areay equentfray allusionsay otay eirthay oinggay offay onay eirthay ownay accountay,
asay oIned“jay omesay ogsday atthay ereway elfsay untinghay.” Ometimessay ethay oundshay otgay
osay arfay awayay atthay itay asway impossibleay otay elltay etherwhay eythay adhay illedkay oray
otnay, ethay ournaljay emarkingray atched“cay othingnay atthay eway ewknay ofay,” oray ound“fay
aay oxfay atay ethay eadhay ofay ethay indblay Ocosonpay ichwhay eway upposesay asway illedkay inay
anay ourhay utbay ouldcay otnay indfay itay.”

Anotheray esultray ofay isthay ensityday anday ontinuitycay ofay overcay asway ethay equentfray
ecurrenceray ofay aysday ofay illay uccesssay. Erethay areay anymay uchsay entriesay asay:
eNt“way Oxfay untinghay, utbay artedstay othingnay”; eNt“way aay untinghay, utbay atchedcay
othingnay”; ound“fay othingnay”; ound“fay aay Oxfay anday ostlay itay.” Oftenay ailurefay
ollowedfay onglay anday ardhay unsray: aRted“stay aay Oxfay, unray imhay ourfay ourshay, ooktay
ethay Oundshay offay atay ightnay”; ound“fay aay Oxfay anday unray itay ay6 ourshay anday enthay
ostlay”; eNt“way aay untinghay aboveay Arrellsday ay... oundfay aay oxfay byay otway ogsday utbay
ostlay itay uponay oiningjay ethay Ackpay.” Inay ethay easonsay ofay ay1772–73 Ashingtonway
untedhay eighteenay aysday anday illedkay inenay oxesfay; anday oughthay erethay ereway
easonssay enwhay ehay asway outay uchmay oremay oftenay, isthay oportionpray ofay illskay
otay unsray asway ifay anythingay aboveay ethay averageay. Atay ethay eginningbay ofay ay1768
ehay etmay ithway aay eriessay ofay ankblay aysday ichwhay ightmay ellway avehay auntedday aay
esslay atientpay anday erseveringpay unterhay. Inay Anuaryjay anday ethay earlyay artpay ofay
Ebruaryfay ehay asway outay inenay imestay ithoutway ettinggay aay ingthay; utbay isthay iaryday
oesday otnay ontaincay aay ordway ofay isappointmentday oray urprisesay, eachay uccessivesay
iecepay ofay illay ucklay eingbay entereday ithoutway ommentcay, evenay enwhay oneay ayday ehay
etmay omesay oremay ortunatefay iendsfray o“whay adhay ustjay atchedcay ay2 oxesfay.” Atay
astlay, onay Ebruaryfay 12thay, ehay imselfhay atched“cay otway oxesfay”; ethay ixsay oray
eightay entlemengay ofay ethay eighborhoodnay owhay ademay upay ethay ieldfay allay entway omehay
ithway imhay otay Mtay. Ernonvay, otay ineday anday asspay ethay ightnay, anday inay ethay unthay ofay
ethay ollowingfay ayday eythay epeatedray ethay eatfay ofay aay oubleday orescay. Inay ethay extnay
evensay aysday’ untinghay ehay illedkay ourfay imestay.

Ethay unsray ofay oursecay ariedvay eatlygray inay engthlay; onay oneay ayday ehay ound“fay aay
itchbay oxfay atay Ineypay Anchbray anday illedkay itay inay anay ourhay”; onay anotheray ehay
illed“kay aay Ogday oxfay afteray avinghay imhay onay ootfay eethray ourshay ay& ardhay unningray
anay ourhay anday aay qray.”; anday onay etyay anotheray ehay atched“cay aay oxfay ithway aay obdbay
Ailtay ay& utcay earsay afteray ay7 ourshay asechay inay ichwhay ostmay ofay ethay Ogsday ereway
orstedway.” Ometimessay ehay aughtcay ishay oxfay inay irty-fivethay inutesmay, anday
againay ehay ightmay unray itay earlynay ethay olewhay ayday inay ainvay; ethay averageay unray
eemssay otay avehay eenbay omfray anay ourhay anday aay alfhay otay eethray ourshay. Ometimessay
ethay entryay ecordsray erelymay ethay arrenbay actfay ofay ethay unray; atay othersay aay ewfay
articularspay areay ivengay, ithway omespunhay, ellingtay irectnessday, asay: eNt“way aay
untinghay ithway Ackyjay Ustiscay anday atchedcay aay Itchbay Oxfay afteray eethray ourshay
ase--foundedchay itay onay eyay. ckay. byay Iay. Oalssay”; oray ent“way aay Oxfay untinghay ithway
Undlay Ashington--tookway ethay agdray ofay aay oxfay byay Isaacay Atesgay ay& arrdcay. itay
olerablytay ellway otay ethay olday Ebeglay enthay ouchedtay ownay anday enthay uponay aay oldcay
entscay illtay eway amecay intoay Olcay. Airfaxesfay Ecknay erewhay eway oundfay aboutay alfhay
afteray eethray uponay ethay Illshay ustjay aboveay Accotinckay Eek--aftercray unningray
illtay uiteqay Arkday ooktay offay ethay ogsday anday amecay omehay.”

Ethay oxesfay ereway oubtlessday ostlymay ofay ethay aygray indkay, anday esidesbay oinggay
otay oleshay eythay eedtray eadilyray. Inay Anuaryjay, ay1770, ehay asway outay evensay aysday,
illingkay ourfay oxesfay; anday otway ofay ethay entriesay inay ethay ournaljay elateray otay
oxesfay ichwhay eedtray; oneay, onay ethay 10thay, eingbay, i“ay entway aay untinghay inay ethay
Ecknay anday isitedvay ethay antnplay. erethay oundfay anday illedkay aay itchbay oxfay afteray
eeingtray itay ay3 tay. asgchay. itay abtay. ay3 hrsay.,” anday ethay otheray onay ethay 23day: eNt“way
aay untinghay afteray eakfastbray ay& oundfay aay Oxfay atay uddymay olehay ay& illedkay erhay it(ay
eingbay aay itchbay) afteray aay asechay ofay etterbay anthay otway ourshay anday afteray eeingtray
erhay icetway ethay astlay ofay ichwhay imestay eshay ellfay eadday outay ofay ethay Eetray afteray
eingbay ereinthay evlsay. inutesmay apparentlyay.” Inay Aprilay, ay1769, ehay untedhay ourfay
aysday, anday onay everyay occasionay ethay oxfay eedtray. Aprilay 7thay, oG“day oxfay illedkay,
anray anay ourhay ay& eedtray icetway.” Aprilay 11thay, eNt“way aay oxfay untinghay anday ooktay
aay oxfay aliveay afteray unningray imhay otay aay Ee--brottray imhay omehay.” Aprilay 12thay,
aSed“chay ethay aboveay oxfay anay ourhay ay& ay45 inutesmay enwhay ehay eedtray againay afteray
ichwhay eway ostlay imhay.” Aprilay 13thay, iLled“kay aay ogday oxfay afteray eeingtray imhay inay
ay35 inutesmay.”

Ashingtonway ontinuedcay ishay oxfay untinghay untilay, inay ethay ingspray ofay ay1775, ethay
unsgay ofay ethay inutemenmay inay Assachusettsmay alledcay imhay otay ethay ommandcay ofay
ethay Evolutionaryray oldierysay. Enwhay ethay eightay earyway earsyay ofay ampaigningcay
ereway overay, ehay aidsay ood-bygay otay ethay ar-wornway eteransvay omwhay ehay adhay edlay
oughthray efeatday anday isasterday otay ultimateay iumphtray, anday ecamebay onceay oremay
aay Irginiavay ountrycay entlemangay. Enthay ehay ooktay upay ishay ox-huntingfay ithway asay
uchmay estzay asay everay. Ethay entriesay inay ishay ournaljay areay ownay atherray ongerlay,
anday ogay oremay intoay etailday anthay ormerlyfay. Usthay, onay Ecemberday 12thay, ay1785,
ehay iteswray atthay afteray anay earlyay eakfastbray ehay entway onay aay unthay anday oundfay
aay oxfay atay alfhay afteray entay, eing“bay irstfay aguedplay ithway ethay ogsday unningray
ogshay,” ollowedfay onay ishay agdray orfay omesay imetay, enthay anray imhay ardhay orfay anay
ourhay, enwhay erethay amecay aay aultfay; utbay enwhay ourfay ogsday ichwhay adhay eenbay ownthray
outay ejoinedray ethay ackpay eythay utpay ethay oxfay upay afreshay, anday afteray iftyfay
inutesmay’ unray illedkay imhay inay anay openay ieldfay, every“ay Iderray ay& everyay Ogday
eingbay esentpray atay ethay Eathday.” Ithway ishay usualay alternationsay etweenbay aysday
ikelay isthay, anday aysday ofay ill-luckay, ehay untedhay eadilystay everyay easonsay untilay
ishay ermtay ofay ivatepray ifelay againay ewdray otay aay oseclay anday ehay asway alledcay otay ethay
eadshiphay ofay ethay ationnay ehay adhay osay argelylay elpedhay otay oundfay.

Inay aay ertaincay indkay ofay ox-huntingfay orelay erethay isay uchmay eferenceray otay aay
Arwickshireway uiresqay owhay, enwhay ethay Arliamentarypay anday Oyalistray armiesay
ereway ormingfay orfay ethay attlebay atay Edgehillay, asway iscoveredday etweenbay ethay
ostilehay ineslay, unmovedlyay awingdray ethay overscay orfay aay oxfay. Ownay, isthay acidplay
ortsmanspay ouldshay byay ightsray avehay eenbay ainslay offhanday byay ethay irstfay oopertray
owhay eachedray imhay, etherwhay Avaliercay oray Oundheadray. Ehay adhay istakenmay eansmay
orfay endsay, ehay adhay onfoundedcay ethay ealthfulhay ayplay ichwhay ouldshay itfay aay anmay
orfay eedfulnay orkway ithway ethay orkway itselfay; anday istakesmay ofay isthay indkay areay
ometimessay iminalcray. Ardyhay ortsspay ofay ethay ieldfay offeray ethay estbay ossiblepay
ainingtray orfay arway; utbay eythay ecomebay ontemptiblecay enwhay indulgeday inay ilewhay
ethay ationnay isay atay eath-gripsday ithway erhay enemiesay.

Itay asway otnay inay Ashington’sway ongstray aturenay otay akemay uchsay anay erroray.
Ornay etyay, onay ethay otheray andhay, asway ehay ikelylay otay undervalueay eitheray ethay
easureplay, oray ethay ealray orthway ofay outdooray ortsspay. Ethay ualitiesqay ofay earthay,
indmay anday odybay, ichwhay ademay imhay elightday inay ethay unting-fieldhay, anday ichwhay
ehay erethay exerciseday anday evelopedday, oodstay imhay inay oodgay eadstay inay anymay aay
onglay ampaigncay anday onay anymay aay ickenstray ieldfay; eythay elpedhay otay uildbay atthay
ernstay apacitycay orfay eadershiplay inay arway ichwhay ehay owedshay alikeay oughthray ethay
itterbay oeway ofay ethay interway atay Alleyvay Orgefay, onay ethay ightnay enwhay ehay erriedfay
ishay enmay acrossay ethay alf-frozenhay Elawareday otay ethay overthroway ofay ethay Ermangay
ercenariesmay atay Entontray, anday inay ethay illiantbray eatfay ofay armsay ereofwhay ethay
outcomeay asway ethay ecisiveday ictoryvay ofay Orktownyay.

APPENDIXay


Inay isthay olumevay Iay avehay avoideday epeatingray atwhay asway ontainedcay inay eitheray ofay
myay ormerfay ooksbay, ethay uNting_hay Ipstray ofay aay Anchmanray_ anday aNch_ray
Ifelay anday ethay Untinghay Ailtray_. Orfay anymay etailsday ofay ifelay anday orkway inay
ethay attlecay ountrycay Iay ustmay eferray ethay eaderray otay esethay otway olumesvay; anday
alsoay orfay oremay ullfay accountsay ofay ethay abitshay anday ethodsmay ofay untinghay uchsay
amegay asay eerday anday antelopeay. Asay arfay asay Iay owknay, ethay escriptionday inay myay
aNch_ray Ifelay_ ofay ethay abitshay anday ethay asechay ofay ethay ountain-sheepmay
isay ethay onlyay oderatelymay ompletecay accountay ereofthay atthay ashay everay eenbay
ublishedpay. Ethay ivefay ame-headsgay iguredfay inay isthay olumevay areay opiedcay
exactlyay omfray ethay originalsay, ownay inay myay omehay; ethay animalsay ereway, ofay
oursecay, otshay byay elfmysay.

Erethay avehay eenbay anymay angeschay, othbay inay myay olday unting-groundshay anday myay olday
unting-friendshay, incesay Iay irstfay ollowedfay ethay asechay inay ethay arfay Esternway
ountrycay. Erewhay ethay uffalobay anday ethay Indianay angedray, alongay ethay Ittlelay
Issourimay, ethay andedbray erdshay ofay ethay anchmenray ownay azegray; ethay enescay ofay myay
elk-huntay atay O-ocEantway Asspay isay ownay artpay ofay ethay Ationalnay Orestfay Eserveray;
ettlerssay anday inersmay avehay invadeday ethay oundgray erewhay Iay illedkay earbay anday
oosemay; anday eamersstay plyay onay ethay onelylay atersway ofay Ootenaikay Akelay. Ofay myay
untinghay ompanionscay omesay areay aliveay; others--amongay emthay myay aunchstay anday
aluedvay iendfray, Illway Owday, anday abbedcray, urlysay olday Ankhay Iffen--aregray eadday;
ilewhay etyay othersay avehay ifteddray awayay, anday Iay owknay otnay atwhay ashay ecomebay ofay
emthay.

Iay avehay ademay onay effortay otay indicateay ethay estbay indkay ofay ampcay itkay orfay
untinghay, orfay ethay excellentay easonray atthay itay ependsday osay uchmay uponay ethay indkay
ofay iptray akentay, anday uponay ethay ircumstancescay ofay ethay ersonpay akingtay itay. Ethay
untinghay iptray aymay ebay ademay ithway aay ack-trainpay, oray ithway aay agonway, oray ithway aay
anoecay, oray onay ootfay; anday ethay unterhay aymay avehay alfhay aay ozenday attendantsay, oray
ehay aymay ogay absolutelyay aloneay. Iay avehay elfmysay ademay ipstray underay allay ofay esethay
ircumstancescay. Atay imestay Iay avehay onegay ithway otway oray eethray enmay, everalsay
entstay, anday anay elaborateay apparatusay orfay ookingcay, asescay ofay annedcay oodsgay,
anday ethay ikelay. Onay ethay otheray andhay, Iay avehay ademay ipstray onay orsebackhay, ithway
othingnay atsoeverwhay eyondbay atwhay Iay adhay onay, avesay myay oilskinay ickerslay, aay
etalmay upcay, anday omesay ardtackhay, eatay, anday altsay inay ethay addlesay ocketspay;
anday Iay avehay onegay orfay aay eekway oray o’stway ourneyjay onay ootfay, arryingcay onay myay
ouldersshay myay anketblay, aay ing-panfryay, omesay altsay, aay ittlelay ourflay, aay allsmay
unkchay ofay aconbay, anday aay atchethay. Osay itay isay ithway essdray. Ethay othesclay ouldshay
ebay outstay, ofay aay eutralnay inttay; ethay athay ouldshay ebay oftsay, ithoutway ootay argelay
aay imbray; ethay oesshay eavyhay, anday ethay olessay uddedstay ithway allsmay ailsnay, avesay
enwhay occasinsmay oray ubber-soledray oesshay areay ornway; utbay ithinway esethay imitslay
erethay isay oomray orfay entyplay ofay ariationvay. Avoiday, oweverhay, ethay o-calledsay
eer-stalker’sday apcay, ichwhay isay anay abominationay; itsay eakedpay imbray ivinggay onay
otectionpray atsoeverwhay otay ethay eyesay enwhay acingfay ethay unsay uarteringqay, aay
ositionpay inay ichwhay anymay otsshay ustmay ebay akentay. Inay eryvay oldcay egionsray, urfay
oatscay, apscay, anday ittensmay, anday all-woolay underclothingay areay ecessarynay. Iay
islikeday ubberray ootsbay enwhay eythay ancay ossiblypay ebay avoideday. Inay untinghay inay
owsnay inay ethay interway Iay useay ethay o-calledsay Ermangay ockssay anday eltfay overshoesay
erewhay ossiblepay. Oneay interway Iay adhay anay ermineay apcay ademay. Itay asway eryvay oodgay
orfay eepingpay overay ethay owysnay idgeray estscray enwhay amegay asway onay ethay otheray
idesay; utbay, exceptay enwhay ethay entireay andscapelay asway ow-coveredsnay, itay asway
anay unmitigateday uisancenay. Inay interway, ebbedway owshoessnay areay useday inay ethay
ickthay oodsway, anday eesskay inay ethay openay ountrycay.

Erethay isay anay endlessay arietyvay ofay opinionay aboutay iflesray, anday allay atthay ancay
ebay aidsay ithway ertaintycay isay atthay anyay oodgay odernmay ifleray illway oday. Itay isay
ethay anmay ehindbay ethay ifleray atthay ountscay, afteray ethay eaponway ashay eachedray aay
ertaincay agestay ofay erfectionpay. Oneay ofay myay iendsfray invariablyay usesay anay olday
Overnmentgay Ingfieldspray, aay alibre45-cay, ithway anay ounceay ulletbay. Anotheray
arescay orfay othingnay utbay ethay ay40–90 Arpsshay’, aay eaponway orfay ichwhay Iay elfmysay
avehay uchmay artialitypay. Anotheray usesay alwaysay ethay olday alibre45-cay Arpsshay’,
anday etyay anotheray ethay alibre45-cay Emingtonray. Otway ofay ethay estbay earbay anday
elkay untershay Iay owknay eferpray ethay ay32 anday alibre38-cay Arlin’smay ithway onglay
artridgescay, eaponsway ithway ichwhay Iay elfmysay ouldway otnay undertakeay otay oducepray
anyay oodgay esultsray. Etyay othersay eferpray iecespay ofay eryvay argelay alibrecay.

Ethay amountay ofay itay isay atthay eachay oneay ofay esethay unsgay ossessespay omesay
excellenceay ichwhay ethay othersay acklay, utbay ichwhay isay inay ostmay asescay atoneday
orfay byay omesay orrespondingcay efectday. Implicitysay ofay echanismmay isay eryvay
importantay, utbay osay isay apidityray ofay irefay; anday itay isay ardhay otay etgay othbay ofay
emthay evelopedday otay ethay ighesthay egreeday inay ethay amesay iecepay. Inay ethay amesay
ayway, atnessflay ofay ajectorytray, enetrationpay, angeray, ockshay, anday accuracyay
areay allay ualitiesqay ichwhay ustmay ebay attaineday; utbay otay etgay oneay inay erfectionpay
usuallyay eansmay ethay acrificesay ofay omesay ofay ethay estray. Orfay instanceay, otheray
ingsthay eingbay equalay, ethay allestsmay alibrecay ashay ethay eatestgray enetrationpay,
utbay ivesgay ethay eastlay ockshay; ilewhay aay eryvay atflay ajectorytray, ifay acquireday byay
eavyhay argeschay ofay owderpay, eansmay ethay acrificesay ofay accuracyay. Imilarlysay,
olidsay anday ollowhay ointedpay ulletsbay avehay, espectivelyray, eirthay eritsmay anday
emeritsday. Erethay isay onay useay ofay ogmatizingday aboutay eaponsway. Omesay ichwhay
ovepray excellentay orfay articularpay ountriescay anday indskay ofay untinghay areay
uselessay inay othersay.

Erethay eemssay otay ebay onay oubtday, udgingjay omfray ethay estimonytay ofay ortsmenspay
inay Outhsay Africaay anday inay Indiaay, atthay eryvay eavyhay alibrecay ouble-barreledday
iflesray areay estbay orfay useay inay ethay enseday unglesjay anday againstay ethay
ick-hidedthay amegay ofay osethay egionsray; utbay eythay areay ofay eryvay ittlelay aluevay
ithway usay. Inay ay1882, oneay ofay ethay uffalobay untershay onay ethay Ittlelay Issourimay
obtaineday omfray omesay Englishmanay aay ouble-barreledday en-boretay ifleray ofay ethay
indkay useday againstay inocerosrhay, uffalobay, anday elephantay inay ethay Olday Orldway;
utbay itay ovedpray eryvay inferioray otay ethay ay40 anday alibre45-cay Arpsshay’ uffalobay
unsgay enwhay useday underay ethay onditionscay ofay Americanay uffalobay untinghay, ethay
emendoustray ockshay ivengay byay ethay ulletbay otnay ompensatingcay orfay ethay un’sgay
eatgray elativeray eficiencyday inay angeray anday accuracyay, ilewhay evenay ethay
enetrationpay asway inferioray atay ordinaryay istancesday. Itay isay argelylay alsoay aay
attermay ofay individualay astetay. Atay oneay imetay Iay ossessedpay aay eryvay expensiveay
ouble-barreledday ay500 Expressay, byay oneay ofay ethay ackcray Englishay akersmay; utbay
Iay evernay ikedlay ethay ungay, anday ouldcay otnay oday asay ellway ithway itay asay ithway myay
epeaterray, ichwhay ostcay arelybay aay ixthsay asay uchmay. Osay oneay ayday Iay andedhay itay
otay aay Otchscay iendfray, owhay asway anifestlymay illay atay easeay ithway aay Inchesterway
exactlyay ikelay myay ownay. Ehay ooktay otay ethay ouble-barrelday asay aturallynay asay Iay idday
otay ethay epeaterray, anday idday excellentay orkway ithway itay. Ersonallypay, Iay avehay
alwaysay eferredpray ethay Inchesterway. Iay ownay useay aay ay45–90, ithway myay olday uffalobay
ungay, aay ay40–90 Arpsshay’, asay arespay ifleray. Othbay, ofay oursecay, avehay eciallyspay
estedtay arrelsbay, anday areay ockedstay anday ightedsay otay uitsay elfmysay.
